 GauravaVilasa
haribhaktivilāsaḥ
prathamo vilāsaḥ
atha maṅgalācaraṇam
caitanyadevaṃ bhagavantam āśraye
śrīvaiṣṇavānāṃ pramude'ñjasā likhan 
āvaśyakaṃ karma vicārya sādhubhiḥ
sārdhaṃ samāhṛtya samastaśāstrataḥ  Hbhv 
bhakter vilāsāṃś cinute prabodhā
nandasya śiṣyo bhagavatpriyasya 
gopālabhaṭṭo raghunāthadāsaṃ
santoṣayan rūpasanātanau ca  Hbhv 
mathurānāthapādābjapremabhaktivilāsataḥ 
jātaṃ bhaktivilāsākhyaṃ tadbhaktāḥ śīlayantv imam  Hbhv 
jīyāsur ātyantikabhaktiniṣṭhāḥ śrīvaiṣṇavā māthuramaṇḍale'tra 
kāśīśvaraḥ kṛṣṇavane cakāstu śrīkṛṣṇadāsaś ca salokanāthaḥ  Hbhv 
tatra lekhyapratijñā
ādau sakāraṇaṃ lekhyaṃ śrīgurvāśrayaṇaṃ tataḥ 
guruḥ śiṣyaḥ parīkṣādir bhagavān manavo 'sya ca  Hbhv 
mantrādhikārī siddhyādiśodhanaṃ mantrasaṃskriyāḥ 
dīkṣā nityaṃ brāhmakāle śubhotthānaṃ pavitratā 
prātaḥ smṛtyādi kṛṣṇasya vādyādaiś ca prabodhanam  Hbhv 
nirmālyottāraṇādyādau maṅgalārātrikaṃ tataḥ 
maitrādikṛtyaṃ śaucācamanaṃ dantasya dhāvanam  Hbhv 
snānaṃ tāntrikasandhyādi devasadmādisaṃskriyā  Hbhv 
tulasyādyāhṛtir gehasnānam uṣṇodakādikam 
vastraṃ pīṭhaṃ cordhvapuṇḍraṃ śrīgopīcandanādikam  Hbhv 
cakrādimudrā mālā ca gṛhasandhyārcanaṃ guroḥ 
māhātmyaṃ cātha kṛṣṇasya dvāraveśmāntarārcanam  Hbhv 
pūjārthāsanam arghyādisthāpanaṃ vighnavāraṇam 
śrīgurvādinatir bhūtaśuddhiḥ prāṇaviśodhanam  Hbhv 
nyāsamudrāpañcakaṃ ca kṛṣṇadhyānāntarārcane 
pūjā padāni śrīmūrtiśālagrāmaśilās tathā  Hbhv 
dvārakodbhavacakrāṇi śuddhayaḥ pīṭhapūjanam 
āvāhanādi tanmudrā āsanādisamarpaṇam  Hbhv 
snapanaṃ śaṅkhaghaṇṭādivādyaṃ nāmasahasrakam 
purāṇapāṭho vasanam upavītaṃ vibhūṣaṇam  Hbhv 
gandhaḥ śrītulasīkāṣṭhacandanaṃ kusumāni ca 
patrāṇi tulasī cāṅgopāṅgāvaraṇapūjanam  Hbhv 
dhūpo dīpaś ca naivedyaṃ pānaṃ homo balikriyā 
avagaṇḍūṣādyāsyavāso divyagandhādikaṃ punaḥ  Hbhv 
rājopacārā gītādi mahānīrājanaṃ tathā 
śaṅkhādivādanaṃ sāmbuśaṅkhanīrājanaṃ stutiḥ  Hbhv 
natiḥ pradakṣiṇā karmādyarpaṇaṃ japa yācane 
āgaḥkṣamāpaṇaṃ nānāgāṃsi nirmālyadhāraṇam  Hbhv 
śaṅkhāmbutīrthaṃ tulasīpūjā tanmṛttikādi ca 
dhātrīsnānaniṣedhasya kālo vṛtter upārjanam  Hbhv 
madhyāhne vaiśadevādiśrāddhaṃ cānarpyam acyute 
vinārcām aśane doṣās tathānarpitabhojane  Hbhv 
naivedyabhakṣaṇaṃ santaḥ satsaṅgo 'sadasaṅgatiḥ 
asadgatir vaiṣṇavopahāsanindādiduṣphalam  Hbhv 
satāṃ bhaktir viṣṇuśāstraṃ śrīmadbhāgavataṃ tathā 
līlākathā ca bhagavaddharmāḥ sāyaṃ nijakriyāḥ  Hbhv 
karmapātaparīhāras trikālārcā viśeṣataḥ 
naktaṃ kṛtyānyatho pūjāphalasiddhyādidarśanam  Hbhv 
viṣṇvarthadānaṃ vividhopacārā nyūnapūraṇam 
śayanaṃ mahimārcāyāḥ śrīmannāmnas tathādbhutaḥ  Hbhv 
nāmāparādhā bhaktiś ca premāthāśrayaṇādayaḥ 
pakṣeṣv ekādaśī sāṅgā śrīdvādaśyaṣṭakaṃ mahat  Hbhv 
kṛtyāni mārgaśīrṣādimāseṣu dvādśeṣv api 
puraścaraṇakṛtyāni mantraṃ siddhasya lakṣaṇam  Hbhv 
mūrtyāvirbhāvanaṃ mūrtipratiṣṭhā kṛṣṇamandiram 
jīrṇoddhṛtiḥ śrītulasīvivāho 'nanyakarma ca  Hbhv 
tatra śrīgurūpasattikāraṇam
kṛpayā kṛṣṇadevasya tadbhaktajanasaṅgataḥ 
bhakter māhātmyam ākarṇya tām icchan sadguruṃ bhajet  Hbhv 
atrānubhūyate nityaṃ duḥkhaśreṇī paratra ca 
duḥsahā śrūyate śāstrāt titīrṣed api tāṃ sudhīḥ  Hbhv 
tathā coktam ekādaśaskandhe BhP 
labdhvā sudurlabham idaṃ bahusambhavānte
mānuṣyam arthadam anityam apīha dhīraḥ 
tūrṇaṃ yateta na pated anumṛtyu yāvan
niḥśreyasāya viṣayaḥ khalu sarvataḥ syāt  Hbhv 
svayaṃ śrībhagavatā ca BhP 
nṛdeham ādyaṃ sulabhaṃ sudurlabhaṃ
plavaṃ sukalpaṃ gurukarṇadhāram 
mayānukūlena nabhasvateritaṃ
pumān bhavābdhiṃ na taret sa ātmahā  Hbhv 
atha śrīgurūpasattiḥ
tatraiva śrīprabuddhayogeśvaroktau BhP 
tasmād guruṃ prapadyeta jijñāsuḥ śreya uttamam 
śābde pare ca niṣṇātaṃ brahmaṇy upaśamāśrayam  Hbhv 
svayaṃ śrībhagavaduktau BhP 
madabhijñaṃ guruṃ śāntam upāsīta madātmakam  Hbhv 
kramadīpikāyāṃ  ca 
vipraṃ pradhvastakāmaprabhṛtiripughaṭaṃ nirmalāṅgaṃ gariṣṭhāṃ
bhaktiṃ kṛṣṇāṅghripaṅkeruhayugalarajorāgiṇīm udvahantam 
vettāraṃ vedaśāstāgamavimalapathāṃ sammataṃ satsu dāntaṃ
vidyāṃ yaḥ saṃvivitsuḥ pravaṇatanumanā deśikaṃ saṃśrayeta  Hbhv 
śrutāv api MuṇḍU  ChāU  
tadvijñānārthaṃ sa gurum evābhigacchet samitpāṇiḥ śrotriyaṃ brahmaniṣṭham 
ācāryavān puruṣo veda  Hbhv 
atha gurūpasattinityatā
śrībhāgavate daśamaskandhe śrutistutau BhP 
vijitahṛṣīkavāyubhir adāntamanas turagaṃ
ya iha yatanti yantum atilolam upāyakhidaḥ 
vyasanaśatānvitāḥ samavahāya guroś caraṇaṃ
vaṇija ivāja santy akṛtakarṇadharā jaladhau  Hbhv 
śrutau ca KaṭhU 
naiṣā tarkeṇa matir āpaneyā
proktānyenaiva sujñānāya preṣṭha  Hbhv 
atha viśeṣataḥ śrīguror lakṣaṇāni
mantramuktāvalyām 
avadātānvayaḥ śuddhaḥ svocitācāratatparaḥ 
āśramī krodharahito vedavit sarvaśāstravit  Hbhv 
śraddhāvān anasūyaś ca priyavāk priyadarśanaḥ 
śuciḥ suveśas taruṇaḥ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ  Hbhv 
dhīmān anuddhatamatiḥ pūrṇo 'hantā vimarśakaḥ 
saguṇo 'rcāsu kṛtadhīḥ kṛtajñaḥ śiṣyavatsalaḥ  Hbhv 
nigrahānugrahe śakto homamantraparāyaṇaḥ 
ūhāpohaprakārajñaḥ śuddhātmā yaḥ kṛpālayaḥ 
ity ādilakṣaṇair yukto guruḥ syād garimānidhiḥ  Hbhv 
agastyasaṃhitāyāṃ ca 
devatopāsakaḥ śānto viṣayeṣv api niḥspṛhaḥ 
adhyātmavid brahmavādī vedaśāstrārthakovidaḥ  Hbhv 
uddhartuṃ caiva saṃhartuṃ samartho brāhmaṇottamaḥ 
tattvajño yantramantrāṇāṃ marmabhettā rahasyavit  Hbhv 
puraścaraṇakṛd dhomamantrasiddhaḥ prayogavit 
tapasvī satyavādī ca gṛhastho gurur ucyate  Hbhv 
viṣṇusmṛtau 
paricaryāyaśolābhalipsuḥ śiṣyād gurur nahi 
kṛpāsindhuḥ susampūrṇaḥ sarvasattvopakārakaḥ  Hbhv 
niḥspṛhaḥ sarvataḥ siddhaḥ sarvavidyāviśāradaḥ 
sarvasaṃśayasaṃchettā nālaso gurur āhṛtaḥ  Hbhv 
śrīnāradapañcarātre śrībhagavannāradasaṃvāde 
brāhmaṇaḥ sarvakālajñaḥ kuryāt sarveṣv anugraham 
tadabhāvād dvijaśreṣṭhaḥ śāntātmā bhagavanmayaḥ  Hbhv 
bhāvitātmā ca sarvajñaḥ śāstrajñaḥ satkriyāparaḥ 
siddhitrayam āyukta ācāryatve'bhiṣecitaḥ  Hbhv 
kṣatraviṭśūdrajātīnāṃ kṣatriyo 'nugrahe kṣamaḥ 
kṣatriyasyāpi ca guror bhāvād īdṛśo yadi  Hbhv 
vaiśyaḥ syāt tena kāryaś ca dvaye nityam anugrahaḥ 
sajātīyena śūdreṇa tādṛśena mahāmate 
anugrahābhiṣekau ca kāryau śūdrasya sarvadā  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca 
varṇottam'tha ca gurau sati yā viśrute'pi ca 
svadeśato 'that vānyatra nedaṃ kāryaṃ śubhārthinā  Hbhv 
vidyamāne tu yaḥ kuryāt yatra tatra viparyayam 
tasyehāmutra nāśaḥ syāt tasmāc chāstroktam ācaret 
kṣatraviṭśūdrajātīyaḥ prātilomyaṃ na dīkṣayet  Hbhv 
pādme ca PadmaP 
mahābhāgavataḥ śreṣṭho brāhmaṇo vai gurur nṛṇām 
sarveṣām eva lokānām asau pūjyo yathā hariḥ  Hbhv 
mahākūlaprasūto 'pi sarvayajñeṣu dīkṣitaḥ 
sahasraśākhādhyāyī ca na guruḥ syād avaiṣṇavaḥ  Hbhv  iti
gṛhītaviṣṇudīkṣāko viṣṇupūjāparo naraḥ 
vaiṣṇavo 'bhihito 'bhijñair itaro 'smād avaiṣṇavaḥ  Hbhv 
tattvasāgare
bahvāśī dīrghasūtrī ca viṣayādiṣu lolupaḥ 
hetuvādarato duṣṭo 'vāgvādī guṇanindakaḥ  Hbhv 
aromā bahuromā ca ninditāśramasevakaḥ 
kāladanto 'sitauṣṭhaś ca durgandhiśvāsavāhakaḥ  Hbhv 
duṣṭalakṣaṇasampanno yadyapi svayam īśvaraḥ 
bahupratigrhāsakta ācāryaḥ śrīkṣayāvahaḥ  Hbhv 
atha śiṣyalakṣaṇāni
mantramuktāvalyām
śiṣyaḥ śuddhānvayaḥ śrīmān vinītaḥ priyadarśanaḥ 
satyavāk puṇyacarito 'dabhradhīr dambhavarjitaḥ  Hbhv 
kāmakrodhaparityāgī bhaktaś ca gurupādayoḥ 
devatāpravaṇaḥ kāyamanovāgbhir divāniśam  Hbhv 
nīrujo nirjitāśeṣapātakaḥ śraddhyānvitaḥ 
dvijadevapitṝṇāṃ ca nityam arcāparāyaṇaḥ  Hbhv 
yuvā viniyatāśeṣakaraṇaḥ karuṇālayaḥ 
ity ādilakṣaṇair yuktaḥ śiṣyo dīkṣādhikāravān  Hbhv 
ekādaśaskandhe ca BhP  
amāny amatsaro dakṣo nirmamo dṛṭhasauhṛdaḥ 
asatvaro 'rthajijñāsur anasūyur amoghavāk  Hbhv 
athāpekṣyāḥ
agastyasaṃhitāyām
alasā malināḥ kliṣṭā dāmbhikāḥ kṛpaṇās tathā 
daridrā rogiṇo ruṣṭā rāgiṇo bhogalālasāḥ  Hbhv 
asūyāmatsaragrastāḥ śaṭhāḥ paruṣavādinaḥ 
anyāyopārjitadhanāḥ paradāraratāś ca ye  Hbhv 
viduṣāṃ vairiṇaś caiva ajñāḥ paṇḍitamāninaḥ 
bhraṣṭavratāś ca ye kaṣṭavṛttayaḥ piśunāḥ khalāḥ  Hbhv 
bahvāśinaḥ krūraceṣṭā durātmanaś ca nindita 
ity evam ādayo 'py anye pāpiṣṭhāḥ puruṣādhamāḥ  Hbhv 
akṛtyebhyo 'nivāryāś ca guruśikṣāsahiṣṇavaḥ 
evambhūtāḥ parityājyāḥ śiṣyatve nopakalpitāḥ  Hbhv 
yady ete hy upakalperan devatākrośabhājanāḥ 
bhavantīha dardrās te putradāravivarjitāḥ  Hbhv 
nārakāś caiva dehānte tiryañcaḥ prabhavanti te  Hbhv 
hayaśīrṣapañcarātre
jaiminiḥ sugataś caiva nāstiko nagna eva ca 
kapilaś cākṣapādaś ca ṣaḍ ete hetuvādinaḥ  Hbhv 
etanmatānusāreṇa vartante ye narādhamāḥ 
te hetuvādinaḥ proktās tebhyas tantraṃ na dāpayet  Hbhv  iti
tayoḥ parīkṣā cānyo 'nyam ekābdaṃ sahavāsataḥ 
vyavahārasvabhāvānubhavenaivābhijāyate  Hbhv 
atha parīkṣaṇam
mantramuktāvalyāṃ
tayor vatsaravāsena jñātānyonyasvabhāvayoḥ 
gurutā śiṣyatā ceti nānyathaiveti niścayaḥ  Hbhv 
śrutiś ca
nāsaṃvatsaravāsine deyāt  Hbhv 
sārasaṅgrahe'pi
sadguruḥ svāśritaṃ śiṣyaṃ varṣm ekaṃ parīkṣayet  Hbhv 
rājñi cāmātyajā doṣāḥ patnīpāpaṃ svabhartari 
tathā śiṣyārjitaṃ pāpaṃ guruḥ prāpnoti niścitam  Hbhv 
kramadīpikāyāṃ tu  
santoṣayed akuṭilādretarāntarātmā
taṃ svair dhanaiś ca vapuṣāpy anukūlavāṇyā 
abdatrayaṅkamalanābhadhiyā'tidhīras
tuṣṭe vivakṣatu gurāv atha mantradīkṣām  Hbhv 
atha viśeṣataḥ śrīgurusevāvidhiḥ
kaurme śrīvyāsagītāyām
udakumbhaṃ kuśān puṣpaṃ samidho 'syāharet sadā 
mārjanaṃ lepanaṃ nityam aṅgānāṃ vāsasāṃ caret  Hbhv 
nāsya nirmālyaśayanaṃ pādukopāsanahāv api 
ākrāmed āsanaṃ chyāyām āsandīṃ vā kadācana  Hbhv 
sādhayed dantakāṣṭhādīn kṛtyaṃ cāsmai nivedayeet  Hbhv 
anāpṛcchya na gantavyaṃ bhavet priyahite rasaḥ 
na pādau sārayed asya sannidhāne kadācana  Hbhv 
jṛmbhāhāsyādikaṃ caiva kaṇṭhaprāvaraṇaṃ tathā 
varjayet sannidhau nityam athāsphoṭanam eva ca  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
śreyas tu guruvad vṛttir nityam eva samācaret 
guruputreṣu dāreṣu guroś caiva svabandhuṣu  Hbhv 
utsādanaṃ vai gātrāṇāṃ snāpanocchiṣṭabhojane 
na kuryād guruputrasya pādayoḥ śaucam eva ca  Hbhv 
guruvat paripūjyāś ca savarṇā guruyoṣitaḥ 
asavarṇās tu sampūjyāḥ pratyutthānābhivādanaiḥ  Hbhv 
abhyañjanaṃ snāpanaṃ ca gātrotsādanam eva ca 
gurupatnyā ca kāryāṇi keśānāṃ ca prasādhanam  Hbhv 
devyāgame śrīśivoktau
guruśayyāsanaṃ yānaṃ pāduke pādapīṭhakam 
snānodakaṃ tathā chāyāṃ laṅghayen na kadācana  Hbhv 
guror agre pṛthakpūjām advaitaṃ ca parityajet 
dīkṣāṃ vyākhyāṃ prabhutvaṃ ca guror agre vivarjayet  Hbhv 
śrīnāradoktau
yatra yatra guruṃ paśyet tatra tatra kṛtāñjali 
praṇamet daṇḍavad bhūmau chinnamūla iva drumaḥ  Hbhv 
guror vākyāsanaṃ yānaṃ pādukopānahau tathā 
vastraṃ chāyāṃ tathā śiṣyo laṅghayen na kadācana  Hbhv 
śrīmanusmṛtau not found
nodāhared guror nāma parokṣam api kevalam 
na caivāsyānukurvīta gatibhāṣaṇaceṣṭitam  Hbhv 
guror gurau sannihite guruvad dhṛtim ācaret 
na cāvisṛṣṭo guruṇā svān gurūn abhivādayet  Hbhv 
śrīnāradapañcarātre
yathā tathā yatra tatra na gṛhṇīyāc ca kevalam 
abhaktyā na guror nāma gṛhṇīyāc ca yatātmavān  Hbhv 
praṇavaḥ śrīs tato nāma viṣṇuśabdād anantaram 
pādaśabdasametaṃ ca natamūrdhāñjalīyutaḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
na tam ājñāpayen mohāt tasyājñāṃ na ca laṅghayet 
nānivedya guroḥ kiñcid bhoktavyaṃ vā guros tathā  Hbhv 
anyatra ca
āyāntam agrato gacched gacchantaṃ tam anuvrajet 
āsane śayane vāpi na tiṣṭhed agrato guroḥ  Hbhv 
yat kiñcid annapānādi priyaṃ dravyaṃ manoramam 
samarpya gurave paścāt svayaṃ bhuñjīta pratyaham  Hbhv 
śrīviṣṇusmṛtau
na guror apriyaṃ kuryāt tāḍitaḥ pīḍito 'pi vā 
nāvamanyeta tadvākyaṃ nāpriyaṃ hi samācaret  Hbhv 
ācāryasya priyaṃ kuryāt prāṇair api dhanair api 
karmaṇā manasā vācā sa yāti paramāṃ gatim  Hbhv 
śrīnāradapañcarātre 
yo vakti nyāyarahitam anyāyena śṛṇoti yaḥ 
tāv ubhau narakaṃ ghoraṃ vrajataḥ kālam akṣayam  Hbhv 
vaiṣṇavatantre 
trāyasva bho jagannātha guro saṃsāravahninā 
dagdhaṃ māṃ kāladaṣṭaṃ ca tvām ahaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  Hbhv  iti
tatra śrīvāsudevasya sarvadevaśiromaṇeḥ 
pādāmbujaikabhāg eva dīkṣā grāhyā manīṣibhiḥ  Hbhv 
prathamaskandhe BhP  
sattvaṃ rajas tama iti prakṛter guṇās tair
yuktaḥ paramapuruṣa eka ihāsya dhatte 
sthityādaye hariviriñcihareti saṃjñāḥ
śreyāṃsi tatra khalu sattvatanor nṝṇāṃ syuḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca BhP  
athāpi yatpādanakhāvasṛṣṭaṃ
jagad viriñcopahṛtārhaṇāmbhaḥ 
seśaṃ punāty anyatamo mukundāt
ko nāma loke bhagavatpadārthaḥ  Hbhv 
śrīdaśamaskandhe BhP  
tan niśamyātha munayo vismitā muktasaṃśayāḥ 
bhūyāṃsaṃ śraddadhur viṣṇuṃ yataḥ śāntir yato 'bhayam  Hbhv 
pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye yamabrāhmaṇasaṃvāde PadmaP  
vyāmohāya carācarasya jagatas te te purāṇāgamās
tāṃ tām eva hi devatāṃ paramikāṃ jalpantu kalpāvadhi 
siddhānte punar eka eva bhagavān viṣṇuḥ samastāgama
vyāpāreṣu vivecanavyatikaraṃ nīteṣu niścīyate  Hbhv 
nārasiṃhe 
satyaṃ satyaṃ punaḥ satyam utkṣipya bhujam ucyate 
vedāc chāstraṃ paraṃ nāsti na devaḥ keśavāt paraḥ  Hbhv 
yataḥ pādme 
arir mitraṃ viṣṃ pathyam adharmo dharmatāṃ vrajet 
suprasanne hṛṣīkeśe viparīte viparyayaḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrībhagavadvākyam
mannimittaṃ kṛtaṃ pāpam api dharmāya kalpate 
mām anādṛtya dharmo 'pi pāpaṃ syān matprabhāvataḥ  Hbhv 
ataevoktaṃ skānde śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde 
vāsudevaṃ parityajya yo 'nyaṃ devam upāsate 
svamātaraṃ parityajya śvapacīṃ vandate hi saḥ  Hbhv 
tatraivānyatra 
vāsudevaṃ parityajya yo 'nyaṃ devam upāsate 
tyaktvāmṛtaṃ sa mūḍhātmā bhuṅkte halāhalaṃ viṣam  Hbhv 
mahābhārate 
yas tu viṣṇuṃ parityajya mohād anyam upāsate 
sa hemarāśim utsṛjya pāṃśurāśiṃ jighṛkṣati  Hbhv

janmarkṣākṣaratau yāvanmantrādimākṣaram 
caturbhiḥ koṣṭhakais tv ekam iti koṣṭhacatuṣṭaye  Hbhv 
punaḥ koṣṭhakakoṣṭheṣu savyato janmabhākṣarāt 
siddhasādhyasusiddhārikramāj jñeyā vicakṣṇaiḥ  Hbhv 
siddhaḥ sidhyati kālena sādhyas tu japahomataḥ 
susiddho grahamātreṇa arir mūlanikṛntanaḥ  Hbhv 
siddhasiddho yathoktena dviguṇāt siddhasādhakaḥ 
siddhasusiddho 'rdhajapāt siddhārir hanti bāndhavān  Hbhv 
sādhyasiddho dviguṇikaḥ sādhyasādhyo hy anarthakaḥ 
tatsusiddhas triguṇitāt sādhyārir hanti gotrajān  Hbhv 
susiddhasiddhordhajapāt tatsādhyas tu guṇādhikāt 
tatsusiddho grahād eva susiddhāriḥ svagotrahā  Hbhv 
arisiddhaḥ sutān hanyād arisādhyas tu kanyakāḥ 
tatsusiddhas tu patnīghnas tadarir hanti sādhakam  Hbhv 
tathā ca tantre
asya ca mantraviśeṣe'pavādaḥ 
nṛsiṃhārkavarāhāṇāṃ prāsādapraṇavasya ca 
vaidikasya ca mantrasya siddhādīn naiva śodhayet  Hbhv 
svapnalabdhe striyā datte mālāmantre ca tryakṣare 
ekākṣare tathā mantre siddhādīn naiva śodhayet  Hbhv 
svakulāny akulatvādi vijñeyaṃ cāgamāntarāt 
na vistarabhayād atra vyarthatvād api likhyate  Hbhv 
śrīmadgopāladevasya sarvaiśvaryapradarśinaḥ 
tādṛkśaktiṣu mantreṣu nahi kiñcid vicāryate  Hbhv 
tathā ca kramadīpikāyām 
sarveṣu varṇeṣu tathāśrameṣu
nārīṣu nānāhvayajanmabheṣu
dātā phalānām abhivāñchitānāṃ
drāg eva gopālakamantra eṣaḥ  Hbhv 
trailokyasaṃmohanatantre ca
aṣṭādaśākṣaramantram adhikṛtya śrīśivenoktam 
na cātra śātravā doṣā narṇasvādivicāraṇā 
ṛkṣarāśivicāro vā na kartavyo manau priye  Hbhv 
kecic chinnāś ca ruddhāś ca kecin madasamuddhatāḥ 
malināḥ stambhitāḥ kecit kīlitā dūṣitā api 
etair doṣair yuto nāyaṃ yatas tribhunottamaḥ  Hbhv  iti
sāmānyataś ca yathā bṛhadgautamīye 
atha kṛṣṇamanūn vakṣye dṛṣṭādṛṣṭaphalapradān 
yān vai vijñāya munayo lebhire muktim añjasā  Hbhv 
gṛhasthā vanagāś caiva yatayo brahmacāriṇaḥ 
striyaḥ śūdrādayaś caiva sarve yatrādhikāriṇaḥ  Hbhv 
nātra cintyo 'riśuddhyādir nārimitrādilakṣaṇam 
na vā prayāsabāhulyaṃ sādhane na pariśramaḥ  Hbhv 
ajñānatūlarāśeś ca analaḥ kṣaṇamātrataḥ 
siddhasādhyasusiddhārirūpā nātra vicāraṇā  Hbhv 
sarveṣāṃ siddhamantrāṇāṃ yato brahmākṣaro manuḥ 
prajāpatir avāpāgryaṃ devarājyaṃ śacīpatiḥ 
avāpus tridaśāḥ svargaṃ vāgīśatvaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ  Hbhv 
ity ādi
tatraivāntare 
viṣṇubhaktyā viśeṣeṇa kiṃ na sidhyati bhūtale 
kīṭādibrahmaparyantaṃ govindānugrahān mune  Hbhv 
sarvasampattinilayāḥ sarvatrāpy akutobhayāḥ 
ity ādi kathitaṃ kiñcin māhātmyaṃ vo munīśvarāḥ  Hbhv 
ākāśe tārakā yadvat sindhoḥ saikatasṛṣṭivat 
etadvijñānamātreṇa labhen muktiṃ caturvidhām  Hbhv 
etadanyeṣu mantreṣu doṣāḥ santi pare ca ye 
tadarthaṃ mantrasaṃskārā lipyante tantrato daśa  Hbhv 
saradātilake 
jananaṃ jīvanaṃ ceti tāḍanaṃ rodhanaṃ tathā 
athābhiṣeko vimalīkaraṇāpyāyane punaḥ 
tarpaṇaṃ dīpanaṃ guptir daśaitā mantrasaṃskriyāḥ  Hbhv 
mantrāṇāṃ mātṛkāmadhyād uddhāro jananaṃ smṛtam 
praṇavāntaritān kṛtvā mantravarṇān japet sudhīḥ  Hbhv 
etaj jīvanam ity āhur mantratantraviśāradāḥ 
manor varṇān samālikhya tāḍayec candanāmbhasā  Hbhv 
pratyekaṃ vāyunā mantrī tāḍanaṃ tad udāhṛtam 
vilikhya mantraṃ taṃ mantrī prasūnaiḥ karavīrajaiḥ  Hbhv 
tanmantrākṣarasaṅkhyātair hanyād yat tena rodhanam 
svatantroktavidhānena mantrī mantrārṇasaṅkhyayā  Hbhv 
aśvatthapallavair mantram abhiṣiñced viśuddhaye 
saṃcintya manasā mantraṃ yotir mantreṇa nirdahet  Hbhv 
mantre mūlatrayaṃ mantrī vimalīkaraṇaṃ tv idam 
tāravyomāgnimanuyugadaṇḍī jyotir manur mataḥ 
kuśodakena japtena pratyarṇaṃ prokṣaṇaṃ manoḥ  Hbhv 
tena mantreṇa vidhivad etad āpyāyanaṃ smṛtam 
mantreṇa vāriṇā yantre tarpaṇaṃ tarpaṇaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv 
tāramāyāramāyogo manor dīpanam ucyate 
japyamānasya mantrasya gopanaṃ tv aprakāśanam  Hbhv 
balitvāt kṛṣṇamantrāṇāṃ saṃskārāpekṣaṇaṃ nahi 
sāmānyoddeśamātreṇa tathāpy etad udīritam  Hbhv 
iti śrīgopālabhaṭṭavilikhite śrībhagavadbhaktivilāse
gauravo nāma prathamo vilāsaḥ 
 DaiksikaVilasa
dvitīyo vilāsaḥ
daikṣikaḥ
taṃ śrīmatkṛṣṇacaitanyaṃ vande jagadgurum 
yasyānukampayā śvāpi mahābdhiṃ santaret sukham  Hbhv 
atha dīkṣāvidhiḥ
dīkṣāvidhir likhyate'trānusṛtya kramadīpikām 
vinā dīkṣāṃ hi pūjāyāṃ nādhikāro 'sti karhicit  Hbhv 
āgame 
dvijānām anupetānāṃ svakarmādhyayanādiṣu 
yathādhikāro nāstīha syāc copanayanād anu  Hbhv 
tathātrādīkṣitānāṃ tu mantradevārcanādiṣu 
nādhikāro 'sty ataḥ kuryād ātmānaṃ śivasaṃstutam  Hbhv 
skānde kārttikaprasaṅge śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde 
te narāḥ paśavo loke kiṃ teṣāṃ jīvane phalam 
yair na labdhā harer dīkṣā nārcito vā janārdanaḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrīrukmāṅgadamohinīsaṃvāde
viṣṇuyāmale ca 
adikṣitasya vāmoru kṛtaṃ sarvaṃ nirarthakam 
paśuyonim avāpnoti dīkṣāvirahito janaḥ  Hbhv 
viśeṣato viṣṇuyāmale 
snehād vā lobhato vāpi yo gṛhṇīyād adīkṣayā 
tasmin gurau saśiṣye tu devatāśāpa āpatet  Hbhv 
viṣṇurahasye ca 
avijñāya vidhānoktaṃ haripūjāvidhikriyām 
kurvan bhaktyā samāpnoti śatabhāgaṃ vidhānataḥ  Hbhv 
divyaṃ jñānaṃ yato dadyāt kuryāt pāpasya saṅkṣayam 
tasmād dīkṣeti sā proktā deśikais tattvakovidaiḥ  Hbhv 
ato guruṃ praṇamyaivaṃ sarvasvaṃ vinivedya ca 
gṛhṇīyād vaiṣṇavaṃ mantraṃ dīkṣāpūrvaṃ vidhānataḥ  Hbhv 
skānde tatraiva śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde 
tapasvinaḥ karmaniṣṭhāḥ śreṣṭhās te vai narā bhuvi 
prāptā yais tu harer dīkṣā sarvaduḥkhavimocinī  Hbhv 
tantrasāgare ca 
yathā kāñcanatāṃ yāti kāṃsyaṃ rasavidhānataḥ 
tathā dīkṣāvidhānena dvijatvaṃ jāyate nṛṇām  Hbhv 
atha dīkṣākālaḥ  tatra māsaśuddhiḥ
āgame 
mantrasvīkaraṇaṃ caitre bahuduḥhaphalapradam 
vaiśākhe ratnalābhaḥ syāj jyaiṣṭhe tu maraṇaṃ dhruvam  Hbhv 
āṣāḍhe bandhunāśāya śrāvaṇe tu bhayāvaham 
prajāhānir bhādrapade sarvatra śubham āśvine  Hbhv 
kārttike dhanavṛddhiḥ syān mārgaśīrṣe śubhapradam 
pauṣe tu jñānahāniḥ syān māghe medhāvivardhanam 
phālgune sarvavaśyatvam ācāryaiḥ parikīrtitam  Hbhv 
kvacic ca 
samṛddhiḥ śrāvaṇe nūnaṃ jñānaṃ syāt kārttike tathā 
phālgune'pi samṛddhiḥ syān malamāsaṃ parityajet  Hbhv 
gautamīye
mantrārambhas tu caitre syāt samastapuruṣārthadaḥ 
vaiśākhe ratnalābhaḥ syāt jyaiṣṭhe tu maraṇaṃ dhruvam  Hbhv 
āṣāḍhe bandhunāśaḥ syāt pūrṇāyuḥ śrāvaṇe bhavet 
prajānāśo bhaved bhādre āśvine ratnasañcayaḥ  Hbhv 
kārttike mantrasiddhiḥ syāt mārgaśīrṣe tathā bhavet 
pauṣe tu śatrupīḍā syāt māghe medhāvivardhanam 
phālgune sarvakāmāḥ syur malamāsaṃ parityajet  Hbhv 
skānde tatraiva śrīrukmāṅgadamohinīsaṃvāde
kārttike tu kṛtā dīkṣā nṝṇāṃ janmanikṛntanī 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena dīkṣāṃ kurvīta kārttike  Hbhv 
śrīmadgopālamantrāṇāṃ dīkṣāyāṃ tu na duṣyati 
caitramāse yad uktā tad dīkṣā tatraiva deśikaiḥ  Hbhv 
atha bāraśuddhiḥ
ravau gurau tathā some kartavyaṃ budhaśukrayoḥ  Hbhv 
atha nakṣatraśuddhiḥ
nāradatantre
rohiṇī śravaṇārdrā ca dhaniṣṭhā cottarātrayaḥ 
puṣyaṃ śatabhiṣaś caiva dīkṣānakṣatram ucyate  Hbhv 
kvacic ca
aśvinīrohiṇīsvātiviśākhāhastabheṣu ca 
jyeṣṭhottarātrayeṣv eva kuryān mantrābhiṣecanam  Hbhv 
atha tithiśuddhiḥ
sārasaṅgrahe
dvitīyā pañcamī caiva ṣaṣṭhī caiva viśeṣataḥ 
dvādaśyām api kartavyaṃ trayodaśyām athāpi ca  Hbhv 
kvacic ca
pūrṇimā pañcamī caiva dvitīyā saptamī tathā 
trayodaśī ca daśamī praśastā sarvakāmadā  Hbhv 
 iti 
evaṃ śuddhe dine śuklapakṣe śukragurūdaye 
sallagne candratārānukūle dīkṣā praśasyate  Hbhv 
athātrāpavādaḥ viśeṣavidhiḥ
rudrayāmale
sattīrthe'rkavidhugrāse tantudāmanaparvaṇoḥ 
mantradīkṣāṃ prakurvīta māsarkṣādi na śodhayet  Hbhv 
sulagnacandratārādibalam atra sadaiva hi 
labdho 'tra mantor dīrghāyuḥsampatsantativardhanaḥ  Hbhv 
sūryagrahaṇakālena samāno nāsti kaścana 
yatra yad yat kṛtaṃ sarvam anantaphaladaṃ bhavet 
na māsatithivārādiśodhanaṃ sūryaparvaṇi  Hbhv 
tattvasāgare ca
durlabhe sadgurūṇāṃ ca sakṛt saṅga upasthite 
tadanujñā yadā labdhā sa dīkṣāvasaro mahān  Hbhv 
grāme vā yadi vāraṇye kṣetre vā divase niśi 
āgacchati gurur daivād yadā dīkṣā tadājñayā  Hbhv 
yadaivecchā tadā dīkṣā guror ājñānurūpataḥ 
na tīrthaṃ na vrataṃ homo na snānaṃ na japakriyā 
dīkṣāyāḥ karaṇaṃ kintu svecchāprāpte tu sadgurau  Hbhv 
atha maṇḍapanirmāṇavidhiḥ
kriyāvatyādibhedena bhaved dīkṣā caturvidhā 
tatra kriyāvatī dīkṣā saṅkṣepeṇaiva likhyate  Hbhv 
bhūmiṃ saṃskṛtya tasyāṅ cārcayitvā vāstudevatāḥ 
saptahastamitaṃ kuryān maṇḍapaṃ ramyavedikam  Hbhv 
aṣṭadhvajaṃ caturdhāraṃ kṣīrapādapatoraṇam 
triguṇīkṛtasūtrāḍhyaṃ kuśamālābhiveṣṭitam  Hbhv 
atha kuṇḍanirmāṇavidhiḥ
tasmiṃś ca diśi kauveryāṃ catuṣkoṇaṃ trimekhalam 
kuṇḍe kuryāc caturviṃśatyaṅgulipramitaṃ budhah  Hbhv 
khātaṃ trimekhalocchrāyasahitaṃ tāvad ācaret 
tasmāt khātād bahiḥ kuryāt kaṇṭham ekāṅgulaṃ dhruvam  Hbhv 
tatrādymekhalocchrāyavistārau caturaṅgulau 
tryaṅgulau tau dvitīyāyās tṛtīyāyā yugāṅgulau  Hbhv 
yoniṃ ca paścime bhāge mekhalātritayopari 
ṣaḍaṅgulāṃ ca vistāre dairghye ca dvādaśāṅgulām  Hbhv 
ekāṅgulāṃ tathocchrāye madhye chidrasamanvitām 
gadādharākṛtiṃ kuryād vidhivan mekhalānvitām  Hbhv 
śatārdhahome kuṇḍaṃ syād ūrdhvamuṣṭikaronmitam  Hbhv 
śatahome'ratnimātram sahasre pāṇinā mitam 
lakṣe caturbhir hastaiś ca koṭau tair aṣṭabhir mitam 
caturasraṃ kuṇḍakhātaṃ kurvītādhaś ca tādṛśam  Hbhv 
homas tv adhikasaṅkhākaḥ kuṇḍe vai nyūnasaṅkhyayā 
kṛte kāryo na c anyūnasaṅkhyākaḥ saṅkhayādhike  Hbhv 
yathāvidhy eva kartavyaṃ kuṇḍaṃ yatnena dhīmatā 
anyathā bahavo doṣā bhaveyur bahuduḥkhadāḥ  Hbhv 
tad uktaṃ tāntrikaiḥ
evaṃ lakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ kuṇḍam iṣṭaphalapradam 
anekadoṣadaṃ kuṇḍaṃ yatra nyūnādhikām bhavet  Hbhv 
tasmāt samyak parīkṣyaiva kartavyaṃ śubham icchatā 
hastamātraṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ vā saṃkṣipte homakarmaṇi  Hbhv 
hārītenāpi 
vistārādhikyahīnatve alpāyur jāyate dhruvam 
khātādhikye bhaved yogī hīne tu dhanasaṃkṣayaḥ 
kuṇḍe vakre ca santāpo maraṇaṃ chinnamekhale  Hbhv 
śokas tu mekhalonatve tadādhikye paśukṣayaḥ 
bhāryānāśo yonihīne kaṇṭhahīne śubhakṣayaḥ  Hbhv 
aṅguliparimāṇaṃ coktam
tiryagyavodarāṇyaṣṭāv ūrdhvā vā brīhayas trayaḥ 
jñeyam aṅgulimānaṃ tu madhyamā madhyaparvaṇā  Hbhv 
 iti 
viśeṣo 'pekṣito 'nyatra sraksruvaprakriyādikaḥ 
jñeyo granthāntarāt so 'trādhikyabhītyā na likhyate  Hbhv 
atha dīkṣāmaṇḍalavidhiḥ
athokṣite pañcagavyair gandhāmbhobhiś ca maṇḍape 
yathāvidhi likhed dīkṣāmaṇḍalaṃ vedikopari  Hbhv 
tanmadhye cāṣṭapatrābjaṃ bahir vṛttatrayaṃ tataḥ 
tato rāśīṃs tataḥ pīṭhaṃ catuṣpādasamanvitam  Hbhv 
tasmād bahiś caturdikṣu likhed vīthīcatuṣṭayam 
śobhāpaśobhākoṇāḍhyaṃ tato dvāracatuṣṭayam  Hbhv 
atha dīkṣāṅgapūjā
prātaḥkṛtyaṃ guruḥ kṛtvā yathāsthānaṃ nyaset tataḥ 
śaṅkhaṃ pūjopacārāṃś ca purolekhyaprakārataḥ  Hbhv 
tatrādau kumbhasthāpanavidhiḥ
gurūn gaṇeśaṃ cābhyarcya pīṭhapūjāṃ vidhāya ca 
padmamadhye nyaset śālīṃs taṇḍulāṃś ca kuśāṃs tathā  Hbhv 
vahner daśakalā yādivarṇādyāś ca kuśopari 
nyasyābhyarcya japaṃs tāraṃ nyaset kumbhaṃ yathoditam  Hbhv 
tāś coktāḥ
dhūmrārcir uṣmā jvalanī jvālinī visphuliṅinī 
suśrīḥ surūpā kapilā havyakavyavahe api  Hbhv 
 iti 
kādyaṣṭhāntair yutā bhādyair ḍāntaiś cārṇair vilomagaiḥ 
sūryasya ca kalāḥ kumbhe dvādaśa nyasya pūjayet  Hbhv 
adhunā tasmin kuṇḍe sūryakalānāṃ nyāsādikaṃ likhatikādyair iti 
kakārādyaiṣ ṭhakārāntair arṇair varṇair yutā dvādaśāpi kalāḥ 
cakāraḥ samuccaye 
bhakārādyair ḍakārāntair varṇair api yutāḥ 
nanu bhakārādīnāṃ dvādaśavarṇānāṃ ḍakārāntatā kathaṃ syāt 
krameṇa kṣakārāntatāprāptes tatrāhavilomagaiḥ vyutkramaprāptaiḥ 
 ayam arthaḥanulomapaṭhitakakārādyaikaikam akṣaraṃ pratilomapaṭhitabhakārādyekaikākṣareṇa sahitam ādau sūryakalāsu saṃyojya nyāsādikaṃ  
kuryād iti  
prayogaś ca kaṃ bhaṃ tapanyai nama ity ādi  Hbhv 
tāś coktāḥ
tapanī tāpanī dhūmrā bhrāmarī jvālinī ruciḥ 
suṣumṇā bhogadā viśvā bodhinī dhāriṇī kṣamā  Hbhv 
 iti 
kubmhāntar nikṣipen mūlamantreṇa kusumaṃ sitam 
sākṣataṃ sasitaṃ svarṇaṃ saratnaṃ ca kuśāṃs tathā  Hbhv 
tataś coktaprakāreṇādhārarūpam agniṃ kumbharūpaṃ sūryaṃ ca vicintya kumbhasya tasya antar madhye śuklakusumādikaṃ kṣipet 
sasitaṃ saśarkaram  tad uktam
prottolayitvā tanmadhye śuklapuṣpaṃ sitāyutam 
svarṇaṃ ratnaṃ ca kūrcaṃ ca mūlenaiva vinikṣipet 
 iti 
yac ca mūlagranthārthād adhikaṃ kiṃcil likhate
tat pūrvagatasya yathoditam ity asyānuvartanād iti jñeyam  Hbhv 
kumbhaṃ ca vidhinā tīrthāmbunā śuddhena pūrayet 
jale cendukulā nyasya sasvarāḥ ṣoḍaśārcayet  Hbhv 
tāś coktāḥ
amṛtā mānadā pūṣā tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭī ratir dhṛtiḥ 
śaśinī candrikā kāntir jyotsnā śrīḥ prītir aṅgadā 
pūrṇā pūrṇāmṛtā ca  Hbhv 
 iti 
śuddhāmbupūrite śaṅkhe kṣiptvā gandhāṣṭakaṃ kalāḥ 
āvāhya sarvās tāḥ prāṇapratiṣṭhām ācaret kramāt  Hbhv 
gandhāṣṭakaṃ coktam
uśīraṃ kuṅkumaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ bālakaṃ cāgurur murā 
jaṭāmāṃsī candanaṃ cetīṣṭaṃ gandhāṣṭakaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv 
 iti 
kaiścic candanakarpūrāgurukuṅkumarocanāḥ 
kakkolakapimāṃsyaś ca gandhāṣṭakam idaṃ matam  Hbhv 
tathaivākārajā varṇaiḥ kādibhir daśabhir daśa 
ukārajāṣṭakārādyaiḥ pakārādyair makārajāḥ  Hbhv 
catasro bindujāḥ ṣādyaiś caturbhir nādajāḥ kalāḥ 
svaraiḥ ṣoḍaśabhir yuktā nyasec chaṅkhe ca ṣoḍaśa  Hbhv 
tāś coktāḥ
sṛṣṭir ṛddhiḥ smṛtir medhā kāntir lakṣmīr dhṛitḥ sthirā 
sthitiḥ siddhir akārotthāḥ kalā daśa samīritaḥ  Hbhv 
jarā ca pālinī śāntir aiśvarī ratikāmike 
varadā hlādinī prītir dīrghā cokārajāḥ kalāḥ  Hbhv 
tīkṣṇā raudrā bhayā nidrā tantīr kṣut krodhanī kriyā 
utkārī caiva mṛtyuś ca makārākṣarajāḥ kalāḥ  Hbhv 
nivṛttiś ca pratiṣṭhā ca vidyā śāntis tathaiva ca 
indhikā dīpikā caiva recikā mocikā parā  Hbhv

pūjitaṃ navanābhe tu ṣoḍaśābjadale tathā 
ācāryadarśitaṃ devaṃ mantramūrtim ayonijam  Hbhv 
kārttike māsi śuddhāyāṃ dvādaśyāṃ tu viśeṣataḥ 
sarvāsu ca yajed devaṃ dvādaśīṣu vidhānataḥ  Hbhv 
saṅkrāntau ca mahābhāge candrasūryagrahe'pi vā 
yaḥ paśyati hariṃ devaṃ pūjitaṃ guruṇā śubhe 
tasya sadyo bhavet tuṣṭiḥ pāpadhvaṃso 'py aśeṣataḥ  Hbhv 
sa sāmānyo hi devānāṃ bhavatīti na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ śūdrāṇāṃ ca parīkṣaṇam 
saṃvatsaraṃ guruḥ kuryāj jātiśaucakriyādibhiḥ  Hbhv 
upasannāṃs tato jñātvā hṛdayenāvadhārayet 
te'pi bhaktimato jñātvā ātmanaḥ parameśvaram 
saṃvatsaraṃ guror bhaktiṃ kuryur viṣṇāv ivācalām  Hbhv 
saṃvatsaraṃ tataḥ pūrṇe guruṃ caiva prasādayet  Hbhv 
bhagavaṃs tvatprasādena saṃsārārṇavatāraṇam 
icchāmas tv aihikīṃ lakṣmīṃ viśeṣeṇa tapodhana  Hbhv 
evam abhyarthya medhāvī guruṃ viṣṇum ivāgrataḥ 
abhyarcya tadanujñāto daśamyāṃ kārttikasya tu  Hbhv 
kṣīravṛkṣasamudbhūtaṃ mantritaṃ parameṣṭhinā 
bhakṣayitvā śayītorvyāṃ devadevasya sannidhau  Hbhv 
svapnān dṛṣṭvā guror agre śrāvayeta vicakṣaṇaḥ 
tataḥ śubhāśubhaṃ tadvad ālapet paramo guruḥ 
ekādaśyām upoṣyātha snātvā devālayaṃ vrajet  Hbhv 
guruś ca maṇḍalaṃ bhūmau kalptāyāṃ tu vartayet 
lakṣaṇair vividhair bhūmiṃ lakṣayitvā vidhānataḥ  Hbhv 
ṣoḍaśāraṃ likhec cakraṃ navanābham athāpi vā 
aṣṭapatram atho vāpi likhitvā darśayed budhaḥ  Hbhv 
netrabandhaṃ prakurvīta sitavastreṇa yatnataḥ 
varṇānukramataḥ śiṣyān purṣpahastān praveśayet  Hbhv 
navanābhaṃ yadā kuryān maṇḍalaṃ varṇakair budhaḥ 
tadānīṃ pūrvato devam indram aindryāṃ tu pūjayet  Hbhv 
lokapālam athāgneyyām agniṃ sampūjayed dvijaḥ 
yamaṃ tad anu yāmyāyāṃ nairṛtyāṃ nirṛtiṃ nyaset 
vāruṇyāṃ varuṇaṃ caiva vāyavyāṃ pavanaṃ yajet  Hbhv 
dhanadaṃ cottare nyasya rudram aiśānagocare 
sampūjyaivaṃ vidhānena dikpatreṣu viśeṣataḥ 
adhaḥpatre tathā viṣṇum arcayet parameśvaram  Hbhv 
pūrvapatre balaṃ pūjya pradyumnaṃ dakṣiṇe tathā 
aniruddhaṃ tathā pūjya paścime cottare tathā 
pūjayed vāsudevaṃ tu sarvapātakaśāntidam  Hbhv 
aiśānyāṃ vinyasec chaṅkham āgneyyāṃ cakram eva ca 
saumyāyāṃ tu gadā pūjyā vāyavyāṃ padmam eva ca  Hbhv 
nairṛtyāṃ muṣalaṃ pūjyaṃ dakṣiṇe garuḍaṃ tathā 
vāmato vinyasel lakṣmīṃ devadevasya buddhimān  Hbhv 
dhanuś caiva ca khaḍgaṃ ca devasya purato nyaset 
śrīvatsaṃ kaustubhaṃ caiva devasya purato 'rcayet  Hbhv 
evaṃ pūjya yathānyāyaṃ devadevaṃ janārdanam 
diṅmaṇḍale ca vinyasya cāṣṭau kumbhān vidhānataḥ 
vaiṣṇavaṃ kalasaṃ caiva navamaṃ tatra kalpayet  Hbhv 
snāpayen muktikāmāṃs tu vaiṣṇavena ghaṭena tu 
śrīkāmān snāpayet tadvad aindreṇātha ghaṭena tu  Hbhv 
jayapratāpakāmāṃs tu āgneyenābhiṣecayet 
mṛtyuñjayavidhānena yāmyena snāpanaṃ tathā  Hbhv 
duṣṭapradhvaṃsnāyālaṃ nairṛtena vidhīyate 
śāntaye vāruṇyenātha pāpanāśāya vāyavam  Hbhv 
dravyasampattikāmasya kauvareṇa vidhīyate 
raudreṇa jñānahetus tu lokapālaghaṭās tv ime  Hbhv 
ekaikena naraḥ snātaḥ sarvapāpavarjitaḥ 
bhaved avyāhatajñānaḥ śrīmāṃś ca puruṣaḥ sadā  Hbhv 
kiṃ punar navabhiḥ snāto naraḥ pātakavarjitaḥ 
jāyate viṣṇusadṛśaḥ sadyo rājāthavā punaḥ  Hbhv 
athavā dikṣu sarvāsu yathāsaṅkhyena lokapān 
pūjayet svasvanāmnā tu ṣaḍbhinnena vidhānataḥ  Hbhv 
evaṃ sampūjya devāṃs tu lokapālān prasannadhīḥ 
paścāt parīkṣitān śiṣyān baddhanetrān praveśayet  Hbhv 
āgneyadhāraṇādagdhān vāyunā vidhūtāṃs tataḥ 
somenāpy āyitān paścāc chrāvayen niyamān budhaḥ  Hbhv 
na ninded abrāhmaṇān devān viṣṇuṃ brāhmaṇam eva ca 
rudram ādiyam agniṃ ca lokapālān grahāṃs tathā 
vandeta vaiṣṇavaṃ cāpi puruṣaṃ pūrvadīkṣitam  Hbhv 
evaṃ tu samayān śrāvya paścād dhomaṃ tu kārayet 
tattvāni śiṣyadeheṣu vinyasya ca viśodhayet  Hbhv 
oṃ namo bhagavate viṣṇave sarvarūpiṇe huṃ svāhā  Hbhv 
ṣoḍaśākṣaramantreṇa homayej jvalitānalaḥ 
garbhādhānādikāś caiva kriyāḥ sarvāś ca kārayet  Hbhv 
tribhis tribhir āhutibhir devadevasya sannidhau 
tato 'panīya dṛgbandhaṃ puraḥ śiṣyaṃ niveśya ca 
prāyaḥ pūrvoktavidhinā mantraṃ tasmai gurur diśet  Hbhv 
homānte dīkṣitaḥ paścād dāpayed gurudakṣiṇām 
hastyaśvaratnakaṭakaṃ hemagrāmādikaṃ nṛpaḥ  Hbhv 
dāpayed gurave prājño madhyamo madhyamāṃ tathā 
dāpayed itaro yugmaṃ sahiraṇyaṃ yathāvidhi  Hbhv 
evaṃ kṛte tu yat puṇyaṃ māhātmyaṃ jāyate dhare 
tad aśakyaṃ tu gaditum api varṣaśatair api  Hbhv 
dīkṣitātmā guror bhūtvā vārāhaṃ śṛṇuyād yadi 
tena vedāḥ purāṇāni sarve mantrāḥ susaṅgrahāḥ  Hbhv 
japtāḥ syuḥ puṣkare tīrthe prayāge sindhusāgare 
devahūte kurukṣetre vārāṇasyāṃ viśeṣataḥ  Hbhv 
graheṇa viṣuve caiva yat phalaṃ japatāṃ bhavet 
tat phalaṃ dviguṇaṃ tasya dīkṣito yaḥ śṛṇoti ca  Hbhv 
devā api tapaḥ kṛtvā dhyāyanti ca vadanti ca 
kadā me bhārate varṣe janma syād bhūtadhāriṇi  Hbhv 
dīkṣitāś ca bhaviṣyāmo vārāhaṃ śṛṇumaḥ kadā 
vārāhaṃ ṣoḍaśātmānaṃ yuktā dehe kadācana 
paśyāmaḥ paramaṃ sthānaṃ yad gatvā na punar bhavet  Hbhv 
evaṃ jalpanti vibudhā manasā cintayanti ca 
vārāhayāgaṃ kārttikyāṃ kadā drakṣyāmahe dhare  Hbhv 
eṣa te vidhir uddiṣṭo mayā te bhūtadhāriṇi 
devagandharvayakṣāṇāṃ sarvathā durlabho hy asau  Hbhv 
evaṃ yo vetti tattvena yaś ca paśyati maṇḍalam 
yaś cemaṃ śṛṇuyād devi sarve muktā iti śrutiḥ  Hbhv 
atha saṅkṣiptadīkṣā
saṅkṣiptaś cātha dīkṣāyā vidhir eṣa vilikhyate 
mukhyakalpe hy aśaktasya janasya syād dhitāya ca  Hbhv 
sumuhūrte'tha samprāpte sarvatobhadramaṇḍale 
nūtanaṃ gandhapuṣpādimaṇḍitaṃ kalasaṃ nyaset  Hbhv 
vastrāvṛtaṃ payaḥ pūrṇaṃ pañcapallavasaṃyutam 
sarvauṣadhipañcaratnamṛtsnāsaptakagarbhitam  Hbhv 
mṛttikāś ca saptoktāḥ
aśvasthānād gajasthānād valmīkāc ca catuṣpathāt 
rājadvārāc ca goṣṭhāc ca nadyāḥ kūlān mṛdaḥ smṛtāḥ  Hbhv 
 iti 
kṛṣṇam abhyarcya taṃ kumbhaṃ kuśakūrcena deśikaḥ 
deyamantreṇa sāṣṭaṃ tu sahasram abhimantrayet  Hbhv 
tadadbhiḥ pūrvavac chiṣyam abhiṣicya diśen manum 
śiṣyo 'rcayed guruṃ bhaktyā yathāśakti dvijān api  Hbhv 
athopadeśas tattvasāgare
atrāpy aśaktaḥ kaścic ced abjam abhyarcya sākṣatam 
tadambhasābhiṣicyāṣṭa vārān mūlena ke karam  Hbhv 
nidhāyāmuṃ japet karṇe upadeśeṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ 
candrasūryagrahe tīrthe siddhakṣetre śivālaye 
mantramātraprakathanam upadeśaḥ sa ucyate  Hbhv 
tatra tatraiva viśeṣaḥ śrīnāradapañcarātre 
vittalobhād vimuktasya svalpavittasya dehinaḥ 
saṃsārabhayabhītasya viṣṇubhaktasya tattvataḥ  Hbhv 
agnāv ājyānvite bījaiḥ salilaiḥ kevalaiś ca vā 
dravyahīnasya kurvīta vacasānugrahaṃ guruḥ  Hbhv 
yaḥ samaḥ sarvabhūteṣu virāgo vītamatsaraḥ 
jitendriyaḥ śucir dakṣaḥ sarvāṅgāvayavānvitaḥ  Hbhv 
karmaṇā manasā vācā bhīte cābhayadaḥ sadā 
samabuddhipadaṃ prāptas tatrāpi bhagavanmayaḥ  Hbhv 
pañcakālaparaś caiva pañcarātrārthavit tathā 
viṣṇutattvaṃ parijñāya ekaṃ cānekabhedagam 
vīkṣayen medinīṃ sarvāṃ kiṃ punaś copasannatān  Hbhv 
atha mantradānamāhātmyam
skānde brahmanāradasaṃvāde 
iha kīrtiṃ vadānyatvaṃ prajāvṛddhiṃ dhanaṃ sukham 
vidyādānena labhate sāttviko nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
yathā surāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ paramaḥ parameśvaraḥ 
tathaiva sarvadānānāṃ vidyādānaṃ paraṃ smṛtam  Hbhv 
yāvac ca pātakaṃ tena kṛtaṃ janmaśatair api 
tat sarvaṃ nāśam āpnoti vidyādānena dehinām  Hbhv 
vidyādānāt paraṃ dānaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati 
yena dattena cāpnoti śivaṃ paramakāraṇam  Hbhv 
iti śrīgopālabhaṭṭavilikhite śrībhagavadbhaktivilāse
daikṣiko nāma dvitīyo vilāsaḥ

śaucīyaḥ
vande'nantādbhutaiśvaryaṃ śrīcaitanyaṃ mahāprabhum 
nīco 'pi yatprasādāt syāt sadācārapravartakaḥ  Hbhv 
puṃso gṛhītadīkṣasya śrīkṛṣṇaṃ pūjayiṣyataḥ 
ācāro likhyate kṛtyaṃ śrutismṛtyanusārataḥ  Hbhv 
atha dīkṣitasya pūjāyā nityatā
labdhvā mantraṃ tu yo nityaṃ nārcayen mantradevatām 
sarvakarmaphalaṃ tasyāniṣṭaṃ yacchati devatā  Hbhv 
atha sadācāraḥ
na kiñcit kasyacit sidhyet sadācāraṃ vinā yataḥ 
tasmād avaśyaṃ sarvatra sadācāro hy apekṣyate  Hbhv 
viṣṇupurāṇe ViP  
vaṛṇāśramācaravatā puruṣeṇa paraḥ pumān 
viṣṇur ārādhyate panthā nānyat tattoṣakāraṇam  Hbhv 
atha sadācārasya nityatā
mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe śrīmadālasālarkasaṃvāde
gṛhasthena sadā kāryam ācāraparipālanam 
na hy ācāravihīnasya sukham atra paratra ca  Hbhv 
yajñadānatapāṃsīha puruṣasya na bhūtaye 
bhavanti yaḥ sadācāraṃ samullaṅghya pravartate  Hbhv 
bhaviṣyottare ca śrīkṛṣṇayudhiṣṭhirasaṃvāde
ācārahīnaṃ na punanti vedāḥ
yadyapy adhītāḥ saha ṣaḍbhir aṅgaiḥ 
chandāṃsy enaṃ mṛtyukāle tyajanti
nīḍaṃ śakuntā iva jātapakṣāḥ  Hbhv 
kapālasthaṃ yathā toyaṃ śvadṛtau vā yathā payaḥ 
duṣṭaṃ syāt sthānadoṣeṇa vṛttahīne tathāśubham 
ācārarahito rājan neha nāmutra nindati  Hbhv 
 iti 
lekhyena smaraṇādīnāṃ nityatvenaiva setsyati 
smaraṇādyātmakasyāpi sadācārasya nityatā  Hbhv 
viṣṇupurāṇe  tatraiva gṛhidharmaprasaṅge 
sadācāravatā puṃsā jitau lokāv ubhāv api  Hbhv 
sādhavaḥ kṣīṇadoṣās tu sacchabdaḥ sādhuvācakaḥ 
teṣām ācaraṇaṃ yat tu sadācāraḥ sa ucyate  Hbhv 
kāśīkhaṇḍe skandāgastyasaṃvāde
anadhyayanaśīlaṃ ca sadācāravilaṅghinam 
sālasyaṃ ca durannādaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ bādhate'ntakaḥ  Hbhv 
tato 'bhyaset prayatnena sadācāraṃ sadā dvijaḥ 
tīrthāny apy abhilaṣyanti sadācārasamāgamam  Hbhv 
bhaviṣyottare ca tatraiva
ācāraprabhavo dharmaḥ santaś cācāralakṣaṇāḥ 
sādhūnāṃ ca yathā vṛttaṃ sa sadācāra iṣyate  Hbhv 
tasmāt kuryāt sadācāraṃ ya icched gatim ātmanaḥ 
sarvalakṣaṇahīno 'pi samucācāravān nṛpa 
śraddadhāno 'nasūyaś ca sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
ācāra eva dharmasya mūlaṃ rājan kulasya ca 
ācārād vicyuto jantur na kulīno na dhārmikaḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
ācāro bhūtijanana ācāraḥ kīrtivardhanaḥ 
ācārād vardhate hy āyur ācāro hanty alakṣaṇam  Hbhv 
ācāra eva nṛpapuṅgava sevyamāno
dharmārthakāmaphalado bhaviteha puṃsām 
tasmāt sadaiva viduṣāvahitena rājan
śāstrodito hy anudinaṃ paripālanīyaḥ  Hbhv 
atha tatra nityakṛtyāni
brāhme muhūrta utthāya kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇeti kīrtayan 
prakṣālya pāṇipādau ca dantadhāvanam ācaret  Hbhv 
ācamya vasanaṃ rātres tyaktvānyat paridhāya ca 
punar ācamane kuryāl lekhyena vidhināgrataḥ  Hbhv 
athecchan paramāṃ śuddhiṃ mūrdhni dhyātvā guroḥ padau 
stutvā ca kīrtayan kṛṣṇaṃ smaraṃś caitad udīrayet  Hbhv 
atha prātaḥsmaraṇakīrtane
jayati jananivāso devakījanmavādo
yaduvarapariṣat svair dorbhir asyann adharmam 
sthiracaravṛjinaghnaḥ susmita śrīmukhena
vrajapuravanitānāṃ vardhayan kāmadevam  Hbhv 
BhP 
smṛte sakalakalyāṇabhājanaṃ yatra jāyate 
puruṣas tam ajaṃ nityaṃ vrajāmi śaraṇaṃ harim  Hbhv 
vidagdhagopālavilāsinīnāṃ
sambhogacihnāṅkitasarvagātram

brahma prapadye navanītacauram  Hbhv 
daśamaskandhe BhP  
udgāyatīnām aravindalocanaṃ
vrajāṅganānāṃ divam aspṛśad dhvaniḥ 
dadhnaś ca nirmanthanaśabdamiśrito
nirasyate yena diśām amaṅgalam  Hbhv 
 iti 
paṭhet punaś ca sādhūnāṃ sampradāyānusārataḥ 
catuḥślokīm imāṃ sarvadoṣaśāntyai śubhāptaye  Hbhv 
prātaḥ smarāmi bhavabhītimahārtiśāntyai
nārāyaṇaṃ garuḍavāhanam abjanābham 
grāhābhibhūtavaravārivāraṇamuktihetuṃ
cakrāyudhaṃ taruṇavārijapatranetram  Hbhv 
prātar namāmi manasā vacasā ca mūrdhnā
pādāravindayugalaṃ paramasya puṃsaḥ 
nārāyaṇasya narakārṇavatāraṇasya
pārāyaṇapravaṇavipraparāyaṇasya  Hbhv 
prātar bhajāmi bhajatām abhayaṅkaraṃ taṃ
prāk sarvajanmakṛtapāpabhayāvahatyai 
yo grāhavaktrapatitāṅghrigajendraghora
śokapraṇāśam akarod dhṛtaśaṅkhacakraḥ  Hbhv 
ślokatrayam idaṃ puṇyaṃ prātaḥ prātaḥ paṭhet tu yaḥ 
lokatrayagurus tasmai dadyād ātmapadaṃ hariḥ  Hbhv 
 iti 
tad etal likhitaṃ kutra kutracid vyavahārataḥ 
kintu svābhīṣṭarūpādi śrīkṛṣṇasya vicintayet  Hbhv 
itthaṃ vidadhyād bhagavatkīrtanasmaraṇādikam 
sarvatīrthābhiṣekaṃ vai bahir antarviśodhanam  Hbhv 
tathā ca skānde skandaṃ prati śrīśivoktau
sakṛn nārāyaṇaety uktvā pumān kalpaśatatrayam 
gaṅgādisarvatīrtheṣu snāto bhavati putraka  Hbhv 
anyatra ca
śayanād utthito yas tu kīrtayen madhusūdanam 
kīrtanāt tasya pāpasya nāśam āyāty aśeṣataḥ  Hbhv 
 iti 
māhātmyaṃ kīrtanasyāgre lekhyaṃ mukhyaprasaṅgataḥ 
smaraṇasya tu māhātmyam adhunā likhyate kiyat  Hbhv 
tatrādau tasya nityatā
pādme bṛhatsahasranāmni stotre 
smartavyaḥ satataṃ viṣṇur vismartavyo na jātucit 
sarve vidhiniṣedhāḥ syur etayor eva kiṅkarāḥ  Hbhv 
skānde kārttikaprasaṅge śrīmadagastyoktau
sā hānis tan mahac chidraṃ sa mohaḥ sa ca vibhramaḥ 
yanmuhūrtaṃ kṣaṇaṃ vāpi vāsudevo na cintyate  Hbhv 
kāśīkhaṇḍe ca śrīdhruvacarite
iyam eva parā hānir upasargo 'yam eva ca 
abhāgyaṃ paramaṃ caitad vāsudevaṃ na yat smaret  Hbhv 
ye muhūrtāḥ kṣaṇā ye ca yāḥ kāṣṭhā ye nimeṣakāḥ 
ṛte viṣṇusmṛter yātās teṣu muṣṭo yamena saḥ  Hbhv 
 iti 
nityatve'py asya māhātmyaṃ vicitraphaladānataḥ 
jñeyaṃ śāstroditaṃ darśapūrṇamāsādivad budhaiḥ  Hbhv 
atha smaraṇamāhātmyam
tatra sarvatīrthasnānādhikatvam
uktaṃ ca smārtair api
māntraṃ pārthivam āgneyaṃ vāyavyaṃ divyam eva ca 
vāruṇaṃ mānasaṃ ceti snānaṃ saptavidhaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv 
śaṃ na āpas tu vai māntraṃ mṛdālambhaṃ tu pārthivam 
bhasmanā snānam āgneyaṃ snānaṃ gorajasānilam  Hbhv 
ātape sati yā vṛṣṭir divyaṃ snānaṃ tad ucyate 
bahir nadyādiṣu snānaṃ vāruṇaṃ procyate budhaiḥ 
dhyānaṃ yan manasā viṣṇor mānasaṃ tat prakīrtanam  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
asāmarthyena kāyasya kāladeśādyapekṣayā 
tulyaphalāni sarvāṇi syur ity āha parāśaraḥ  Hbhv 
snānānāṃ mānasaṃ snānaṃ manvādyaiḥ paramaṃ smṛtam 
kṛtena yena mucyante gṛhasthā api vai dvijāḥ  Hbhv 
paramaśodhaktavam
gāruḍe śrīnāradoktau
viṣṇudharme ca pulasytyoktau 
apavitraḥ pavitro vā sarvāvasthāṃ gato 'pi vā 
yaḥ smaret puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ sa bāhyābhyantaraḥ śuciḥ  Hbhv 
yadyapy upahataḥ pāpair manasāyantadustaraiḥ 
tathāpi saṃsmaran viṣṇuṃ sa bāhyābhyantaraḥ śuciḥ  Hbhv 
śrīviṣṇupurāṇe ViP  
prāyaścittāny aśeṣāṇi tapaḥ karmātmakāni vai 
yāni teṣām aśeṣāṇāṃ kṛṣṇānusmaraṇaṃ param  Hbhv 
kṛte pāpe'nutāpo vai yasya puṃsaḥ prajāyate 
prāyaścittaṃ tu tasyaikaṃ harisaṃsmaraṇaṃ param  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca ViP  
kalikalmaṣam atyugraṃ narakārtipradaṃ nṝṇām 
prayāti vilayaṃ sadyaḥ sakṛd yatrānusaṃsmṛte  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye ṇārP  śukrabalisaṃvāde 
harir harati pāpāni duṣṭacittair api smṛtaḥ 
anicchayāpi saṃspṛṣṭo dahaty eva hi pāvakaḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva ṇārP  prāyaścittaprasaṅgānte
mahāpātakayukto vā yukto vā sarvapātakaiḥ 
sa vai vimucyate sadyo yasya viṣṇuparaṃ manaḥ  Hbhv 
brahmavaivarte 
karmaṇā manasā vācā yaḥ kṛtaḥ pāpasañcayaḥ 
so 'py aśeṣaḥ kṣayaṃ yāti smṛtvā kṛṣṇāṅghrapaṅkajam  Hbhv 
ataevoktaṃ skānde kārttikaprasaṅge śrīparāśareṇa 
yamamārgaṃ mahāghoraṃ narakāṃś ca yamaṃ tathā 
svapne'pi na naraḥ paśyed yaḥ smared garuḍadhvajam  Hbhv 
ṣaṣṭhaskandhe BhP  śrīśukena 
sakṛn manaḥ kṛṣṇapadāravindayor
niveśitaṃ tadguṇarāgi yair iha 
na te yamaṃ pāśabhṛtaś ca tadbhaṭān
svapne 'pi paśyanti hi cīrṇaniṣkṛtāḥ  Hbhv 
sarvāpadvimocakatvam
śrīviṣṇupurāṇe ViP  śrīprahlādoktau 
dantā gajānāṃ kulśāgraniṣṭhurāḥ
śīrṇā yad ete na balaṃ mamaitat 
mahāvipatpātavināśano 'yaṃ
janārdanānusmaraṇānubhāvaḥ  Hbhv 
vāmanapurāṇe ca 
viṣṭayo vyatipātāś ca ye'nye durnītisambhavāḥ 
te sarve smaraṇād viṣṇor nāśam āyānty upadravāḥ  Hbhv 
pādme māghamāhātmye devadyutistutau 
yasya smaraṇamātreṇa na moho na ca durgatiḥ 
na rogo na ca duḥkhāni tam anantaṃ namāmy aham  Hbhv 
durvāsanonmūlanatvam
dvādaśaskandhe BhP  
yathā hemni sthito vahnir durvarṇaṃ hanti dhātujam 
evam ātmagato viṣṇur yoginām aśubhāśayam  Hbhv 
sarvamaṅgalakāritvam
pāṇḍavagītāyām
lābhas teṣāṃ jayas teṣāṃ kutas teṣāṃ parābhavaḥ 
yeṣām indīvaraśyāmo hṛdayasthajanārdanaḥ  Hbhv 
sarvasatkarmaphaladatvam
skānde kārttikaprasaṅge'gastyoktau
deveṣu yajñeṣu tapaḥsu caiva
dāneṣu tīrtheṣu vrateṣu caiva 
iṣṭeṣu pūrteṣu ca yat pradiṣṭaṃ
nṝṇāṃ smṛte tatphalam acyute ca  Hbhv 
karmasādguṇyakāritvam
bṛhannāradīye ṇārP 
nyūnātiriktatā siddhā kalau vedoktakarmaṇām 
harisaṃsmaraṇam evātra sampūrṇaphaladāyakam  Hbhv 
smṛtau ca
pramādāt kurvatāṃ karma pracyavetādhvareṣu yat 
smaraṇād eva tad viṣṇoḥ sampūrṇaṃ syād iti śrutiḥ  Hbhv 
sarvakarmādhikatvam
bṛhannāradīye kaliprasaṅge ṇārP 
tulāpuruṣadānānāṃ rājasūyāśvamedhayoḥ 
phalaṃ viṣṇoḥ smṛtisamaṃ na jātu dvijasattama  Hbhv 
dvādaśaskandhe BhP 
vidyātapaḥprāṇanirodhamaitrī
tīrthābhiṣekavratadānajapyaiḥ 
nātyantaśuddhiṃ labhate 'ntarātmā
yathā hṛdisthe bhagavaty anante  Hbhv 
viṣṇupurāṇe ViP  hiraṇyakaśipuṃ prati śrīprahlādoktau 
bhayaṃ bhayānām apahāriṇi sthite
manasy anante mama kutra tiṣṭhati 
yasmin smṛte janmajarodbhavāni
bhayāni sarvāṇy apayānti tāta  Hbhv 
tatraivānyatra ViP  
viṣṇusaṃsmaraṇāt kṣīṇasamastakleśasaṃcayaḥ 
muktiṃ prayāti svargāptis tasya vighno 'numīyate  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye ṇārP  
varaṃ vareṇyaṃ varadaṃ purāṇaṃ
nijaprabhābhāvitasarvalokam 
saṅkalpitārthapradam ādidevaṃ
smṛtvā vrajen muktipadaṃ manuṣyaḥ  Hbhv 
skānde
yasya smaraṇamātreṇa janmasaṃsārabandhanāt 
vimucyate namas tasmai viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave  Hbhv 
tatraiva kārttikaprasaṅge śrīparāśaroktau
tadaiva puruṣo mukto janmaduḥkhajarādibhiḥ 
bhaktyā tu parayā nūnaṃ yadaiva smarate harim  Hbhv 
bhagavatprasādanam
bṛhannāradīye ṇārP  
yena kenāpy upāyena smṛto nārāyaṇo 'vyayaḥ 
api pātakayuktasya prasannaḥ syān na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
śrīvaikuṇṭhalokaprāpakatvam
vāmanapurāṇe
anādyanantam ajarāmaraṃ hariṃ
ye saṃsmaranty aharahar niyataṃ narā bhuvi 
tat sarvagaṃ brahma paraṃ purāṇaṃ
te yānti vaiṣṇavapadaṃ dhurvam avyayaṃ ca  Hbhv 
pādme  devadūtavikuṇḍalasaṃvāde yamasya dūtānuśāsane
smaranti ye sakṛd bhūtāḥ prasaṅgenāpi keśavam 
te vidhvastākhilāghaughā yanti viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam  Hbhv 
brahmapurāṇe viṣṇurahasye 
śāṭhyenāpi narā nityaṃ ye smaranti janārdanam 
te 'pi yānti tanuṃ tyaktvā viṣṇulokam anāmayam  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare
nirāśīr nirmamo yas tu viṣṇor dhyānaparo bhavet 
tatpadaṃ samavāpnoti yatra gatvā na śocati  Hbhv 
sārūpyaprāpaṇam
kāśīkhaṇḍe śrībindumādhavaprasaṅge agnibindustutau
ye tvāṃ trivikrama sadā hṛdi śīlayanti
kādambinīrucir arociṣam ambujākṣa 
saudāminīvilasitāṃśukavītamūrte
te'pi spṛśanti tava kāntim acintyarūpām  Hbhv 
śrībhagavadgītāsu ṅītā  
antakāle ca mām eva smaran muktvā kalevaram 
yaḥ prayāti sa madbhāvaṃ yāti nāsty atra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
daśamaskandhe BhP  pṛthukopākhyāne 
smarataḥ pādakamalam ātmānam api yacchati 
kiṃ nv arthakāmān bhajato nātyabhīṣṭān jagadguruḥ  Hbhv 
vaiṣṇave
vāsudeve mano yasya japahomārcanādiṣu 
tasyāntarāyo maitreya devendratvādi satphalam  Hbhv 
gāruḍe
mahatas tapaso mūlaṃ prasavaḥ puṇyasantateḥ 
jīvitasya phalaṃ svādu niyataṃ smaraṇaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv 
dvitīyaskandhe BhP  
etāvān sāṅkhyayogābhyāṃ svadharmapariniṣṭhayā 
janmalābhaḥ paraḥ puṃsām ante nārāyaṇasmṛtiḥ  Hbhv 
ataeva jarāsandhaniruddhanṛpavargaiḥ prārthitaṃ daśamaskandhe BhP  
taṃ naḥ samādiśopāyaṃ yena te caraṇābjayoḥ 
smṛtir yathā na viramed api saṃsaratām iha  Hbhv 
śrīnāradenāpi BhP  
dṛṣṭaṃ tavāṅghriyugalaṃ janatāpavargaṃ
brahmādibhir hṛdi vicintyam agādhabodhaiḥ 
saṃsārakūpapatitottaraṇāvalambaṃ
dhyāyaṃś carāmy anugṛhāṇa yathā smṛtiḥ syāt  Hbhv 
 iti 
kṛṣṇasmaraṇamāhātmyamahābdhir dustaro dhiyā 
yo yiyāsati tatpāraṃ sa hi caitanyavañcitaḥ  Hbhv 
tataḥ pādodakaṃ kiñcit prāk pītvā tulasīdalaiḥ 
gṛhītenācaret tena svamūrdhany abhiṣecanam  Hbhv 
athādau śrīguruṃ natvā śrīkṛṣṇasya padābjayoḥ 
kiñcid vijñāpayan sarvasvakṛtyāny arpayen namet  Hbhv 
atha prātaḥ praṇāmaḥ
vāmanapurāṇe 
sarvamaṅgalamaṅgalyaṃ vareṇyaṃ varadaṃ śivam 
nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya sarvakarmāṇi kārayet  Hbhv 
atha vijñāpanam
viṣṇudharmottare 
yadutsavādikaṃ karma tat tvayā prerito hare 
kariṣyāmi tvayā jñeyam iti vijñāpanaṃ mama  Hbhv 
prātaḥ prabodhito viṣṇo hṛṣīkeśena yat tvayā 
yad yat kārayasīśāna tat karomi tavājñayā  Hbhv 
trailokyacaitanyamayādideva
śrīnātha viṣṇo bhavadājñayaiva 
prātaḥ samutthāya tava priyārthaṃ
saṃsārayātrām anuvartayiṣye  Hbhv 
saṃsārayātrām anuvartamānaṃ
tvadājñayā śrīnṛhare'ntarātman 
spardhātiraskārakalipramāda
bhayāni mā mābhibhavantu bhūman  Hbhv 
jānāmi dharmaṃ na ca me pravṛttir
jānāmy adharmaṃ na ca me nivṛttiḥ 
tvayā hṛṣīkeśa hṛdi sthitena
yathā niyukto 'smi tathā karomi  Hbhv 
atha praṇāmavākyāni
mahābhārate 
namo brahmaṇyadevāya gobrāhmaṇahitāya ca 
jagaddhitāya kṛṣṇāya govindāya namo namaḥ  Hbhv 
garuḍapurāṇe
asuravibudhasiddhair jñāyate yasya nāntaḥ
sakalamunibhir antaś cintyate yo viśuddhaḥ 
nikhilahṛdi niviṣṭo vetti yaḥ sarvasākṣī
tam ajam amṛtam īśaṃ vāsudevaṃ nato 'smi  Hbhv 
viṣṇupurāṇe ViP 
yajñibhir yajñapuruṣo vāsudevaś ca sātvataḥ 
vedāntavedibhir viṣṇuḥ procyate yo nato 'smi tam  Hbhv 
evaṃ vijñāpayan dhyāyan kīrtayaṃś ca yathāvidhi 
praṇāmānācarec chaktyā catuḥsaṅkhyāvarān budhaḥ  Hbhv 
śrīgopīcandanenordhvapuṇḍraṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi 
āsīta prāṅmukho bhūtvā śuddhasthāne śubhāsane  Hbhv 
tathā ca nāradīyapañcarātre
nirgatyācamya vidhivat praviśya ca punaḥ sudhīḥ 
āsane prāṅmukho bhūtvā vihite copaviśya vai  Hbhv 
sampradāyānusāreṇa bhūtaśuddhiṃ vidhāya ca 
prāṇāyāmāṃś ca vidhivat kṛṣṇaṃ dhyāyet yathoditam  Hbhv 
tathā coktam
upapātakeṣu sarveṣu pātakeṣu mahatsu ca 
praviśya rajanīpādaṃ viṣṇudhyānaṃ samācaret  Hbhv 
vaihāyasapañcarātre ca
tathaiva rātriśeṣaṃ tu kālaṃ sūryodayāvadhi 
kartavyaṃ sajapaṃ dhyānaṃ nityam ārādhakena vai  Hbhv 
vibhajya pañcadhā rātriṃ śeṣe devārcanādikam 
japaṃ homaṃ tathā dhyānaṃ nityaṃ kurvīta sādhakaḥ  Hbhv 
ataeva viṣṇusmṛtau
rātres tu paścime yāme muhūrtau brāhmya ucyate  Hbhv 
 iti 
pādodapānādīnāṃ ca sa vidhir mahimāgrataḥ 
lekhyo 'dhunā tu dhyānasya sa saṅkṣepeṇa likhyate  Hbhv 
tāpanīyaśrutiṣu ṅṭū  
satpuṇḍarīkanayanaṃ meghābhaṃ vaidyutāmbaram 
dvibhujaṃ jñānamudrāḍhyaṃ vanamālinam īśvaram  Hbhv 
gopagopīgavāvītaṃ suradrumatalāśritam 
dviyālaṅkaraṇopetaṃ ratnapaṅkajamadhyagam  Hbhv 
kālindījalakallolasaṅgimārutasevitam 
cintayaṃś cetasā kṛṣṇaṃ mukto bhavati saṃsṛteḥ  Hbhv 
mṛtyuñjayasaṃhitānusāroditasāradātilake ca 
smared vṛndāvane ramye mohayantam anāratam 
govindaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ gopakanyāḥ sahasraśaḥ  Hbhv 
ātmano vadanāmbhojapreritākṣimadhuvratāḥ 
kāmabāṇena vivaśāś ciram āśleṣeṇotsukāḥ  Hbhv 
muktāhāralasatpīnottuṅgastanabharānatāḥ 
srastadhammillavasanā madaskhalitabhāṣaṇāḥ  Hbhv 
dantapaṅktiprabhodbhāsispandamānādharāñcitāḥ 
vilobhayantīr vividhair vibhramair bhāvagarbhitaiḥ  Hbhv 
phullendīvarakāntim induvadanaṃ barhāvataṃsapriyaṃ
śrīvatsāṅkam udārakaustubhadharaṃ pītāmbaraṃ sundaram 
gopīnāṃ nayanotpalārcitatanuṃ gogopasaṅghāvṛtaṃ
govindaṃ kalaveṇuvādanaparaṃ divyāṅgabhūṣaṃ bhaje  Hbhv 
 iti 
śrīgautamīyatantrādau taddhyānaṃ prathitaṃ param 
agrato 'trāpi saṃlekhyaṃ yad iṣṭaṃ tatra tad bhajet  Hbhv 
bṛhatśātātāpasmṛtau
pakṣopavāsād yat pāpaṃ puruṣasya praṇaśyati 
prāṇāyāmaśatenaiva yat pāpaṃ naśyate nṝṇām  Hbhv 
prāṇāyāmasahasreṇa yat pāpaṃ naśyate nṝṇām 
kṣaṇamātreṇa tat pāpaṃ harer dhyānāt praṇaśyati  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharme
sarvapāpaprasakto 'pi dhyāyan nimiṣam acyutam 
bhūtas tapasvī bhavati paṅktipāvanapāvanaḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇupurāṇe  ca
dhyāyen nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ snānādiṣu ca karmasu 
prāyaścittaṃ hi sarvasya duṣkṛtasyeti niścitam  Hbhv 
kalidoṣaharatvam
bṛhannāradīye kaliprasaṅge ṇārP  
samastajagadādhāraṃ paramārthasvarūpiṇam 
ghore kaliyuge prāpte viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati  Hbhv 
sarvadharmādhikāritvam
skānde kārttikamāhātmye agastyoktau
kintv asya bahubhis tīrthaiḥ kiṃ tasya bahubhir vrataiḥ 
yo nityaṃ dhyāyate devaṃ nārāyaṇam ananyadhīḥ  Hbhv 
mokṣapradatvam
bṛhannāradīye kaliprasaṅge ṇārP  
ye mānavā vigatarāgaparāvarajñā
nārāyaṇaṃ suraguruṃ satataṃ smaranti 
dhyānena tena hata kilbiṣacetanās te
mātuḥ payodhararasaṃ na punaḥ pibanti  Hbhv 
śrīvaikuṇṭhaprāpakatvam
skānde śrībrahmoktau
muhūrtam api yo dhyāyen nārāyaṇam atandritaḥ 
so 'pi sadgatim āpnoti kiṃ punas tatparāyaṇaḥ  Hbhv 
pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye yamabrāhmaṇasaṃvāde PadmaP 
dhyāyanti puruṣaṃ divyam acyutaṃ ye smaranti ca 
labhante te'cyutasthānaṃ śrutir eṣā purātanī  Hbhv 
sārūpyaprāpaṇam
ekādaśaskandhe BhP  
vaireṇa yaṃ nṛpatayaḥ śiśupālapauṇḍra
śālvādayo gativilāsavilokanādyaiḥ 
dhyāyanta ākṛtadhiyaḥ śayanāsanādau
tatsāmyam āpur anuraktadhiyāṃ punaḥ kim  Hbhv 
svataḥ paramaphalatvam
caturthaskandhe BhP  śrīpṛthūktau 
bhajanty atha tvām ata eva sādhavo
vyudastamāyāguṇavibhramodayam 
bhavatpadānusmaraṇād ṛte satāṃ
nimittam anyad bhagavan na vidmahe  Hbhv 
skandapurāṇe brahmoktau ca 
āloḍya sarvaśāstrāṇi vicārya ca punaḥ punaḥ 
idame eva suniṣpannaṃ dhyeyo nārāyaṇaḥ sadā  Hbhv 
ataevoktaṃ hāyaśīrṣapañcarātre nārāyaṇavyūhastave 
ye tyaktalokadharmārthā viṣṇubhaktivaśaṃ gatāḥ 
dhyāyanti paramātmānaṃ tebhyo 'pīha namo namaḥ  Hbhv 
 iti 
smaraṇe yat tan māhātmyaṃ taddhyāne'py akhilaṃ viduḥ 
bhedaḥ kalpyeta sāmānyaviśeṣābhyāṃ tayoḥ kiyān  Hbhv 
atha śrībhagavatprabodhanam
tato devālaye gatvā ghaṇṭādyudghoṣapūrvakam 
prabodhya stutibhiḥ kṛṣṇaṃ nīrājyaṃ prārthayed idam  Hbhv 
tṛtīyaskandhe BhP  
so 'sāv adabhrakaruṇo bhagavān vivṛddha
premasmitena nayanāmburuhaṃ vijṛmbhan 
utthāya viśvavijayāya ca no viṣādaṃ
mādhvyā girāpanayatāt puruṣaḥ purāṇaḥ  Hbhv 
devaprapannārtihara prasādaṃ kuru keśava 
avalokanadānena bhūyo māṃ pārayācyuta  Hbhv 
 iti 
devālayaṃ praviśyātha stotrāṇīṣṭāni kīrtayan 
kṛṣṇasya tulasīvarjaṃ nirmālyam apasārayet  Hbhv 
atha nirmālyottāraṇam
atrismṛtau
prātaḥkāle sadā kuryān nirmālyottāraṇaṃ budhaḥ 
tṛṣitāḥ paśavo baddhāḥ kanyakā ca rajasvalā 
devatā ca sanirmālyā hanti puṇyaṃ purākṛtam  Hbhv 
nārasiṃhe śrīyamoktau
devamālyāpanayanaṃ devāgāre samūhanam 
snāpanaṃ sarvadevānāṃ gopradānasamaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv 
nāradapañcarātre
yaḥ prātar utthāya vidhāya nityaṃ
nirmālyam īśasya nirākaroti 
na tasya duḥkhaṃ na daridratā ca
nākālamṛtyur na ca rogamātram  Hbhv 
aruṇodayavelāyāṃ nirmālyaṃ śalyatāṃ vrajet 
prātas tu syān mahāśalyaṃ ghaṭikāmātrayogataḥ  Hbhv 
atiśalyaṃ vijānīyāt tato vajraprahāravat 
aruṇodayavelāyāṃ śalyaṃ tat kṣamate hariḥ  Hbhv 
ghaṭikāyām atikrāntau kṣudraṃ pātakam āvahet 
muhūrte samatikrānte pūrṇaṃ pātakam ucyate  Hbhv 
atipātakam ev syāt ghaṭikānāṃ catuṣṭaye 
muhūrtatritaye pūrṇe mahāpātakam ucyate  Hbhv 
tataḥ paraṃ brahmavadho mahāpātakapañcakam 
prahare pūrṇatāṃ yāte prāyaścittaṃ tato na hi  Hbhv 
nirmālyasya vilambe tu prāyaścittam athocyate 
atikrānte muhūrtārdhe sahasraṃ japam ācaret  Hbhv 
pūrṇe muhūrte sañjāte sahasraṃ sārdham ucyate 
sahasradvitīyaṃ kuryāt ghaṭikānāṃ catuṣṭaye  Hbhv 
muhūrtatritaye'tīte ayutaṃ japam ācaret 
prahare pūrṇatāṃ yāte puraścaraṇam ucyate 
prahare samatikrānte prāyaścittaṃ na vidyate  Hbhv 
atha śrīmukhaprakṣālanam
śrīhastāṅghrimukhāmbhojakṣālanāya ca tadgṛhe 
gaṇḍūṣāṇi jalair dattvā dantakāṣṭhaṃ samarpayet  Hbhv 
jihvollekhanikāṃ dattvā pāduke śuddhamṛttikām 
salilaṃ ca punar dadyād vāso 'pi mukhamārjanam  Hbhv 
tataḥ śrītulasīṃ puṇyām arpayet bhagavatpriyām 
tanmāhātmyaṃ ca tanmukhyaprasaṅge lekhyam agrataḥ  Hbhv 
atha dantakāṣṭhārpaṇamāhātmyam
viṣṇudharmottare
dantakāṣṭhapradānena dantasaubhāgyam ṛcchati 
jihvollekhanikāṃ dattvā virogas tv abhijāyate  Hbhv 
pādukāyāḥ pradānena gatim iṣṭām avāpnuyāt 
mṛdbhāgadānād devasya bhūmim āpnoty anuttamām  Hbhv 
atha maṅgalanīrājanam
paṭhitvātha priyān ślokān mahāvāditranisvanaiḥ 
prabhor nīrājanaṃ kuryān maṅgalākhyaṃ jagaddhitam  Hbhv 
nīrājanaṃ tv idaṃ sarvaiḥ kartavyaṃ śucivigrahaiḥ 
paramaśraddhayotthāya draṣṭavyaṃ ca sadā naraiḥ  Hbhv 
strīṇāṃ puṃsāṃ ca sarveṣām etat sarveṣṭapūrakam 
samastadainyadāridryaduritādyupaśāntikṛt  Hbhv 
atha prātaḥsnānārthodyamaḥ
tato 'ruṇodayasyānte snānārthaṃ niḥsared bahiḥ 
kīrtayan kṛṣṇanāmāni tīrthaṃ gacched anantaram  Hbhv 
tathā ca śukrasmṛtau
brāhme muhūrte cotthāya śucir bhūtvā samāhitaḥ 
svastikādyāsanaṃ baddhvā dhyātvā kṛṣṇapādāmbujam  Hbhv 
tato nirgatya nilayānnāmānīmāni kīrtayet 
śrīvāsudevāniruddhapradyumnādhokṣajācyuta 
śrīkṛṣṇānanta govinda saṅkarṣaṇa namo 'stu te  Hbhv 
gatvā tīrthādikaṃ tatra nikṣipya snānasādhanam 
vidhinācarya maitryādikṛtyaṃ śaucaṃ vidhāya ca 
ācamya khāni saṃmārjya snānaṃ kuryāt yathocitam  Hbhv 
atha maitryādikṛtyavidhiḥ
śrīviṣṇupurāṇe ViP  aurvasagarasaṃvāde gṛhidharmakathane
tataḥ kalye samutthāya kuryān mūtraṃ nareśvara 
nairṛtyām iṣuvikṣepam atītyādhikaṃ gṛhāt  Hbhv 
dūrādāvasathān mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ ca samutsṛjet 
pādāv asecanocchiṣṭe prakṣipen na gṛhāṅgaṇe  Hbhv 
ātmacchāyāṃ taroś chāyāṃ gosūryāgnyanilāṃs tathā 
guruṃ dvijādīṃś ca budho na meheta kadācana  Hbhv 
na kṛṣṭe śasyamadhye vā govraje janasaṃsadi 
na vartmani na nadyāditīrtheṣu puruṣarṣabha  Hbhv 
nāpsu naivāmbhasas tīre na śmaśāne samācaret 
utsargaṃ vai purīṣasya mūtrasya ca visarjanam  Hbhv 
udaṅmukho divotsargaṃ viparītamukho niśi 
kurvītānāpadi prājño mūtrotsargaṃ ca pārthiva  Hbhv 
tṛṇair ācchādya vasudhāṃ vastraprāvṛtamastakaḥ 
tiṣṭhen nāticiraṃ tatra naiva kiñcid udīrayet  Hbhv 
tathā kaurme vyāsagītāyām
nidhāya dakṣiṇe karṇe brahmasūtram udaṅmukhaḥ 
antardhāpya mahīṃ kāṣṭhaiḥ patrair loṣṭrais tṛṇena vā  Hbhv 
prāvṛtya tu śiraḥ kuryād vinmūtrasya visarjanam 
na caivābhimukhaḥ strīṇāṃ gurubrāhmaṇayor gavām 
na devadevālayor nāpām api kadācana  Hbhv 
nadīṃ jyotīṃṣi vīkṣitvā na vāyvagnimukho 'pi vā 
prayādityaṃ pratyanalaṃ pratisomaṃ tathaiva ca  Hbhv 
kāśīkāṇḍe śrīskandāgastyasaṃvāde
tataś cāvaśyakaṃ kartuṃ nairṛtīṃ diśam āśrayet 
grāmād dhanuḥśataṃ gacchen nagarāc ca caturguṇam  Hbhv 
karṇopavītyudagvaktro divase sandhyayor api 
vinmūtre visṛjen maunī niśāyāṃ dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ  Hbhv 
nālokayed diśo bhāgān jyotiś cakraṃ nabho 'malam 
vāmena pāṇinā śiśnaṃ dhṛtvottiṣṭhet prayatnavān  Hbhv 
tatraivāgre
na mūtraṃ govraje kuryān na valmīke na bhasmani 
na garteṣu sasattveṣu na tiṣṭhan na vrajann api  Hbhv 
yathāsukhamukho rātrau divā chāyāndhakārayoḥ 
bhītiṣu prāṇabādhāyāṃ kuryān malavisarjanam  Hbhv 
viṣṇupurāṇe BhP  tatraiva
valmīkamūṣikotkhātāṃ mṛdaṃ nāntarjalāt tathā 
śaucāvaśiṣṭāṃ gehāc ca na dadyāl lepasambhavām  Hbhv 
antaḥprāṇyavapannāṃ ca halotkhātāṃ ca pārthiva 
parityajen mṛdaś caitāḥ sakalāḥ śaucasādhane  Hbhv 
ekā liṅge gude tisras daśa vāmakare nṛpa 
hastadvaye saptānyā mṛdaḥ śaucopapādikāḥ  Hbhv 
yamasmṛtau
tisras tu pādayor deyāḥ śuddhikāmena nityaśaḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
tisras tu mṛttikā deyāḥ kṛtvā tu nakhaśodhanam  Hbhv 
kāśīkhaṇḍe ca tatraiva
guhye dadyān mṛdaṃ caikāṃ pāyau pañcāmbusāntarāḥ 
daśa vāmakare cāpi sapta pāṇidvaye mṛdaḥ  Hbhv 
ekaikāṃ pādayor dadyāt tisraḥ pāṇyor mṛdaḥ smṛtāḥ 
itthaṃ śaucaṃ gṛhī kuryād gandhalepakṣayāvadhi  Hbhv 
kramād dviguṇam etat tu brahmacaryādiṣu triṣu 
divā vihitaśaucāc ca rātrāv ardhaṃ samācaret  Hbhv 
rujārdhaṃ ca tadardhaṃ ca pathi caurādipīḍite 
tadardhayoṣitāṃ cāpi svāsthye nyūnaṃ na kārayet 
ārdradhātrīphalonmānā mṛdaḥ śauce prakīrtitāḥ  Hbhv 
śaṅkhasmṛtau
mṛttikā tu samuddiṣṭā triparvī pūryate yayā  Hbhv 
dakṣasmṛtau
ardhaprasṛtimātrā tu prathamā mṛttikā smṛtā 
dvitīyā ca tṛtīyā ca tadardhaṃ parikīrtitā  Hbhv 
atha kevalamūtrotsarge
dakṣaḥ
ekā liṅge tu savye trir ubhayor mṛddvayaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv 
brāhme
pādayor dve gṛhītvā ca suprakṣālitapāṇinā 
ācamya tu tataḥ śuddhaḥ smṛtvā viṣṇuṃ sanātanam  Hbhv 
viṣṇupurāṇe BhP  tatraiva
acchenāgandhaphenena jalenābudbudena ca 
ācāmeta mṛdaṃ bhūyas tathā dadyāt samāhitaḥ  Hbhv 
niṣpāditāṅghriśaucas tu pāpāv abhyukṣya vai punaḥ 
triḥ pibet salilaṃ tena tathā dviḥ parimārjayet  Hbhv 
śīrṣaṇyāni tataḥ khāni mūrdhānaṃ ca mṛdā labhet 
bāhū nābhiṃ ca toyena hṛdayaṃ cāpi saṃspṛśet  Hbhv 
atra ca viśeṣo dakṣeṇoktaḥ
prakṣālya hastau pādau ca triḥ pibed ambu vīkṣitam 
saṃvṛttāṅguṣṭhamūlena dviḥ pramṛjyāt tato mukham  Hbhv 
saṃhatya tisṛbhiḥ pūrvam āsyam evam upaspṛśet 
aṅguṣṭhena pradeśinyā ghrāṇaṃ paścād anantaram  Hbhv 
aṅguṣṭhānāmikābhyāṃ tu cakṣuḥśrotre punaḥ punaḥ 
kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhayor nābhiṃ hṛdayaṃ tu talena vai 
sarvābhis tu śiraḥ paścād bāhū cāgreṇa saṃspṛśet  Hbhv 
tathā kāśīkhaṇḍe tatraiva
prāg āsya udagāsyo vā sūpaviṣṭaḥ śucau bhuvi 
upaspṛśed vihīnāyāṃ tuṣāṅgārāsthibhasmabhiḥ  Hbhv 
anuṣṇābhir aphenābhir adbhir hṛdgābhir atvaraḥ 
brāhmaṇo brahmatīrthena dṛṣṭipūtanābhir ācamet  Hbhv 
kaṇṭhagābhir nṛpaḥ śudhyet tālugābhis tathorujaḥ 
strīśūdrāvāsyasaṃsparśamātreṇāpi visudhyataḥ  Hbhv 
yājñavalkyasmṛtau
pādakṣālanaśeṣeṇa nācāmet vāriṇā dvijaḥ 
yady ācamet srāvayitvā bhūmau baudhāyano 'bravīt  Hbhv 
bharadvājasmṛtau
pāṇinā dakṣiṇenaiva saṃhatāṅgulinācamet 
muktāṅguṣṭhakaniṣṭhena nakaspṛṣṭā apas tyajet  Hbhv 
kaurme ca vyāsagītāyām
bhuktvā pītvā ca suptvā ca snātvā rathyopasarpaṇe 
auṣṭhau vilomakau spṛṣṭvā vāso viparidhāya ca  Hbhv 
retomūtrapurīṣāṇām utsarge'nṛtabhāṣaṇe 
ṣthīvitvādhyayanārambhe kāśaśvāsāgame tathā  Hbhv 
catvaraṃ vā śmaśānaṃ vā samabhyasya dvijottamaḥ 
sandhyor ubhayos tadvad ācānto 'py ācamet punaḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
śiraḥ prāvṛtya kaṇṭhaṃ vā muktakacchaśikho 'pi vā 
akṛtvā pādayoḥ śaucam ācānto 'py aśucir bhavet  Hbhv 
sopānatkau jalastho vā noṣṇīṣī cācamed budhaḥ 
na caiva varṣadhārābhir hastocchiṣṭe tathā budhaḥ  Hbhv 
naikahastārpiuttajalair vinā sūtreṇa vā punaḥ 
na pādukāsanastho vā bahir jānur athāpi vā  Hbhv 
atha vaiṣṇavācamanam
triḥpāne keśavaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ mādhavam apy atha 
prakṣālane dvayoḥ pāṇyor govindaṃ viṣṇum apy ubhau  Hbhv 
madhusūdanam ekaṃ ca mārjane'nyaṃ trivikramam  Hbhv 
unmārjane'py adharayor vāmanaśrīdharāv ubhau  Hbhv 
prakṣālane punaḥ pāṇyor hṛṣīkeśaṃ ca pādayoḥ 
padmanābhaṃ prokṣaṇe tu mūrdhno dāmodaraṃ tataḥ  Hbhv 
vāsudevaṃ mukhe saṅkarṣaṇaṃ pradyumnam ity ubhau 
nāsayor netrayugale'niruddhaṃ puruṣottamam 
adhokṣajaṃ nṛsiṃhaṃ ca karṇayor nābhito 'cyutam  Hbhv 
janārdanaṃ ca hṛdaye upendraṃ mastake tataḥ 
dakṣiṇe tu hariṃ bāhau vāme kṛṣṇaṃ yathāvidhi 
namo 'nantaṃ ca caturthyantam ācāmet kramato japan  Hbhv 
aśaktaḥ kevalam dakṣaṃ spṛśet karṇaṃ tathā ca vāk 
kurvītālabhanaṃ vāpi dakṣiṇaśravaṇasya vai  Hbhv 
atha dantadhāvanavidhiḥ
tatra kātyāyanaḥ
utthāya netraṃ prakṣālya śucir bhūtvā samāhitaḥ 
parijapya ca mantreṇa bhakṣayed dantadhāvanam  Hbhv 
mantraś cāyam
āyur balaṃ yaśo varcaḥ prajā paśuvasūni ca 
brahma prajñāṃ ca medhāṃ ca tvaṃ no dhehi vanaspate  Hbhv 
tasya nityatā
kāśīkhaṇḍe
atho mukhaviśuddhyarthaṃ gṛhṇīyād dantadhāvanam 
ācānto 'py aśucir yasmād akṛtvā dantadhāvanam  Hbhv 
vārāhe ca
dantakāṣṭham akhāditvā yas tu mām upasarpati 
sarvakālakṛtaṃ karma tena caikena naśyati  Hbhv 
atha dantakāṣṭhaniṣiddhadināni
manuḥ
caturdaśyaṣṭamīdarśapaurṇamāsyarkasaṅkramaḥ 
eṣu strītailamāṃsāni dantakāṣṭhāni varjayet  Hbhv 
saṃvartakaḥ
ādye tithau navamyāṃ ca kṣaye candramasas tathā 
ādityvāre śaure ca varjayed dantadhāvanam  Hbhv 
kātyāyanaḥ
pratipaddarśaṣaṣṭhīṣu navamyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ 
dantānāṃ kāṣṭhasaṃyogo dahaty āsaptamaṃ kulam  Hbhv 
vṛddhavaśiṣṭhaḥ
upavāse tathā śrāddhena khāded dantadhāvanam 
dantānāṃ kāṣṭhasaṃyogo hanti saptakulāni vai  Hbhv 
anyatra ca
pratipaddaraṣaṣṭhīṣu navamyekādaśīravau 
dantānāṃ kāṣṭhasaṃyogo hanti puṇyaṃ purākṛtam  Hbhv 
atha tatra pratinidhiḥ
dinaeṣv eteṣu kāṣṭhair hi dantānāṃ dhāvanasya tu 
niṣiddhatvāt tṛṇaiḥ kuryāt tathā kāṣṭhetaraiś ca tat  Hbhv 
tathā ca vyāsaḥ
pratipaddarśaṣaṣṭhīṣu navamyāṃ dantadhāvanam 
parṇair anyatra kāṣṭhaiś ca jīvollekhhaḥ sadaiva hi  Hbhv 
paiṭhīnasiḥ
alābhe ca niṣedhe vā kāṣṭhānāṃ dantadhāvanam 
parṇādinā viśuddhena jihvollekhaḥ sadaiva hi  Hbhv 
atha tatraivāpavādaḥ
kāṣṭhaiḥ pratipadādau yan niṣiddhaṃ dantadhāvanam 
tṛṇaparṇais tu tat kuryād amām ekādaśīṃ vinā  Hbhv 
ata eva vyāsasya vacanāntaram
alābhe dantakāṣṭhānāṃ niṣiddhāyāṃ tathā tithau 
apāṃ dvādaśagaṇḍūṣair vidadhyād dantadhāvanam  Hbhv 
kāśīkhaṇḍe tatraiva
mukhe paryuṣite yasmād bhaved aśucibhāg naraḥ 
tataḥ kuryāt prayatnena śuddhyarthaṃ dantadhāvanam  Hbhv 
upavāse'pi no duṣyed dantadhāvanam añjanam 
gandhālaṅkārasadvastrapuṣpamālānulepanam  Hbhv 
atha dantakāṣṭhāni
smṛtau
sarva kaṇṭakinaḥ puṇyāḥ āyurdāḥ kṣīriṇaḥ smṛtāḥ 
kaṭutiktakaṣāyāś ca balārogyasukhapradāḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
palāśānāṃ dantakāṣṭhaṃ pāduke caiva varjayet 
varjayec ca prayatnena baṭaṃ vāśvattham eva ca  Hbhv 
kaurme śrīvyāsagītāyām
madhyāṅgulisamasthaulyaṃ dvādaśāṅgulasammitam 
satvacaṃ dantakāṣṭhaṃ yat tadagre na tu dhārayet  Hbhv 
kṣīrivṛkṣasamudbhūtaṃ mālatīsambhavaṃ śubham 
apāmārgaṃ ca bilvaṃ vā karavīraṃ viśeṣatah  Hbhv 
varjayitvā ninitāni gṛhītvaikaṃ yathoditam 
parihṛtya dinaṃ pāpaṃ bhakṣayed vai vidhānavit  Hbhv 
na pāṭayet dantakāṣṭhaṃ nāṅgulyagreṇa dhārayet 
prakṣālya bhuktvā taj jahyāt śucau deśe samāhitaḥ  Hbhv 
kāśīkhaṇḍe ca tatraiva
kaniṣṭhāgraparīṇāhaṃ satvacaṃ nirvraṇaṃ ṛjum 
dvādaśāṅgulamānaṃ ca sārdraṃ syād dantadhāvanam 
jihvollekhanikām vāpi kuryāc cāpākṛtiṃ śubhām  Hbhv 
rāmārcanacandrikāyām ca
dantollekho vitastyā bhavati parimitād annam ity ādimantrāt
prātaḥ kṣīryādikāṣṭhād vaṭakhadirapalāśair vinārkāmrabilvaiḥ 
bhuktvā gaṇḍūṣaṣaṭkaṃ dvir api kuśam ṛte deśinīm aṅgulībhir
nandābhūtāṣṭaparvaṇy api na khalu navamyarkasaṅkrāntipāte  Hbhv 
atha keśaprasādhanādiḥ
tataś cācamya vidhivat kṛtvā keśaprasādhanam 
smṛtvā praṇavagāyatryau nibadhnīyāc chikhāṃ dvijaḥ  Hbhv 
tathā coktaṃ
na dakṣiṇāmukho nordhvaṃ kuryāt keśaprasādhanam 
smṛtvoṅkāraṃ ca gāyatrīṃ nibadhnīyāc cikhāntataḥ  Hbhv 
atha snānam
viṣṇupurāṇe BhP  tatraiva
nadīnadataḍāgeṣu devakhātajaleṣu ca 
nityakriyārthaṃ snāyīta giriprasravaṇeṣu ca  Hbhv 
kūpeṣūddhṛtatoyena snānaṃ kurvīta vā bhuvi 
snāyītoddhṛtatoyena athavā bhuvy asambhave  Hbhv 
atha snānanityatā
tatra kātyāyanaḥ
yathāhani tathā prātar nityaṃ snāyād anāturaḥ 
atyantamalinaḥ kāyo navacchidrasamanvitaḥ 
sravat eva divārātrau prātaḥsnānaṃ viśodhanam  Hbhv 
dakṣaḥ
prātar madhyāhnayoḥ snānaṃ vānaprasthagṛhasthayoḥ 
yates trisavanaṃ snānaṃ sakṛt tu brahmacāriṇaḥ  Hbhv 
sarve cāpi sakṛt kuryur aśaktau codakaṃ vinā  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
aśiraskaṃ bhavet snānam aśaktau karmiṇāṃ sadā 
ārdreṇa vāsasā vāpi pāṇinā vāpi mārjanam  Hbhv 
śaṅkhaś ca
asnātas tu pumān nārho japādihavanādiṣu  Hbhv 
kaurme vyāsagītāyām
prātaḥsnānaṃ vinā puṃsāṃ pāpitvaṃ karmasu smṛtam 
home jape viśeṣeṇa tasmāt snānaṃ samācaret  Hbhv 
kāśīkhaṇḍe
prasvedalālasādyāklinno nidrādhīno yato naraḥ 
prātaḥsnānāt tato 'rhaḥ syān mantrastotrajapādiṣu  Hbhv 
pādme ca devahūtivikuṇḍalasaṃvāde PadmaP  
snānaṃ vinā tu yo bhuṅkte malāśī sa sadā naraḥ 
asnāyino 'śuces tasya vimukhāḥ pitṛdevatāḥ  Hbhv 
snānahīno naraḥ pāpaḥ snānahīno naro 'śuciḥ 
asnāyī narakaṃ bhuṅkte puṃskīṭādiṣu jāyate  Hbhv 
atha snānamāhātmyam
mahābhārate  udyogaparvaṇi śrīviduroktau
guṇā daśa snānaśīlaṃ bhajante
balaṃ rūpaṃ svaravarṇapraśuddhiḥ 
sparśaś ca gandhaś ca viśuddhatā ca
śrīḥ saukumāryaṃ pravarāś ca nāryaḥ  Hbhv 
pādme ca  tatraiva
yāmyaṃ hi yātanāduḥkhaṃ nityasnāyī na paśyati 
nityasnānena pūyante api pāpakṛto narāḥ  Hbhv 
prātaḥsnānaṃ hared vaiśya bāhyābhyantarajaṃ malam 
prātaḥsnānena niṣpāpo naro na nirayaṃ vrajet  Hbhv 
ye punaḥ srotasi snānam ācarantīha parvaṇi 
tenaiva narakaṃ yānti na jāyante kuyoniṣu  Hbhv 
duḥsvapnā duṣṭacintāś ca bandhyā bhavanti sarvadā 
prātaḥsnānena śuddhānāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ viśāṃ vara  Hbhv 
atrismṛtau
snāne manaḥprasādaḥ syād devā abhimukhāḥ sadā 
saubhāgyaṃ śrīḥ sukhaṃ puṣṭiḥ puṇyaṃ vidyā yaśo dhṛtiḥ  Hbhv 
mahāpāpāny alakṣmīṃ ca duritaṃ durvicintitam 
śokaduḥkhādi harate prātaḥsnānaṃ viśeṣataḥ  Hbhv 
kaurme tatraiva
prātaḥsnānaṃ praśaṃsanti dṛṣṭādṛṣṭakaraṃ hi tat 
prātaḥsnānena pāpāni pūyante nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
kāśīkhaṇḍe ca
prātaḥsnānāt yataḥ śudhyet kāyo 'yaṃ malinaḥ sadā 
chidrito navabhiś chidraiḥ sravaty eva divāniśam  Hbhv 
utsāhamedhāsaubhāgyarūpasampatpravartakam 
manaḥprasannatāhetuḥ prātaḥsnānaṃ praśasyate  Hbhv 
prātaḥ prātas tu yat snānaṃ saṃjāte cāruṇodvaye 
prājāpatyasamaṃ prāhus tan mahāghavighātakṛt  Hbhv 
prātaḥsnānaṃ haret pāpam alakṣmīṃ glānim eva ca 
aśucitvaṃ ca duḥsvapnaṃ tuṣṭiṃ puṣṭiṃ prayacchati  Hbhv 
nopasarpanti vai duṣṭāḥ prātaḥsnāyijanaṃ kvacit 
dṛṣṭādṛṣṭaphalaṃ tasmāt prātaḥsnānaṃ samācaret  Hbhv 
snānamātraṃ tathā prātaḥsnānaṃ cātra niyojitam 
yadyapy anyo 'nyamilite pṛthag jñeye tathāpy amū  Hbhv 
atha snānavidhiḥ
atha tīrthagatas tatra dhautavastraṃ kuśāṃs tathā 
mṛttikāṃ ca taṭe nyasya snāyāt svasvavidhānataḥ  Hbhv 
adhautena tu vastreṇa nityanaimittikīṃ kriyām 
kurvan na phalam āpnoti kṛtā cen niṣphalā bhavet  Hbhv 
dhautāṅghripāṇir ācāntaḥ kṛtvā saṅkalpam ādarāt 
gaṅgādismaraṇaṃ kṛtvā tīrthāyārghyaṃ samarpayet  Hbhv 
sāgarasvananirghoṣadaṇḍahastāsurāntaka 
jagatsraṣṭar jaganmardin namāmi tvāṃ sureśvara  Hbhv 
imaṃ mantraṃ samuccārya tīrthasnānaṃ samācaret 
anyathā tatphalasyārdhaṃ tīrtheśo harati svayam  Hbhv

devadeva jagannātha śaṅkhacakragadādhara 
dehi viṣṇo mamānujñāṃ tava tīrthaniṣevaṇe  Hbhv 
 iti 
vidhivan mṛdam ādāya tīrthatoye praviśya ca 
pravāhābhimukho nadyāṃ syād anyatrārkasammukhaḥ  Hbhv 
digbandhaṃ vidhinācarya tīrthāni parikalpya ca 
āvāhayed bhagavatīṃ gaṅgām ādityamaṇḍalāt  Hbhv 
darbhapāṇiḥ kṛtaprāṇāyāmaḥ kṛṣṇapadāmbujam 
dhyātvā tannāma saṅkīrtya nimajjet puṇyavāriṇi  Hbhv 
ācamya mūlamantraṃ ca saprāṇāyāmakaṃ japan

kṛtvāghamarṣaṇāntaṃ ca nāmabhiḥ keśavādibhiḥ 
tatra dvādaśadhā toye nimajjya snānam ācaret  Hbhv 
tatra viśeṣaḥ
śrīnāradapañcarātre
prasiddheṣu ca tīrtheṣu yady anyasyābhidhāṃ smaret

 iti 
iti vaidikatāntrikamiśrito vidhiḥ

 śrīnāradāmbarīṣasaṃvāde

auṃ namo nārāyaṇāya mūlamantra udāhṛtaḥ  Hbhv

 ityādi 
saptavārābhijaptena karasampuṭayojite

 iti

 iti

padmapurāṇe

kaurme tatraiva
prākkuleṣu tataḥ sthitvā darbheṣu susamāhitaḥ

manusmṛtau

yata upāsate devīṃ gāyatrīṃ vedamātaram  Hbhv

 iti

atha matāntaratāntrikasandhyāvidhiḥ

sā coktā

 iti

brahmāṇaṃ tarpayet pūrvaṃ viṣṇuṃ rudraṃ prajāpatīn 
devā yakṣās tathā nāgā gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ  Hbhv 
krūrāḥ sarpāḥ suparṇāś ca taravo jambhakādayaḥ 
vidyādharā jaladharās tathaivākāśagāminaḥ  Hbhv 
nirādhārāś ca ye jīvā pāpadharmaratāś ca ye 
teṣām āpyāyanāyaitad dīyate salilaṃ mayā  Hbhv 
kṛtopavīto devebhyo nivītī ca bhavet tataḥ 
manuṣyāṃs tarpayed bhaktyā ṛṣiputrān ṛṣīṃs tathā  Hbhv 
sanakaś ca sanandaś ca tṛtīyaś ca sanātanaḥ 
kapilaś cāsuriś caiva voḍhuḥ pañcaśikhas tathā 
sarve te tṛptim āyāntu maddattenāmbunā sadā  Hbhv 
marīcim atryaṅgirasau pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum 
pracetasaṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca bhṛguṃ nāradam eva ca 
devabrahmaṛṣīn sarvāṃs tarpayet sākṣatodakaiḥ  Hbhv 
apasavyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvāsavyaṃ jānu ca bhūtale 
agniṣv āttās tathā saumyā bahiṣmantas tathoṣmapāḥ  Hbhv 
kavyānalau barhiṣadas tathā caivājyapāḥ punaḥ 
tarpayet pitṛbhaktyā ca satilokdakacandanaiḥ  Hbhv 
yamāya dharmarājāya mṛtyave cāntakāya ca 
vaivasvatāya kālāya sarvabhūtākṣayāya ca  Hbhv 
auḍumbarāya dadhnāya nīlāya parameṣṭhine 
vṛkodarāya citrāya citraguptāya vai namaḥ  Hbhv 
darbhapāṇiḥ suprayataḥ pitṝn svān tarpayet tataḥ  Hbhv 
pitrādīn nāmagotreṇa tathā mātāmahān api 
santarpya vidhinā sarvān imaṃ mantram udīrayet  Hbhv 
ye'bāndhavā bāndhavā vā ye'nyajanmani bāndhavāḥ 
te tṛptim akhilāṃ yāntu ye cāsmattoyakāṅkṣiṇaḥ  Hbhv 
 iti

snāne mṛdgrahaṇānantaram

kāśīkāṇḍe

 śrīnāradāmbarīṣasaṃvāde

śrīvaiṣṇavālaṅkāraḥ

atha śrībhagavanmandirasaṃskāraḥ
mandiraṃ mārjayed viṣṇor vidhāyācamanādikam

bhaktyā tat parito limped abhukṣec ca tadaṅganam  Hbhv

śrīviṣṇudharmottare

tāvanty abdāni sa sukhī nākam āsādya modate  Hbhv 
śrīvārāhe
