athopalepanamāhātmyam
tatraiva
gomayaṃ gṛhya vai bhūmiṃ mama veśmopalepayet 
yāvatas tu padāṃs tatra samantād upalepayet 
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi madbhakto jāyate tathā  Hbhv 
samīpe yadi vā dūre yaś cālayati gomayam 
yāvat tasya padāgrāṇi tāvat svarge mahīyate  Hbhv 
śālmalau tatparibhraṣṭo rājā bhavati dhārmikaḥ 
madbhaktaś caiva jāyate sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ  Hbhv 
yaś cālepayate bhūmiṃ gomayena dṛḍhavrataḥ 
tasya dṛṣṭvānulepaṃ tu mama tuṣṭiḥ prajāyate  Hbhv 
goś ca yasyāḥ purīṣeṇa kriyate bhūmilepanam 
ekenaiva tu lepena goyonyā vipramucyate  Hbhv 
sthānopalepane bhūme salilaṃ yo dadāti me 
tasya puṇyaṃ mahābhāge śṛṇu tattvena niṣkalam  Hbhv 
yāvanti jalabindūni lipyamānasya sundari 
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate  Hbhv 
yāvanto bindavaḥ kecit pānīyasya vasundhare 
tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi krauñcadvīpe mahīyate  Hbhv 
krauñcadvīpāt paribhraṣṭaḥ sarvadharmaparāyaṇaḥ 
sarvasaṅgān parityajya mama lokaṃ ca gacchati  Hbhv 
śrīviṣṇudharmottare
kṛtvopalepanaṃ viṣṇor naras tv āyatane sadā 
gomayena śubhān lokān ayatnād eva gacchati  Hbhv 
hastapramāṇaṃ bhūbhāgam upalipya narādhipa 
devarāmāśataṃ nāke labhate satataṃ naraḥ  Hbhv 
nārasiṃhe
gomayena mṛdā toyair yaḥ kuryād upalepanam 
cāndrāyaṇaphalaṃ prāpya viṣṇuloke mahīyate  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrīdharmarājasya dūtānuśāsane
saṃmārjanaṃ yaḥ kurute gomayenopalepanam 
karoti bhavane viṣṇos tyājyaṃ teṣāṃ kulatrayam  Hbhv 
athābhukṣaṇamāhātmyam
śrīviṣṇudharmottare
abhyukṣaṇaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt pānīyena surālaye 
sa śāntatāpo bhavati nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  Hbhv 
abhyukṣaṇaṃ tu yaḥ kuryād devadevājire naraḥ 
sarvapāpavinirmukto vāruṇaṃ lokam aśnute  Hbhv 
sarvatobhadrapadmādīn abhijñaḥ svastikāni ca 
viracayya vicitrāṇi maṇḍayed dharimandiram  Hbhv 
tathā ca nārasiṃhe
saṃmārjanopalepābhyāṃ raṅgapadmādiśobhanam 
kuryāt sthānaṃ mahāviṣṇoḥ sojjvalāṅgaṃ mudānvitaḥ  Hbhv 
atha maṇḍalamāhātmyam
skandapurāṇe kārttikaprasaṅge
agamyagamane pāpam abhakṣyasya ca bhakṣaṇe 
sarvaṃ tannāśam āpnoti maṇḍayitvā harer gṛham  Hbhv 
aṇumātraṃ tu yaḥ kuryān maṇḍalaṃ keśavāgrataḥ 
mṛdā dhātuvikāraiś ca divi kalpaśataṃ vaset  Hbhv 
śālagrāmaśilāgre tu yaḥ kuryāt svastikaṃ śubham 
kārttike tu viśeṣeṇa punāty āsaptamaṃ kulam  Hbhv 
maṇḍalaṃ kurute nityaṃ yā nārī keśavāgrataḥ 
saptajanmāni vaidhavyaṃ na prāpnoti kadācana  Hbhv 
gṛhītvā gomayaṃ yā tu maṇḍalaṃ keśavāgrataḥ 
bhartur viyogaṃ nāpnoti santateś ca dhanasya ca  Hbhv 
prāṅgaṇaṃ varṇakopetaṃ svastikaiś ca samanvitam 
devasya kurute yas tu krīḍate bhuvanatraye  Hbhv 
nāradīye
mṛdā dhātuvikārair vā varṇakair gomayena vā 
viṣṇuloke'tha tatra rathaiḥ saspṛhaṃ vīkṣyate sukhī  Hbhv 
haribhaktisudhodaye
upalipyālayaṃ viṣṇoś citrayitvātha varṇakaiḥ 
viṣṇuloke'tha tatrasthaiḥ saspṛhaṃ vīkṣyate sukhī  Hbhv 
atha svastikalakṣaṇam
āgame
vidiggatacatuṣkāṇi bhittvā ṣoḍaśadhā sudhīḥ 
mārjayet svastikākāraṃ śvetapītāruṇāsitaiḥ  Hbhv 
tatra ca pañcarātravacanam
rajāṃsi pañcavarṇāni maṇḍalārthaṃ hi kārayet 
śālitaṇḍulacūrṇena śuklaṃ vā yavasambhavam  Hbhv 
raktakuṅkumasindūragairikādisamudbhavam 
haritālodbhavaṃ pītaṃ rajanīsambhavaṃ kvacit 
kṛṣṇaṃ dagdhair haridyavair haritpītair vimiśritam  Hbhv 
atha tatra dhvajapatākādyāropaṇam
tato dhvajapatākādi vinyasya harimandire 
vicitraṃ bhūṣayet tac ca bhagavadbhaktimān naraḥ  Hbhv 
atha dhvarāropaṇamāhātmyam
dhvajam āropayed yas tu prāsādopari bhaktitaḥ 
tasya brahmapade vāsaḥ krīḍate brahmaṇā saha  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye  
yaḥ kuryād viṣṇubhavane dhvajāropaṇam uttamam 
saṃpūjyate viriñcyādyaiḥ kim anyair bahubhāṣitaiḥ  Hbhv 
tatraivāgre ca ṇārP  
paṭo dhvajasya viprendra yāvac calati vāyunā 
tāvanti pāpajālāni naśyanty eva na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
mahāpātakayukto vā yukto vā sarvapātakaiḥ 
dhvajaṃ viṣṇugṛhe kṛtvā mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ  Hbhv 
āropitaṃ dhvajaṃ dṛṣṭvā ye'bhinandanti dhārmikāḥ 
te'pi sarve pramucyante mahāpātakakoṭibhiḥ  Hbhv 
iti
evaṃ bṛhannāradīye khyātaṃ yac cānyad adbhutam 
dhvajāropaṇamāhātmyaṃ tad draṣṭavyam ihākhilam  Hbhv 
atha patādāropaṇamāhātmyam
dvārakāmāhātmye
kṛṣṇālayaṃ yaḥ kurute patākābhiś ca śobhitam 
sadaiva tasya loke tu vāsas tasya na cānyataḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare
patākāṃ ca śubhāṃ dattvā tathā keśavaveśmani 
vāyulokam avāpnoti bahūn abdagaṇān dvijaḥ  Hbhv 
dodhūyate yathā sā tu vāyunā keśavālaye 
tathā tasyāpi sakalaṃ dehāt pāpaṃ vidhūyate  Hbhv 
atha vandanamālākadalīstambhāropaṇamāhātmyam
dvārakāmāhātmye tatraiva
bhūpa vandanamālāṃ tu kurute kṛṣṇaveśmani 
devakanyāvṛtair lakṣaiḥ sevyate suranāyakaiḥ  Hbhv 
yaḥ kuryāt kṛṣṇabhavanaṃ kadalīstambhaśobhitam 
nandate cāpsaroyuktaḥ svāgataṃ tasya devarāṭ  Hbhv 
atha pīṭhapātravastrādisaṃskāraḥ
tatra tāmrādipātraṃ yat prabhor vastrādikaṃ ca yat 
pīṭhādikaṃ ca tat sarvaṃ yathoktaṃ ca viśodhayet  Hbhv 
tatra pīṭhasya saṃskāraḥ
nārasiṃhe
pādapīṭhaṃ ca kṛṣṇasya bilvapatreṇa dharṣayet 
uṣṇāmbunā ca prakṣālya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  Hbhv 
atha taijasādipātrāṇāṃ saṃskāraḥ
mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe
uḍumbarāṇām amlena kṣāreṇa trapusīsayoḥ 
bhasmāmbubhiś ca kāmsyānāṃ śuddhiḥ plāvo dravasya ca  Hbhv 
vāyupurāṇe ca
maṇivajrapravālānāṃ muktāśaṅkhopalasya ca 
siddhārthakānāṃ kalkena tilakalkena vā punaḥ  Hbhv 
brāhme
suvarṇarūpyaśaṅkhāśmaśuktiratnamayāni ca 
kāṃsyāyastāmraraityāni trapusīsamayāni ca  Hbhv 
nirlepāni tu śudhyanti kevalenodakena tu 
śūdrocchiṣṭhāni śodhyāni tridhā kṣārāmlavāribhiḥ  Hbhv 
iti
atiduṣṭaṃ tu pātrādi viśodhyātithyakarmaṇe 
yuñjyāt tatparivartāya prabhukarmāntarāya vā  Hbhv 
etasya parivartena prabhave'nyat samarpayet 
ity ayaṃ sarvato loke sadācāro virājate  Hbhv 
manuḥ 
tāmrāyaḥkāṃsyaraityānāṃ trapuṇaḥ sīsakasya ca 
śaucaṃ yathārhaṃ kartavyaṃ kṣārāmlodakavāribhiḥ  Hbhv 
śaṅkhaḥ
amlodakena tāmrasya sīsasya trapuṇas tathā 
kṣāreṇa śuddhiṃ kāṃsyasya lauhasya ca vinirdiśet  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
sūtikocchiṣṭhabhāṇḍasya surādyupahatasya ca 
triḥsaptamārjanāc chuddhir na tu kāṃsyasya tāpanam  Hbhv 
anyatra ca
tāmram amlena śudhyena na cedāmiṣalepanam 
āmiṣeṇa tu yal liptaṃ punar dāhena śudhyanti  Hbhv 
brāhme
sūtikāśavaviṇmūtrarajaḥsvalahatāni ca 
prakṣeptavyāni tāny agnau yac ca yāvat sahed api  Hbhv 
ata eva devalaḥ
lohānāṃ dahanāc chuddhir bhasmanā gomayena vā 
dahanāt khananād vāpi śailānām ambhasāpi vā  Hbhv 
kāṣṭhānāṃ takṣaṇāc chuddhir mṛdgomayajalair api 
mṛṇmayānāṃ tu pātrāṇāṃ dahanāc chuddhir iṣyate  Hbhv 
manuḥ 
madyair mūtraiḥ purīṣair vā ṣṭhīvanaih pūyaśoṇitaiḥ 
saṃspṛṣṭaṃ naiva śuddhyeta punaḥpākena mṛnmayam  Hbhv 
vṛddhaśātātapaḥ
saṃhatānāṃ tu pātrāṇāṃ yad ekam upahanyate 
tasyaivaṃ śodhanaṃ proktaṃ sāmānyadravyaśuddhikṛt  Hbhv 
atha vastrādīnāṃ saṃskāraḥ
tatra śaṅkhaḥ
tāntavaṃ malinaṃ pūrvam adbhiḥ kṣāraiś ca śodhayet 
aṃśubhiḥ śoṣayitvā vā vāyunā vā samāharet  Hbhv 
ūrṇāpaṭṭāṃśukakṣaumadukūlāvikacarmaṇām 
alpāśauce bhavec chuddhiḥ śoṣaṇaprokṣaṇādibhiḥ  Hbhv 
tāny evāmedhyaliptāni nenijyād gaurasarṣapaiḥ 
dhānyakalkaiḥ parṇakalkaiḥ rasaiś ca phalabalkalaiḥ  Hbhv 
tulikādyupadhānāni puṣparatnāmbarāṇi ca 
śodhayitvātape kiṃcit karair unmārjayen muhuḥ  Hbhv 
paścāc ca vāriṇā prokṣya śucīty evam udāharet 
tāny apy atimalāktāni yathāvat pariśodhayet  Hbhv 
śātātapaḥ
kusumbhakuṅkumāraktās tathā lākṣārasena ca 
prakṣālanena śudhyanti caṇḍālasparśane tathā  Hbhv 
yamaḥ
kṛṣṇājinānāṃ vātaiś ca bālānāṃ mṛdbhir ambhasā 
gomūtreṇāsthidantānāṃ kṣaumāṇāṃ gaurasarṣapaiḥ  Hbhv 
śaṅkhaḥ
siddhārthakānāṃ kalkena dantaśṛṅgamayasya ca 
gobālaiḥ phalapātrāṇām asthnāṃ syāc chṛṅgavat tathā  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
niryāsānāṃ guḍānāṃ ca lavaṇānāṃ tathaiva ca 
kusumbhakusumānāṃ ca ūrṇākārpāsayos tathā 
prokṣaṇāt kathitā śuddhir ity āha bhagavān yamaḥ  Hbhv 
manuḥ  
adbhis tu prokṣaṇaṃ śaucaṃ bahūnāṃ dhānyavāsasām 
prakṣālanena tv alpānām adbhiḥ śaucaṃ vidhīyate  Hbhv 
cailavatcarmaṇāṃ śuddhir vaidalānāṃ tathāeva ca 
śākamūlaphalānāṃ ca dhānyavatśuddhir iṣyate  Hbhv 
prokṣaṇāt tṛṇakāṣṭhaṃ ca palālaṃ caiva śudhyati 
mārjanaupāñjanair veśma punaḥpākena mṛtmayam  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca manu 
yāvan nāpaity amedhyāktād gandho lepaś ca tatkṛtaḥ 
tāvan mṛdvāri cādeyaṃ sarvāsu dravyaśuddhiṣu  Hbhv 
bṛhaspatiḥ
vastravaidalacarmādeḥ śuddhiḥ prakṣālanaṃ smṛtam 
atiduṣṭasya tanmātraṃ tyajec chittvā tu śuddhaye  Hbhv 
viṣṇuḥ
mṛtparṇatṛṇakāṣṭhānāṃ śvāsthicāṇḍālavāyasaiḥ 
sparśane vihitaṃ śaucaṃ somasūryāṃśumārutaiḥ  Hbhv 
baudhāyanaḥ
āsanaṃ śayanaṃ yānaṃ nāvaḥ panthās tṛṇāni ca 
mārutārkeṇa śudhyanti pakveṣṭaracitāni ca  Hbhv 
atha dhānyādīnāṃ saṃskāraḥ
tatra baudhāyanaḥ
vrīhayaḥ prokṣaṇād adbhiḥ śākamūlaphalāni ca 
tanmātrasyāpahārād vā nistuṣīkaraṇena ca  Hbhv 
śaṅkhaḥ
śrapaṇaṃ ghṛtatailānāṃ plāvanaṃ gorasasya ca 
bhāṇḍāni plāvayed adbhiḥ śākamūlaphalāni ca  Hbhv 
brāhme
dravadravyāṇi bhūrīṇi pariplāvyāni cāmbhasā  Hbhv 
śasyāni vrīhayaś caiva śākamūlaphalāni ca 
tyaktvā tu dūṣitaṃ bhāgaṃ plāvyāny atha jalena tu  Hbhv 
bṛhaspatiḥ
tāpanaṃ ghṛtatailānāṃ plāvanaṃ gorasasya ca 
tanmātram uddhṛtaṃ śudhyet kaṭhinaṃ tu payodadhi  Hbhv 
avilīnaṃ tathā sarpir vilīnaṃ śrapaṇena tu 
ādhāradoṣe tu nayet pātrāt pātrāntaraṃ dravam  Hbhv 
ghṛtaṃ ca pāyasaṃ kṣīraṃ tathaikṣavaraso guḍaḥ 
śūdrabhāṇḍasthitaṃ takraṃ tathā madhu na duṣyati  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca manuḥ 
ucchiṣṭena tu saṃspṛṣṭo dravyahastaḥ kathaṃ cana 
anidhāyaiva tad dravyam ācāntaḥ śucitām iyāt  Hbhv 
iti
anye'pi śuddhividhayo dravyāṇāṃ smṛtiśāstrataḥ 
apekṣyā vaiṣṇavair jñeyās tattadvistāraṇair alam  Hbhv 
atha pūjārthatulasīpuṣpādyāharaṇam
praṇamyātha mahāviṣṇuṃ prārthyānujñāṃ tu vaiṣṇavaḥ 
samāharet śrītulasīṃ puṣpādi ca yathoditam  Hbhv 
yac ca hārītavacanam
snānaṃ kṛtvā tu ye kecit puṣpaṃ gṛhṇanti vai dvijāḥ 
devatās tan na gṛhṇanti bhasmībhavati kāṣṭhavat  Hbhv 
iti
tac ca madhyāhnasnānaviṣayam
yata uktaṃ pādme  vaiśākhamāhātmye
asnātvā tulasīṃ chittvā devārthaṃ pitṛkarmaṇi 
tat sarvaṃ niṣphalaṃ yāti pañcagavyena śudhyati  Hbhv 
atha gṛhasnānavidhiḥ
svagṛhe vācaran snānaṃ prakṣālyāṅghrī karau tathā 
ācamyāyamya ca prāṇān kṛtanyāso hariṃ smaret  Hbhv 
tato gaṅādikaṃ smṛtvā tulasīmiśritair jalaiḥ 
pūrṇe pātre samastāni tīrthāny āvāhayet kṛtī  Hbhv 
āvāhanamantraś cāyam
gaṅge ca yamune caiva godāvari sarasvati 
narmade sindhu kāveri jale'smin sannidhiṃ kuru  Hbhv 
iti 
athavā jāhnavīm eva sarvatīrthamayīṃ budhaḥ 
āvāhayed dvādaśabhir nāmabhir jalabhājane  Hbhv 
dvādaśanāmāni
nalinī nandinī sītā mālinī ca mahāpagā 
viṣṇupādārghyasambhūtā gaṅgā tripathagāminī 
bhāgīrathī bhogavatī jāhnavī tridaśeśvarī  Hbhv 
padmapurāṇe  ca vaiśākhamāhātmye
nandinīty eva te nāma vedeṣu nalinīti ca 
dakṣā pṛthvī ca vihagā viśvagāthā śivapriyā  Hbhv 
vidyādharī mahādevī tathā lokaprasādinī 
kṣemaṃkarī jāhnavī ca śāntā śāntipradāyinī  Hbhv 
athācamya guruṃ smṛtānujñāṃ prārthya ca pūrvavat 
kṛṣṇapādābjato gaṅgāṃ patantīṃ mūrdhni cintayet  Hbhv 
tathā coktaṃ śrīnāradapañcarātre
svasthitaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ mantramūrtiṃ prabhuṃ smaret 
anantādityasaṅkāśaṃ vāsudevaṃ caturbhujam  Hbhv 
śaṅkhacakragadāpadmadharaṃ pītāmbarāvṛtam 
śyāmalaṃ śāntavadanaṃ prasannaṃ varadekṣaṇam  Hbhv 
divyacandanaliptāṅgaṃ cārahāsamukhāmbujam 
anekaratnasaṃchannajvalanmakarakuṇḍalam  Hbhv 
vanamālāparivṛtaṃ nāradādibhir arcitam 
keyūravalayopetaṃ suvarṇamukuṭojjvalam 
sarvāṅgasundaraṃ devaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam  Hbhv 
tatpādapaṅkajād dhārāṃ nipatantīṃ svamūrdhani 
cintayed brahmarandhreṇa praviśantīṃ svakāṃ tanum 
tayā saṃkṣālayet sarvam antardehagataṃ malam  Hbhv 
tatkṣaṇād virajā mantrī jāyate sphaṭikopamaḥ 
idaṃ snānāntaraṃ māntrāt sahasram adhikaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv 
iti
sakṛn nārāyaṇety ādi vacanaṃ tatra kīrtayet 
snānakāle tu tannāma saṃsmarec ca mahāprabhum  Hbhv 
tathā ca kūrmapurāṇe
āpo nārāyaṇodbhūtās tā evāsyāyanaṃ yathaḥ 
tasmān nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ snānakāle smared budhaḥ  Hbhv 
iti
snāyād uṣṇodakenāpi śakto 'py āmalakais tathā 
tilais tailaiś ca saṃvarjya pratiṣiddhadināni tu  Hbhv 
athoṣṇodakasnānam
ṣaṭtriṃśanmate
āpaḥ svabhāvato medhyā viśeṣād agniyogataḥ 
tena santaḥ praśaṃsanti snānam uṣṇena vāriṇā  Hbhv 
yamaś ca
āpaḥ svayaṃ sadā pūtā vahnitaptā viśeṣataḥ 
tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu uṣṇāmbhaḥ pāvanaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv 
yac coktaṃ śaṅkhena
snātasya vahnitaptena tathaivātapavāriṇā 
śarīraśuddhir vijñeyā na tu snānaphalaṃ bhavet  Hbhv 
iti
tat tu kāmyanaimittikaviṣayam 
ata evoktaṃ gargeṇa
kuryān naimittikaṃ snānaṃ śītādbhiḥ kāmyam eva ca 
nityaṃ yādṛcchikaṃ caiva yathāruci samācaret  Hbhv 
atha tatra niṣiddhadināni
tatra yamaḥ
putrajanmani saṅkrāntau grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ 
aspṛśyasparśane caiva na snāyād uṣṇavāriṇā  Hbhv 
vṛddhamanuḥ
paurṇamāsyāṃ tathā darśe yaḥ snāyād uṣṇavāriṇā 
sa gohatyākṛtaṃ pāpaṃ prāpnotīha na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
athāmalakasnānam
tatra mārkaṇḍeyaḥ
tuṣyaty āmalakair viṣṇur ekādaśyāṃ viśeṣataḥ 
śrīkāmaḥ sarvadā snānaṃ kurvītāmalakair naraḥ  Hbhv 
saptamyāṃ na spṛśet tailaṃ nīlīvastraṃ na dhārayet 
na cāpy āmalakaṃ snāyān na kuryāt kalahaṃ naraḥ  Hbhv 
bhṛguḥ
amāṃ ṣaṣṭhīṃ saptamīṃ ca navamīṃ ca trayodaśīm 
saṅkrāntau ravivāre ca snānamālakais tyajet  Hbhv 
yājñavalkyaḥ
dhātrīphalair amāvasyāsaptamīnavamīṣu ca 
yaḥ snāyāt tasya hīyante tejaś cāyurdhanaṃ sutāḥ  Hbhv 
atha tilasnānam
tatra bṛhaspatiḥ
sarvakālaṃ tilaiḥ snānaṃ punar vyāso 'bravīn muniḥ  Hbhv 
ṣaṭtriṃśanmate
tathā saptamyamāvasyāsaṅkrāntigrahaṇeṣu ca 
dhanaputrakalatrārthī tilaspṛṣṭaṃ na saṃspṛśet  Hbhv 
atha tailasnānam
tatraiva
ṣaṣṭhyāṃ tailam anāyuṣyaṃ caturthīṣv api ca parvasu  Hbhv 
yogīyājñavalkyaḥ
daśamyāṃ tailam apṛṣṭvā yaḥ snāyād avicakṣaṇaḥ 
catvāri tasya naśyanti āyuḥ prajñā yaśodhanam  Hbhv 
mohāt pratipadaṃ ṣaṣṭhīṃ kuhūṃ riktātithiṃ tathā 
tailenābhyañjayed yas tu caturbhiḥ parihīyate  Hbhv 
pañcadaśyāṃ caturdaśyāṃ saptamyāṃ ravisaṅkrame 
dvādaśyāṃ saptamīṃ ṣaṣṭhīṃ tailasparśaṃ vivarjayet  Hbhv 
anyac ca
saptamyāṃ na spṛśet tailaṃ navamyāṃ pratipady api 
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃm amāvasyāṃ viśeṣataḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
snāne vā yadi vāsnāne pakkatailaṃ na duṣyati  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca atrismṛtau
tailābhyukto ghṛtābhyakto viṇmūtre kurute dvijaḥ 
ahorātroṣito bhūtvā pañcagavyena śudhyati  Hbhv 
athāṅgam alam uttārya snātvā vidhivad ācaret 
nāsālagnena culukodakenaivāghamarṣaṇam  Hbhv 
tato gurvādipādodaiḥ prāgvat kṛtvābhiṣecanam 
kāryo 'bhiṣekaḥ śaṅkhena tulasīmiśritair jalaiḥ  Hbhv 
atha tulasījalābhiṣekamāhatmyam
gāruḍe
mārjayaty abhiṣeke tu tulasyā vaiṣṇavo naraḥ 
sarvatīrthamayaṃ dehaṃ tatkṣaṇāt dvija jāyate  Hbhv 
tulasīdalajasnāne ekādaśyāṃ viśeṣataḥ 
mucyate sarvapāpebhyo yadyapi brahmahā bhavet  Hbhv 
tanmūlamṛttikābhyaṅgaṃ kṛtvā snāti dine dine 
daśāśvamedhāvabhṛtaṃ labhate snānajaṃ phalam  Hbhv 
tulasīdalasaṃmiśraṃ toyaṃ gaṅgāsamaṃ viduḥ 
yo vahec chirasā nityaṃ dhṛtā bhavati jāhnavī  Hbhv 
pādodakaṃ tāmrapātre kṛtvā satulasīdalam 
śaṅkhaṃ kṛtvābhiṣiñceta mūlenaiva svamūrdhani  Hbhv 
tanmāhātmye coktaṃ pādme kārttikamāhātmye
dvārakācakrasaṃyuktaśālagrāmaśilājalam 
śaṅkhe kṛtvā tu nikṣiptaṃ snānārthaṃ tāmrabhājane 
tulasīdalasaṃyuktaṃ brahmahatyāvināśanam  Hbhv 
iti
snānaśāṭītareṇaiva vāsasāmbhāṃsi gātrataḥ 
saṃmārjya vāsasī dadhyāt paridhānottarīyake  Hbhv 
atha vastradhāraṇavidhiḥ
tatrātriḥ
adhautaṃ kārudhautaṃ vā paredyudhautam eva vā 
kāṣāyaṃ malinaṃ vastraṃ kaupīnaṃ ca parityajet  Hbhv 
na cārdram eva vasanaṃ paridadhyāt kadācana  Hbhv 
nagno malinavastraḥ syāt nagnaś cārdhapaṭas tathā 
nagno dviguṇavastraḥ syān nagno raktapaṭas tathā  Hbhv 
nagnaś ca syūtavastraḥ syān nagnaḥ snigdhapaṭas tathā 
dvikaccho 'nuttarīyaś ca nagnaś cāvastra eva ca  Hbhv 
śrautaṃ smārtaṃ tathā karma na nagnaś cintayed api 
mohāt kurvann adho gacchet tad bhaved āsuraṃ smṛtam  Hbhv 
japahomopavāseṣu dhautavastradharo bhavet 
alaṅkṛtaḥ śucir maunī śrāddhādau ca jitendriyaḥ  Hbhv 
gobhilaḥ
ekavastro na bhuñjīta na kuryād devanārcanam  Hbhv 
trailokyasammohanapañcarātre
śuklavāso bhaven nityaṃ raktaṃ caiva vivarjayet  Hbhv 
aṅgirāḥ
śaucaṃ sahasraromāṇāṃ vāyvagnyarkenduraśmibhiḥ 
retaḥspṛṣṭaṃ śavaspṛṣṭam āvikaṃ naiva duṣyati  Hbhv 
anyatra ca
chinnaṃ vā sandhitaṃ dagdhm āvikaṃ na praduṣyati 
āvikena tu vastreṇa mānavaḥ śrāddham ācaret 
gayāśrāddhasamaṃ proktaṃ pitṛbhyo dattam akṣayam  Hbhv 
na kuryāt sandhitaṃ vastraṃ devakarmaṇi bhūmipa 
na dagdhaṃ na ca vai chinnaṃ pārakyaṃ na tu dhārayet  Hbhv 
kākaviṣṭhāsamaṃ hy uktam avidhautaṃ ca yad bhavet 
rajakād āhṛtaṃ yac ca na tad vastraṃ bhavec chuci  Hbhv 
kīṭaspṛṣṭaṃ tu yad vastraṃ purīṣaṃ yena kāritam 
mūtraṃ vā maithunaṃ vāpi tad vastraṃ parivarjayet  Hbhv 
āvikaṃ tu sadā vastraṃ pavitraṃ rājasattama 
pitṛdevamanuṣyāṇāṃ kriyāyāṃ ca praśasyate  Hbhv 
dhautādhautaṃ tathā dagdhaṃ sandhitaṃ rajakāhṛtam 
śukramūtraraktaliptaṃ tathāpi paramaṃ śuci  Hbhv 
agnir āvikavastraṃ ca brahmaṇāś ca tathā kuśāḥ 
caturṇāṃ na kṛto doṣo brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā  Hbhv 
kiṃ cānyatra
dhārayed vāsasī śuddhe paridhānottarīyake 
acchinnasudaśe śukle ācāmet pīṭhasaṃsthitaḥ  Hbhv 
atha pīṭham
bahvṛcapariśiṣṭe
yatīnām āsanaṃ śuklaṃ kūrmākāraṃ tu kārayet 
anyeṣāṃ tu catuṣpādaṃ caturasraṃ tu kārayet  Hbhv 
gośakṛnmayaṃ bhinnaṃ tathā palāśapaippalam 
lohabaddhaṃ sadaivārkaṃ varjayed āsanaṃ budhaḥ  Hbhv 
athāsanavidhiḥ
tatraiva
dānam ācamanaṃ homaṃ bhojanaṃ devatārcanam 
prauḍhapādo na kurvīta svādhyāyaṃ caiva tarpaṇam  Hbhv 
āsanārūḍhapādas tu jānunor vātha jaṅghayoḥ 
kṛtāvaskthiko yas tu prauḍhapādaḥ sa ucyate  Hbhv 
iti
tato bhūmigatāṅghriḥ san niviśyācamya darbhabhṛt 
ūrdhvapuṇḍrādikaṃ kuryāt śrīgopīcandanādinā  Hbhv 
tatrādāv anulepena bhagavaccaraṇābjayoḥ 
nirmālyena prasādena sarvāṇy aṅgāni mārjayet  Hbhv 
tad uktaṃ brāhme śrībhagavatā
śālagrāmaśilālagnaṃ candanaṃ dhārayet sadā 
sarvāṅgeṣu mahāśuddhisiddhaye kamalāsana  Hbhv 
iti
tato dvādaśabhiḥ kuryān nāmabhiḥ keśavādibhiḥ 
dvādaśāṅgeṣu vidhivad ūrdhvapuṇḍrāṇi vaiṣṇavaḥ  Hbhv 
atha dvādaśatilakavidhiḥ
padmapurāṇe uttarakhaṇḍe 
lalāṭe keśavaṃ dhyāyen nārāyaṇam athodare 
vakṣaḥsthale mādhavaṃ tu govindaṃ kaṇṭhakūpake  Hbhv 
viṣṇuṃ ca dakṣiṇe kukṣau bāhau ca madhusūdanam 
trivikramaṃ kandhare tu vāmanaṃ vāmapārśvake  Hbhv 
śrīdharaṃ vāmabāhau tu hṛṣīkeśaṃ tu kandhare 
pṛṣṭhe tu padmanābhaṃ ca kaṭyāṃ dāmodaraṃ nyaset  Hbhv 
tatprakṣālanatoyaṃ tu vāsudeveti mūrdhani  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca 
ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ lalāṭe tu sarveṣāṃ prathamaṃ smṛtam 
lalāṭādikrameṇaiva dhāraṇaṃ tu vidhīyate  Hbhv 
iti
evaṃ nyāsaṃ samācarya sampradāyānusārataḥ 
nyaset kirīṭamantraṃ ca mūrdhni sarvārthasiddhaye  Hbhv 
atha kirīṭamantraḥ
oṃ śrīkirīṭakeyūrahāramakarakuṇḍalacakraśaṅkhagadāpadmahastapītāmbaradhara
śrīvatsāṅkitavakṣaḥsthala śrībhūmisahitasvātmajyotir dīptikarāya sahasrādityatejase
namo namaḥ  Hbhv 
iti
athordhvapuṇḍranityatā
pādme śrībhagavaduktau
matpriyārthaṃ śubhārthaṃ vā rakṣārthe caturānana 
matpūjāhomakāle ca sāyaṃ prātaḥ samāhitaḥ 
madbhakto dhārayen nityam ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ bhayāpaham  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrīnāradoktau
yajño dānaṃ tapo homaḥ svādhyāyaḥ pitṛtarpaṇam 
vyarthaṃ bhavati tat sarvam ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ vinā kṛtam  Hbhv 
tatraivottarakhaṇḍe
ūrdhvapuṇḍrair vihīnas tu kiṃcit karma karoti yaḥ 
iṣṭāpūrtādikaṃ sarvaṃ niṣphalaṃ syān na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
ūrdhvapuṇḍrair vihīnas tu sandhyākarmādikaṃ caret 
tat sarvaṃ rākṣasaṃ nityaṃ narakaṃ cādhigacchati  Hbhv 
anyac ca
ūrdhvapuṇḍre tripuṇḍraṃ yaḥ kurute narādhamaḥ 
bhaṅktvā viṣṇugṛhaṃ puṇḍraṃ sa yāti narakaṃ dhruvam  Hbhv 
ata eva pādme śrīnāradoktau
yac charīraṃ manuṣyāṇām ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ vinā kṛtam 
draṣṭavyaṃ naiva tat tāvat śmaśānasadṛśaṃ bhavet  Hbhv 
padmapurāṇe
ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ mṛdā saumyaṃ lalāṭe yasya dṛśyate 
sa cāṇḍālo 'pi śuddhātmā pūjya eva na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
skānde
tiryakpuṇḍraṃ na kurvīta samprāpte maraṇe'pi ca 
naivānyan nāma ca brūyāt pumān nārārāyaṇād ṛte  Hbhv 
dhārayed viṣṇunirmālyaṃ dhūpaśeṣaṃ vilepanam 
vaiṣṇavaṃ kārayet puṇḍraṃ gopīcandanasambhavam  Hbhv 
tatraiva kārttikaprasaṅge
yasyordhvapuṇḍraṃ dṛśyeta lalāṭe no narasya hi 
taddarśanaṃ na kartavyaṃ dṛṣṭvā sūryaṃ nirīkṣayet  Hbhv 
anyatrāpi
vaiṣṇavānāṃ brāhmaṇānām ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ vidhīyate 
anyeṣāṃ tu tripuṇḍraṃ syād iti brahmavido viduḥ  Hbhv 
tripuṇḍraṃ yasya viprasya ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ na dṛśyate 
taṃ spṛṣṭvāpy athavā dṛṣṭvā sacelaṃ snānam ācaret  Hbhv 
ūrdhvapuṇḍre na kurvīta vaiṣṇavānāṃ tripuṇḍrakam 
kṛtatripuṇḍramartyasya kriyā na prītaye hareḥ  Hbhv 
ataevottarakhaṇḍe
aśvatthapatrasaṅkāśo veṇupatrākṛtis tathā 
padmakuṭmalasaṅkāśo mohanaṃ tritayaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv 
athordhvapuṇḍramāhātmyam
skānde kārttikaprasaṅge
ūrdhvapuṇḍro mṛdā śubhro lalāṭe yasya dṛśyate 
caṇḍālo 'pi viśuddhātmā yāti braham sanātanam  Hbhv 
ūrdhvapuṇḍre sthitā lakṣmīr ūrdhvapuṇḍre sthitaṃ yaśaḥ 
ūrdhvapuṇḍre sthitā muktir ūrdhvapuṇḍre sthito hariḥ  Hbhv 
padmapurāṇe
ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ mudā saumyaṃ lalāṭe yasya dṛśyate 
sa cāṇḍālo 'pi śuddhātmā pūjya eva na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
tatraivottarakhaṇḍe śivomāsaṃvāde  
ūrdhvapuṇḍrasya madhye tu viśāle sumanohare 
lakṣmyā sārdhaṃ samāsīno devadevo janārdanaḥ  Hbhv 
tasmād yasya śarīre tu ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ dhṛto bhavet 
tasya dehaṃ bhagavato vimalaṃ mandiraṃ śubham  Hbhv 
ūrdhvapuṇḍradharo vipraḥ sarvalokeṣu pūjitaḥ 
vimānavaram āruhya yāti viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam  Hbhv 
ūrdhvapuṇḍradharaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate 
namaskṛtvāthavā bhaktyā sarvadānaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
ūrdhvapuṇḍradharaṃ vipraṃ yaḥ śrāddhe bhojayiṣyati 
ākalpakoṭipitaras tasya tṛptā na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
ūrdhvapuṇḍradharo yas tu kuryāc chrāddhaṃ śubhānane 
kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi gayāśrāddhaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
yajñadānatapaścaryājapahomādikaṃ ca yat 
ūrdhvapuṇḍradharaḥ kuryāt tasya puṇyam anantakam  Hbhv 
śrībrahmāṇḍapurāṇe
aśucir vāpya nācāro manasā pāpam ācaran 
śucir eva bhaven nityam ūrdhvapuṇḍrāṅkito naraḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrībhagavadvacanam
ūrdhvapūṇḍradharo martyo mriyate yatra kutracit 
śvapāko 'pi vimānastho mama loke mahīyate  Hbhv 
ūrdhvapūṇḍradharo martyo gṛhe yasyānnam aśnute 
tadā viṃśatkulaṃ tasya narakād uddharāmy ahaṃ  Hbhv 
athohvapūṇḍrairmāṇavidhiḥ
śrībrahmāṇḍapurāṇe
vīkṣyādarśe jale vāpi yo vidadhyāt prayatnataḥ 
ūrdhvapūṇḍraṃ mahābhāga sa yāti paramāṃ gatim  Hbhv 
daśāṅgulapramāṇaṃ tu uttamottamam ucyate 
navāṅgulaṃ madhyamaṃ syād aṣṭāṅgulam ataḥ param  Hbhv 
etair aṅgulibhedais tu kārayen na nakhaiḥ spṛśet  Hbhv 
padmapurāṇe uttarakhaṇḍe tatraiva   
ekāntino mahābhāgāḥ sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ 
sāntarālaṃ prakurvīran puṇḍraṃ haripadākṛtim  Hbhv 
śyāmaṃ śāntikaraṃ proktaṃ raktaṃ vaśyakaraṃ tathā 
śrīkaraṃ pītam ity āhuḥ śvetaṃ mokṣakaraṃ śubham  Hbhv 
vartulaṃ tiryag achidraṃ hrasvaṃ dīrghaṃ tataṃ tanum 
vakraṃ virūpaṃ baddhāgraṃ chinnamūlaṃ padacyutam  Hbhv 
aśubhaṃ rūkṣam āsaktaṃ tathā nāṅgulikalpitam 
vigandham avasahyaṃ ca puṇḍram āhur anarthakam  Hbhv 
ārabhya nāsikāmūlaṃ lalāṭāntaṃ likhen mṛdā 
nāsikāyās trayo bhāgā nāsāmūlaṃ pracakṣyate  Hbhv 
samārabhya bhruvor madhyam antarālaṃ prakalpayet  Hbhv 
tatraiva  
nirantarālaṃ yaḥ kuryād ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ dvijādhamaḥ 
sa hi tatra sthitaṃ viṣṇuṃ śriyaṃ caiva vyapohati  Hbhv 
acchidram ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ tu ye kurvanti dvijādhamāḥ 
teṣāṃ lalāṭe satataṃ śunaḥ pādo na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
tasmāc chidrānvitaṃ puṇḍraṃ daṇḍākāraṃ suśobhanam 
viprāṇāṃ satataṃ kāryaṃ strīṇāṃ ca śubhadarśane  Hbhv 
harimandiralakṣaṇam
nāsādikeśaprayantam ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ suśobhanam 
madhye chidrasamāyuktaṃ tad vidyād harimandiram  Hbhv 
vāmapārśve sthito brahmā dakṣiṇe ca sadāśivaḥ 
madhye viṣṇuṃ vijānīyāt tasmān madhyaṃ na lepayet  Hbhv 
vāyupurāṇe sevāparādhe
adhṛtvā cordhvapuṇḍraṃ ca hareḥ pūjāṃ karoti yaḥ 
tiryakpuṇḍradharo yas tu yajed devaṃ janārdanam  Hbhv 
accidreṇordhvapuṇḍreṇa bhasmanā tiryagaṅginā 
adhṛtvā śaṅkhacakre ca cety ādinā doṣa uktaḥ  Hbhv 
śrutiś ca yajurvedasya hiraṇyakeśauryaśakhāyām
hareḥ padākrāntim ātmani dhārayati yaḥ 
sa parasya priyo bhavati sa puṇyavān 
madhye chidram ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ
yo dhārayati sa muktibhāg bhavati  Hbhv 
iti
tilakaracanāṅguliniyamaḥ
smṛtiḥ
anāmikā kāmadoktā madhyam āyuskarī bhavet 
aṅguṣṭhaḥ puṣṭidaḥ proktas tarjanī mokṣadāyinī  Hbhv 
athordhvapuṇḍramṛttikāḥ
padmapurāṇe  tatraiva
parvatāgre nadītīre bilvamūle jalāśaye 
sindhutīre ca valmīke harikṣetre viśeṣataḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇoḥ snānodakaṃ yatra pravāhayati nityaśaḥ 
puṇḍrāṇāṃ dhāraṇārthāya gṛhṇīyāt tatra mṛttikām  Hbhv 
śrīraṅge veṅkaṭādrau ca śrīkūrme dvārake śubhe 
prayāge nārasiṃhādrau vārāhe tulasīvane  Hbhv 
gṛhītvā mṛttikāṃ bhaktyā viṣṇupādajalaiḥ saha 
dhṛtvā puṇḍrāṇi cāṅgeṣu viṣṇusāyujyam āpnuyāt  Hbhv 
tatraiva
yat tu divyaṃ harikṣetre tasyaiva mṛdam āharet  Hbhv 
uktaṃ ca pādme śrīnāradena
brahmaghno vātha goghno vā haitukaḥ sarvapāpakṛt 
gopīcandanasamparkāt pūto bhavati tatkṣaṇāt  Hbhv 
gopīcandanakhaṇḍaṃ tu yo dadātii hi vaiṣṇave 
kulam ekottaraṃ tena sambhavet tāritaṃ śatam  Hbhv 
skandapurāṇe
śaṅkhacakrāṅkitatanuḥ śirasā mañjarīdharaḥ 
gopīcandanaliptāṅgo dṛṣṭaś cet tad aghaṃ kṛtaḥ  Hbhv 
gopīmṛttulasī śaṅkhaḥ śālagrāmaḥ sacakrakaḥ 
gṛhe'pi yasya pañcaite tasya pāpabhayaṃ kutaḥ  Hbhv 
kāśīkhaṇḍe ca śrīyamena
śrīkhaṇḍe kva sa āmodaḥ svarovarṇaḥ kva tādṛśaḥ 
tat pāvitryaṃ kva vai tīrthe śrīgopīcandane yathā  Hbhv 
atha gopīcandanordhvapuṇḍramāhātmyam
uktaṃ ca garuḍapurāṇe nāradena
yo mṛttikāṃ dvāravatīsamudbhavāṃ
kare samādāya lalāṭapaṭṭake 
karoti nityaṃ tv atha cordhvapuṇḍraṃ
kriyāphalaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ sadā bhavet  Hbhv 
kriyāvihīnaṃ yadi mantrahīnaṃ
śraddhāvihīnaṃ yadi kālavarjitam 
kṛtvā lalāṭe yadi gopīcandanaṃ
prāpnoti tat karmaphalaṃ sadā kṣayam  Hbhv 
gopīcandanasambhavaṃ suruciraṃ puṇḍraṃ lalāṭe dvijo
nityaṃ dhārayate yadi dvijapate rātrau divā sarvadā 
yat puṇyaṃ kurujāṅgale ravigrahe mādhyāṃ prayāge tathā
tat prāpnoti khagendra viṣṇusadane santiṣṭhate devavat  Hbhv 
yasmin gṛhe tiṣṭhati gopīcandanaṃ
bhaktyā lalāṭe manujo bibharti 
tasmin gṛhe tiṣṭhati sarvadā hariḥ
śraddhānvitaḥ kaṃsahā vihaṅgama  Hbhv 
yo dhārayet kṛṣṇapurīsamudbhavāṃ
sadā pavitrāṃ kalikilbiṣāpahām 
nityaṃ lalāṭe harimantrasaṃyutāṃ
yamaṃ na paśyed yadi pāpasaṃvṛtaḥ  Hbhv 
yasyāntakāle khaga gopīcandanaṃ
bāhvor lalāṭE hṛdi mastake ca 
prayāti lokaṃ kamalālayaṃ prabhor
gobālaghātī yadi brahmahā bhavet  Hbhv 
grahā na pīḍanti na rakṣasāṃ gaṇāḥ
yakṣāḥ piśācoragabhūtadānavāḥ 
lalāṭapaṭṭe khaga gopīcandanaṃ
santiṣṭhate yasya hareḥ prasādataḥ  Hbhv 
padmapurāṇe śrīgotamena
ambarīṣa mahāghasya kṣayārthe kuru vīkṣaṇam 
lalāṭe yaiḥ kṛtaṃ nityaṃ gopīcandanapuṇḍrakam  Hbhv 
kāśīkhaṇḍe ca śrīyamena
dūtāḥ śṛṇuta yadbhālaṃ gopīcandanalāñchitam 
jvaladindhanavat so 'pi tyājyo dūre prayatnataḥ  Hbhv 
iti
atha tasyopari śrīmattulasīmūlamṛtsnayā 
tatraiva vaiṣṇavaiḥ kāryam ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ manoharam  Hbhv 
atha śrītulasīmūlamṛttikāpuṇḍramāhātmyam
tanmṛdaṃ gṛhya yaiḥ puṇḍraṃ lalāṭe dhāritaṃ naraiḥ 
pramāṇakaṃ kṛtaṃ tais tu mokṣāya gamanaṃ prati  Hbhv 
tatraiva ca kārttikamāhātmye brahmanāradasaṃvāde
tulasīmṛttikāpuṇḍraṃ lalāṭe yasya dṛśyate 
dehaṃ na spṛśati pāpaṃ kriyamāṇas tu nārada  Hbhv 
garuḍapurāṇe
tulasīmṛttikāpuṇḍraṃ yaḥ karoti dine dine 
tasyāvalokanāt pāpaṃ yāti varṣakṛtaṃ nṛṇām  Hbhv 
iti
tasyopariṣṭhād bhagavannirmālyam anulepanam 
tathaiva dhāryam evaṃ hi trividhaṃ tilakaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv 
tato nārāyaṇīṃ mudrāṃ dhārayet prītaye hareḥ 
matsyakūrmādicihnāni cakrādīny āyudhāni ca  Hbhv 
atha mudrādhāraṇanityatā
smṛtau
aṅkitaḥ śaṅkhacakrābhyām ubhayor bāhumūlayoḥ 
samarcayed dhariṃ nityaṃ nānyathā pūjanaṃ bhavet  Hbhv 
ādityapurāṇe
śaṅkhacakrordhvapuṇḍrādirahitaṃ brāhmaṇādhamam 
gardabhaṃ tu samāropya rājā rāṣṭrāt pravāsayet  Hbhv 
gāruḍe śrībhagavaduktau
sarvakarmādhikāraś ca śucīnām eva coditaḥ 
śucitvaṃ ca vijānīyān madīyāyudhadhāraṇāt  Hbhv 
pādme cottarakhaṇḍe
śaṅkhacakrādibhiś cihnair vipraḥ priyatamair hareḥ 
rahitaḥ sarvadharmebhyaḥ pracyuto narakaṃ vrajet  Hbhv 
śrutau ca yajuḥkaṭhaśākhāyām
dhṛtordhvapuṇḍraḥ kutacakradhārī
viṣṇuṃ paraṃ dhyāyati yo mahātmā 
svareṇa mantreṇa sadā hṛdi sthitaṃ
parātparaṃ yan mahato mahāntam  Hbhv 
atharvaṇi ca
ebhir vayam urukramasya cihnair
aṅkitā loke subhagā bhavema 
tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ
ye gacchanti lāṅchitāḥ  Hbhv 
 ity ādi 
ataeva brahmapurāṇe
kṛṣṇāyudhāṅkitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sammānaṃ na karoti yaḥ 
dvādaśābdārjitaṃ puṇyaṃ cāphalayopagacchati  Hbhv 
atha mudrādhāraṇamāhātmyam
skānde śrīsanatkumāramārkaṇḍeyasaṃvāde
yo viṣṇubhakto viprendra śaṅkhacakrādicihnitaḥ 
sa yāti viṣṇulokaṃ vai dāhapralayavarjitam  Hbhv 
tatra vāntyatra ca
nārāyaṇāyudhair nityaṃ cihnitaṃ yasya vigraham 
pāpakoṭiyuktasya tasya kiṃ kurute yamaḥ  Hbhv 
śaṅkhoddhāre tu yat proktaṃ vasatāṃ varṣakoṭibhiḥ 
tat phalaṃ likhite śaṅkhe pratyahaṃ dakṣiṇe bhuje  Hbhv 
yat phalaṃ puṣkare nityaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣadarśane 
śaṅkhopari kṛte padme tat phalaṃ samavāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
vāme bhuje gadā yasya likhitā dṛśyate kalau 
gadādharo gayāpuṇyaṃ pratyahaṃ tasya yacchati  Hbhv 
yac cānandapure proktaṃ cakrasvāmīsamīpataḥ 
gadādhollikhite cakre tat phalaṃ kṛṣṇadarśane  Hbhv 
śrībhagavaduktau
yaḥ punaḥ kalikāle tu matpurīsambhavāṃ mṛdam 
matsyakūrmādikāṃ cihnaṃ gṛhītvā kurute naraḥ  Hbhv 
dehe tasya praviṣṭo 'haṃ jānantu tridaśottamāḥ 
tasya me nāntaraṃ kiṃcit kartavyaṃ śreya icchatā  Hbhv 
mamāvatāracihnāni dṛśyante yasya vigrahe 
martyair martyo na vijñeyaḥ sa nūnaṃ māmakī tanūḥ  Hbhv 
pāpaṃ sukṛtarūpaṃ tu jāyate tasya dehinaḥ 
mamāyudhāni tasyāṅge likhitāni kalau yuge  Hbhv 
ubhābhyām api cihnābhyāṃ yo 'ṅkito matsyamudrayā 
kūrmayāpi svakaṃ tejo nikṣiptaṃ tasya vigrahe  Hbhv 
śaṅkhaṃ ca padmaṃ ca gadāṃ rathāṅgaṃ
matsyaṃ ca kūrmaṃ racitaṃ svadehe 
karoti nityaṃ sukṛtasya vṛddhiṃ
pāpakṣayaṃ janmaśatārjitasya  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde
kṛṣṇaśastrāṅkakavacaṃ durbhedyaṃ devadānavaiḥ 
adṛśyaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ śatrūṇāṃ rakṣasām api  Hbhv 
lakṣmīḥ sarasvatī durgā sāvitrī harivallabhā 
nityaṃ tasya vased dehe yasya śaṅkhāṅkitā tanuḥ  Hbhv 
gaṅgā gayā kurukṣetraṃ prayāgaṃ puṣkarādi ca 
nityaṃ tasya sadā tiṣṭhed yasya padāṅkitaṃ vapuḥ  Hbhv 
yasya kaumodakīcihnaṃ bhuje vāme kalipriya 
pratyahaṃ tatra draṣṭavyo gaṅgāsāgarasaṅgamaḥ  Hbhv 
savye kare gadādhastad rathāṅgaṃ tiṣṭhate yadi 
kṛṣṇena sahitaṃ tatra trailokyaṃ sacarācaram  Hbhv 
trayo 'gnayas trayo devā viṣṇos trīṇi padāni ca 
nivasanti sadā yasya yasya dehe sudarśanam  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
kṛṣṇāyudhāṅkitā mudrā yasya nārāyaṇī kare 
ūrdhvalokādhikārī ca sa jñeyas tridaśāṃ patiḥ  Hbhv 
kṛṣṇamudrāprayuktas tu daivaṃ pitryaṃ karoti yaḥ 
nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāmyaṃ pratyahaṃ cākṣayaṃ bhavet  Hbhv 
pīḍayanti na tatraiva grahā ṛkṣāṇi rāśayaḥ 
aṣṭākṣarāṅkitā mudrā yasya dhātumayī kare  Hbhv 
vārāhe śrīsanatkumāroktau
kṛṣṇāyudhāṅkitaṃ dehaṃ gopīcandanamṛtsnayā 
prayāgādiṣu tīrtheṣu sa gatvā kiṃ kariṣyati  Hbhv 
yadā yasya prapaśyeta dehaṃ śaṅkhādicihnitam 
tadā tasya jagatsvāmī tuṣṭo harati pātakam  Hbhv 
bhavate yasya dehe tu ahorātraṃ dine dine 
śaṅkhacakragadāpadmaṃ likhitaṃ so 'cyutaḥ svayam  Hbhv 
nārāyaṇāyudhair yuktaṃ kṛtvātmānaṃ kalau yuge 
kurute puṇyakarmāṇi merutulyāni tāni vai  Hbhv 
śaṅkhādināṅkito bhaktyā śrāddhaṃ yaḥ kurute dvija 
vidhihīnaṃ tu sampūrṇaṃ pitṝṇāṃ tu gayāsamam  Hbhv 
yathāgnir dahate kāṣṭhaṃ vāyunā prerito bhṛśam 
tathā dahyanti pāpāni dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇāyudhāni vai  Hbhv 
brāhmye śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde
viṣṇunāmāṅkitāṃ mudrām aṣṭākṣarasamanvitām 
śaṅkhādikāyudhādikair yuktāṃ svarṇarūpyamayīm api  Hbhv 
dhatte bhāgavato yas tu kalikāle viśeṣataḥ 
prahlādasya samo kṣeyo nānyathā kalavallabha  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
śaṅkhāṅkitatanur vipro bhuṅkte yasya ca veśmani 
tadannaṃ svayam aśnāti pitṛbhiḥ saha keśavaḥ  Hbhv 
kṛṣṇāyudhāṅkito yas tu śmaśāne mriyate yadi 
prayāge yā gatiḥ proktā sā gatis tasya nārada  Hbhv 
kṛṣṇāyudhaiḥ kalau nityaṃ maṇḍitaṃ yasya vigraham 
tatrāśrayaṃ prakurvanti vivadhā vāsavādayaḥ  Hbhv 
yaḥ karoti hareḥ pūjāṃ kṛṣṇaśastrāṅkito naraḥ 
aparādhasahasrāṇi nityaṃ harati keśavaḥ  Hbhv 
kṛtvā kāṣṭhamayaṃ bimbaṃ kṛṣṇaśastrais tu cihnitam 
yo hy aṅkayati cātmānaṃ tatsamo nāsti vaiṣṇavaḥ  Hbhv 
pāṣaṇḍapatitavrātyair nāstikālāpapātakaiḥ 
na lipyate kalikṛtaiḥ kṛṣṇaśastrāṅkito naraḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
aṣṭākṣarāṅkitā mudrā yasya dhātumayī bhavet 
śaṅkhapadmādibhir yuktā pūjyate'sau surāsuraiḥ  Hbhv 
dhṛtā nārāyaṇī mudrā prahlādena purā kṛte 
vibhīṣaṇena balinā dhruveṇa ca śukena ca  Hbhv 
māndhātṛṇāmbarīṣeṇa mārkaṇḍapramukhair dvijaiḥ 
śaṅkhādicihnitaiḥ śastrair dehe kṛtvā kalipriya 
ārādhya keśavāt prāptaṃ samīhitaphalaṃ mahat  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
gopīcandanamṛtsnāyā likhitaṃ yasya vigrahe 
śaṅkhapadmādicakraṃ vā tasya dehe vased dhariḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrīsanatkumāroktau
yasya nārāyaṇī mudrā dehaṃ śaṅkhādicihnitam 
dhātrīphalakṛtā mālā tulasīkāṣṭhasambhavā  Hbhv 
dvādaśākṣaramantrais tu niyuktāni kalevare 
āyudhāni ca viprasya matsamaḥ sa ca vaiṣṇavaḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
yasya nārāyaṇī mudrā dehe śaṅkhādi cihnitā 
sarvāṅgaṃ cihnitaṃ yasya sastrair nārāyaṇodbhavaiḥ 
praveśo nāsti pāpasya kavacaṃ tasya vaiṣṇavam  Hbhv 
anyatra ca
ebhir bhāgavataiś cihnaiḥ kalikāle dvijātayaḥ 
bhavanti martyaloke te śāpānugrahakārakāḥ  Hbhv 
atha mudrādhāraṇavidhiḥ
gautamīye
cakraṃ ca dakṣiṇe bāhau śaṅkhaṃ vāme'pi dakṣiṇe 
gadāṃ vāme gadādhastāt punaś cakraṃ ca dhārayet  Hbhv 
śaṅkhopari tathā padmaṃ punaḥ padmaṃ ca dakṣiṇe 
khaḍgaṃ vakṣasi cāpaṃ ca saśaraṃ śīrṣṇi dhārayet  Hbhv 
iti pañcāyudhāny ādau dhārayed vaiṣṇavo janaḥ 
matsyaṃ ca dakṣiṇe haste kūrmaṃ vāmakare tathā  Hbhv 
tathā coktaṃ 
dakṣiṇe tu bhuje vipro vibhṛṣād vai sudarśanam 
matsyaṃ padmaṃ cāpare'tha śaṅkhaṃ padmaṃ gadās tathā  Hbhv 
iti
sāmpradāyikaśiṣṭānām ācārāc ca yathāruci 
śaṅkhacakrādicihnāni sarveṣv aṅgeṣu dhārayet  Hbhv 
bhaktyā nijeṣṭadevasya dhārayel lakṣaṇāny api  Hbhv 
cakraśaṅkhau ca dhāryate saṃmiśrāv eva kaiścana  Hbhv 
śrīgopīcandanenaivaṃ cakrādīni budho 'nvaham 
dhārayec chayanādau tu taptāni kila tāni hi  Hbhv 
atha cakrādīnāṃ lakṣaṇāni
dvādaśāraṃ tu ṣaṭkoṇaṃ valayatrayasaṃyutam 
cakraṃ syād dakṣiṇāvartaṃ śaṅkhaṃ ca śrīhareḥ smṛtaḥ  Hbhv 
gadāpadmādikaṃ lokasiddham eva mataṃ budhaiḥ 
mudrā vā bhagavannāmāṅkitā vāṣṭākṣarādibhiḥ  Hbhv 
atha mālādidhāraṇam
tataḥ kṛṣṇārpitā mālā dhārayet tulasīdalaiḥ 
padmākṣais tulasīkāṣṭhaiḥ phalair dhātryāś ca nirmitāḥ  Hbhv 
dhārayet tulasīkāṣṭhabhūṣaṇāni ca vaiṣṇavaḥ 
mastake karṇayor bāhvoḥ karayoś ca yathāruci  Hbhv 
atha mālādhāraṇavidhiḥ
skānde
sannivedyaiva haraye tulasīkāṣṭhasambhavām 
mālāṃ paścāt svayaṃ dhatte sa vai bhāgavatottamaḥ  Hbhv 
haraye nārpayed yas tu tulasīkāṣṭhasambhavām 
mālāṃ dhatte svayaṃ mūḍhaḥ sa yāti narakaṃ dhruvam  Hbhv 
kṣālitāṃ pañcagavyena mūlamantreṇa mantritām 
gāyatryā cāṣta kṛtvā vai mantritāṃ dhūpayec ca tām 
vidhivat parayā bhaktyā sadyojātena pūjayet  Hbhv 
tulasīkāṣṭhasambhūte māle kṛṣṇajanapriye 
bibharmi tvām ahaṃ kaṇṭhe kuru māṃ kṛṣṇavallabham  Hbhv 
yathā tvaṃ vallabhā viṣṇor nityaṃ viṣṇujanapriyā 
tathā māṃ kuru deveśi nityaṃ viṣṇujanapriyam  Hbhv 
dāne lādhātur uddiṣṭo lāsi māṃ harivallabhe 
bhaktebhyaś ca samastebhyas tena mālā nigadyase  Hbhv 
evaṃ samprārthya vidhivan mālāṃ kṛṣṇagale'rpitām 
dhārayed vaiṣṇavo yo vai sa gacched vaiṣṇavaṃ padam  Hbhv 
tatraiva kārttikaprasaṅge
dhātrīphalakṛtāṃ mālāṃ kaṇṭhasthāṃ yo vahen na hi 
vaiṣṇavo na sa vijñeyo viṣṇupūjārato yadi  Hbhv 
gāruḍe
dhārayanti na ye mālāṃ haitukāḥ pāpabuddhayaḥ 
narakān na nivartante dagdhāḥ kopāgninā hareḥ  Hbhv 
ata eva skānde
na jahyāt tulasīmālāṃ dhātrīmālāṃ viśeṣataḥ 
mahāpātakasaṃhantrīṃ dharmakāmārthadāyinīm  Hbhv 
atha mālādhāraṇamāhātmyam
agastyasaṃhitāyām
nirmālyatulasīmālāyukto yaś cārcayed dharim 
yad yat karoti tat sarvam anantaphaladaṃ bhavet  Hbhv 
nāradīye
ye kaṇṭhalagnatulasīnalinākṣamālā
ye vā lalāṭaphalke lasad ūrdhvapuṇḍrāḥ 
ye bāhumūlaparicihnitaśaṅkhacakrās
te vaiṣṇavā bhuvanam āśu pavitrayanti  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
bhujayugam api cihnair aṅkitaṃ yasya viṣṇoḥ
paramapuruṣanāmnāṃ kīrtanaṃ yasya vāci 
ṛjutaram api puṇḍraṃ mastake yasya kaṇṭhe
sarasijamaṇimālā yasya tasyāsmi dāsaḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare śrībhagavaduktau
tulasīkāṣṭhamālāṃ ca kaṇṭhasthāṃ vahate tu yaḥ 
apy aśauco 'py anācāro mām evaiti na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
skānde
dhātrīphalakṛtā mālā tulasīkāṣṭhasambhavā 
dṛśyate yasya dehe tu sa vai bhāgavatottamaḥ  Hbhv 
tulasīdalajāṃ mālāṃ kaṇṭhasthāṃ vahate tu yaḥ 
viṣṇūttīrṇā viśeṣeṇa sa namasyo divaukasām  Hbhv 
tulasīdalajā mālā dhātrīphalakṛtāpi ca 
dadāti pāpināṃ muktiṃ kiṃ punar viṣṇusevinām  Hbhv 
tatraiva kārttikaprasaṅge
yaḥ punas tulasīmālāṃ kṛtvā kaṇṭhe janārdanam 
pūjayet puṇyam āpnoti pratipuṣpaṃ gavāyutam  Hbhv 
yāval luṭhati kaṇṭhasthā dhātrīmālā narasya hi 
tāvat tasya śarīre tu prītyā luṭhati keśavaḥ  Hbhv 
spṛśec ca yāni lomāni dhātrīmālā kalau nṛṇām 
tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi vasate keśavālaye  Hbhv 
yāvad dināni vahate dhātrīmālāṃ kalau naraḥ 
tāvadyugasahasrāṇi vaikuṇṭhe vasatir bhavet  Hbhv 
mālāyugmaṃ vahed yas tu dhātrītulasisaṃbhavam 
vahate kaṇṭhadeśe tu kalpakoṭiṃ divaṃ vaset  Hbhv 
gāruḍe ca mārkaṇḍeyoktau
tulasīdalajāṃ mālāṃ kṛṣṇottīrṇā vahet tu yaḥ 
patre patre'śvamedhānāṃ daśānāṃ labhate phalam  Hbhv 
tulasīkāṣṭhasambhūtāṃ yo mālāṃ vahate naraḥ 
phalaṃ yacchati daitāriḥ pratyahaṃ dvārakodbhavam  Hbhv 
nivedya viṣṇave mālāṃ tulasīkāṣṭhasambhavam 
vahate yo naro bhaktyā tasya vai nāsti pātakam  Hbhv 
sadā prītamanās tasya kṛṣṇa devakīnandanaḥ 
tulasīkāṣṭhasambhūtāṃ yo mālāṃ vahate naraḥ 
prāyaścittaṃ na tasyāsti nāśaucaṃ tasya vigrahe  Hbhv 
tulasīkāṣṭhasambhūtāṃ śiraso yasya bhūṣaṇam 
bāhvoḥ kare ca martyasya dehe tasya sadā hariḥ  Hbhv 
tulasīkāṣṭhamālābhir bhūṣitaḥ puṇyam ācaret 
pitṝṇāṃ devatānāṃ ca kṛtaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ kalau  Hbhv 
tulasīkāṣṭhamālāṃ tu pretarājasya dūtakāḥ 
dṛṣṭvā naśyanti dūreṇa vātoddhūtaṃ yathā dalam  Hbhv 
tulasīkāṣṭhamālābhir bhūṣito bhramate yadi 
duḥsvapnaṃ durnimittaṃ ca na bhayaṃ śastrajaṃ kvacit  Hbhv 
atha gṛhe sandhyopāsanavidhiḥ
sandhyopāstyādikaṃ karma tataḥ kuryāt yathāvidhi 
kṛṣṇapādodakenaiva tatra devāditarpaṇam  Hbhv 
śirasā viṣṇunirmālyaṃ pādodenāpi tarpaṇam 
pitṝṇāṃ devatānāṃ ca vaiṣṇavais tu samaṃ matam  Hbhv 
sandhyopāstau ca vaśiṣṭhavacanam
gṛhe tv ekaguṇā sandhyā goṣṭhe daśaguṇā smṛtā 
śatasāhasrikā nadyām anantā viṣṇusannidhau  Hbhv 
atha śrīgurupūjā
pūjayiṣyaṃs tataḥ kṛṣṇam ādau sannihitaṃ gurum 
praṇamya pūjayed bhaktyā dattvā kiṃcid upāayanam  Hbhv 
smṛtimahārṇave
riktapāṇir na paśyeta rājānaṃ bhiṣajaṃ gurum 
nopāyanakaraḥ putraṃ śiṣyaṃ bhṛtyaṃ nirīkṣayet  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca śrībhagavaduktau
prathamaṃ tu guruṃ pūjya tataś caiva mamārcanam 
kurvan siddhim avāpnoti hy anyathā niṣphalaṃ bhavet  Hbhv 
śrīnāradena ca
gurau sannihite yas tu pūjayed anyam agrataḥ 
sa durgatim avāpnoti pūjanaṃ tasya niṣphalam  Hbhv 
śrutiṣu śvetu 
yasya deve parā bhaktiḥ yathā deve tathā gurau 
tasyaite kathitā hy arthāḥ prakāśante mahātmanaḥ  Hbhv 
ekādaśaskandhe  śrībhagavaduktau
ācāryaṃ māṃ vijānīyān nāvamanyeta karhicit 
na martyabuddhyāsūyeta sarvadevamayo guruḥ  Hbhv 
daśamaskandhe BhP  ca 
nāham ijyāprajātibhyāṃ tapasopaśamena ca 
tuṣyeyaṃ sarvabhūtātmā guruśuśrūṣayā yathā  Hbhv 
saptamaskandhe BhP 
yasya sākṣād bhagavati jñānadīpaprade gurau 
martyāsaddhīḥ śrutaṃ tasya sarvaṃ kuñjaraśaucavat  Hbhv 
anyatrāpi
sādhakasya gurau bhaktiṃ mandīkurvanti devatāḥ 
yan no 'tītya vrajed viṣṇuṃ śiṣyo bhaktyā gurau dhruvan  Hbhv 
manusmṛtau 
ajño bhavati vai bālaḥ pitā bhavati mantradaḥ 
ajñaṃ hi bālam ity āhuḥ pitety eva tu mantradam  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
gurur brahmā gurur viṣṇur gurur devo maheśvaraḥ 
gurur eva paraṃ brahma tasmāt sampūjayet sadā  Hbhv 
vāmanakalpe
yo mantraḥ sa guruḥ sākṣāt yo guruḥ sa hariḥ smṛtaḥ 
gurur yasya bhavet tuṣṭas tasya tuṣṭo hariḥ svayam 
guroḥ samāsane naiva na caivoccāsane vaset  Hbhv 
viṣṇurahasye
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena yathāvidhi tathā gurum 
abhedenārcayet yas tu sa muktiphalam āpnuyāt  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharme śrībhāgavate ca hariścandrasya
gurusuśrūṣaṇaṃ nāma sarvadharmottamottamam 
tasmād dharmāt paro dharmaḥ pavitraṃ naiva vidyate  Hbhv 
kāmakrodhādikaṃ yad yad ātmano 'niṣṭakāraṇam 
etat sarvaṃ gurau bhaktyā puruṣo hy añjasā jayet  Hbhv 
pādme
pitur ādhikyabhāvena ye'rcayanti guruṃ sadā 
bhavanty atithayo loke brahmaṇas te viśāṃ vara  Hbhv 
tatraiva devahūtistutau
bhaktir yathā harau me'sti tadvan niṣṭhā gurau yadi 
mamāsti tena satyena svaṃ darśayatu me hariḥ  Hbhv 
adityapurāṇe
avidyo vā savidyo vā gurur eva janārdanaḥ 
mārgastho vāpy amārgastho gurur eva sadā gatiḥ  Hbhv 
anyatra ca
harau ruṣṭe gurus trātā gurau ruṣṭe na kaścana 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena gurum eva prasādayet  Hbhv 
brahmavaivarte
api ghnantaḥ śapanto vā viruddhā api ye krudhāḥ 
guravaḥ pūjanīyās te gṛhaṃ natvā nayeta tān  Hbhv 
tat ślāghyaṃ janma dhanyaṃ tat dinaṃ puṇyātha naḍikā 
yasyāṃ guruṃ praṇamate samupāsya tu bhaktitaḥ  Hbhv 
upadeṣṭāram āmnāyagataṃ pariharanti ye 
tān mṛtān api kravyādāḥ kṛtaghnān nopabhuñjate  Hbhv 
bodhaḥ kaluṣitas tena daurātmyaṃ prakaṭīkṛtam 
gurur yena parityaktas tena tyaktaḥ purā hariḥ  Hbhv 
anyatra ca 
pratipadya guruṃ yas tu mohād vipratipadyate 
sa kalpakoṭiṃ narake pacyate puruṣādhamaḥ  Hbhv 
pañcarātre 
avaiṣṇavopadiṣṭena mantreṇa nirayaṃ vrajet 
punaś ca vidhinā samyag grāhayed vaiṣṇavād guroḥ  Hbhv 
agastyasaṃhitāyāṃ 
ye gurvājñāṃ na kurvanti pāpiṣṭhāḥ puruṣādhamāḥ 
na teṣāṃ narakakleśanistāro munisattama  Hbhv 
yaiḥ śiṣyaiḥ śaśvad ārādhyā guravo hy avamānitāḥ 
putramitrakalatrādisampadbhyaḥ pracyutā hi te  Hbhv 
adhikṣipya guruṃ mohāt paruṣaṃ pravadanti ye 
śūkaratvaṃ bhavaty eva teṣāṃ janmaśateṣv api  Hbhv 
ye gurudrohiṇo mūḍhāḥ satataṃ pāpakāriṇaḥ 
teṣāṃ ca yāvat sukṛtaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ syān na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
ataḥ prāg gurum abhyarcya kṛṣṇabhāvena buddhimān 
tryavarān asamān kuryāt praṇāmān daṇḍapātavat  Hbhv 
ata eva kaurme śrīvyāsagītāyām
vyatyasta pāṇinā kāryam upasaṅgrahaṇaṃ guroḥ 
savyena savyaḥ spraṣṭavyo dakṣiṇena tu dakṣiṇaḥ  Hbhv 
iti
atha śrīgurupādānāṃ prāpyānujñāṃ ca sādhakaḥ 
prāk saṃskṛtaṃ harer gehaṃ pravekṣyan pāduke tyajet  Hbhv 
tathā cāpastamba
agnyāgāre gavāṃ goṣṭhe devabrāhmaṇasannidhau 
jape bhojanakāle ca pāduke parivarjayet  Hbhv 
iti
tataḥ śrībhagavatpūjāmandirasyāṅganaṃ gataḥ 
prakṣālya hastau pādau ca dvirācamanam ācaret  Hbhv 
tathā ca mārkaṇḍeye
devārcanādikāryāṇi tathā gurvabhivādanam 
kurvīta samyag ācamya tadvad eva bhujikriyām  Hbhv 
iti
iti śrīgopālabhaṭṭavilikhite śrībhagavadbhaktivilāse
śrīvaiṣṇavālaṅkāro nāma
caturtho vilāsaḥ 
 AdhisthanikaVilasa
pañcamavilāsaḥ
ādhiṣṭhānikaḥ
śrīcaitanyaprabhuṃ vande bālo 'pi yadanugrahāt 
taren nānāmatagrāhavyāptaṃ pūjākramārṇavam  Hbhv 
sanātanaḥ śrīcaitanyāya namaḥ 
bālo 'jñaḥ 
pakṣe śiśuḥ 
nānāvidhamatāny eva grāhas tair vyāptam 
pūjāyāḥ kramo vidhiḥ 
vidhyanukramo vā sa evārṇavas tam  HbhvC 
śrīmadgopāladevasyāṣṭādaśākṣarayantrataḥ 
likhyate'rcāvidhir gūḍhaḥ kramadīpikayekṣitaḥ  Hbhv 
sanātanaḥ aṣṭādaśākṣaramantreṇa yo 'rcāvidhiḥ pūjāprakāraḥ sa likhyate 
yadyapi daśākṣarādināpi pūjāvidhau bhedo nāsti
tathāpi nyāsādibhedāpekṣayā
tathā likhitam 
gūḍho 'pi kramadīpikayā śrīkeśavācāryaviracitayā īkṣitaḥ darśitaḥ san 
ataḥ kramadīpikoktānusāreṇa lekhya iti bhāvaḥ  HbhvC 
āgamoktena mārgeṇa bhagavān brāhmaṇair api 
sadaiva pūjyo 'to lekhyaḥ prāya āgamiko vidhiḥ  Hbhv 
tathā ca viṣṇuyāmale
kṛte śrutyuktamārgaḥ syāt tretāyāṃ smṛtibhāvitaḥ 
dvāpare tu purāṇoktaḥ kalāv āgamasambhavaḥ  Hbhv 
aśuddhāḥ śūdrākalpā hi brāhmaṇāḥ kalisambhavāḥ 
teṣām āgamamārgeṇa śuddhir na śrautavartmanā  Hbhv 
sanātanaḥ teṣām āgamamārgeṇa śrautavartmanety anena tair api āgamikavidhinaiva pūjā kāryeti bhāvaḥ 
tathā caikādaśaskandhe BhP  nānātantravidhānena kalāv api tathā śṛṇu iti 
tatra śrīdharasvāmipādāḥnānātantravidhāneneti kalau tantramārgasya prādhānyaṃ darśayati iti  HbhvC 
atha dvārapūjā
śrīkṛṣṇadvāradevebhyo dattvā pādyādikaṃ tataḥ 
gandhapuṣpair arcayet tān yathāsthānaṃ yathākramam  Hbhv 
sanātanaḥ tān śrīkṛṣṇadvāradevān
praṇavādicaturthyantaṃ devanāma namo 'ntakam ity agre lekhyatvād atraivaṃ prayogaḥśrīkṛṣṇadvāradevatābhyo namaḥ 
anena mantreṇa pādyārdhyādikaṃ dattvā gandhādibhiḥ punar viśeṣeṇa pūjayed ity arthaḥ 
evam agre'pi saparivārebhyaḥ śrīkṛṣṇapārṣadebhyo namaḥ ity ādi prayogo draṣṭavyaḥ  HbhvC 
dvārāgre saparīvārān bhūpīṭhe kṛṣṇapārṣadān 
tadagre garuḍaṃ dvārasyordhve dvāraśriyaṃ yajet  Hbhv 
prāgdvārobhayapārśve tu yajec caṇḍapracaṇḍakau 
dvāre ca dakṣiṇe dhātṛvidhātārau ca paścime  Hbhv 
jayaṃ ca vijayaṃ caiva balaṃ prabalam uttare 
dvandvaśastv evam abhyarcya dehalyāṃ vāstupuruṣam  Hbhv 
sanātanaḥ evaṃ sāmānyena sarveṣām eva pūjāvidhir likhitaḥ 
idānīṃ yathāsthānaṃ yathākramam iti yal likhitaṃ
tad eva vivicya likhatidvārāgra iti dvārābhyām 
tatrāpy ādau dvārasyāgre yat bhūrūpaṃ pīṭhaṃ
tatra samastaparivārānvitān śrīkṛṣṇapārṣadān yajet pūjayet 
anantaraṃ tasya dvārasyāgre garuḍaṃ 
yadyapi dvāraśriyo 'rcanaṃ prabalārcanānantaram eva kramadīpikāyām uktam
tathāpi iṣṭveti kṭvāpratyayena caṇḍādipūjātaḥ pūrvakāla eveti bodhitam 
tathaivaa sadācārāt 
kiṃ ca dvandva ity agre likhanāt
caṇḍapracaṇḍābhyāṃ namaḥ ity evaṃ yugmatvena prayogo jñeyaḥ  HbhvC 
dvārāntaḥpārśvayor gaṅgāṃ yamunāṃ ca tato 'rcayet 
tatpārśvayoḥ śaṅkhanidhiṃ tathā padmanidhiṃ yajet  Hbhv 
sanātanaḥ dvārasyāntaḥ abhyantare tatpārśvadvaye tayor gaṅgāyamunayoḥ pārśvadvaye  HbhvC 
gaṇeśaṃ mandirasyāgnikoṇe durgāṃ ca nairṛte 
vāṇīṃ vāyavya aiśāne kṣetrapālaṃ tathārcayet  Hbhv 
sanātanaḥ āgneye koṇe gaṇeśam arcayet 
tathā coktaṃ kramadīpikāyām 
parivārārāḥ kṛtāḥ sarve punaḥ śrīviṣṇupārṣadāḥ 
dvārāgrābalipīṭhe'rcyāḥ pakṣīndraś ca tadagrataḥ 
caṇḍapracaṇḍau prāg dhātṛvidhātārau ca dakṣiṇe 
jayaḥ savijayaḥ paścād balaḥ prabala uttare 
ūrdhve dvāraśriyaṃ ceṣṭvā dvāry etān yugmaśo 'rcayet 
pūjyo vāstupumāṃs tatra tatra dvāḥpīthamadhyataḥ 
dvārāntaḥpārśvayor arcyā gaṅgā ca yamunā nadī 
koṇeṣu vighnaṃ durgāṃ ca vāṇīṃ kṣetre samarcayet 
 iti 
dvāḥśākhām āśrayan vāmāṃ saṅkocyāṅgāni dehalīm 
aspṛṣṭvā praviśed veśma nyasyan prāg dakṣiṇaṃ padam  Hbhv 
sanātanaḥ vāmāṃ svavāmabhāgavartinīṃ dvāraśākhāṃ āśrayan īṣat spṛṣad nijāṅgāni saṃkocya dehalīm aspṛṣṭvā na laṅghayitvety arthaḥ 
dakṣiṇaṃ padaṃ prāk ādau nyasyan 
dakṣiṇapādanyāsakrameṇety arthaḥ 
veśma śrībhagavanmandiraṃ harer gehaṃ pravekṣyann iti pūrvalikhanāt 
praviśet tanmadhyaṃ śanaiḥ pūjako gacchet  HbhvC 
tathā ca sāradātilake
kiṃcit spṛśan vāmaśākhāṃ dehalīṃ laṅghayan guruḥ 
aṅgaṃ saṅkocayann antaḥ praviśed dakṣiṇāṅghriṇā  Hbhv 
sanātanaḥ gurur iti dīkṣāvidhānoktaḥ  HbhvC 
atha gṛhapraveśamāhātmyam
tanmāhātmyaṃ ca haribhaktisudhodaye
praviśann ālayaṃ viṣṇor arcanārthaṃ subhaktimān 
na bhūyaḥ praviśan mātuḥ kukṣikārāgṛhaṃ sudhīḥ  Hbhv 
atha gṛhāntaḥpūjā
nairṛte vāstupuruṣaṃ brahmāṇam api pūjayet 
āsanastho yajet tāṃs tān anyatra bhagavadgṛhāt  Hbhv 
tatpūjāmantraś coktaḥ
praṇavādicaturthyantaṃ devanāma namo 'ntakam 
pūjāmantram idaṃ proktaṃ sarvatrārcanakarmaṇi  Hbhv 
 iti 
atha kṛṣṇāgratas tiṣṭhan kṛtvā digbandhanaṃ kṣipet 
puṣpākṣatān samastāsu dikṣu tatroktamantrataḥ  Hbhv 
atha pūjārthāsanam
tataś cāsanamantreṇābhimantryābhyarcya cāsanam 
tasminn upaviśet padmāsanena svastikena vā  Hbhv 
tatra kṛṣṇārcakaḥ prāyo divase prāṅmukho bhavet 
udaṅmukho rajanyāṃ tu sthiramūrtiś ca sammukhaḥ  Hbhv 
tatra ca ekādaśaskandhe BhP 
āsīnaḥ prāg udagvārcet sthirāyāntv atha sammukhaḥ  Hbhv 
athāsanamantraḥ
āsanamantrasya merupṛṣṭha ṛṣiḥ sutalaṃ chandaḥ 
kūrmo devatā āsanābhimantreṇa viniyogaḥ  Hbhv 
pṛthvi tvayā dhṛtā lokā devi tvaṃ viṣṇunā dhṛtā 
tvaṃ ca dhāraya māṃ nityaṃ pavitraṃ kuru cāsanam  Hbhv 
athāsanavidhiḥ
nāradapañcarātre
vaṃśāśmadārudharaṇītṛṇapallavanirmitam 
varjayed āsanaṃ vidvān dāridryavyādhiduḥkhadam 
kṛṣṇājinaṃ kambalaṃ vā nānyad āsanam iṣyate  Hbhv 
anyatra ca
kṛṣṇājinaṃ vyāghracarma kauṣeyaṃ vetranirmitam 
vastrājinaṃ kambalaṃ vā kalpayed āsanaṃ mṛdu  Hbhv 
atha viśeṣata āsanadoṣavidhiḥ
nāradapañcarātre
vaṃśād āhur daridratvaṃ pāṣāṇe vyādhisambhavam 
dharaṇyāṃ duḥkhasambhūtiṃ daurbhāgyaṃ dāravāsane  Hbhv 
tṛṇāsane yaśohāniṃ pallave cittavibhramam 
darbhāsane vyādhināśaṃ kambalaṃ duḥkhamocanam  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca śrībhagavadgītāsu ṅītā 
śucau deśe pratiṣṭhāpya sthiram āsanam ātmanaḥ 
nātyucchritaṃ nātinīcaṃ cailājinakuśottaram  Hbhv 
 iti 
yathokatam upaviśyātha sampradāyānusārataḥ 
śaṅkhādipūjāsambhārān nyaset tattatpadeṣu tān  Hbhv 
atha pātrāsādanam
svasya vāmāgrataḥ śaṅkhaṃ sādhāraṃ sthāpayed budhaḥ 
tatraivārdhyādipātrāṇi nyasyec ca dvāri bhāgaśaḥ  Hbhv 
tulasīgandhapuṣpādibhājanāni ca dakṣiṇe 
vāme ca sthāpayet pārśve kalasaṃ pūrṇam ambhasā  Hbhv 
dakṣiṇe ghṛtadīpaṃ ca tailadīpaṃ ca vāmataḥ 
sambhārānaparān nyaset svadṛṣṭiviṣaye pade 
karaprakṣālanārthaṃ ca pātram ekaṃ svapṛṣṭhataḥ  Hbhv 
atha pātrāṇi tanmāhātmyaṃ ca
devīpurāṇe
nānāvicitrarūpāṇi puṇḍarīkākṛtīni ca 
śaṅkhanīlotpalābhāni pātrāṇi parikalpayet  Hbhv 
ratnādiracitāny eva kāñcīmūlayutāni ca 
yathāśobhaṃ yathālābhaṃ tathā pātrāṇi kārayet  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
haṃsapātreṇa sarvāṇi cepsitāni labhen mune 
arghyaṃ dattvā tathā raupyeṇāyurājyaṃ śubhaṃ bhavet 
tāmrapātreṇa saubhāgyaṃ dharmaṃ mṛṇmayasambhavam  Hbhv 
vārāhe
sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ kāṃsyaṃ yena dīyate bhājanam 
tān sarvān samparityajya tāmraṃ tu mama rocate  Hbhv 
pavitrāṇāṃ pavitraṃ yo maṅgalānāṃ ca maṅgalam 
viśuddhānāṃ śuciṃ caiva tāmraṃ saṃsāramokṣaṇam  Hbhv 
dīkṣitānāṃ viśuddhānāṃ mama karmaparāyaṇaḥ 
sadā tāmreṇa kartavyam evaṃ bhūmi mama priyam  Hbhv 
 iti 
kecic ca tāmrapātreṣu gavyāder yogadoṣataḥ 
tāmrātiriktam icchanti madhuparkasya bhājanam  Hbhv 
tathaiva śaṅkham evārdhyapātram icchanti kecana 
śaṅkhe kṛtvā tu pānīyaṃ sapuṣpaṃ salilākṣatam 
arghyaṃ dadāti devasyety evaṃ skānde'bhidhānataḥ  Hbhv 
atha maṅgalaghaṭasthāpanam
maṅgalārthaṃ ca kalasaṃ sajalaṃ karakānvitam 
phalādisahitaṃ divyaṃ nyased bhagavato 'grataḥ  Hbhv 
tathā ca skānde
kumbhaṃ sakarakaṃ divyaṃ phalakarpūrasaṃyutam 
nyased arcanakāle tu kṛṣṇasyātīva vallabham  Hbhv 
 iti 
kiṃ ca
sanīraṃ ca sakarpūraṃ kumbhaṃ kṛṣṇāya yo nyaset 
kalpaṃ tasya na pāpekṣāṃ kurvanti prapitāmahāḥ  Hbhv 
athārghyādipātrāṇi
prakṣiped arghyapātre tu gandhapuṣpākṣatān yavān 
kuśāgratiladūrvāś ca siddhārthān api sādhakaḥ 
kecic cātra jalādīni dravyāṇy aṣṭau vadanti hi  Hbhv 
yata uktaṃ bhaviṣye
āpaḥ kṣīraṃ kuśāgrāṇi dadhyakṣatatilas tathā 
yavāḥ siddhārthakāś caivam arghyo 'ṣṭāṅgaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  Hbhv 
pādyapātre ca kamalaṃ dūrvā śyāmākam eva ca 
nikṣiped viṣṇupatrīṃ cety evaṃ dravyacatuṣṭayam  Hbhv 
tathaivācamanīyārthaṃ pātre dravyatrayaṃ budhaḥ 
jātīphalaṃ lavaṅgaṃ ca kakkolam api nikṣipet  Hbhv 
madhuparkīyapātre ca gavyaṃ dadhi payo ghṛtam 
madhukhaṇḍam apīty evaṃ nikṣiped dravyapañcakam  Hbhv 
kecit trīṇy eva pātre'smin dravyāṇīcchanti sādhavaḥ  Hbhv 
yata uktaṃ śrīviṣṇudharme
ghṛtaṃ dadhi tathā kṣaudraṃ madhuparko vidhīyate  Hbhv 
ādivārāhe ca
dadhisarpir madhusamaṃ pātre auḍumbare mama 
madhunas tu alābhe tu guḍena saha miśrayet  Hbhv 
ghṛtasyālābhe suśroṇi lājaiś ca saha miśrayet 
tathā dadhno 'py alābhe tu kṣīreṇa saha miśrayet  Hbhv 
teṣām abhāve puṣpādi tattadbhāvanayā kṣipet 
nāradas tv āha vimalenodakenaiva pūryate  Hbhv 
mūlena pātreṇaikena maṣṭakṛtvo 'bhimantrayet 
kuryāc ca teṣāṃ pātrāṇāṃ rakṣaṇaṃ cakramudrayā  Hbhv 
pūjām ārabhamāṇo hi yathoktāsanam āsthitaḥ 
paṭhen maṅgalaśāntiṃ tāṃ yārcane sammatā satām  Hbhv 
atha maṅgalaśāntiḥ
oṃ bhadraṃ karṇebhiḥ śṛṇuyāma devā
bhadraṃ paśyemākṣabhir yajatrā 
sthirair aṅgais tuṣṭuvāṃsas tanubhir
vyaśema devahitaṃ yad āyuḥ  Hbhv 
svasti na indro vṛddhaśravāḥ 
svasti naḥ pūṣā viśvadevāḥ 
svasti nas tārkṣo 'riṣṭanemiḥ 
svasti no bṛhaspatir dadhātu  Hbhv 
 iti 
paṭhan oṃ śāntiḥ śrīkṛṣṇapādapadmārādhaneṣu śāntir bhavatu 
 iti 
atha vighnanivāraṇam
apasarpantu te bhūtā ye bhūtā bhuvi saṃsthitāḥ 
ye bhūtā vighnakartāras te naśyantu śivājñayā  Hbhv 
ity udīryāstramantreṇa vāmapādasya pārṣṇinā 
ghātais tribhir budho vighnān bhaumān sarvān nivārayet  Hbhv 
āntarīkṣāṃś ca tenaivordhvordhvatālatrayeṇa hi 
nirasyotsārayed divyān māntriko divyadṛṣṭitaḥ  Hbhv 
śrīgurvādinatiḥ
tataḥ kṛtāñjalir vāme śrīguruṃ paramaṃ gurum 
parameṣṭhiguruṃ ceti named guruparamparām  Hbhv 
gaṇeśaṃ dakṣiṇe bhāge durgām agre'tha pṛṣṭhataḥ 
kṣetrapālaṃ named bhaktyā madhye cātmeṣṭadaivatam  Hbhv 
tataś cāstreṇa saṃśodhya karau kurvīta tena hi 
tālatrayaṃ diśāṃ bandham agniprākāram eva ca  Hbhv 
atha bhūtaśuddhiḥ
śarīrākārabhūtānāṃ bhūtānāṃ yad viśodhanam 
avyayabrahmasamparkād bhūtaśuddhir iyaṃ matā  Hbhv 
bhūtaśuddhiṃ vinā kartur japahomādikāḥ kriyāḥ 
bhavanti niṣphalāḥ sarvā yathāvidhy apy aniṣṭhitāḥ  Hbhv 
tatprakāraś ca
karakacchapikāṃ kṛtvātmānaṃ buddhyā hṛdabjataḥ 
śiraḥsahasrapatrābje paramātmani yojayet 
pṛthivyādīni tattvāni tasmin līnāni bhāvayet  Hbhv 
vāmahastaṃ tathottānam adho dakṣiṇabandhitam 
karakacchapikā mudrā bhūtaśuddhau prakīrtitā  Hbhv 
dehaṃ saṃśoṣya dagdhvedam āplāvyāmṛtavarṣataḥ 
utpādya draḍhayitvāsupratiṣṭhāṃ vidhinācaret  Hbhv 
ātmānam evaṃ saṃśodhya nītvā kṛṣṇārcanārhatām 
vātsalyād dhṛdgataṃ kṛṣṇaṃ yaṣṭuṃ hṛt punar ānayet  Hbhv 
tathā ca trailokyasaṃmohanatantre
nābhisthavāyunā dehaṃ sapāpaṃ śodhayed budhaḥ 
vahninā hṛdayasthena dahet tac ca kalevaram  Hbhv 
sahasrāre mahāpadme lalāṭasthe sthitaṃ vidhum 
sampūrṇamaṇḍalaṃ śuddhaṃ cintayed amṛtātmakam  Hbhv 
tasmād galitadhārābhiḥ plāvayed bhasmasād budhaḥ 
ābhir varṇamayībhiś ca pañcabhūtātmakaṃ vapuḥ 
pūrvavad bhāvayed devīm  Hbhv 
 ity ādi 
kiṃ cāgre
tatas tasmāt samākṛṣya praṇavena tu mantravit 
tat tejo hṛdaye nyasya cintayed viṣṇum avyayam  Hbhv 
kiṃ vā cintanamātreṇa bhūtaśuddhiṃ vidhāya tām 
prāṇāyāmāṃś tataḥ kuryāt sampradāyānusarataḥ  Hbhv 
atha prāṇāyāmaḥ
recaḥ ṣoḍaśamātrābhiḥ pūro dvātriṃśatā bhavet 
catuḥṣaṣṭhyā bhavet kumbha evaṃ syāt prāṇasaṃyamaḥ  Hbhv 
virecya pavanaṃ pūrvaṃ saṃkocya gudamaṇḍalam 
pūrayitvā vidhānena svaśaktyā kumbhake sthitaḥ  Hbhv 
tatra praṇavam abhyasyan bījaṃ vā mantram ūrdhvagam 
ṛṣyādismaraṇaṃ kṛtvā kuryād dhyānam atandritaḥ  Hbhv 
tad dhyānaṃ coktam
viṣṇuṃ bhāsvatkirīṭāṅgadavalayakalākalpahārodarāṅghri
śroṇībhūṣaṃ savakṣomaṇimakaramahākuṇḍalāmṛṣṭagaṇḍam 
hastodyacchaṅkhacakrāmbujagadam amalaṃ pītakauśeyavāsaṃ
vidyotadbhāsam udyaddinakarasadṛśaṃ padmasaṃsthaṃ namāmi  Hbhv 
kvacic ca
rudras tu recake brahmā pūrake dhyeyadevatā 
śrīviṣṇuḥ kumbhake jñeyo dhyānasthānaṃ guror mukhāt  Hbhv 
tathā hi
nābhisthāne pūrakeṇa cintayet kamalāsanam 
brahmāṇaṃ raktagaurāṅgaṃ caturvaktraṃ pitāmaham  Hbhv 
nīlotpaladalaśyāmaṃ hṛdi madhye pratiṣṭhitam 
caturbhujaṃ mahātmānaṃ kumbhakena tu cintayet  Hbhv 
recekanaiśvaraṃ dhyānaṃ lalāṭe sarvapāpaham 
śuddhasphaṭikasaṅkāśaṃ kuryād vai nirmalaṃ budhaḥ  Hbhv 
 iti 
ekāntibhiś ca bhagavān sarvadevamayaḥ prabhuḥ 
kṛṣṇaḥ priyajanopetaś cintanīyo hi sarvataḥ  Hbhv 
atha prāṇāyāmamāhātmyam
pādme  devahūtivikuṇḍalasaṃvāde
yamalokaṃ na paśyanti prāṇāyāmaparāyaṇāḥ 
api duṣkṛtakarmāṇas tair eva hatakilbiṣāḥ  Hbhv 
divase divase vaiśya prāṇāyāmās tu ṣoḍaśa 
api brahmahaṇaṃ sākṣāt punanty aharahaḥ kṛtāḥ  Hbhv 
tapāṃsi yāni tapyante vratāni niyamāś ca ye 
gosahasrapradānaṃ ca prāṇāyāmas tu tatsamaḥ  Hbhv 
ambubinduṃ yaḥ kuśāgreṇa māse māse naraḥ pibet 
saṃvatsaraśataṃ sāgraṃ prāṇāyāmas tu tatsamaḥ  Hbhv 
pātakaṃ tu mahad yac ca tathā kṣudropapātakam 
prāṇāyāmaiḥ kṣaṇāt sarvaṃ bhasmasāt kurute naraḥ  Hbhv 
 iti 
nyāsān vinā japaṃ prāhur āsuraṃ viphalaṃ budhāḥ 
ato yathāsampradāyaṃ nyāsān kuryād yathāvidhi  Hbhv 
tatrādau mātṛkānyāsaḥ
ṛṣicchandodevatādi smṛtvādau mātṛkāmanoḥ 
śirovaktrahṛdādau ca nyasya taddhyānam ācaret  Hbhv 
tac coktam
pañcāśallipibhir vibhaktamukhadoḥpanmadhyavakṣaḥsthalīṃ
bhāvanmaulinibaddhacandraśakalām āpīnatuṅgastanīm 
mudrām akṣaguṇaṃ sudhāḍhyakalasaṃ vidyāṃ ca hastāmbujair
bibhrāṇāṃ viśadaprabhāṃ trinayanāṃ vāgdevatām āśraye  Hbhv 
akārādīn kṣakārāntān varṇānādau tu kevalān 
lalāṭādiṣu cāṅgeṣu nyased vidvān yathākramam  Hbhv 
tac ca vivicyoktam
lalāṭamukhabimbākṣiśrutighrāṇeṣu gaṇḍayoḥ 
oṣṭhadantottamāṅgāsye doḥpatsandhyagrakeṣu ca  Hbhv 
pārśvayoḥ pṛṣṭhato nābhau jaṭhare hṛdaye'ṃsake 
kakudyase ca hṛtpūrvaṃ pāṇipādayuge tataḥ 
jaṭharānanayor nyasen mātṛkārṇān yathākramam  Hbhv 
 iti 
sānusvārān visargāḍhyān sānusvāravisargakān 
nyased bhūyo 'pi tān vidvān evaṃ vāracatuṣṭayam  Hbhv 
atha mātṛkānyāsaḥ
kaṇṭhahṛnnābhiguhyeṣu pāyubhrūmahdyayos tathā 
sthite ṣoḍaśapatrābje krameṇa dvādaśacchade  Hbhv 
daśapatre ca ṣaṭpatre catuṣpatre dvipatrake 
nyased ekaikapatrānte sabindvekaikam akṣaram  Hbhv 
atha keśavādinyāsaḥ
smṛtvā ṛṣyādikāṃ varṇān mūrtibhiḥ keśavādibhiḥ 
kīrtyādibhiḥ śaktibhiś ca nyaset tān pūrvavat kramāt  Hbhv 
nyasec caturthīn atyantā mūrtīḥ śaktīś ca yādibhiḥ 
saptadhātūn prāṇajīvau krodham apy ātmane'ntakān  Hbhv 
tatra dhyānam
udyatpradyotanaśataruciṃ taptahemāvadānaṃ
pārśvadvandve jaladhisutayā viśvadhātryā ca juṣṭam 
nānāratnollasitavividhākalpam āpītavastraṃ
viṣṇuṃ vande darakamalakaumodakīcakrapāṇim  Hbhv 
atha śrīmūrtayaḥ
prathamaṃ keśavo nārāyaṇaḥ paścāc ca mādhavaḥ 
govindaś ca tathā viṣṇur madhusūdana eva ca  Hbhv 
trivikramo vāmano 'tha śrīdharaś ca tataḥ param 
ṛṣīkeśaḥ padmanābhas tato dāmodaras tathā  Hbhv 
vāsudevaḥ saṅkarṣaṇaḥ pradyumno 'thāniruddhakaḥ 
cakrī gadī tathā śārṅgī khaḍgī śaṅkhī halī tathā  Hbhv 
muṣalī ca tathā śūlī pāśī caivāṅkuśī tathā 
mukundo nandajaś caiva tathā nandī naras tathā  Hbhv 
narakajid dhariḥ kṛṣṇaḥ satyaḥ sātvata eva ca 
tataḥ śauris tathā śūras tataḥ paścāj janārdanaḥ  Hbhv 
bhūdharo viśvamūrtiś ca vaikuṇṭhaḥ puruṣottamaḥ 
balo balānujo bālo vṛṣaghno vṛṣa eva ca  Hbhv 
haṃso varāho vimalo nṛsiṃhaś ceti mūrtayaḥ  Hbhv 
atha śaktayaḥ
kīrtiḥ kāntis tuṣṭipuṣṭī dhṛtiḥ śāntiḥ kriyā dayā 
medhā harṣā tathā śraddhā lajjā lakṣmīḥ sarasvatī  Hbhv 
prītī ratir jayā durgā prabhā satyā ca caṇḍikā 
vāṇī vilāsinī caiva vijayā virajā tathā  Hbhv 
viśvā ca vinadā caiva sunandā ca smṛtis tathā 
ṛddhiḥ samṛddhiḥ śuddhiś ca buddhir mūrtir natiḥ kṣamā  Hbhv 
ramomā kledinī klinnā vasudā vasudhā parā 
parāyaṇā ca sūkṣmā ca sandhyā prajñā prabhā niśā  Hbhv 
amoghā vidyutety ekapañcāśat śaktayo matāḥ 
dadāty ayaṃ keśavādinyāso 'trākhilasampadam  Hbhv 
amutrācyutasārūpyaṃ nayati nyāsamātrataḥ  Hbhv 
tad uktaṃ
dhyātvaivaṃ paramapumāṃsam akṣarair yo
vinyased dinam anu keśavādiyuktaiḥ 
medhāyuḥsmṛtidhṛtikīrtikāntilakṣmī
saubhāgyaiś ciram upabṛṃhito bhavet saḥ  Hbhv 
anyatra ca
keśavādir ayaṃ nyāso nyāsamātreṇa dehinaḥ 
acyutatvaṃ dadāty eva satyaṃ satyaṃna saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
 iti 
yaś ca kuryād imaṃ nyāsaṃ lakṣmībījapuraḥsaram 
bhaktiṃ muktiṃ ca bhuktiṃ ca kṛṣṇaṃ ca labhate'cirāt  Hbhv 
tathā coktam
amum eva ramāpuraḥsaraṃ
prabhajed yo manujo vidhiṃ budhaḥ 
samupetya ramāṃ prathīyasīṃ
punar ante haritāṃ vrajaty asau  Hbhv 
atha tattvanyāsaḥ
makārādikakārāntavarṇair yuktaṃ sabindukaiḥ 
namaḥ parāyeti pūrvam ātmane nama ity anu  Hbhv 
nāma jīvāditattvānāṃ nyaset tattatpade kramāt 
nyāsenānena loko hi bhavet pūjādhikāravān  Hbhv 
tatrādau sakale nyasej jīvaprāṇau kalevare 
hṛdaye maty ahaṅkāramanāṃsīti trayaṃ tataḥ  Hbhv 
śabdaṃ sparśaṃ tato rūpaṃ rasaṃ gandhaṃ ca mastake 
mukhe hṛdi ca guhye ca pādayoś ca yathākramam  Hbhv 
śrotraṃ tvacaṃ dṛśaṃ jihvāṃ ghrāṇaṃ svasvapade tataḥ 
vākpāṇipāyūpasthāni svasvapade tathā  Hbhv 
ākāśavāyutejāṃsi jalaṃ pṛthvīṃ ca mūrdhani 
vadane hṛdaye liṅge pādayoś ca yathākramam  Hbhv 
hṛdi hṛtpuṇḍarīkaṃ ca dviṣaṭdvyaṣṭadaśādikam 
kalāvyāpteti pūrvaṃ ca sūryacandrāgnimaṇḍalam 
varṇaiḥ saha sarephaiś ca kramān nyaset sabindukaiḥ  Hbhv 
vāsudevaṃ ṣakāreṇa parameṣṭhiyutaṃ ca ke 
yakāreṇa mukhe saṅkarṣaṇaṃ nyaset pumanvitam  Hbhv 
hṛdi nyasel lakāreṇa pradyumnaṃ viśvasaṃyutam 
aniruddhaṃ nivṛttyāḍhyaṃ vakāreṇa ca guhyake 
nārāyaṇaṃ ca sarvāḍhyaṃ lakāreṇaiva pādayoḥ  Hbhv 
nṛsiṃhaṃ kopasaṃyuktaṃ tadbījenākhilātmani 
tattvanyāso 'yam acirāt kṛṣṇasānnidhyakārakaḥ  Hbhv 
tathā coktam
atattvavyāptyarūpasya tatprāpter hetunā punaḥ 
tattvanyāsam iti prāhur nyāsatattvavido budhāḥ  Hbhv 
yaḥ kuryāt tattvavinyāsaṃ sa pūto bhavati dhruvam 
tadātmanānupraviśya bhagavān iha tiṣṭhati 
yataḥ sa eva tattvāni sarvaṃ tasmin pratiṣṭhitam  Hbhv 
atha punaḥ prāṇāyāṃaviśeṣaḥ
prāṇāyāmāṃs tataḥ kuryān mūlamantraṃ japan kramāt 
vārau dvau caturaḥ ṣaṭ ca recapūrakakumbhakaḥ  Hbhv 
athavā recakādīṃs tān kuryād vārāṃs tu ṣoḍaśa 
dvātriṃśac ca catuḥṣaṣṭhiṃ kāmabījaṃ japan kramāt  Hbhv 
tathā ca kramadīpikāyām 
recayen mārutaṃ dakṣayā dakṣiṇaḥ
pūrayed vāmayā madhyanāḍyā punaḥ 
dhārayed īritaṃ recakāditrayaṃ syāt
kalādantavidyākhyamātrācyukam  Hbhv 
sanātanaḥ tad eva kramadīpikoktyā saṃvādayan tatraiva kiṃcid viśeṣaṃ ca darśayatirecayed iti 
dakṣayā dakṣiṇanāḍyā
dakṣiṇaḥ vidvān janaḥ 
madhyanāḍyā suṣumṇayā dhārayet 
evaṃ recakapūrakakumbhakākhyaṃ trayaṃ syāt 
recakādiṣu triṣu krameṇāvadhikālam āhakalāḥ ṣoḍaśa 
dantā dvātriṃśat 
vidyāś catuḥṣaṣṭhis tattatsaṅkhyakamātrātmakam ity arthaḥ 
mātrā cavāmāṅguṣṭhena vāmakaniṣṭhādyaṅgulīnāṃ pratyekaṃ parvatrayasamparkakālaḥ 
vāmahastena vāmajānumaṇḍalasya prādakṣiṇyena sparśakālo vā 
tatrāpy aṅguliniyamo 'py uktaḥ
kaniṣṭhānāmikāṅguṣṭhair yan nāsāpuṭadhāraṇam 
prāṇāyāmaḥ sa vijñeyas tarjanīmadhyame vinā 
 iti 
tatra teṣu prāṇāyāmeṣu purvaṃ recakādiṣu saṅkhyoktā 
atra ca prāṇāyāmeṣv iti bhedaḥ  HbhvC 
tatra kālaḥ saṅkhyādikaṃ ca
tatraiva 
purato japasya parato 'pi
vihitam atha tattrayaṃ budhaiḥ 
ṣoḍaśa ya iha samācared dineśaḥ
paripūyate sa khalu māsato 'ṃ haṃsaḥ  Hbhv 
sanātanaḥ japasya purata ādau parataḥ ante ca iti prāṇāyāmeṣu kālaḥ 
tat trayaṃ prāṇāyāmatrayam iti saṅkhyā 
yo jano dinaśaḥ pratyahaṃ ṣoḍaśaprāṇāyāmān ācaret
sa māsataḥ māsenaikena aṃhasaḥ pāpāt paripūyate śuddho bhavatīti sāmānyataḥ phalam 
paraṃ ca sarvaṃ purvaṃ likhitam eva  HbhvC 
atha pīṭhanyāsaḥ
tato nijatanūm eva pūjāpīṭhaṃ prakalpayet 
pīṭhasyādhāraśaktyādīn nyaset svāṅgeṣu tāravat  Hbhv 
ādhāraśaktiṃ prakṛtiṃ kūrmānantau ca tatra tu 
pṛthivīṃ kṣīrasindhuṃ ca śvetadvīpaṃ ca bhāsvaram  Hbhv 
śrīratnamaṇḍapaṃ caiva kalpavṛkṣaṃ tathā hṛdi 
nyaset pradakṣiṇatvena dharmajñāne tato 'ṃsayoḥ  Hbhv 
ūrvor vairāgyam aiśvaryaṃ tathaivādharmam ānane 
trike'jñānam avairāgyam anaiśvaryaṃ ca pārśvayoḥ  Hbhv 
hṛdabje'nantapadmaṃ ca sūryenduśikhinān tathā 
maṇḍalāni kramād varṇaiḥ praṇavāṃśaiḥ sabindukaiḥ  Hbhv 
sattva rajas tamaś cātmāntarātmānau ca tatra hi 
paramātmānam apy ātmādyādyavarṇaiḥ sabindukaiḥ  Hbhv 
jñānātmānaṃ ca bhuvaneśvarībījena saṃyutam 
tasyāṣṭadikṣu madhye'pi navaśaktīś ca dikkramāt  Hbhv 
tāś coktāḥ
vimalotkarṣiṇī jñānā kriyā yogeti śaktayaḥ 
prahvī satyā tatheśānānugrahā navam smṛtā  Hbhv 
 iti 
nyaset tadupariṣṭhāc ca pīṭhamantraṃ yathoditam 
ṛṣyādikaṃ smared asyāṣṭādaśārṇamanos tataḥ  Hbhv 
jñeyāś caikāntibhiḥ kṣīrasamudrādicatuṣṭayam 
kramāc chrīmathurāvṛndāvanaṃ tatkuñjanīpakāḥ  Hbhv 
tato pīṭhanyāsaḥ
tathā ca brahmasaṃhitāyām ādipuruṣarahasyastotre 
sa yatra kṣīrābdhiḥ sravati surabhībhyaś ca sumahān
nimeṣārdhākhyo vā vrajati na hi yatrāpi samayaḥ 
bhaje śvetadvīpaṃ tam aham iha golokam iti yaṃ
vidantas te santaḥ kṣitiviralacārāḥ katipaye  Hbhv 
kramadīpikāyāṃ 
evaṃ hṛdayaṃ bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarvānvitaś ca bhūtātmā 
ṅe'ntāḥ savāsudevāḥ sarvātmayutaṃ ca saṃyogaṃ  Hbhv 
yogāvadhaś ca padmaṃ pīṭhāt ṅeyuto natiś cānte 
pīṭhamahāmanur vyaktaḥ paryāpto 'yaṃ saparyāsu  Hbhv 
sanātanaḥ tāraḥ praṇavaḥ 
tato hṛdayaṃ nama iti padam 
tataś ca bhagavān iti viṣṇur iti ca 
sarvānvitaḥ sarvaśabdayukto bhūtātmā sarvabhūtātmeti 
ete trayaḥ savāsudevā vāsudevasahitāḥ pratyekaṃ ṅe'ntāś caturthyantāḥ 
tataś ca sarvātmanā yutaṃ saṃyogaṃ sarvātmasaṃyogam iti napuṃsakatvam ārṣam 
tataś ca yogasyāvadhau ante padmaṃ yogapadmam iti 
tadante ṅeyuktaś caturthyantaḥ pīṭhātmā 
tadante ca natiḥ namaḥśabdaḥ 
evaṃ oṃ namo bhagavate viṣṇave sarvabhūtātmane vāsudevāya sarvātmasaṃyogayogapadmapīṭhātmane nama iti siddham 
tathā ca śāradātilake
namo bhagavate brūyād viṣṇave ca padaṃ vadet 
sarvabhūtātmane vāsudevāyeti vadet tataḥ 
sarvātmasaṃyogapadād yogapadmapadaṃ punaḥ 
pīṭhātmane hṛdanto 'yaṃ mantras tārādir īritaḥ 
 iti 
sanatkumārakalpe ca
oṃ namaḥ padam ābhāṣya tathā bhagavatepadam 
vāsudevāya ity uktvā sarvātmeti padaṃ tathā 
saṃyogayogety uktvā ca tathā pīṭhātmane padam 
vahnipatnīsamāyuktaḥ pīṭhamantra itīritaḥ 
 iti  
atha ṛṣyādismaraṇam
oṃ aṣṭādaśākṣaramantrasya śrīnārada ṛṣir gāyatrīcchandaḥ
sakalalokamaṅgalo nandatanayo devatā
hrīṃ bījaṃ
svāhā śaktiḥ
kṛṣṇaḥ prakṛtir
durgādhiṣṭhātrī devatā
abhimatārthe viniyogaḥ  Hbhv 
tathā ca saṃmohanatantre śivomāsaṃvāde
ṛṣir nārada ity ukto gāyatrīcchanda ucyate 
gopaveśadharaḥ kṛṣṇo devatā parikīrtitaḥ  Hbhv 
bījaṃ manmathasaṃjñaṃ tu priyā śaktir havir bhujaḥ 
tvam eva parameśāni asyādhiṣṭhātṛdevatā 
caturvargaphalāvāptyai viniyogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  Hbhv 
athāṅganyāsaḥ
catuś caturbhir varṇaiś ca catvāry aṅgāni kalpayet 
dvābhyām astrākhyam aṅgaṃ ca tasyety aṅgāni pañca vai  Hbhv 
nyasyec ca vyāpakatvena tāny aṅgāni karadvaye 
tāny aṅgulīṣu pañcātha kecid varṇān svarān api  Hbhv 
te coktāḥ
drāvaṇakṣobhaṇākarṣavaśīkṛtsrāvaṇās tathā 
śoṣaṇo mohanaḥ sandīpanas tāpanamādanau  Hbhv 
 iti 
kiṃ ca
namo 'ntaṃ hṛdayaṃ cāṅgaiḥ śiraḥ svāhānvitaṃ śikhām 
vaṣaḍyutaṃ ca kavacaṃ huṃyugastraṃ ca phaḍyutam  Hbhv 
nyasyanti punar aṅguṣṭhau tarjanyau madhyame tathā 
anāmike kaniṣṭhe ca kramād aṅgaiś ca pañcabhiḥ  Hbhv 
punaś ca hṛdayādīni tathāṅguṣṭhādikāni ca 
nyasyanti yugapat sarvāṇy aṅgais taiḥ pañcabhiḥ kramāt  Hbhv 
nyasyanti ca ṣaḍaṅgāni hṛdayādīni tanmanoḥ 
hṛdayādiṣu caiteṣāṃ pañcaikaṃ dikṣu ca kramāt  Hbhv 
ṣaḍaṅgāni coktāni sammohanatantre sanatkumārakalpe
varrṇenaikena hṛdayaṃ tirbhir eva śiro matam 
caturbhiś ca śikhā proktā tathaiva kavacaṃ matam
