atha svadehe pīṭhapūjā
gurūn mūrdhni gaṇeśaṃ ca mūlādhāre'bhipūjya tam 
pīṭhanyāsānusāreṇa pīṭhaṃ cātmani pūjayet  Hbhv 
atha devāṅgeṣu mantrāṅgādinyāsaḥ
tato japan kāmabījaṃ tristhānasthaṃ paraṃ mahaḥ 
mūlamantrātmakaṃ bījenaikībhūtaṃ vicintayet  Hbhv 
tac ca pañcāṅganyāsena sākāraṃ sveṣṭadaivatam 
vicintya pañcāṅgādīni nyasyet tasmin yathātmani  Hbhv 
kuryur bhagavati prādurbhūte kṛṣṇe ca vaiṣṇavāḥ 
tattannyāsān abhedāya manor bhagavatā saha  Hbhv 
kecin nyasyanti tattvādīnn avyaktāni yathoditam 
mantrārṇaiḥ svarahaṃsādyair bhūṣaṇeṣu prabhoḥ kramāt  Hbhv 
atha bāhyopacārair antaḥpūjā
tasmin pīṭhe tam āsīnaṃ bhagavantaṃ vibhāvayan 
āsanādyais tu puṣpāntair yathāvidhy arcayed budhaḥ  Hbhv 
tato mukhe'rcayed veṇuṃ vanamālāṃ ca vakṣasi 
dakṣastanordhve śrīvatsaṃ savye tatraiva kaustubham  Hbhv 
vaiṣṇavaś candanenāmum ālipyopakaniṣṭhayā 
prāgvad dīpaśikhākāratilakāni dviṣaḍ likhet  Hbhv 
yathoktaṃ pañcabhiḥ puṣpāñjalibhiś cābhipūjya tam 
dhūpaṃ dīpaṃ ca naivedyaṃ mukhavāsādi cārpayet  Hbhv 
gītādibhiś ca santoṣya kṛṣṇam asmai tato 'khilam 
aśakto bahir arcāyām arpayej japam ācaret  Hbhv 
athāntaryāgamāhātmyam
vaiṣṇavatantre
aśvamedhasahasrāṇi vājapeyaśatāni ca 
ekasya dhyānayogasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye 
śrīvāmanaprādurbhāve
yannāmoccāraṇād eva sarve naśyanty upadravāḥ 
stotrair vā arhaṇābhir vā kim u dhyānena kathyate  Hbhv 
nāradapañcarātre śrībhagavannāradasaṃvāde
ayaṃ yo mānaso yāgo jarāvyādhibhayāpahaḥ 
sarvapāpaughaśamano bhāvābhāvakaro dvija 
satatābhyāsayogena dehabandhād vimocayet  Hbhv 
yaś caivaṃ parayā bhaktyā sakṛt kuryān mahāmate 
kramoditena vidhinā tasya tuṣyāmy ahaṃ mune  Hbhv 
smaraṇadhyānayoḥ pūrvaṃ māhātmyaṃ likhitaṃ ca yat 
jñeyaṃ tadadhikaṃ cātrāntaryāgāṅgatayā tayoḥ  Hbhv 
evaṃ yathāsampradāyaṃ śaktyā yāvanmanaḥsukham 
antaḥpūjāṃ vidhāyādāv ārabheta bahis tataḥ  Hbhv 
tathā coktaṃ nāradena
dhyātvā ṣoḍaśasaṅkhyātair upacāraiś ca mānasaiḥ 
samyag ārādhanaṃ kṛtvā bāhyapūjāṃ samācaret  Hbhv 
atha bahiḥpūjā
anujñāṃ dehi bhagavan bahir yoge mama prabho 
śrīkṛṣṇam ity anujñāpya bahiḥ pūjāṃ samācaret  Hbhv 
tatra tv anekaśaḥ santi pūjāsthānāni tatra ca 
śrīmūrtayo bahuvidhāḥ śālagrāmaśilās tathā  Hbhv 
atha pūjāsthānāni
saṃmohanatantre
śālagrāme manau yantre sthaṇḍile pratimādiṣu 
hareḥ pūjā tu kartavyā kevale bhūtale na tu  Hbhv 
ekādaśaskandhe BhP  śrīmaduddhavasaṃvāde
sūryo 'gnir brāhmaṇā gāvo vaiṣṇavaḥ khaṃ maruj jalam 
bhūr ātmā sarvabhūtāni bhadra pūjāpadāni me  Hbhv 
sūrye tu vidyayā trayyā haviṣāgnau yajeta mām 
ātithyena tu viprāgrye goṣv aṅga yavasādinā  Hbhv 
vaiṣṇave bandhusatkṛtyā hṛdi khe dhyānaniṣṭhayā 
vāyau mukhyadhiyā toye dravyais toyapuraḥsaraiḥ  Hbhv 
sthaṇḍile mantrahṛdayair bhogair ātmānam ātmani 
kṣetrajñaṃ sarvabhūteṣu samatvena yajeta mām  Hbhv 
dhiṣṇyeṣv ity eṣu madrūpaṃ śaṅkhacakragadāmbujaiḥ 
yuktaṃ caturbhujaṃ śāntaṃ dhyāyann arcet samāhitaḥ  Hbhv 
atha śrīmūrtayaḥ
tatraiva BhP 
śailī dārumayī lauhī lepyā lekhyā ca saikatī 
manomayī maṇimayī pratimāṣṭavidhā matā  Hbhv 
calācaleti dvividhā pratiṣṭhā jīvamandiram 
udvāsāvāhane na staḥ sthirāyām uddhavārcane  Hbhv 
asthirāyāṃ vikalpaḥ syāt sthaṇḍile tu bhaved dvayam 
snapanaṃ tv avilepyāyām anyatra parimārjanam  Hbhv 
gopālamantroddiṣṭatvāt tacchrīmūrtir apekṣitā 
tathāpi vaiṣṇavaprītyai lekhyāḥ śrīmūrtayo 'khilāḥ  Hbhv 
atha śrīmūrtilakṣaṇāni
śrīhayaśīrṣapañcarātre śrībhagavatśrīhayaśīrṣabrahmasaṃvāde
ādimūrtir vāsudevaḥ saṅkarṣaṇam athāsṛjat 
caturmūrtiḥ paraṃ proktaṃ ekaiko bhidyate tridhā 
keśavādiprabhedena mūrtidvādaśakaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv 
paṅkajaṃ dakṣiṇe dadyāt pāñcajanyaṃ tathopari 
vāmopari gadā yasya cakraṃ cādho vyavasthitam 
ādimūrtes tu bhedo 'yaṃ keśaveti parkīrtyate  Hbhv 
adharottarabhāvena kṛtam etat tu yatra vai 
nārāyaṇākhyā sā mūrtiḥ sthāpitā bhuktimuktidā  Hbhv 
savyādhaḥ paṅkajaṃ yasya pāñcajanyaṃ tathopari 
dakṣiṇordhve gadā yasya cakraṃ cādho vyavasthitam 
ādimūrtes tu bhedo 'yaṃ mādhaveti prakīrtyate  Hbhv 
dakṣiṇādhaḥsthitaṃ cakraṃ gadā yasyopari sthitā 
vāmordhvasaṃsthitaṃ padmaṃ śaṅkhaṃ cādho vyavasthitam 
saṅkarṣaṇasya bhedo 'yaṃ govindeti prakīrtyate  Hbhv 
dakṣiṇopari padmaṃ tu gadā cādho vyavasthitā 
saṅkarṣaṇasya bhedo 'yaṃ viṣṇur ity abhiśabdyate  Hbhv 
dakṣiṇopari śaṅkhaṃ ca cakraṃ cādhaḥ pradarśyate 
vāmopari tathā padmaṃ gadā cādhaḥ pradarśyate 
madhusūdananāmāyaṃ bhedaḥ saṅkarṣaṇasya ca  Hbhv 
vāmordhvasaṃsthitaṃ cakram adhaḥ śaṅkhaṃ pradarśyate 
brahmāṇḍagaṃ vāmapādaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ śeṣapṛṣṭhagam  Hbhv 
dakṣiṇordhvaṃ sahasrāraṃ pāñcajanyam adhaḥsthitam 
saptatālapramāṇena vāmanaṃ kārayet sadā  Hbhv 
ūrdhvaṃ dakṣiṇataś cakram adhaḥ padmaṃ vyavasthitam 
padmā padmakarā vāme pārśve yasya vyavasthitā  Hbhv 
sthito vāpy upaviṣṭo vā sānurāgo vilāsavān 
pradyumnasya hi bhedo 'yaṃ śrīdhareti prakīrtyate  Hbhv 
dakṣiṇordhvaṃ mahācakraṃ kaumudī tadadhaḥsthitā 
vāmordhve nalinaṃ yasya adhaḥ śaṅkhaṃ virājate 
hṛṣīkeśeti vijñeyaḥ sthāpitaḥ sarvakāmadaḥ  Hbhv 
dakṣiṇordhve puṇḍarīkaṃ pāñcajanyam adhas tathā 
vāmordhve saṃsthitaṃ cakraṃ kaumudī tadadhaḥsthitā 
padmanābheti sā mūrtiḥ sthāpitā mokṣadāyinī  Hbhv 
dakṣiṇordhve pāñcajanyam adhastāt tu kuśeśayam 
savordhve kaumudī caiva hetirājam adhaḥsthitam 
aniruddhasya bhedo 'yaṃ dāmodara iti smṛtaḥ  Hbhv 
eteṣāṃ tu striyau kārye padmavīṇādhare śubhe  Hbhv 
iti krameṇa mārgādhimāsādhipāḥ keśavādayo dvādaśa 
atha caturviṃśatimūrtayaḥ
siddhārthasaṃhitāyām
vāsudevo gadāśaṅkhacakrapadmadharo mataḥ 
padmaṃ śaṅkhaṃ tathā cakraṃ gadāṃ vahati keśavaḥ  Hbhv 
śaṅkhaṃ padmaṃ gadāṃ cakraṃ dhatte nārāyaṇaḥ sadā 
gadāṃ cakraṃ tathā śaṅkhaṃ padmaṃ vahati mādhavaḥ  Hbhv 
cakraṃ padmaṃ tathā śaṅkhaṃ gadāṃ ca puruṣottamaḥ 
padmaṃ kaumodakīṃ śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ dhatte'py adhokṣajaḥ  Hbhv 
saṅkarṣaṇo gadāśaṅkhapadmacakradharaḥ smṛtaḥ 
cakraṃ gadāṃ padmaśaṅkhau govindo dharate bhujaiḥ  Hbhv 
gadāṃ padmaṃ tathā śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ viṣṇur bibharti yaḥ 
cakraṃ śaṅkhaṃ tathā padmaṃ gadāṃ ca madhusūdanaḥ  Hbhv 
gadāṃ sarojaṃ cakraṃ ca śaṅkhaṃ dhatte'cyutaḥ sadā 
śaṅkhaṃ kaumodakīṃ cakram upendraḥ padmam udvahet  Hbhv 
cakraśaṅkhagadāpadmadharaḥ pradyumna ucyate 
padmaṃ kaumodakīṃ cakraṃ śaṅkhaṃ dhatte trivikramaḥ  Hbhv 
śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ gadāṃ padmaṃ vāmano vahate sadā 
padmaṃ cakraṃ gadāṃ śaṅkhaṃ śrīdharo vahate bhujaiḥ  Hbhv 
cakraṃ padmaṃ gadāṃ śaṅkhaṃ narasiṃho bibharti yaḥ 
padmaṃ sudarśanaṃ śaṅkhaṃ gadāṃ dhatte janārdanaḥ  Hbhv 
aniruddhaś cakragadāśaṅkhapadmalasadbhujaḥ 
hṛṣīkeśo gadāṃ cakraṃ padmaṃ śaṅkhaṃ ca dhārayet  Hbhv 
padmanābho vahet śaṅkhaṃ padmaṃ cakraṃ gadāṃ tathā 
padmaṃ cakraṃ gadāṃ śaṅkhaṃ dhatte dāmodaraḥ sadā  Hbhv 
śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ sarojaṃ ca gadāṃ vahati yo hariḥ 
śaṅkhaṃ kaumodakīṃ padmaṃ cakraṃ viṣṇur bibharti yaḥ  Hbhv 
etāś ca mūrtayo jñeyā dakṣiṇādhaḥkarakramāt  Hbhv 
matsyapurāṇe ca
etaduddeśataḥ proktaṃ pratimālakṣaṇaṃ tathā 
vistareṇa na śaknoti bṛhaspatir api dvijāḥ  Hbhv 
 iti 
sevāniṣṭhā hareḥ śrīmadvaiṣṇavāḥ pāñcarātrikāḥ 
prākaṭyād akhilāṅgānāṃ śrīmūrtiṃ bahu manyate  Hbhv 
sevyā nijanijair eva mantraiḥ svasveṣṭamūrtayaḥ 
śālagrāmātmake rūpe niyamo naiva vidyate  Hbhv 
dvibhujā jaladaśyāmā tribhaṅgī madhurākṛtiḥ 
sevyā dhyānānurūpaiś ca mūrtiḥ kṛṣṇasya daivataiḥ  Hbhv 
anyāś ca vividhā śrīmadavatārādimūrtayaḥ 
prādurbhāvavidhāv agre lekhyās tattadviśeṣataḥ  Hbhv 
nityakarmaprasaṅge'tra mūrtijanmapratiṣṭhayoḥ 
vidhir na likhituṃ yogyaḥ sa tu lekhiṣyate'grataḥ  Hbhv 
atha śālagrāmaśilāḥ
gautamīyatantre
gaṇḍakyāś caiva deśe ca śālagrāmasthalaṃ mahat 
pāṣāṇaṃ tadbhavaṃ yat tat śālagrāmam iti smṛtam  Hbhv 
skandapurāṇe
snigdhā kṛṣṇā pāṇḍarā vā pītā nīlā tathaiva ca 
vakrā rukṣā ca raktā ca mahāsthūlā tv alāñchitā  Hbhv 
kapilā dardurā bhagnā bahucakraikacakrikā 
bṛhanmukhī bṛhaccakrā lagnacakrāthavā punaḥ 
baddhacakrāthavā kācid bhagnacakrā tv adhomukhī  Hbhv 
atha tāsāṃ varṇādibhedena guṇadoṣau
tatraiva
snigdhā siddhikarī mantre kṛṣṇā kīrtiṃ dadāti ca 
pāṇḍarā pāpadahanī pītā putraphalapradā  Hbhv 
nīlā sandiśate lakṣmīṃ raktā rogapradāyikā 
rakṣā codvegadā nityaṃ vakrā dāridryadāyikā  Hbhv 
sthūlā nihati caivāyur niṣphalā tu alāñchitā 
kapilā karburā bhagnā bahucakraikacakrikā  Hbhv 
bṛhanmukhī bṛhaccakrā lagnacakrāthavā punaḥ  Hbhv 
baddhacakrāthavā yā syād bhagnacakrā tv adhomukhī 
pūjayed yaḥ pramādena duḥkham eva labheta saḥ  Hbhv 
agnipurāṇe ca
tathā vyālamukhī bhagnā viṣayā baddhacakrikā 
vikārāvartanābhiś ca nārasiṃhī tathaiva ca  Hbhv 
kapilā vibhramāvartā rekhāvartā ca yā śilā 
duḥkhadā sā tu vijñeyā sukhadā na kadācana  Hbhv 
snigdhā śyāmā tathā muktāmāyā vā samacakrikā 
ghoṇimūrtir anantākhyā gambhīrā sampuṭā tathā  Hbhv 
sūkṣmamūrtir amūrtiś ca sammukhā siddhidāyikā 
dhātrīphalapramāṇā yā kareṇobhayasampuṭā 
pūjanīyā prayatnena śilā caitādṛśī śubhā  Hbhv 
iṣṭā tu yasya yā mūrtiḥ sa tāṃ yatnena pūjayet 
pūjite phalam āpnoti ihaloke paratra ca  Hbhv 
doṣāś caite sakāmārcanaviṣayāḥ
yata uktaṃ śrībhagavatā brāhme
khaṇḍitaṃ sphuṭitaṃ bhagnaṃ pārśvabhinnaṃ vibheditam 
śālagrāmasamudbhūtaṃ śailaṃ doṣāvahaṃ na hi  Hbhv 
śrīrudreṇa ca skānde
khaṇḍitaṃ truṭitaṃ bhagnaṃ śālagrāme na doṣabhāk 
iṣṭā tu yasya yā mūrtiḥ sa tāṃ yatnena pūjayet  Hbhv 
tathā
cakraṃ vā kevalaṃ tatra padmena saha saṃyutam 
kevalā vanamālā vā harir lakṣmyā saha sthitaḥ  Hbhv 
mukhyāḥ snighdādayas tatrāmukhyā raktādayo matāḥ 
mukhyābhāve tv amukhyā hi pūjyā ity ucyate paraiḥ  Hbhv 
atha tāsām eva lakṣaṇaviśeṣeṇa saṃjñaviśeṣaḥ
brāhme śrībhagavadbrahmasaṃvāde
nivasāmi sadā brahman śālāgrāmākhyaveśmani 
tatraiva rathacakrāṅkabhedanāmāni me śṛṇu  Hbhv 
dvāradeśe same cakre dṛśyate nāntarīyake 
vāsudevaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ śuklābhaś cātiśobhanaḥ  Hbhv 
dve cakre ekalagne tu pūrvabhāgas tu puṣkalaḥ 
saṅkarṣaṇākhyo vijñeyo raktābhiś cātiśobhanaḥ  Hbhv 
pradyumnaḥ sūkṣmacakras tu pītadīptis tathaiva ca 
śuṣiraṃ chidrabahulaṃ dīrghākāraṃ tu tad bhavet  Hbhv 
aniruddhas tu nīlābho vartulaś cātiśobhanaḥ 
rekhātrayaṃ tu tad dvāri pṛṣṭhaṃ padmena lāñchitam  Hbhv 
saubhāgyaṃ keśavo dadyāt catuṣkoṇo bhavet tu yaḥ 
śyāmaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ vidyān nābhicakraṃ tathonnatam  Hbhv 
dīrgharekhāsamopetaṃ dakṣiṇe śuṣiraṃ pṛthu 
ūrdhvaṃ mukhaṃ vijānīyāt dvāre ca harirūpiṇam  Hbhv 
kāmadaṃ mokṣadaṃ caiva arthadaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ 
parameṣṭhī lohitabhaḥ padmacakrasamanvitaḥ  Hbhv 
bilvākṛtis tathā pṛṣṭhe śuṣiraṃ cātipuṣkalam 
kṛṣṇavarṇas tathā viṣṇuḥ sthūle cakre suśobhanaḥ 
bramacaryeṇa pūjyo 'sāv anyathā vighnado bhavet  Hbhv 
kvacic ca
kapilo narasiṃho 'tha pṛthucakre ca śobhane 
brahmacaryādhikārī syān nānyathā pūjanaṃ bhavet  Hbhv 
narasiṃhas tribinduḥ syāt kapilaḥ pañcabindukaḥ 
brahmacaryeṇa pūjyaḥ syād anyathā sarvavighnadaḥ  Hbhv 
sthūlaṃ cakradvayaṃ madhye guḍalākṣāsavarṇakam 
dvāropari tathā rekhā padmākārā suśobhanā  Hbhv 
sphuṭitaṃ viṣamaṃ cakraṃ nārasiṃhaṃ tu kāpilam 
sampūjya muktim āpnoti saṃgrāme vijayī bhavet  Hbhv 
pādme kārttikamāhātmye ca
yasya dīrghaṃ mukhaṃ pūrvakathitair lakṣaṇair yutam 
rekhāś ca keśarākārā nārasiṃho mato hi saḥ  Hbhv 
brāhme PadmaP 
vārāhaṃ śaktiliṅge ca cakre ca viṣame smṛte 
indranīlanibhaṃ sthūlaṃ trirekhālāñchitaṃ śubham  Hbhv 
pādme ca tatraiva
varāhākṛtir ābhugnaś cakrarekhāsv alaṅkṛtaḥ 
vārāha iti sa prokto bhuktimuktiphalapradaḥ  Hbhv 
brāhma eva
dīrghā kāñcanavarṇā yā bindutrayavibhūṣitā 
matsyākhyā sā śilā jñeyā bhuktimuktiphalapradā  Hbhv 
kvacic ca
matsyarūpaṃ tu deveśaṃ dīrghākāraṃ tu yad bhavet 
bindutrayam āyuktaṃ kāsyavarṇaṃ viśobhanam  Hbhv 
brāhma PadmaP  eva
kūrmas tathonnataḥ pṛṣṭhe vartulāvartapūritaḥ 
haritaṃ varṇam ādhatte kaustubhena ca cihnitaḥ  Hbhv 
pādme ca tatraiva
kūrmākārā ca cakrāṅkā śilā kūrmaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  Hbhv 
brāhma PadmaP  eva
hayagrīvo 'ṅkuśākāro rekhā cakraśamīpagāḥ 
bahucakrasamāyuktaṃ pṛṣṭhe nīradanīlakam  Hbhv 
kvacic ca
hayagrīvāṅkuśākāre rekhāḥ pañca bhavanti hi 
bahubindusamākīrṇe dṛśyante nīlarūpakāḥ  Hbhv 
pādme ca tatraiva
hāyagrīvā yathā lambā rekhāṅkā yā śilā bhavet 
tathāsau syād dhayagrīvaḥ pūjito jñānado bhavet  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
aśvākṛti mukhaṃ yasya sākṣamālaṃ śiras tathā 
padmākṛtir bhaved vāpi hayaśīrṣas tv asau mataḥ  Hbhv 
brāhme PadmaP  eva
vaikuṇṭham maṇivarṇābhaṃ cakram ekaṃ tathā dhvajam 
dvāropari tathā rekhā padmākārā suśobhanā  Hbhv 
śrīdharas tu tathā devaś cihnito vanamālayā 
kadambakusumākāro rekhāpañcakabhūṣitaḥ  Hbhv 
vartulaś cātihrasvaś ca vāmanaḥ parikīrtitaḥ 
atasīkusumaprakhyo bindunā pariśobhitaḥ  Hbhv 
anyatra ca
vāmanākhyo bhaved devo hrasvo yaḥ syān mahādyutiḥ 
ūrdhvacakras tv adhaś cakraḥ so 'bhīṣṭārthaprado 'rcitaḥ  Hbhv 
brāhme PadmaP  eva
sudarśanas tathā devaḥ śyāmavarṇo mahādyutiḥ 
vāmapārśve gadācakre rekhe caiva tu dakṣiṇe  Hbhv 
pādme kārttikamāhātmye
cakrākāreṇa paṅktiḥ sā yatra rekhāmayī bhavet 
sa sudarśana ity evaṃ khyātaḥ pūjāphalapradaḥ  Hbhv 
brāhme PadmaP 
dāmodaras tathā sthūlo madhye cakraṃ pratiṣṭhitam 
dūrvābhaṃ dvārasaṅkīrṇaṃ pītā rekhā tathaiva ca  Hbhv 
pādme ca tatraiva
uparyadhaś ca cakre dve nātidīrghaṃ mukhe bilam 
cakre ca rekhā lambaikā sa ca dāmodaraḥ smṛtaḥ  Hbhv 
anyatra ca
sthūlo dāmodaro jñeyaḥ sūkṣmarandhro bhavet tu yaḥ 
cakre ca madhyadeśasthe pūjitaḥ sukhadaḥ sadā  Hbhv 
nānāvarṇo hy anantākhyo nāgabhogena cihnitaḥ 
anantaḥ sa tu vijñeyaḥ sarvapūjāphalapradaḥ  Hbhv 
pādme ca tatraiva
anantacakro bahubhiś cihnair apy upalakṣitaḥ 
anantaḥ sa tu vijñeyaḥ sarvapūjāphalapradaḥ  Hbhv 
PadmaP 
dṛśyate śikhare liṅgaṃ śālagrāmasamudbhavam 
yasya yogeśvaro nāma brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati  Hbhv 
āraktaḥ padmanābhākhyaṃ paṅkajacchatrasaṃyutam 
tulasyā pūjayen nityaṃ daridras tv īśvaro bhavet  Hbhv 
candrākṛtiṃ hiraṇyākhyaṃ raśmijālaṃ vinirdiśet 
suvarṇarekhābahulaṃ sphaṭikadyutiśobhitam  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
ardhacandrākṛtir devo hṛṣīkeśa udāhṛtaḥ 
tam arcya labhate svargaṃ viṣayāṃś ca samīhitām  Hbhv 
vāmapārśve same cakre kṛṣṇavarṇaḥ sa bindukaḥ 
lakṣmīnṛsiṃho vikhyāto bhuktimuktiphalapradaḥ  Hbhv 
trivikramas tathā devaḥ śyāmavarṇo mahādyutiḥ 
vāmapārśve tathā cakre rekhā caiva tu dakṣiṇe  Hbhv 
pradakṣiṇāvartakṛtavanamālāvibhūṣitā 
yā śilā kṛṣṇasaṃjñā sā dhanadhānyasukhapradā  Hbhv 
gautamīye
bahubhir janmabhiḥ puṇyair yadi kṛṣṇaśilāṃ labhet 
goṣpadena tu cihnena janus tena samāpyate  Hbhv 
catasro yatra dṛśyante rekhāḥ pārśvasamīpagāḥ 
dve cakre madhyadeśe tu sā śilā tu caturmukhā  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca pādme tatraiva
vajrakīṭodbhavā rekhāḥ paṅktībhūtāś ca yatra vai 
śālagrāmaśilā yā sā viṣṇupañjarasaṃjñitā  Hbhv 
nāgavat kuṇḍalībhūtarekhāpaṅktiḥ sa śeṣakaḥ 
padmākāre ca paṅktī dve madhye lambā ca rekhikā 
garuḍaḥ sa tu vijñeyaś catuś cakro janārdanaḥ  Hbhv 
catuś cakraḥ sūkṣmadvāro vanamālāṅkitodaraḥ 
lakṣmīnārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān bhuktimuktiphalapradaḥ  Hbhv 
etal lakṣaṇayuktās tu śālagrāmaśilāḥ śubhāḥ 
yāś ca tāsv api sūkṣmāḥ syus tāḥ praśastakarāḥ smṛtāḥ  Hbhv 
tathā ca śrībhagavadbrahmasaṃvāde tatraiva
yathā yathā śilā sūkṣmā mahat puṇyaṃ tathā tathā 
tasmāt tāṃ pūjayen nityaṃ dharmakāmārthasiddhaye  Hbhv 
tatrāpy āmalakītulyā sūkṣmā cātīva yā bhavet 
tasyām eva sadā brahman śriyā saha vasāmy aham  Hbhv 
atha śrīśālagrāmaśilāmāhātmyam
śālagrāmaśilāsparśāt koṭijanmāghanāśanam 
kiṃ punar yajanaṃ tatra harisānnidhyakārakam  Hbhv 
pādme māghamāhātmye tatraiva
yaḥ pūjayed dhariṃ cakre śālagrāmaśilodbhave 
rājasūyasahasreṇa teneṣṭaṃ prativāsaram  Hbhv 
yad āmananti vedāntā brahma nirguṇam acyutam 
tatprasādo bhaven nṛṇāṃ śālagrāmaśilārcanāt  Hbhv 
mahākāṣṭhasthito vahnir mathyamānaḥ prakāśate 
yathā tathā harir vyāpī śālagrāme prakāśate  Hbhv 
api pāpasamācārāḥ karmaṇy anadhikāriṇaḥ 
śālagrāmārcakā vaiśya naiva yānti yamālayam  Hbhv 
na tathā ramate lakṣmyāṃ na tathā nijamandire 
śālagrāmśilācakre yathā sa ramate sadā  Hbhv 
agnihotraṃ hutaṃ tena dattā pṛthvī sasāgarā 
yenārcito hariś cakre śālagrāmaśilodbhave  Hbhv 
kāmaiḥ krodhaiḥ pralobhaiś ca vyāpto yo 'tra narādhamaḥ 
so 'pi yāti harer lokaṃ śālagrāmaśilārcanāt  Hbhv 
yaḥ pūjayati govindaṃ śālagrāme sadā naraḥ 
āhūtasamplavaṃ yāvat na sa pracyavate divaḥ  Hbhv 
vinā tīrthair vinā dānair vinā yajñair vinā matim 
muktiṃ yāti naro vaiśya śālagrāmaśilārcanāt  Hbhv 
narakaṃ garbhavāsaṃ ca tiryaktvaṃ kṛmiyonitām 
na yāti vaiśya pāpo 'pi śālagrāme'cyutārcakaḥ  Hbhv 
dīkṣāvidhānamantrajñaś cakre yo balim āharet 
sa yāti vaiṣṇavaṃ dhāma satyaṃ satyaṃ mayoditam  Hbhv 
naivedyair vividhaiḥ puṣpair dhūpair dīpair vilepanaiḥ 
gītavāditrastotrādyaiḥ śālagrāmaśilārcanam  Hbhv 
kurute mānavo yas tu kalau bhaktiparāyaṇaḥ 
kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi ramate sannidhau hareḥ  Hbhv 
liṅgais tu koṭibhir dṛṣṭair yat phalaṃ pūjitais tu taiḥ 
śālagrāmaśilāyāṃ tu ekenāpīha tat phalam  Hbhv 
śālagrāmaśilārūpī yatra tiṣṭhati keśavaḥ 
tatra devāsurā yakṣā bhuvanāni caturdaśa  Hbhv 
śālagrāmaśilāyāṃ tu yaḥ śrāddhaṃ kurute naraḥ 
pitaras tasya tiṣṭhanti tṛptāḥ kalpaśataṃ divi  Hbhv 
śālagrāmaśilā yatra tattīrthaṃ yojanatrayam 
yatra dānaṃ japo homaḥ sarvaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ bhavet  Hbhv 
śālagrāmasamīpe tu krośamātraṃ samantataḥ 
kīkaṭo 'pi mṛto yāti vaikuṇṭhabhavanaṃ nara  Hbhv 
śālagrāmaśilācakraṃ yo dadyād dānam uttamam 
bhūcakraṃ tena dattaṃ syāt saśailavanakānanam  Hbhv 
skānde kārttikamāhātmye padma  śrīśivaskandasaṃvāde
śālagrāmaśilāyāṃ tu trailokyaṃ sacarācaram 
mayā saha mahāsena līnaṃ tiṣṭhati sarvadā  Hbhv 
dṛṣā praṇamitā yena snāpitā pūjitā tathā 
yajñakoṭisamaṃ puṇyaṃ gavāṃ koṭiphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
kāmāsakto 'pi yo nityaṃ bhaktibhāvavivarjitaḥ 
śālagrāmaśilāṃ vipra sampūjyaivācyuto bhavet  Hbhv 
śālagrāmaśilābimbaṃ hatyākoṭivināśanam 
smṛtaṃ saṅkīrtitaṃ dhyātaṃ pūjitaṃ ca namaskṛtam  Hbhv 
śālagrāmaśilāṃ dṛṣṭvā yānti pāpāny anekaśaḥ 
siṃhaṃ dṛṣṭvā yathā yānti vane mṛgagaṇā bhayāt  Hbhv 
namaskaroti manujaḥ śālagrāmaśilārcane 
pāpāni vilayaṃ yānti tamaḥ sūryodaye yathā  Hbhv 
kāmāsakto 'thavā kruddhaḥ śālagrāmaśilārcanam 
bhaktyā vā yadi vā'bhaktyā kṛtvā muktim avāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
vaivasvataṃ bhayaṃ nāsti tathā maraṇajanmanoḥ 
yaḥ kathāṃ kurute viṣṇoḥ śālagrāmaśilāgrataḥ  Hbhv 
gītair vādyais tathā stotraiḥ śālagrāmaśilārcanam 
kurute mānavo yas tu kalau bhaktiparāyaṇaḥ 
kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi ramate viṣṇusadmani  Hbhv 
śālagrāmanamaskāre'bhāvenāpi naraiḥ kṛte 
bhayaṃ naiva kariṣyanti madbhaktā ye narā bhuvi  Hbhv 
madbhaktibaladarpiṣṭhā matprabhuṃ na namanti ye 
vāsudevaṃ na te jñeyā madbhaktāḥ pāpino hi te  Hbhv 
śālagrāmaśilāyāṃ tu sadā putra vasāmy aham 
dattaṃ devena tuṣṭena svasthānaṃ mama bhaktitaḥ  Hbhv 
padmakoṭisahasrais tu pūjite mayi yat phalam 
tat phalaṃ koṭiguṇitaṃ śālagrāmaśilārcane  Hbhv 
pūjito haṃ na tair martyair namito 'haṃ na tair naraiḥ 
na kṛtaṃ martyaloke yaiḥ śālagrāmaśilārcanam  Hbhv 
śālagrāmaśilāgre tu yaḥ karoti mamārcanam 
tenārcito 'haṃ satataṃ yugānām ekaviṃśatim  Hbhv 
kim arcitair liṅgaśatair viṣṇubhaktivivarjitaiḥ 
śālagrāmaśilābimbaṃ nārcitaṃ yadi putraka  Hbhv 
anarhaṃ mama naivedyaṃ patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ jalam 
śālagrāmaśilālagnaṃ sarvaṃ yāti pavitratām  Hbhv 
yo hi māheśvaro bhūtvā vaiṣṇavaliṅgam uttamam 
dveṣṭi vai yāti narakaṃ yāvad indrāś caturdaśa  Hbhv 
sakṛd apy arcite bimbe śālagrāmaśilodbhave 
muktiṃ prayānti manujā nūnaṃ sāṅkhyena varjitāḥ  Hbhv 
malliṅgaiḥ koṭibhir dṛṣṭair yat phalaṃ pūjitais tu taiḥ 
śālagrāmaśilāyāṃ tu ekenāpi hi tad bhavet  Hbhv 
tasmād bhaktyā ca madbhaktaiḥ prītyarthe mama putraka 
kartavyaṃ satataṃ bhaktyā śālagrāmaśilārcanam  Hbhv 
śālagrāmaśilārūpī yatra tiṣṭhati keśavaḥ 
tatra devāsurā yakṣā bhuvanāni caturdaśa  Hbhv 
śālagrāmaśilāgre tu sakṛt piṇḍena tarpitāḥ 
vasanti pitaras tasya na saṅkhyā tatra vidyate  Hbhv 
pramāṇam asti sarvasya sukṛtasya hi putraka 
phalaṃ pramāṇahīnaṃ tu śālagrāmaśilārcane  Hbhv 
yo dadāti śilāṃ viṣṇoḥ śālagrāmasamudbhavām 
viprāya viṣṇubhaktāya teneṣṭaṃ bahubhiḥ makhaiḥ  Hbhv 
atraprabhṛti ślokā ākare na dṛśyante
mānuṣye durlabhā loke śālagrāmodbhavā śilā 
prāpyate na vinā puṇyaiḥ kalikāle viśeṣataḥ  Hbhv 
sa dhanyaḥ puruṣo loke saphalaṃ tasya jīvitam 
śālagrāmaśilā śuddhā gṛhe yasya ca pūjitā  Hbhv 
saṃniyamyendriyagrāmaṃ śālagrāmaśilārcanam 
yaḥ kuryān mānavo bhaktyā puṣpe puṣpe'śvamedhabhāk  Hbhv 
kāle vā yadi vākāle śālagrāmaśilārcanam 
bhaktyā vā yadi vābhaktyā yaḥ karoti sa puṇyabhāk  Hbhv 
dveṣeṇāpi ca lobhena dambhena kapaṭena vā 
śālagrāmodbhavaṃ devaṃ dṛṣṭvā pāpāt pramucyate  Hbhv 
aśucir vā durācāraḥ satyaśaucavivarjitaḥ 
śālagrāmaśilāṃ spṛṣṭvā sadya eva śucir bhavet  Hbhv 
tilaprasthaśataṃ bhaktyā yo dadāti dine dine 
tat phalaṃ samavāpnoti śālagrāmaśilārcane  Hbhv 
patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ mūlaṃ toyaṃ dūrvākṣataṃ suta 
jāyate meruṇā tulyaṃ śālagrāmaśilārpitam  Hbhv 
vidhihīno 'pi yaḥ kuryāt kriyāmantravivarjitaḥ 
cakrapūjām avāpnoti samyak śāstroditaṃ phalam  Hbhv 
tatraiva cānyatra
skandhe kṛtvā tu yo 'dhvānaṃ vahate śailanāyakam 
tenoḍhaṃ tu bhavet sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram  Hbhv 
brahmahatyādikaṃ pāpaṃ yat kiñcit kurute naraḥ 
tat sarvaṃ nirdahaty āśu śālagrāmaśilārcanam  Hbhv 
na pūjanaṃ na mantrāś ca na japo na ca bhāvanā 
na stutir nopacāraś ca śālagrāmaśilārcane  Hbhv 
śālagrāmaśilā yatra tat tīrthaṃ yojanatrayam 
tatra dānaṃ ca homaś ca sarvaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ bhavet  Hbhv 
śālagrāmaśilāyāṃ tu yaḥ śrāddhaṃ kurute naraḥ 
pitaras tasya tiṣṭhanti tṛptāḥ kalpaśataṃ divi  Hbhv 
śālagrāmasamīpe tu krośamātraṃ samantataḥ 
kīkaṭo 'pi mṛto yāti vaikuṇṭhabhuvanaṃ naraḥ  Hbhv 
pādme ca
śālagrāmaśilācakraṃ yo dadyād dānam uttamam 
bhūcakraṃ tena dattaṃ syāt saśailavanakānanam  Hbhv 
garuḍapurāṇe
tiṣṭhanti nityaṃ pitaro manuṣyās
tīrthāni gaṅgādikapuṣkarāṇi 
yajñāś ca medhā hy api puṇyaśailāś
cakrāṅkitā yasya vasanti gehe  Hbhv 
pādme kārttikamāhātmye śrīyamadhūmrakeśasaṃvāde
śālagrāmaśilāyāṃ tu yair naraiḥ pūjito hariḥ 
saṃśodhya teṣāṃ pāpāni muktaye buddhito bhavet  Hbhv 
kārttike mathurāyāṃ tu sārūpyaṃ diśate hariḥ 
śālagrāmaśilāyāṃ vai pitṝṇ uddiśya pūjitaḥ 
kṛṣṇaḥ samuddharet tasya pitṝn etān svalokatām  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye  ca yajñadhvajopākhyānānte
śālagrāmaśilārūpī yatra tiṣṭhati keśavaḥ 
na bādhante'surās tatra bhūtavetālakādayaḥ  Hbhv 
śālagrāmaśilā yatra tattīrthaṃ tat tapovanam 
yataḥ sannihitas tatra bhagavān madhusūdanaḥ  Hbhv 
śālagrāmaśilās tāś ca yadi dvādaśa pūjitāḥ 
śataṃ vā pūjitaṃ bhaktyā tadā syād adhikaṃ phalam  Hbhv 
atha bāhulye tāsāṃ phalaviśeṣaḥ
pādme māghamāhātmye  devadūtavikuṇḍalasaṃvāde
śilā dvādaśa bho vaiśya śālagrāmaśilodbhavāḥ 
vidhivat pūjitā yena tasya puṇyaṃ vadāmi te  Hbhv 
koṭidvādaśaliṅgais tu pūjitaiḥ svarṇapaṅkajaiḥ 
yat syād dvādaśakāleṣu dinenaikena tad bhavet  Hbhv 
yaḥ punaḥ pūjayed bhaktyā śālagrāmaśilāśatam 
uṣitvā sa harer loke cakravartīha jāyate  Hbhv 
skānde kārttikamāhātmye padma  śrīśivaskandasaṃvāde
dvādaśaiva śilā yo vai śālagrāmasamudbhavāḥ 
arcayed vaiṣṇavo nityaṃ tasya puṇyaṃ nibodha me  Hbhv 
koṭiliṅgasahasrais tu pūjitair jāhnavītaṭe 
kāśīvāse yugāny aṣṭau dinenaikena tad bhavet  Hbhv 
kiṃ punar bahunā yas tu pujayed vaiṣṇavo naraḥ 
na hi brahmādayo devāḥ saṃkhyāṃ kurvanti puṇyataḥ  Hbhv 
atha tatkrayavikrayaniṣedhaḥ
tatraiva padma 
śālagrāmaśilāyāṃ yo mūlyam udghātayen naraḥ 
vikretā cānumantā ca yaḥ parīkṣām udīrayet  Hbhv 
sarve te narakaṃ yānti yāvad āhūtasamplavam 
ataḥ saṃvarjayed vipra cakrasya krayavikrayam  Hbhv 
atha pratiṣṭhā niṣedhaḥ
tatraiva
śālagrāmaśilāyāṃ tu pratiṣṭhā naiva vidyate 
mahāpūjāṃ tu kṛtvādau pūjayet tāṃ tato budhaḥ  Hbhv 
 iti 
ato 'dhiṣṭhānavargeṣu sūryādiṣv iva mūrtiṣu 
śālagrāmaśilaiva syād adhiṣṭhānottamaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv 
atha sarvādhiṣṭhānaśraiṣṭhyam
pādme  tatraiva
hṛdi sūrye jale vātha pratimāsthaṇḍileṣu ca 
samabhyarcya hariṃ yānti narās te vaiṣṇavaṃ padam  Hbhv 
athavā sarvadā pūjyo vāsudevo mumukṣubhiḥ 
śālagrāmeśilācakre vajrakīṭavinirmite  Hbhv 
adhiṣṭhānaṃ hi tad viṣṇoḥ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam 
sarvapuṇyapradaṃ vaiśya sarveṣām api muktidam  Hbhv 
tatraiva kārttikamāhātmye yamadhūmrakeśasaṃvāde
pūjā ca vihitā tasya pratimāyāṃ nṛpātmaja 
śailī dārumayī lauhī lepyā lekhyā ca saikatā 
manomayī maṇimayī śrīmūrtir aṣṭadhā smṛtā  Hbhv 
śālagrāmaśilāyāṃ tu sākṣāt śrīkṛṣṇasevanam 
nityaṃ saṃnihitas tatra vāsudevo jagadguruḥ  Hbhv 
skānde kārttikamāhātmye śrīśivaskandasaṃvāde
suvarṇārcā na ratnārcā na śilārcā surottama 
śālagrāmaśilāyāṃ tu sarvadā vasate hariḥ  Hbhv 
ata evoktam
hatyāṃ hanti yadaṅghrisaṅgatulasī steyaṃ ca toyaṃ pade
naivedyaṃ bahumadyapānaduritaṃ gurvaṅganāsaṅgajam 
śrīśādhīnamatiḥ sthitir harijanais tatsaṅgajaṃ kilbiṣaṃ
śālagrāmaśilānṛsiṃhamahimā ko 'py eṣa lokottaraḥ  Hbhv 
śālagrāmaśilārūpabhagavanmahimāmbudheḥ 
ūrmīn gaṇayituṃ śakyaḥ śrīcaitanyāśrito 'pi kaḥ  Hbhv 
atha śālagrāmaśilāpūjānityatā
pādme
śālagrāmaśilāpūjā vinā yo 'śnāti kiñcana 
sa caṇḍālādiviṣṭhāyām ākalpaṃ jāyate kṛmiḥ  Hbhv 
skānde ca
gauravācalaśṛṅgāgrair bhidyate yasya vai tanuḥ 
na matir jāyate yasya śālagrāmaśilārcane  Hbhv 
 iti 
evaṃ śrībhagavān sarvaiḥ śālagrāmaśilātmakaḥ 
dvijaiḥ strībhiś ca śūdraiś ca pūjyo bhagavataḥ paraiḥ  Hbhv 
tathā skānde śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde cāturmāsyavrate śālagrāmaśilārcāprasaṅge
brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ sacchūdrāṇām athāpi vā 
śālagrāme'dhikāro 'sti na cānyeṣāṃ kadācana  Hbhv 
tatraivānyatra
striyo vā yadi vā śūdrā brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyādayaḥ 
pūjayitvā śilācakraṃ labhante śāśvataṃ padam  Hbhv 
 iti 
ato niṣedhakaṃ yad yad vacanaṃ śrūyate sphuṭam 
avaiṣṇavaparaṃ tat tad vijñeyaṃ tattvadarśibhiḥ  Hbhv 
yathā
brāhmaṇasyaiva pūjyo 'haṃ śucer apy aśucer api 
strīśūdrakarasaṃsparśo vajrād api suduḥsahaḥ  Hbhv 
praṇavoccāraṇārcaiva śālagrāmaśilārcanāt 
brāhmaṇīgamanāc caiva śūdraś caṇḍālatām iyāt  Hbhv 
sanātanaḥ tad eva śrīnāradoktyā pramāṇayatibrāhmaṇeti 
satāṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ śūdrāṇāṃ
śālagrāme śrīśālagrāmaśilārcane
anyeṣām asatāṃ śūdrāṇām 
ataeva śūdram adhikṛtyoktaṃ vāyupurāṇe
ayācakaḥ pradātā syāt kṛṣiṃ vṛttyartham ācaret 
purāṇaṃ śṛṇuyān nityaṃ śālagrāmaṃ ca pūjayet 
 iti 
 evaṃ mahāpurāṇānāṃ vacanaiḥ sahabrāhmaṇasyaiva pūjyo 'ham iti vacanasya virodhān mātsaryaparaiḥ smārtaiḥ kaiścit kalpitam iti mantavyam 
yadi ca yuktyā siddhaṃ samūlaṃ syāt tarhi cāvaiṣṇaviḥ śūdrais tādṛśībhiś ca strībhis tatpūjā na kartavyā
yathāvidhi gṛhītaviṣṇudīkṣākaiś ca taiḥ kartvyeti vyavasthāpanīyam 
yataḥ śūdreṣv antyajeṣv api madhye ye vaiṣṇavās te śūdrādayo na kilocyante 
tathā ca nāradīye
śvapaco 'pi mahīpāla viṣṇor bhakto dvijodhikaḥ iti 
itihāsasamuccaye
na śūdrā bhagavadbhaktaṃ niṣādaṃ śvapacaṃ tathā 
vīkṣate jātisāmānyāt sa yāti narakaṃ dhruvam 
 iti 
pādme ca
na śūdrā bhagavadbhaktās te tu bhāgavatā narāḥ 
sarvavarṇeṣu te śūdrā ye na bhaktā janārdane 
 iti 
etadādikaṃ cāgre vaiṣṇavamāhātmye vistareṇa vyaktaṃ bhāvi 
kiṃ ca bhagavaddīkṣāprabhāvena śūdrādīnām api viprasāmyaṃ siddham eva 
tathā ca tatrayathā kāñcanatāṃ yāti ity ādi 
etac ca prāgdīkṣāmāhātmye likhitam eva 
ata eva tṛtīyaskandhe devahūtivākyam BhP 
yannāmadheyaśravaṇānukīrtanād
yatprahvaṇād yatsmaraṇād api kvacit 
śvādo 'pi sadyaḥ savanāya kalpate
kutaḥ punas te bhagavan nu darśanāt 
 iti 
savanāya yajanāya kalpate yogyo bhavatīty arthaḥ 
ata eva vipraiḥ saha vaiṣṇavānām ekatraiva gaṇanā 
tathā ca haribhaktisudhodaye śrībhagavadbrahmasaṃvāde
tīrthāny aśvatthataravo gāvo viprās tathā svayam 
madbhaktāś ceti vijñeyāḥ pañca te tanavo mama 
 iti 
caturthaskandhe BhP  śrīpṛthumahārājavarṇane
sarvatrāskhalitādeśaḥ saptadvīpaikadaṇḍadhṛk 
anyatra brāhmaṇakulād anyatrācyutagotrataḥ 
 iti 
īmahārājasyoktau BhP 
mā jātu tejaḥ prabhaven maharddhibhis
titikṣayā tapasā vidyayā ca 
dedīpyamāne ñjitadevatānāṃ
kule svayaṃ rājakulād dvijānām 
 iti 
 atra śrīsvāmipādānāṃ ṭīkāmahatyaś ca tā ṛddhayaś ca tābhir yadrājakulasya tejas tat tasmāt sakāśād dvijānāṃ viprāṇāṃ kule ajito devatāpūjyo  
yeṣāṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ 
teṣāṃ kule mā jātu prabhavet 
kadācid api prabhavaṃ na karotu 
kathambhūte 
samṛddhibhir vināpi svayam eva titikṣādibhir dedīpyamāna iti 
purañjanoktau BhP  ca
tasmin dadhe damam ahaṃ tava vīrapatni
yo 'nyatra bhūsurakulāt kṛtakilbiṣas tam 
paśye na vītabhayam unmuditaṃ trilokyām
anyatra vai muraripor itaratra dāsāt 
 iti 
tatrāpi saiva ṭīkāhe vīrapatni 
yas te kṛtāparādhaḥ 
tasminn ahaṃ brāhmaṇakulād anyatra anyasmin muraripudāsād itaratra ca damaṃ dadhe
daṇḍaṃ karomīty adi 
īdṛśāni ca vacanāni śrībhāgavatādau bahūny eva santi 
itthaṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ brāhmaṇaiḥ saha sāmyam eva sidhyati 
 kiṃ caviprād dviṣaḍguṇayutāt BhP  ity ādivacanair vaiṣṇavabrāhmaṇebhyo nīcajātijātānām api vaiṣṇavānāṃ śraiṣṭhyaṃ nirdiśyatetarām 
ata evoktaṃ śrībhagavatā śrīhayagrīveṇa śrīhayaśīrṣapañcarātre śrīpuruṣottamapratiṣṭhānte
mūrtipānāṃ tu dātavyā deśikārdhena dakṣiṇā 
tadardhaṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ tu tadardhaṃ taddvijanmanām 
 iti 
ato yuktam eva likhita sarvair bhagavataḥ paraiḥ pūjya iti 
tathā ca brahmavaivarte priyavratopākhyāne dharmavyādhasyāpi śrīśālagrāmaśilāpūjanam uktam
tataḥ sa vismitaḥ śrutvā dharmavyādhasya tadvacaḥ 
tasthau sa ca samānīya darśayāmāsa tav ubhau 
niniktavasanau vṛddhāvāsanasthau nijau gurū 
śālagrāmaśilāṃ caiva tatsamīpe supūjitam 
 iti 
atrācāraś casatāṃ madhyadeśe'smin viśeṣato dakṣiṇadeśe ca mahattamānāṃ śrīvaiṣṇavānāṃ pramāṇam iti dik 
evaṃ śrībhāgavatapāṭhaādāv apy adhikāro vaiṣṇavānāṃ draṣṭavyaḥ 
yato vidhiniṣedhā bhagavadbhaktānāṃ na bhavantīti devarṣibhūtāptanṝṇāṃ pitṝṇām BhP  ity ādivacanaiḥ 
tathā karmaparityāgādināpi na kaścid doṣo ghaṭata iti tāvat karmāṇi kurvīta BhP  iti
yadā yasyānugṛhṇāti bhagavān BhP  ity ādi vacanaiś ca vyaktaṃ bodhitam evāsti 
etat sarvam agre śrīvaiṣṇavamāhātmye vistareṇa vyaktaṃ bhāvi  HbhvC 
śvādatvam atra śvabhakṣakajātiviśeṣatvam eva śvānam attīti nirukter vartamānaprayogāt kravyādavat tacchīlatvaprāpteḥ 
kādācitkabhakṣaṇaprāyaścittavivakṣāyāṃ tv atītaḥ prayogaḥ kriyeta 
rūḍhir yogam apaharatīti nyāyena ca tad virudhyate 
ataeva śvapaca iti tair vyākhyātam 
savanaṃ cātra somayāga ucyate 
tataś cāsya bhagavannāmaśravaṇādyekatarāt sadya eva savanayogyatāpratikūladurjātitvaprārambhakaprārabdhapāpanāśaḥ pratipadyate 
 uddhavaṃ prati bhagavatā ca  tasmāt bhaktiḥ punāti manniṣṭhā śvapākān api sambhavāt BhP  iti kaimutyārtham eva proktam ity āyāti 
kintu yogyatvam atra śvapacatvaprāpakaprārabdhapāpavicchinnatvamātram ucyate 
savanārthaṃ tu guṇāntarādhānam apekṣata eva 
brāhmaṇakumārāṇāṃ śaukre janmani yogyatve saty api sāvitradaiksyajanmāpekṣāvat 
sāvitrādijanmani tu sadācāraprāpter iti savane pravṛttir na yujyate 
tasmāt pūjyatvamātre tātparyam ity abhipretya ṭīkākṛdbhir apy uktam anena pūjyatvaṃ lakṣyata iti 
tathāpi jātidoṣaharatvena prārabdhahāritvaṃ tu vyaktam evāyātam 
sandhāryaā vaiṣṇavair yatnāc chālagrāmaśilā'suvat 
sā cārcyā dvārakācakrāṅkitopetaiva sarvadā  Hbhv 
brāhme tatraiva
śālagrāmodbhavo devo devo dvāravatībhavaḥ 
ubhayoḥ saṅgamo yatra muktis tatra na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
skānde śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde
cakrāṅkitā śilā yatra śālagrāmaśilāgrataḥ 
tiṣṭhate muniśārdūla vardhante tatra sampadaḥ  Hbhv 
tatraivānyatra
pratyahaṃ dvādaśa śilāḥ śālagrāmasya yo 'rcayet 
dvāravatyāḥ śilāyuktāḥ sa vaikuṇṭhe mahīyate  Hbhv 
atha śrīdvārakācakrāṅkalakṣaṇāni
śrīprahlādasaṃhitāyām
ekaḥ sudarśano dvābhyāṃ lakṣmīnārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ 
tribhis trivikramo nāma caturbhiś ca janārdanaḥ  Hbhv 
pañcabhir vāsudevas tu ṣaḍbhiḥ pradyumna ucyate 
saptabhir baladevas tu aṣṭabhiḥ puruṣottamaḥ  Hbhv 
navabhiś ca navavyūho daśabhir daśamūrtikaḥ 
ekādaśaiś cāniruddho dvādaśair dvādaśātmakaḥ 
anyeṣū bahucakreṣu anantaḥ parikīrtitaḥ  Hbhv 
atha dvādaśacakrāṅkamāhātmyam
vārāhe
ye kecic caiva pāṣāṇā viṣṇucakreṇa mudritāḥ 
teṣāṃ sparśanamātreṇa mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ  Hbhv 
gāruḍe
sudarśanādyās tu śilāḥ pūjitāḥ sarvakāmadāḥ  Hbhv 
skānde ca
bhaktyā vā yadi vābhaktyā cakrāṅkaṃ pūjayen naraḥ 
api cet sudurācāro mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
dvārakāmāhātmye ca dvārakāgatānāṃ śrībrahmādīnām uktau
etad vai cakratīrthaṃ tu yac chilā cakracihnitā 
muktidā pāpināṃ loke mlecchadeśe'pi pūjitā  Hbhv 
atha teṣv eva cakrabhedena phalabhedaḥ
kapilapañcarātre
ekacakras tu pāṣāṇo dvāravatyāḥ suśobhanaḥ 
sudarśanābhidho yo 'sau mokṣaikaphaladāyakaḥ  Hbhv 
lakṣmīnārāyaṇo dvābhyāṃ bhuktimuktiphalapradaḥ 
ebhiś cācyutarūpo 'sau phalam aindraṃ prayacchati  Hbhv 
caturbhujaś catuścakraś caturvargaphalapradaḥ 
pañcabhir vāsudevaś ca janmamṛtyubhayāpahaḥ  Hbhv 
ṣaḍbhiḥ pradyumna evāsau lakṣmīṃ kāntiṃ dadāti saḥ 
saptabhir balabhadro 'sau gotrakīrtivivardhanaḥ  Hbhv 
dadāti vāñchitaṃ sarvam aṣṭabhiḥ puruṣottamaḥ 
navacakro nṛsiṃhas tu phalaṃ yacchaty anuttamam  Hbhv 
rājyaprado daśabhis tu daśāvatārakaḥ smṛtaḥ 
ekādaśabhir aiśvaryam aniruddhaḥ prayacchati  Hbhv 
nirvāṇaṃ dvādaśātmāsau saukhyadaś ca supūjitaḥ  Hbhv 
atha varṇādibhedena doṣaguṇāḥ pūjyatvāpūjyatve ca
tatraiva
kṛṣṇa mṛtyuprado nityaṃ dhūmraś caiva bhayāvahaḥ 
asvāsthyaṃ karburo dadyān nīlas tu dhanahānidaḥ  Hbhv 
chidro dāridryaduḥkhāni dadyāt sampūjito dhruvam 
pāṇḍaras tu mahad duḥkhaṃ bhagno bhāryāviyogadaḥ  Hbhv 
putrapautradhanaiśvaryasukham atyantam uttamam 
dadāti śuklavarṇaś ca tasmād enaṃ samarcayet  Hbhv 
śrīprahlādasaṃhitāyām
kṛṣṇā mṛtyupradā nityaṃ kapilā ca bhayāvahā 
rogārtiṃ karburā dadyāt pītā vittavināśinī  Hbhv 
dhūmrābhā vittanāśāya bhagnā bhāryāvināśikā 
sacchidrā ca trikoṇā ca tathā viṣamacakrikā 
ardhacandrākṛtir yā ca pūjyās tā na bhavanti hi  Hbhv 
gārgyagālavayoḥ
sukhadā samacakrā tu dvādaśī cottamā śubhā 
vartulā caturasrā ca narāṇāṃ ca sukhapradā  Hbhv 
trikoṇā viṣamā caiva chidrā bhagnā tathaiva ca 
ardhacandrākṛtir yā tu pūjārhā na bhavet tu sā 
phalaṃ notpadyate tatra pūjitāyāṃ kadācana  Hbhv 
iti śrīgopālabhaṭṭavilikhite śrībhagavadbhaktivilāse
ādhiṣṭhāniko nāma
pañcamo vilāsaḥ 
 SnapanikaVilasa
ṣaṣṭhavilāsaḥ
snāpanikaḥ
śrīcaitanyaprasādena tadrūpaṃ gokulotsavam 
manojñaṃ yaṣṭukāmasya mūrtyarcāvidhir ucyate  Hbhv 
svayaṃ vyaktāḥ sthāpanāś ca mūrtayo dvividhā matāḥ 
svayaṃ vyaktāḥ svayaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ sthāpanās tu pratiṣṭhayā  Hbhv 
yathā ca pādmottarakhaṇḍe PadmaP 
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi tadarcāvasathaṃ hareḥ 
sthāpanaṃ ca svayaṃ vyaktaṃ dvividhaṃ tat prakīrtitam  Hbhv 
śilāmṛddārulohādyaiḥ kṛtvā pratikṛtiṃ hareḥ 
śrautasmārtāgamaproktavidhinā sthāpanaṃ hi yat  Hbhv 
tat sthāpanaṃ iti proktaṃ svayaṃ vyaktaṃ hi me śṛṇu 
yasmin sannihito viṣṇuḥ svam eva nṝṇāṃ bhuvi  Hbhv 
pāṣāṇadārvor ātmeśaḥ svayaṃ vyaktaṃ hi tat smṛtam 
durlabhatvāt svayaṃ vyaktamūrteḥ śrīvaiṣṇavottamaḥ 
yathāvidhi pratiṣṭhāpya sthāpitāṃ mūrtim arcayet  Hbhv 
haribhaktisudhodaye
naikaṃ svavaṃśaṃ tu naras tārayaty akhilaṃ jagat 
arcāyām īpsitaṃ nṝṇāṃ phalaṃ yāgādidurlabham 
pratimām āśrito 'bhīṣṭapradāṃ kalpalatāṃ yathā  Hbhv 
athaśrīmūrteḥ prasādanam ātmādiśuddhayaś ca
śrīmūrtiṃ kṣālanārhāṃ tu śastagandhajalādinā 
praksālayet tad anyāṃ tu mūlamantreṇa mārjayet  Hbhv 
śrīmūrtihṛdayaṃ spṛṣṭvā svamantraṃ cāṣṭadhā japet 
evaṃ prasādanaṃ mūrter ātmanas tatprasādanāt 
śuddhir ekā dvitīyā tu syād avyagratayāpi ca  Hbhv 
sthānaśuddhis tathā dravyaśuddhiś ca likhitā purā 
iti prakārabhedena bhavec chuddhicatuṣṭayam  Hbhv 
uktaṃ ca śrīnāradena
puṣpeṇāmbu gṛhītvā tu prokṣayete sarvasādhanam 
malasnānaṃ tataḥ kuryāt pātre devaṃ nidhāya ca  Hbhv 
anyenāpi
puṣpākṣatādidravyānāṃ kuryān mantrādiśodhanam 
kṣālanenāmbulepāder mūrtiśuddiṃ samācaret 
avyagratvenātmaśuddhiṃ ksitiśuddhiṃ tataś caret  Hbhv 
 iti 
mantraśuddhiṃ parāṃ cittaśuddhiṃ cecchanti kecana 
evaṃ ṣaṭ śuddhayaḥ puṇyāḥ sampradāyānusārataḥ  Hbhv 
atha pīṭhapūjā
tāmrādipīṭhe śrīkhaṇḍādyālipte'ṣṭadalaṃ likhet 
sakarṇikaṃ trivṛttāḍhyaṃ padmaṃ ṣoḍaśakeśaram  Hbhv 
sadalāgraṃ catuṣkoṇaṃ caturdvāravibhūṣitam 
pūjāyantraṃ samuddhṛtya pīṭhārcāṃ tatra sādhayet  Hbhv 
pīṭhe bhagavato vāme śrīgurūn gurupādukām 
nāradādīn pūrvasiddhān yajed anyāṃś ca vaiṣṇavān  Hbhv 
dakṣiṇe cārcayed durgāṃ gaṇeśaṃ ca sarasvatīm 
tatra prāglikhitanyāsasyānusāreṇa pūjayet  Hbhv 
madhye ādhāraśaktyādīn dharmādīṃś ca vidikṣv atha 
adharmādīṃś caturdikṣv anantādīn madhyataḥ punaḥ  Hbhv 
śaktīr navāṣṭapatreṣu karṇikāyāṃ ca pūjayet 
tathā tadupariṣṭhāc ca pīṭhamantraṃ yathoditam  Hbhv 
tatpīṭhe mūlamantreṇa śrīmūrtiṃ sthāpayed atha 
puṣpāñjaliṃ gṛhitveṣṭadevarūpaṃ vicintayet  Hbhv 
tataś ca mūlamantreṇa kṣiptvā puṣpāñjalitrayam 
nijeṣṭadevamūrteś ca param aikyaṃ vibhāvayet  Hbhv 
athāvāhanādīni
tato devārcane prauḍhapādatāyā niṣedhanāt 
bhūmai nihitapādaḥ san kuryād āvāhanādikam  Hbhv 
yac cāvāhyam adhiṣṭhānaṃ tatrāvāhanam ācaret 
śālagrāmasthāpane ca nāvāhanavisarjane  Hbhv 
tathā coktam
udvāsāvāhane na staḥ sthāvare vai yathā tathā 
śālagrāmārcane naiva hy āvāhanavisarjane  Hbhv 
śālagrāme tu bhagavān āvirbhūto yathā hariḥ 
na tathānyatra sūryādau vaikuṇṭhe'pi ca sarvagaḥ  Hbhv 
athāvāhanādividhiḥ
āvāhanādimudrāś ca saṃdarśyāvāhanaṃ budhaḥ 
tathā saṃsthāpanaṃ sannidhāpanaṃ sannirodhanam  Hbhv 
sakalīkaraṇaṃ cāvaguṇṭhanaṃ ca yathāvidhi 
amṛtīkaraṇaṃ kuryāt paramīkaraṇaṃ tathā  Hbhv 
tathāvāhanādyarthaḥ
āgame
āvāhanaṃ cādareṇa sammukhīkaraṇaṃ prabhoḥ 
bhaktyā niveśanaṃ tasya saṃsthāpanamudrāhṛtam  Hbhv 
tavāsmīti tvadīyatvadarśanaṃ sannidhāpanam 
kriyāsamāptiparyantaṃ sthāpanaṃ sannirodhanam  Hbhv 
saklaīkaraṇaṃ coktaṃ tatsarvāṅgaprakāśanam 
ānandaghanatātyantaprakāśo hy avaguṭhanam  Hbhv 
amṛtīkaraṇaṃ sarvair evāṅgair avaruddhatā 
paramīkaraṇaṃ nāmābhīṣṭasampādanaṃ param  Hbhv 
athāvāhanamāhātmyam
nārasiṃhe
āgaccha narasiṃheti āvāhyākṣatapuṣpakaiḥ 
etāvatāpi rājendra sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  Hbhv 
 iti
nyased yathāsampradāyaṃ deve'ṅgādīni pūrvavat 
śaṅkhacakrādikāś cātha mudrā vidvān pradarśayet  Hbhv 
tathā ca tattvasāgare
āvāhanādimudrāś ca darśayitvā tataḥ punaḥ 
aṅganyāsaṃ ca devasya kṛtvā mudrāḥ pradarśayet  Hbhv 
atha mudrāḥ
āgame
āvāhanīṃ sthāpanīṃ ca tathānyāṃ sannidhāpanīm 
saṃnirodhakarīṃ cānyāṃ sakalīkaraṇīṃ parām  Hbhv 
tathāvaguṇṭhanīṃ paścād amṛtīkaraṇīṃ tathā 
paramīkaraṇaṃ cānyā prāg aṣṭau darśayed imāḥ  Hbhv 
śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ gadāṃ padmaṃ muṣalaṃ śārṅgam eva ca 
khaḍgaṃ pāśāṅkuśī tadvad vainateyaṃ tathaiva ca  Hbhv 
śrīvatsakaustubhau veṇum abhītivaradau tathā 
vanamālāṃ tathā mantrī darśayet kṛṣṇapūjane  Hbhv 
mudrā cāpi prayoktavyā nityaabilvaphalākṛtiḥ 
ity etāś ca punaḥ saptadaśa mudrāḥ pradarśayet  Hbhv 
gandadigdhau karau kṛtvā mudrāḥ sarvatra yojayet 
yo 'nyathā kurute mūḍho na siddhaḥ phalabhāg bhavet  Hbhv 
atha mudrāmāhātmyam
agastyasaṃhitāyām
etābhiḥ saptadaśabhir mudrābhis tu vicaksaṇaḥ 
yo vai mām arcayen nityaṃ mohayet sa sureśvaram 
drāpayed api viprendra tataḥ prārthitam āpnuyat  Hbhv 
kramadīpikāyāṃ  bilvamudrām adhikṛtya 
manovāṇīdehair yad iha ca purā vāpi vihitaṃ
tvamatyā matyā vā tad akhilam asau duṣkṛticayam 
imāṃ mudrāṃ jānan kṣapayati naras taṃ suragaṇā
namanty asyādhīnā bhavati satataṃ sarvajanatā  Hbhv 
athāsanādyarpaṇam
tato nikṣipya devasyopari puṣpāñjalitrayam 
dattvāsanārthaṃ puspaṃ ca svāgataṃ vidhinācaret  Hbhv 
āsanādyupacāreṣu mudrāḥ ṣoḍaśa darśayet 
prasiddhāḥ padmasvastyādyā vidvān ṣoḍaśasu kramāt  Hbhv 
śrīkṛṣṇāyārpayed arghyaṃ pādyam ācamanīyakam 
madhuparkaṃ punaś cācamanīyaṃ ca vidhir yathā  Hbhv 
tathā ca smṛtyarthasāre 
āvāhanāsanaṃ pādyam arghyam ācamanīyakam 
snānam ācamanaṃ vastrācamanaṃ copavītakam  Hbhv 
ācamanaṃ gandhapuṣpaṃ dhūpadīpaṃ prakalpayet 
naivedyaṃ punar ācāmaṃ natvā stutvā visarjayet  Hbhv 
anyatra ca 
ādau puṣpāñjaliṃ dattvā pādārcanam ataḥ param 
pādyam arghaṃ tv ācamanaṃ madhuparkaṃ yathoditam  Hbhv 
abhyaṅgodvartane kṛtvā mahāsnānaṃ samācaret 
abhiṣekāṅgavastraṃ ca dattvā nīrājayed dharim  Hbhv 
 iti
śrīmūrtau tu śirasy arghyaṃ dadyāt pādyaṃ ca pādayoḥ 
mukhe cācamanīyaṃ trir madhuparkaṃ ca tatra hi  Hbhv 
sarveṣv apy upacāreṣu pādyādiṣu pṛthak pṛthak 
ādau puṣpāñjaliṃ kecid icchanti bhagavatparāḥ  Hbhv 
athāsanādyarpaṇamāhātmyam
narasiṃhapurāṇe 
dattvāsanam athārghyaṃ ca pādyam ācamanīyakam 
devadevasya vidhinā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare 
āsanānāṃ pradānena sthānaṃ sarvatra vindati 
godānaphalam āpnoti tathā pādyaprado naraḥ  Hbhv 
tatas tv arhaṇadānena sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate 
tathaivācamaīyasya dātā brāhamaṇasattamāḥ  Hbhv 
tīrthatoyaṃ tathā dattvā devasyācamanaṃ punaḥ 
svargalokam avāpnoti sarvapāpavivarjitaḥ 
naras tv ācamanīyasya dātā bhavati nirmalaḥ  Hbhv 
madhuparkasya dānena paraṃ padam ihāśnute  Hbhv 
viṣṇupurāṇe  ca 
madhuparkavidhiṃ kṛtvā madhuparkaṃ prayacchati 
brahman sa yāti paramaṃ sthānam etan na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
atha snānam
vijñāpya devaṃ snānārthaṃ pāduke purato 'rpayet 
mahāvidyādinā taṃ ca snānasthānaṃ tato nayet  Hbhv 
prāgvat tatrāsanaṃ pādyaṃ tatraivācamanīyakam 
nivedya darśayen mudrām amṛtīkaraṇīṃ budhaḥ  Hbhv 
śālagrāmaśilārūpaṃ tato devaṃ niveśayet 
snānapātre nijābhīṣṭāṃ calāṃ śrīmūrtim eva vā  Hbhv 
atha snānapātram
skandapurāṇe 
kṛtvā tāmramaye pātre yo 'rcayen madhusūdanam 
phalam āpnoti pūjāyāḥ pratyahaṃ śatvārṣikam  Hbhv 
yo 'rcayen mādhavaṃ bhaktyā aśvatthadalasaṃsthitam 
pratyahaṃ labhate puṇyaṃ padmayutasamudbhavam  Hbhv 
rambhādalopari hariṃ kṛtvā yo 'bhyarcayen naraḥ 
varṣāyutaṃ bhavet pītaḥ keśavaḥ priyayā saha  Hbhv 
ye paśyanti sakṛd bhaktyā padmapatropari sthitam 
bhaktyā padmālayākāntaṃ tair āptaṃ durlabhaphalam  Hbhv 
 iti
tataḥ śaṅkhenābhiṣekaṃ kuryād ghaṇṭādiniḥsvanaiḥ 
mūlenāṣṭākṣareṇāpi dhūpayann antarāntarā  Hbhv 
tatra tu prathamaṃ bhaktyā vidadhīta sugandhibhiḥ 
divyais tailādibhir dravyair abhyaṅgaṃ śrīhareḥ śanaiḥ  Hbhv 
athābhyaṅgadravyāṇi tanmāhātmyaṃ ca
skande 
mālatījātim ādāya sugandhānāṃ tu vā punaḥ  Hbhv 
tathānyapuṣpajātīnāṃ gṛhītvā bhaktito narāḥ 
ye snāpayanti deveśam utsave vai harer dine  Hbhv 
medinīdānatulyaṃ hi phalam uktaṃ svayambhuvā 
yaḥ punaḥ puṣpatailena divyauṣadhiyutena hi  Hbhv 
abhyaṅgaṃ kurute viṣṇor madhye kṣiptvā tu kuṅkumam 
romāñcitatanur bhūtvā priyayā saha mādhavaḥ 
prītyā bibharti svotsaṅge manvantaraśataṃ hariḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare ca 
gandhatailāni divyāni sugandhīni śucīni ca 
keśavāya naro dattvā gandharvaiḥ saha modate  Hbhv 
atha pañcāmṛtasnapanam
tataḥ śaṅkhabhṛtenaiva kṣīreṇa snāpayet kramāt 
dadhnā ghṛtena madhunā khaṇḍena ca pṛthak pṛthak  Hbhv 
pañcāmṛtādyaiḥ snapanaṃ sadā necchanti tat priyāḥ 
kintu taiḥ kāladeśādiviśeṣe kārayanti tat  Hbhv 
atha tatparimāṇam
brahmapurāṇe 
devānāṃ pratimā yatra ghṛtābhyaṅgas tato bhavet 
palāni tasya deyāni śraddhayā pañcaviṃśatiḥ  Hbhv 
aṣṭottarapalaśataṃ deyaṃ ca sarvadā 
dve sahasre palānāṃ tu mahāsnāne ca saṅkhyayā  Hbhv 
dātavye yena sarvāsu dikṣu niryāti tadghṛtam  Hbhv 
 iti
dugdhādāv api saṅkhyeyam evaṃ jñeyā manīṣibhiḥ 
palasaṅkhyā ca vijñeyā yājñavalkyādivākyataḥ  Hbhv 
tathā hi 
pañcakṛṣṇalako māṣas te suvarṇas tu ṣoḍaśa 
suvarṇānāṃ ca catvāraḥ palam ity abhidhīyate  Hbhv 
 iti
kiṃ ca 
snānārthaṃ surabhīkṣīraṃ mahiṣyādyās tu kutsitāḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare ca 
śarīraduḥkhaśamanaṃ manoduḥkhavināśanam 
kṣīreṇa snapanaṃ viṣṇoḥ kṣīrābhodhipradaṃ tathā  Hbhv 
agnipurāṇe 
gavāṃ śatasya viprebhyaḥ samyagdattasya yat phalam 
ghṛtaprasthena tad viṣṇor labhet snānān na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
indradyumnena samprāptā saptadvīpā vasundharā 
ghṛtodakena saṃyuktā pratimā snāpitā kila  Hbhv 
pratimāsaṃ sitāṣṭamyāṃ ghṛtena jagatāṃ patim 
snāpayitvā samabhyarcya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  Hbhv 
jñānato 'jñānato vāpi yat pāpaṃ kurute naraḥ 
tat kṣālayati sandhyāyāṃ ghṛtasnapanatoṣitaḥ  Hbhv 
yeṣu kṣīravahā nadyo pāyasakardamāḥ 
tān lokān puruṣā yānti kṣīrasnapanakā hareḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharme śrīpulastyaprahlādasaṃvāde ca 
dvādaśyāṃ pañcadaśyāṃ ca gavyena havisā hareḥ 
snāpanaṃ daityaśārdūla mahāpātakanāśanam  Hbhv 
dadhyādīnāṃ vikārāṇāṃ kṣīrataḥ sambhavo yathā 
tathaivāśeṣakāmānāṃ kṣīrasnānaṃ tato hareḥ  Hbhv 
nārasiṃhe 
payasā yas tu deveśaṃ snāpayed garuḍadhvajam 
sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā viṣṇuloke mahīyate  Hbhv 
snāpya dadhnā sakṛd viṣṇuṃ nirmalaṃ priyadarśanam 
viṣṇulokam avāpnoti sevyamānaḥ surottamaḥ  Hbhv 
duḥsvapnaśamanaṃ jñeyam amaṅgalyavināśanam 
māṅgalyavṛddhidaṃ dadhnā snapanaṃ narapuṅgava  Hbhv 
yaḥ karoti harer arcāṃ madhunā snāpitāṃ naraḥ 
agniloke sa moditvā punar viṣṇupure vaset  Hbhv 
madhunā snapanaṃ kṛtvā saubhāgyam adhigacchati 
lokamitrāṇy avāpnoti tathaivekṣurasena ca  Hbhv 
śrīdvārakāmāhātmye ca śrīmārkaṇḍeyendradyumnasaṃvāde 
kṣīrasnānaṃ prakurvanti ye narā viṣṇumūrdhani 
tenāśvamedhajaṃ puṇyaṃ bindunā bindunā smṛtam  Hbhv 
kṣīrād daśaguṇaṃ dadhnā ghṛtaṃ tasmād daśottaram 
ghṛtād daśaguṇaṃ kṣaudraṃ khaṇḍaṃ tasmād daśottaram  Hbhv 
puṣpodakaṃ ca gandhodaṃ vardhate ca daśottaram 
mantrodakaṃ ca darbhodaṃ tathaiva nṛpasattama  Hbhv 
drākṣārasaṃ cūtarasaṃ śatavājimakhaiḥ samam 
tathaiva tīrthanīraṃ ca phalaṃ yacchati bhūmipa  Hbhv 
snāpanaṃ kṛṣṇadevasya yaḥ karoti svaśaktitaḥ 
phalam āpnoti tat proktaṃ niṣkāmo muktim āpnuyāt  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare
tīrthodakāni puṇyāni svayam ānīya mānavaḥ 
tailasya snapanaṃ dattvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  Hbhv 
atha snapane dhūpane dhūpanamāhātmyam
skānde 
snānakāle tu kṛṣṇasya aguruṃ dahate tu yaḥ 
praviṣṭo nāsikārandhraṃ pāpaṃ janmāyutaṃ dahet  Hbhv 
udvartanaṃ ca tailāder apasāraṇakāraṇam 
devasya kārayed dravyair upayuktyair anantaram  Hbhv 
athodvartanaṃ tanmāhātmyaṃ ca
nārasiṃhe 
yavagodhūmaiś cūrṇair udvartyoṣṇena vāriṇā 
prakṣālya devadeveśaṃ vāruṇaṃ lokam āpnuyāt  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare ca 
godhūmayavacūrṇais tu tam utsādya janārdanam 
lodhracūrṇakasaṅkīrṇair balarūpaṃ tathāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
masūramāsacūrṇaṃ ca kuṅkumakṣodasaṃyutam 
nivedya devadevāya gandharvaiḥ saha modate  Hbhv 
vārāhe 
kalāyakasya cūrṇena piṣṭacūrṇena vā punaḥ 
tenaivodvartanaṃ kuryād gandhapuṣpaiś ca saṃyutam 
yadīcchet paramāṃ siddhiṃ mama karmaparāyaṇaḥ  Hbhv 
 iti
tataḥ samarpayet kūrcam uṣīrādivinirmitam 
malāpakarṣaṇādyarthaṃ śrīmanmūrtyaṅgasandhitaḥ  Hbhv 
atha kūrcaṃ tanmāhātmyam
viṣṇudharmottare 
uṣīrakūrcakaṃ dattvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate 
dattvā gobālajaṃ kūrcaṃ sarvāṃs tāpān vyapohati 
dattvā cāmarakaṃ kūrcaṃ śriyam āpnoty anuttamam  Hbhv 
atha śuddhajalasnapanam
tataḥ koṣṇena saṃsnāpya saṃskṛtena sugandhinā 
śītalenāmbunā śaṅkhabhṛtena snāpayet punaḥ  Hbhv 
tad uktam ekādaśaskandhe BhP  
candanośīrakarpūra kuṅkumāguruvāsitaiḥ 
salilaiḥ snāpayen mantrair nityadā vibhave sati  Hbhv 
atha jalaparimāṇam
bhaviṣye 
snāne palaśataṃ deyam abhyaṅge pañcaviṃśatiḥ 
palānāṃ dve sahasre tu mahāsnānaṃ prakīrtitam  Hbhv 
tatra yājñavalkyaḥ
na naktodakapuṣpādyair arcanaṃ snānam arhati  Hbhv 
viṣṇuḥ
na naktaṃ gṛhītodakena daivakarma kuryāt  Hbhv 
hārītaḥ
rātrāv etā āpo varuṇaṃ prāviśanta
tasmān na rātrau gṛhṇīyāt  Hbhv 
atha snapanamāhātmyam
nārasiṃhe
nirmālaym apanīyātha toyena snāpya keśavam 
narasiṃhākṛtiṃ rājan sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  Hbhv 
godānajaṃ phalaṃ prāpya yānenāmbaraśobhinā 
narasiṃhapuraṃ prāpya modate kālam akṣayam  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
snāpya toyena bhaktyā tu narasiṃhaṃ narādhipa 
sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇulokaṃ mahīyate  Hbhv 
narasiṃhaṃ tu saṃsnāpya karpūrāguruvāriṇā 
canddraloke sa moditvā paścād viṣṇupuraṃ vaset  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
kuśapuṣpodakenāpi viṣṇulokam avāpnuyāt 
ratnodakena sāvitraṃ kauveraṃ hemavāriṇā  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare 
ratnodakapradānena śriyam āpnoty anuttamām 
bījodakapradānena kriyāsāphalyam āpnuyāt  Hbhv 
puṣpatoyapradānena śrīmān bhavati mānavaḥ 
phalatoyapradānena saphalāṃ vindate kriyām  Hbhv 
hayaśīrṣapañcarātre
sugandhinā yas toyena snāpayej jalaśāyinam 
brahmalokam avāpnoti yāvad indrāś caturdaśa  Hbhv 
gāruḍe 
tulasīmiśratoyena snāpayanti janārdanam 
pūjayanti ca bhāvena dhanyās te bhuvi mānavāḥ  Hbhv
agnipurāṇe
mahāsnānena govindaṃ samyak saṃsnāpya mānavaḥ 
yaṃ yaṃ prārthayate kāmaṃ taṃ taṃ prāpnoty asaṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
pādme śrīpulastyabhagīrathasaṃvāde
snānam abhyarcanaṃ yas tu kurute keśave sadā 
tasya puṇyasya yā saṅkhyā nāsti sā jñāne gocarā  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare 
snānārthaṃ devadevasya yas tu gandhaṃ prayacchati 
bhavanti vaśagās tasya nāryaḥ sarvatra sarvadā  Hbhv 
puṣpadānāt tathā loke bhavatīha phalānvitaḥ 
dattvā mṛgamadasnānaṃ sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
sarvauṣadhipradānena vājimedhaphalaṃ labhet 
dattvā jātīphalaṃ mukhyaṃ saphalāṃ vindati kriyām  Hbhv 
atha sarvauṣadhiḥ
murā māsī vacā kuṣṭhaṃ śaileyaṃ rajanīdvayam 
śaṭī campakamustaṃ ca sarvauṣadhigaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ  Hbhv 
gandhaś cāgame
gandhaś candanakarpūrakālāgurubhir īritaḥ  Hbhv 
atha śaṅkhamāhātmyam
skānde śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde
śaṅkhasthitena toyena yaḥ snāpayati keśavam 
kapilāśatadānasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ  Hbhv 
śaṅke tīrthodakaṃ kṛtvā yaḥ snāpayati mādhavam 
dvādaśyāṃ bindumātreṇa kulānāṃ tārayec chatam  Hbhv 
kapilākṣīram ādāya śaṅkhe kṛtvā janārdanam 
yaḥ snāpayati dharmātmā yajñāyutaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
anyagosambhavaṃ kṣīraṃ śaṅkhe kṛtvā tu nārada 
yaḥ snāpayati deveśaṃ rājasūyaphalaṃ labheet  Hbhv 
śaṅkhe kṛtvā ca pānīyaṃ sākṣataṃ kusumānvitam 
snāpayed devadeveśaṃ hanyāt pāpaṃ cirārjitam  Hbhv 
sākṣataṃ kusumopetaṃ śaṅkhe toyaṃ sacandanam 
yaḥ kṛtvā snāpayed devaṃ mama loke vasec ciram  Hbhv 
kṣiptvā gandhodakaṃ śaṅkhe yaḥ snāpayati keśavam 
namo nārāyaṇāyeti mucyate yonisaṅkaṭān  Hbhv 
nādyaṃ taḍāgajaṃ vāri vāpīkūpahradādijam 
gāṅgeyaṃ ca bhavet sarvaṃ kṛtaṃ śaṅkhe kalipriya  Hbhv 
trailokye yāni tīrthāni vāsudevasya cājñayā 
śaṅkhe tiṣṭhanti viprendra tasmāt śaṅkhaṃ sadārcayet  Hbhv 
śaṅkhe kṛtvā tu pānīyaṃ sapuṣpaṃ satilākṣatam 
arghyaṃ dadāti devasya sasāgaradharāphalam  Hbhv 
arghyaṃ dattvā tu śaṅkhena yaḥ karoti pradakṣiṇam 
pradakṣiṇīkṛtā tena saptadvīpā vasundharā  Hbhv 
darśanenāpi śaṅkhasya kiṃ punaḥ sparśane kṛte 
vilayaṃ yānti pāpāni himaṃ sūryodaye yathā  Hbhv 
nitye naimittike kāmye snānārcanavilepane 
śaṅkham udvahate yas tu śvetadvīpe vasec ciram  Hbhv 
natvā śaṅkhaṃ kare dhṛtvā mantreṇānena vaiṣṇavaḥ 
yaḥ snāpayati govindaṃ tasya puṇyam anantakam  Hbhv 
mantraḥ
tvaṃ purā sāgarotpanno viṣṇunā vidhṛtaḥ kare 
mānitaḥ sarvadevaiś ca pāñcajanya namo 'stu te  Hbhv 
tava nādena jīmūtā vitrasyanti surāsurāḥ 
śaśāṅkāyutadīptābha pāñcajanya namo 'stu te  Hbhv 
garbhā devārinārīṇāṃ vilīyante sahasradhā 
tava nādena pātāle pāñcajanya namo 'stu te  Hbhv 
vārāhe ca
dakṣiṇāvartaśaṅkhena tilamiśrodakena ca 
udake nābhimātre tu yaḥ kuryād abhiṣecanam  Hbhv 
prāk srotasi ca nadyāṃ vai naras tv ekāgramānasaḥ 
yāvaj jīvakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇād eva naśyati  Hbhv 
dakṣiṇāvartaśaṅkhena pātre auḍumbare sthitam 
udakaṃ yaḥ pratīccheta śirasā kṛṣṇamānasaḥ 
tasya janmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇād eva naśyati  Hbhv 
āgame
bṛhattvaṃ snigdhatācchatvaṃ śaṅkhasyeti guṇatrayam  Hbhv 
āvartabhaṅgadoṣas tu hemayogān na jāyate 
nālikāyāṃ svabhāvena yadi chidraṃ bhaven nahi  Hbhv 
 iti
ghaṇṭāvādyaṃ ca nitarāṃ snānakāle praśasyate 
yato bhagavato viṣṇos tat sadā paramaṃ priyam  Hbhv 
āvāhanārghye dhūpe ca puṣpanaivedyayojane 
nityam etāṃ prayuñjīta tanmantreṇābhimantritām  Hbhv 
tanmantraḥ
jayadhvaniṃ tato mantramātaḥ svāhety udīrya ca 
abhyarcya vādayan ghaṇṭāṃ dhūpaṃ nīcaiḥ pradāpayet  Hbhv 
pūjākālaṃ vinānyatra hitaṃ nāsyāḥ pracālanam 
na tayā ca vinā kuryāt pūjanaṃ siddhilālasaḥ  Hbhv 
atha ghaṇṭāmāhātmyam
uktaṃ ca skānde śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde
snānārcanakriyākāle ghaṇṭānādaṃ karoti yaḥ 
purato vāsudevasya tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu  Hbhv 
varṣakoṭisahasrāṇi varṣakoṭiśatāni ca 
vasate devaloke tu apsarogaṇasevitaḥ  Hbhv 
sarvavādyamayī ghaṇṭā keśavasya sadā priyā 
vādanāl labhate puṇyaṃ yajñakoṭisamudbhavam  Hbhv 
vāditraninadais tūryagītamaṅgalanisvanaiḥ 
yaḥ snāpayati govindaṃ jīvanmukto bhaved dhi saḥ  Hbhv 
vāditrāṇām abhāve tu pūjākāle hi sarvadā 
ghaṇṭāśabdo naraiḥ kāryaḥ sarvavādyamayī yataḥ  Hbhv 
sarvavādyamayī ghaṇṭā devadevasya vallabhā 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena ghaṇṭānādaṃ tu kārayet  Hbhv 
manvantarasahasrāṇi manvantaraśatāni ca 
ghaṇṭānādena deveśaḥ prīto bhavati keśavaḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare śrībhagavatprahlādasaṃvāde
śṛṇu daityendra vakṣyāmi ghaṇṭāmāhātmyam uttamam 
prahlāda tvatsamo nāsti madbhakto bhuvanatraye  Hbhv 
mama nāmāṅkitā ghaṇṭā purato mama tiṣṭhati 
arcitā vaiṣṇavagṛhe tatra māṃ viddhi daityaja  Hbhv 
vainateyāṅkitāṃ ghaṇṭāṃ sudarśanayutāṃ yadi 
mamāgre sthāpayed yas tu dehe tasya vasāmy aham  Hbhv 
yas tu vādayate ghaṇṭā vainateyena cihnitām 
dhūpe nīrājanae snāne pūjākāle vilepane  Hbhv 
mamāgre pratyahaṃ vatsa pratyekaṃ labhate phalam 
mamāyutaṃ goyutaṃ ca cāndrāyaṇaśatodbhavam  Hbhv 
vidhibāhyakṛtā pūjā saphalā jāyate nṝṇām 
ghaṇṭānādena tusṭo 'haṃ prayacchāmi svakaṃ padam  Hbhv 
nāgāricihnitā ghaṇṭā rathāṅgena samanvitā 
vādanāt kurute nāśaṃ janmamṛtyubhayasya ca  Hbhv 
garuḍenāṅktāṃ ghaṇṭāṃ dṛṣṭvāhaṃ pratyahaṃ sadā 
prītiṃ karoti daityendra lakṣmīṃ prāpya yathādhanaḥ  Hbhv 
dṛṣṭvāmṛtaṃ yathā devāḥ prītiṃ kurvanty aharniśam 
suparṇe ca tathā prītiṃ ghaṇṭāśikharasaṃsthite  Hbhv 
svakareṇa prakurvanti ghaṇṭānādaṃ svabhaktitaḥ 
madīyārcanakāle tu phalaṃ koṭyaindavaṃ kalau  Hbhv 
anyatra ca
ghaṇṭādaṇḍasya śikhare sacakraṃ sthāpayet tu yaḥ 
garuḍaṃ vai priyaṃ viṣṇoḥ sthāpitaṃ bhuvanatrayam  Hbhv 
sacakra ghaṇṭānādaṃ tu mṛtyukāle śṛṇoti yaḥ 
pāpakoṭiyutasyāpi naśyanti yamakiṅkarāḥ  Hbhv 
sarve doṣāḥ pralīyante ghaṇṭānāde kṛte harau 
devatānāṃ munīndrāṇāṃ pitṝṇām utsavo bhavet  Hbhv 
abhāve vainateyasya cakrasyāpi na saṃśayaḥ 
ghaṇṭānādena bhaktānāṃ prasādaṃ kurute hariḥ  Hbhv 
gṛhe yasmin bhaven nityaṃ ghaṇṭā nāgārisaṃyutā 
na sarpāṇāṃ bhayaṃ tatra nāgnividyutsamudbhavam  Hbhv 
yasya ghaṇṭā gṛhe nāsti śaṅkhaś ca purato hareḥ 
kathaṃ bhāgavataṃ nāma gīyate tasya dehinaḥ  Hbhv 
 iti
ato bhagavataḥ prītyai ghaṇṭā śrīgaruḍānvitā 
saṅgṛhyā vaiṣṇavair yatnāc cakreṇopari maṇḍitā  Hbhv 
snāne śaṅkhādivādyāṃ tu nāmasaṅkīrtanaṃ hareḥ 
gītaṃ nṛtyaṃ purāṇādipaṭhanaṃ ca praśasyate  Hbhv 
atha snāne vādyādimāhātmyam
skandapurāṇe
snānakāle tu kṛṣṇasya śaṅkhādīnāṃ tu vādanam 
kurute brahmaloke tu vasate brahmavāsaram  Hbhv 
snānakāle tu samprāpte kṛṣṇasyāgre tu nartanam 
gītaṃ caiva punāty atra ṛcoktaṃ vadanena hi  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde
mṛdaṅgavādyena yutaṃ paṇavena samanvitam 
arcanaṃ vāsudevasya sanṛtyaṃ mokṣadaṃ nṝṇām  Hbhv 
gītaṃ vādyaṃ ca nṛtyaṃ ca tathā pustakavācanam 
pūjākāle tu kṛṣṇasya sarvadā keśavapriyam  Hbhv 
nṛtyavādyādyabhāve tu kuryāt pustakavācanam 
pūjākāle tv idaṃ putra sarvadā prītidāyakam  Hbhv
pustakasyāpy abhāve tu viṣṇunāmasahasrakam 
stavarājaṃ miniśreṣṭha gajendrasya ca mokṣaṇam  Hbhv 
pūjākāle tu devasya gītāstotram anusmṛtiḥ 
pañcastaavā mahābhāga mahāprītikarā hareḥ  Hbhv 
vihāya gītavādyāni pūjākāle sadā hareḥ 
paṭhanīyaṃ mahābhaktyā viṣṇor nāmasahasrakam  Hbhv 
dvārakāmāhātmye
snānakāle tu kṛṣṇasya jayaśabdaṃ karoti yaḥ 
karatāḍanasaṃyuktaṃ gītaṃ nṛtyaṃ prakurvate  Hbhv 
unmattaceṣṭāṃ kurvāṇo hasan jalpan yathecchayā 
nottānaśāyī bhavati mātur aṅke nareśvara  Hbhv 
atha sahasranāmamāhātmyam
tatraiva
snānakāle tu devasya paṭhen nāmasahasrakam 
pratyaksaraṃ labhet puṇyaṃ kapilāgośatodbhavam  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare
kṛtvā nāmasahasreṇa stutiṃ tasya mahātmanaḥ 
viyogam āpnoti naraḥ sarvānarthair na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
skānde śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde
viṣṇor nāmasahasraṃ tu pūjākāle paṭhanti ye 
vedānāṃ caiva puṇyānāṃ phalam āpnoti mānavaḥ  Hbhv 
ślokenaikena devarṣe sahasranāmakasya yat 
paṭhitena phalaṃ proktaṃ na tat kratuśatair api  Hbhv 
mantrahīnaṃ kriyāhīnaṃ yat kṛtaṃ pūjanaṃ hareḥ 
paripūrṇaṃ bhavet sarvaṃ sahasranāmakīrtanāt  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
jñānājñānakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ paṭhitvā viṣṇusannidhau 
nāmnāṃ sahasraṃ viṣṇos tu prajahāti mahārujam  Hbhv 
brahmahatyādipāpāni kāmacārakṛtāny api 
vilayaṃ yānti vai nūnam anyapāpe tu kā kathā  Hbhv 
siddhyanti sarvakāryāṇi manasā cintitāni ca 
yaḥ paṭhet prātar utthāya viṣṇor nāmasahasrakam  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrīkṛṣṇārjunasaṃvāde
adhītās tena vai vedāḥ surāḥ sarvasamarcitāḥ 
nāmnāṃ sahasraṃ yo 'dhīte muktis tasya kare sthitā  Hbhv 
kurvat pāpasahasrāṇi bhuñjāno 'pi yatas tataḥ 
paṭhen nāmasahasras tu durgandhaṃ na sa paśyati  Hbhv 
muktvā nāmasahasras tu nānyo dharmo 'sti kaścana 
kalau prāpte guḍākeśa satyam etan mayeritam  Hbhv 
yajñair dānais tapabhiś ca stavaiḥ prītir na me'rjuna 
santuṣṭis tu na cānyena vinā nāmasahasrakam  Hbhv 
stavaṃ nāmasahasrākhyaṃ ye na jānanti vai kalau 
bhramanti te narīa loke sarvadharmabahiṣkṛtāḥ  Hbhv 
stavaṃ nāmasahasrākhyaṃ likhitaṃ yasya veśmani 
pūjyate mama sānnidhye pūjāṃ gṛhṇāmi tasya vai  Hbhv 
yasmin nāmasahasraṃ me gṛhe tiṣṭhati sarvadā 
likhitaṃ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha tatra no viśate kaliḥ  Hbhv 
tasmāt tvam api kaunteya madbhakto manmanā bhava 
paṭhan nāmasahasraṃ me sarvān kāmān avāpsyasi  Hbhv 
aham ārādhitaḥ pūrvaṃ brahmaṇā lokakartṛṇā 
tato nāmasahasraṃ me prāptaṃ lokahitaṃ param  Hbhv 
nāradena tataḥ pūrvaṃ prāptaṃ ca parameṣṭhinaḥ 
nāradena tataḥ proktavṛṣīṇām ūrdhvaretasām  Hbhv 
ṛṣibhis tu mahābāho devaloke prakāśitam 
martyaloke manuṣyāṇāṃ vyāsena paribhāṣitam  Hbhv 
tapasogreṇa mahatā śaṅkareṇa mahātmanā 
matprasādād anuprāptaṃ guhyānām uttamottamam  Hbhv 
dattaṃ bhavānyai rudreṇa nāmnāṃ me hi sahasrakam 
viśrutaṃ triṣu lokeṣu mayā te parikīrtitam  Hbhv 
aśeṣārtiharaṃ pārtha mama nāmasahasrakam 
sadyaḥ prītikaraṃ puṇyaṃ surāṇām amṛtaṃ yathā  Hbhv 
aṣṭādaśapurāṇānāṃ sārem etad dhanañjaya 
mayoddhṛtya samākhyātaṃ tava nāmasahasrakam  Hbhv 
sahasranāmamāhātmyaṃ devo jānāti śaṅkaraḥ 
sahasranāmamāhātmyaṃ yaḥ paṭhec chṛṇuyād api 
aparādhasahasreṇa na sa lipyet kadācana  Hbhv 
atha śrībhagavadgītāmāhātmyam
skānde avantīkhaṇḍe śrīvyāsoktau 
gītā sugītā kartavyā kim anyaiḥ śāstravistaraiḥ 
yā svayaṃ padmanābhasya mukhapadmād viniḥsṛtā  Hbhv 
sarvaśāstramayī gītā sarvadevamayī yataḥ 
sarvadharmamayī yasmāt tasmād etāṃ samabhyaset  Hbhv 
śālagrāmaśilāgre tu gītādhyāyaṃ paṭhet tu yaḥ 
manvantarasahasrāṇi vasate brahmaṇaḥ pure  Hbhv 
hatvā hatvā jagat sarvaṃ muṣitvā sacarācaram 
pāpair na lipyate caiva gītādhyāyī kathañcana  Hbhv 
teneṣṭaṃ kratubhiḥ sarvair dattaṃ tena gavāyutam 
gītām abhyasyatā nityaṃ tenāptaṃ padam avyayam  Hbhv 
gītādhyāyaṃ paṭhed yas tu ślokaṃ ślokārdham eva vā 
bhavapāpavinirmukto yāti viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam  Hbhv 
yo nityaṃ viśvarūpākhyam adhyāyaṃ paṭhati dvijaḥ 
vibhūtiṃ devadevasya tasya puṇyaṃ vadāmy aham  Hbhv 
vedair adhītair yat puṇyaṃ setihāsaiḥ purātanaiḥ 
ślokenaikena tat puṇyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
ābrahmastambaparyantaṃ jagattṛptiṃ karoti saḥ 
viśvarūpaṃ sadādhyāyaṃ vibhūtiṃ ca paṭhet tu yaḥ  Hbhv 
ahany ahani yo martyo gītādhyāyaṃ paṭhet tu vai 
dvātriṃśadaparādhāṃs tu kṣamate tasya keśavaḥ  Hbhv 
likhitvā vaiṣṇavānāṃ ca gītāśāstraṃ prayacchati 
dine dine ca yajate hariṃ cātra na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
caturṇām eva vedānāṃ sāram uddhṛtya viṣṇunā 
trailokyasyopakārāya gītāśāstraṃ prakāśitam  Hbhv 
bhāratāmṛtasarvasvaṃ viṣṇor vaktrād viniḥsṛtam 
gītāgaṅgodakaṃ pītvā punar janma na vidyate  Hbhv 
dharmaṃ cārthaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca mokṣaṃ cāpīcchatā sadā 
śrotavyā paṭhanīyā ca gītā kṛṣṇamukhodgatā  Hbhv 
yo naraḥ paṭhate nityaṃ gītāśāstraṃ dine dine 
vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhyo yāti viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam  Hbhv 
atha purāṇapāṭhādimāhātmyam
pādme devadūtavikuṇḍalasaṃvāde PadmaP  
vicārayanti ye śāstraṃ vedābhyāsaratāś ca ye 
purāṇaṃ saṃhitāṃ ye ca śrāvayanti paṭhanti ca  Hbhv 
vyākurvanti smṛtiṃ ye ca ye dharmapratibodhakāḥ 
vedānteṣu niṣaṇṇā ye tair iyaṃ jagatī dhṛtā  Hbhv 
tattadabhyāsamāhātmyaiḥ sarve te hatakilbiṣāḥ 
gacchanti brahmaṇo lokaṃ yatra moho na vidyate  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrīśivomāsaṃvāde 
antaṃ gato 'pi vedānāṃ sarvaśāstrārthavedy api 
puṃso 'śrutapurāṇasya na samyag gatidarśanam  Hbhv 
vedārthād adhikaṃ manye purāṇārthaṃ ca bhāmini 
purāṇam anyathā kṛtvā tiryagyonim avāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye ca ṇārP    
purāṇeṣv arthavādatvaṃ ye vadanti narādhamāḥ 
tair arjitāni puṇyāni kṣayaṃ yānti dvijottamāḥ  Hbhv 
purāṇeṣu dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ sarvadharmapravaktṛṣu 
pravadanty arthavādatvaṃ ye te narakabhājanāḥ  Hbhv 
anāyāsena yaḥ puṇyānīcchatīha dvijottamāḥ 
śrotavyāni bhaktyā tenaiva purāṇāni na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
purārjitāni pāpāni naśam āyānti tasya vai 
purāṇaśravaṇe buddhis tasyaiva bhavati dhruvam  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca 
purāṇe vartamāne'pi pāpapāśena yantritaḥ 
anādṛtyānyagāthāsu saktabuddhiḥ pravartate  Hbhv 
atha vastrārpaṇam
snānamudrāṃ pradarśyātha śuddhasūkṣmāṅgavāsasā 
śanaiḥ saṃmārjya gātrāṇi divye vastre samarpayet  Hbhv 
madhyadeśīyanepathyādyanusāreṇa bhaktitaḥ 
ke'py atra kañcukosṇīṣādyambarāṇy arpayanti ca  Hbhv 
tathā ca matsye
tattaddeśīyabhūṣāḍhyāṃ tattanmūrtiṃ ca kārayet  Hbhv 
ekādaśaskandhe BhP  
alaṅkurvīta saprema madbhakto māṃ yathocitam  Hbhv 
bhaviṣye ca
vāsobhiḥ pūjayed viṣṇuṃ yny evātmapriyāṇi tu 
tathānyaiś ca śubhiar divyair arcayec ca dukūlaiḥ  Hbhv 
vāsāṃsi ca vicitrāṇi sāravanti śucīni ca 
dhūpitāni harer dadyāt vikeśāni navāni ca  Hbhv 
bhūṣayed bahubhir vastrair vicitraiḥ kañcukādibhiḥ 
bhogānantaram eveti bahūnāṃ sammataṃ satām  Hbhv 
atha śrīmadaṅgamārjanamāhātmyam
dvārakāmāhātmye
kṛṣṇaṃ snānārdragātraṃ tu vastreṇa parimārjati 
tasya lakṣārjitasyāpi bhavet pāpasya mārjanam  Hbhv 
atha vastrārpaṇamāhātmyam
nārasiṃhe
vastrābhyām acyutaṃ bhaktyā paridhāpya vicitritam 
somaloke vasitvā tu viṣṇuloke mahīyate  Hbhv 
skānde śrīśivomāsaṃvāde
vastrāṇi supavitrāṇi sāravanti mṛdūni ca 
rūpavanti harer dattvā sadaśāni navāni ca  Hbhv 
yāvad vastrasya tantunā parimāṇaṃ bhavaty atha 
tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi viṣṇuloke mahīyate  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare 
rāṅkavasya pradānena sarvān kānām avāpnuyāt 
kārpāsikaṃ vastrayugaṃ yaḥ pradadyāj janārdane  Hbhv 
yāvanti tasya tantūni hastamātramitāni tu 
tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi viṣṇuloke mahīyate  Hbhv 
mahārghatā yathā tasya sādhudeśodbhavo yathā 
sūkṣmatā ca yathā viprās tathā proktaṃ phalaṃ mahat  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca tatraivānyatra 
śuklavastrapradānena śriyam āpnoty anuttamām 
mahārajanaraktena saubhāgyaṃ mahad aśnute  Hbhv 
tathā kuṅkumaraktena strīṇāṃ vallabhatāṃ vrajet 
nīlīraktaṃ vinā raktaṃ śeṣaraṅgair dvijottamāḥ 
dattvā bhavati dharmātmā sarvavyādhivivarjitaḥ  Hbhv 
kauśeyāni ca vastrāṇi sumṛdūni laghūni ca 
yaḥ prayacchati devāya so 'śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
rāṅkavā mṛgalomyāś ca kadalyāś ca tathā śubhā 
yo dadyād devadevāya so 'śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
nānābhaktivicitrāṇi cīrajāni navāni ca 
dattvā vāsāṃsi śubhrāṇi rājasūyaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
dvārakāmāhātmye ca
nānādeśasamudbhūtaiḥ suvastraiś ca sukomalaiḥ 
dhūpayitvā subhaktyā ca pradhāpayati mādhavam 
manvantarāṇi vasate tantusaṃkhyaṃ harer gṛhe  Hbhv 
atha vastrārpaṇe niṣiddham
viṣṇudharmottare
nīlīraktaṃ tathā jīrṇaṃ vastram anyadhṛtaṃ tathā 
devadevāya yo dadyāt sa tu pāpair hi yujyate  Hbhv 
atrāpavādaḥ
tatraiva
āvike paṭṭavastre ca nīlīrāgo na duṣyati  Hbhv 
atha yajñopavītam
vastrasyārpaṇamudrāṃ ca pradarśya paridhāpya tat 
upavītaṃ samārpyātha tanmudrāṃ ca pradarśayet  Hbhv 
athopavītārpaṇamāhātmyam
trivṛt śuklaṃ ca pītaṃ ca paṭṭasūtrādinirmitam 
yajñopavītaṃ govinde dattvā vedāntago bhavet  Hbhv 
nandipurāṇe
yajñopavītadānena surebhyo brāhmaṇāya vā 
bhaved vidvāṃś caturvedī śuddhadhīr nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
atha pādyatilakācamanāni
atha pādyaṃ nivedyādāv ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ manoharam 
nirmāya bhāle kṛṣṇasya dadyād ācamanaṃ tataḥ  Hbhv 
atha bhūṣaṇam
tato devāya divyāni bhūṣaṇāni nivedya ca 
paridhāpya yathāyuktaṃ tanmudrāṃ ca pradarśayet  Hbhv 
atha bhūṣaṇārpaṇamāhātmyam
skānde śivomāsaṃvāde
maṇimauktikasaṃyuktaṃ dattvābharaṇam uttamam 
svaśaktyā bhūṣaṇaṃ dattvā agniṣṭomaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
guñjāmātraṃ suvarṇasya yo dadyād viṣṇumūrdhani 
indrasya bhavane tiṣṭhed yāvad āhūtasamplavam  Hbhv 
tasmād ābharaṇaṃ devi dātavyaṃ viṣṇave sadā 
nārāyaṇo bhavet prīto bhaktyā paramayā mubhe  Hbhv 
nandipurāṇe
alaṅkāraṃ tu yo dadyād viprāyātha surāya vā 
sa gacched vāruṇaṃ lokaṃ nānābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ 
jātaḥ pṛthivyāṃ kāena bhaved dvīpapatir nṛpaḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare
karṇābharaṇadānena bhavec chrutidharo naraḥ 
aśvamedham avāpnoti saubhāgyaṃ cāpi vindati  Hbhv 
karṇapūrapradānena śrutiṃ sarvatra vindati  Hbhv 
mūrdhābharaṇadānena bhūr dhanyo bhūtale bhavet 
catuḥsamudravalayāṃ praśāsti ca vasundharām  Hbhv 
tatraiva tṛtīyakhaṇḍe
vibhūṣaṇapradānena mūrdhanyo bhūtale bhavet 
ramyāṇi ratnacitrāṇi saurvarṇāni dvijottamāḥ  Hbhv 
dattvābharaṇajātāni rājasūyaphalaṃ labhet 
pādāṅgulīyadānena guhyakādhipatir bhavet  Hbhv 
pādābharaṇadānena sthānaṃ sarvatra vindati  Hbhv 
śroṇīsūtrapradānena mahīṃ sāgaramekhalām 
praśāsti nihatāmitro nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  Hbhv 
saubhāgyaṃ mahad āpnoti kiṅkiṇīṃ pradadad dhareḥ 
hastāṅgulīyadānena paraṃ saubhāgyam āpnuyāt  Hbhv 
tathaivāṅgadadānena rājā bhavati bhūtale 
keyūradānād bhavati śaturpakṣakṣayaṅkaraḥ  Hbhv 
graiveyakāṇi dattvā ca sarvaśāstrārthavid bhavet 
nāryaś ca vaśagās tasya bhavati dvijapuṅgavāḥ  Hbhv 
dattvā pratisarān mukhyān na bhūtair abhibhūyate  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca tatraiva
kṛtrimaṃ ca pradātavyaṃ tathaivābharaṇaṃ divjāḥ 
pratirūpakṛtaṃ dattvā kṣipraṃ puṣṭyā prayujyate  Hbhv 
pādme
śaṅkhacakragadādīni pādādyavayaveṣu ca 
sauvarṇābharaṇaṃ kṛtvā viṣṇuloke mahīyate  Hbhv 
nārasiṃhe
suvarṇābharaṇair divyair hārakeyūrakuṇḍalaiḥ 
mukuṭaiḥ kaṭakādyaiś ca yo viṣṇuṃ pūjayen naraḥ  Hbhv 
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sarvabhūṣaṇabhūṣitaḥ 
indraloke vased dhīmān yāvad indraś caturdaśa  Hbhv 
garuḍapurāṇe
yasyārcā tiṣṭhate viṣṇor hemabhūṣaṇabhūṣitā 
ratnair muktāviśeṣeṇa ahany ahani vāsava  Hbhv 
kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi tasya vai bhuvane hareḥ 
vāso bhavati devendra kathitaṃ brahmaṇā mama  Hbhv 
yaḥ paśyati naraḥ kṛṣṇaṃ hemabhūṣaṇabhūṣitam 
sakṛd bhaktyā kalau śakra punāty āsaptamaṃ kulam  Hbhv 
 iti
bahulaṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ bhogāt paścād evānulepanam 
puṣpaṃ cecchanti santo 'nulepanārcānubhūṣaṇam  Hbhv 
samprārthyātha prabhuṃ prāgvat nivedya śucipāduke 
vādyagītātapatrānyaiḥ pūjāsthānaṃ punar nayet  Hbhv 
prāgvad dattvāsanādīni gandhaṃ tanmudrayārpayet 
śaṅkhe nidhāya tulasīdalenaivātha candanam  Hbhv 
atha gandhaḥ
āgame
candanāgurukarpūrapaṅkaṃ gandham ihocyate  Hbhv 
gāruḍe
kastūrikāyā dvau bhāgau catvāraś candanasya tu 
kuṅkumasya trayaś caikaḥ śaśinaḥ syāc catuḥsamam  Hbhv 
karpūraṃ candanaṃ darpaḥ kuṅkumaṃ ca catuḥsama 
sarvaṃ gandham iti proktaṃ samastasuravallabham  Hbhv 
vārāhe
karpūraṃ kuṅkumaś caiva varaṃ tagaram eva ca 
rasyaṃ ca candanaṃ caiva aguruṃ guggulaṃ tathā 
etair vilepanaṃ dadyāt śubhaṃ cāru vicakṣaṇaḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottarāgnipurāṇayoḥ
sugandhaiś ca murāmāṃsīkarpūrāgurucandanaiḥ 
tathānyaiś ca śubhair dravyair arcayej jagatīpatim  Hbhv 
vaśiṣṭhasaṃhitāyām
karpūrāgurumiśreṇa candanenānulepayet 
mṛgadarpaṃ viśeṣeṇa abhīṣṭaṃ cakrapāṇinaḥ  Hbhv 
skānde śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde
gandhebhyaś candanaṃ puṇyaṃ candanād agurur varaḥ 
kṛṣṇāgurus tataḥ śreṣṭhaḥ kuṅkumaṃ tu tato 'dhikam  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare
na dātavyaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha ato 'nyad anulepanam 
anulepanamukhyaṃ tu candanaṃ parikīrtitam  Hbhv 
nāradīye
yathā viṣṇoḥ sadābhīṣṭaṃ naivedyaṃ śālisambhavam 
śukenoktaṃ purāṇe ca tathā tulasicandanam  Hbhv 
agastyasaṃhitāyāṃ ca
saṃghṛṣya tulasīkāṣṭhaṃ yo dadyād rāmamūrdhani 
karpūrāgurukastūrīkuṅkumaṃ na ca tatsamam  Hbhv 
athānulepanamāhātmyam
skānde brahmanāradasaṃvāde śaṅkhamāhātmye
vilepayanti deveśaṃ śaṅkhe kṛtvā tu candanam 
paramātmā parāṃ prītiṃ karoti śatvārṣikīm  Hbhv 
gāruḍe
tulasīdalalagnena candanena janārdanam 
vilepayanti yo nityaṃ labhate vāñchitaṃ phalam  Hbhv 
nārasiṃhe
kuṅkumāguruśrīkhaṇḍakardamair acyutākṛtim 
vilipya bhaktyā rājendra kalpakoṭiṃ vased divi  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottarāgnipurāṇayoḥ
candanāgurukarpūrakuṅkumośīrapadmakaiḥ 
anulipto harir bhaktyā varān bhogān prayacchati  Hbhv 
kāleyakaṃ turuṣkaṃ ca raktacandanam uttamam  Hbhv 
nṛṇāṃ bhavanti dattāni puṇyāni puruṣottama  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare
candanenānulepyainaṃ candraloka avāpnuyāt 
śārīrair mānasair duḥkhais tathaiva ca vimucyate  Hbhv 
kuṅkumenānulepyainaṃ sūryaloke mahīyate 
saubhāgyam uttamaṃ loke tathā prāpnoti mānavaḥ  Hbhv 
karpūreṇānulpiyainaṃ vāruṇaṃ lokam āpnuyāt 
śārīrair mānasair duḥkhais tathaiva ca vimucyate  Hbhv 
dattvā mṛgamadaṃ mukhyaṃ yaśasā ca virājate 
dattvā jātaphalakṣodaṃ kriyāsāphalyam aśnute  Hbhv 
ramyeṇāgurusāreṇa anulipya janārdanam 
saubhāgyam atulaṃ loke balaṃ prāpnoti cottamam  Hbhv 
tathā bakulaniryāsair agniṣṭomaphalaṃ labhet 
bakulāgurumiśreṇa candanena sugandhinā 
samālipya jagannāthaṃ puṇḍarīkaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
ekīkṛtya tu sarvāṇi samālipya janārdanam 
aśvamedhasya mukhyasya phalaṃ prāpnoty asaṃśayam  Hbhv 
yo 'nulimpeta deveśaṃ kīrtitair anulepanaiḥ 
pārthivādyāni yāvanti paramāṇūni tatra vai  Hbhv 
tāvad abdāni lokeṣu kāmacārī bhavaty asau 
keśasaugandhyajananaṃ kṛtvā mṛgamadaṃ naraḥ  Hbhv 
sarvakāmasamṛddhasya yajñasya phalam aśnute  Hbhv 
yaḥ prayacchati gandhāni gandhayuktīkṛtāni ca 
gandharvatvaṃ dhruvaṃ tasya saubhāgyaṃ tathottamam  Hbhv 
atha śrītulasīkāṣṭhacandanamāhātmyam
gāruḍe śrīnāradadhundhumāranṛpasaṃvāde
yo dadāti harer nityaṃ tulasīkāṣṭhacandanam 
yugāni vasate svarge hy anantāni narottama  Hbhv 
mahāviṣṇau kalau bhaktyā dattvā tulasīcandanam 
yo 'rcayen mālatīpuṣpair na bhūyastanapo bhavet  Hbhv 
tulasīkāṣṭhasambhūtaṃ candanam yacchato hareḥ 
nirdahet pātakaṃ sarvaṃ pūrvajanmaśataiḥ kṛtam  Hbhv 
sarveṣām api devānāṃ tulasīkāṣṭhacandanam 
pitṝṇāṃ ca viśeṣeṇa sadābhīṣṭaṃ harer yathā  Hbhv 
mṛtyukāle tu samprāpte tulasīkāṣṭhacandanam 
bhavate yasya dehe tu harir bhūtvā hariṃ vrajet  Hbhv 
tāvan malayajaṃ viṣṇor bhāti kṛṣṇāgurur nṛpa 
yāvan na dṛśyate puṇyaṃ tulasīkāṣṭhacandanam  Hbhv 
tāvat kastūrikāmodaḥ karpūrasya sugandhinā 
yāvan na dīyate viṣṇos tulasīkāṣṭhacandanam  Hbhv 
kalau yacchanti ye viṣṇau tulasīkāṣṭhacandanam 
dhundhumāra na vai martyāḥ punar āyānti te bhuvi  Hbhv 
yo hi bhāgavato bhūtvā kalau tulasīcandanam 
nārpayati sadā viṣṇor na sa bhāgavato naraḥ  Hbhv 
prahlādasaṃhitāyāṃ
na tena sadṛśo loke vaiṣṇavo vidyate bhuvi 
yaḥ prayacchati kṛṣṇāya tulasīkāṣṭhacandanam  Hbhv 
tulasīdārujātena candanena kalau naraḥ 
vilipya bhaktito viṣṇuṃ ramate sannidhau hareḥ  Hbhv 
tulasīkāṣṭhajātena candanena vilepanam 
yaḥ kuryād viṣṇutoṣāya kapilāgophalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
tulasīkāṣṭhasambhūtaṃ candanaṃ yas tu sevate 
mṛtyukāle viśeṣeṇa kṛtapāpo 'pi mucyate  Hbhv 
yo dadāti pitṝṇāṃ tu tulasīkāṣṭhacandanam 
teṣāṃ sa kurute tṛptiṃ śrāddhe vai śatavārṣikīm  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare ca
tulasīcandanāktāṅgaḥ kurute kṛṣṇapūjanam 
pūjanena dinaikena labhate śatavārṣikīm  Hbhv 
vilepanārthaṃ kṛṣṇasya tulasīkāṣṭhacandanam 
mandire vasate yasya tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu  Hbhv 
tilaprasthāṣṭakaṃ dattvā yat puṇyaṃ cottarāyaṇe 
tat tulyaṃ jāyate puṇyaṃ prasādāc cakrapāṇinaḥ  Hbhv 
 iti
deyaṃ malayajābhāve śītalatvāt kadambajam 
yathā kiñcit sugandhitvāc candanaṃ devadārujam  Hbhv 
gāruḍe
harer malayajaṃ śreṣṭham abhāve devadārujam  Hbhv 
athānulepe niṣiddhāni
viṣṇudharmottare
dāridryaṃ padmakaṃ kuryād asvāsthyaṃ raktacandanam 
uśīraṃ cittavibhraṃśam anye kuryur upadravam  Hbhv 
 iti
padmakādi na dātavyam aihikaṃ hīcchatā sukham 
mukhyālābhe tu tat sarvaṃ dātavyaṃ bhagavatparaiḥ  Hbhv 
tato bhagavataḥ kuryād anulepād anantaram 
vidvān vicitrair vyajanaiś cāmarair api vījanam  Hbhv 
vījanamāhātmyaṃ ca

anulipya jagannāthaṃ tālavṛntena vījayet 
vāyulokam avāpnoti puruṣas tena karmaṇā  Hbhv 
cāmarair vījayed yas tu devadevaṃ janārdanam 
tilaprasthapradānasya phalam āpnoty asaṃśayam  Hbhv 
vyajanenātha vastreṇa subhaktyā mātariśvana 
devadevasya rājendra kurute tāpavāraṇam  Hbhv

aṣṭamavilāsaḥ
prātararcāsamāpanaḥ
śrīcaitanyaprabhuṃ vande yatpādāśrayavīryataḥ 
saṃgṛhṇāty ākaravrātād raṅko ratnāvalīmayam  Hbhv 
atha dhūpanaṃ
tataś ca dhūpam utsṛjya nīcais tanmudrayārpayet 
kṛṣṇaṃ saṅkīrtayan ghaṇṭam vāmahastena vādayan  Hbhv 
tathā ca bahvṛcapariśiṣṭe 
dhūpasya vijane caiva dhūpenāṅgavidhūpane 
nīrājaneṣu sarveṣu viṣṇor nāmāni kīrtayet  Hbhv 
jayaghoṣaṃ prakurvīta kāruṇyaṃ cābhikīrtayet 
tathā maṅgalaghoṣaṃ ca jagadbījasya ca stutim  Hbhv 
anyatra ca 
tataḥ samarpayed dhūpaṃ ghaṇṭavādyajayasvanaiḥ 
dhūpasthānaṃ samabhyarcya tarjanyā vāmayā hareḥ  Hbhv 
tatra mantraḥ 
vanaspatirasotpanno gandhāḍhyo gandha uttamaḥ 
aghreyaḥ sarvadevānāṃ dhūpo 'yaṃ pratigṛhyatam  Hbhv 
atha dhūpaḥ
vāmanapurāṇe 
ruhikākhyaṃ kaṇo dārusihlakaṃ cāguruḥ sitā 
śaṅkho jātiphalaṃ śrīśe dhūpāni syuḥ priyāṇi vai  Hbhv 
mūlāgame
saguggulvaguruśīrasitājyamadhucandanaiḥ 
sārāṅgāravinikṣiptaiḥ kalpayed dhūpam uttamam  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare ca 
tathaiva śubhagandhā ye dhūpas te jagataḥ pateḥ 
vāsudevasya dharmajñair nivedya dānaveśvara  Hbhv 
atha dhūpeṣu niṣiddhaṃ
na dhūparthe jīvajatam  Hbhv 
tatraivāpavādaḥ
vinā mṛgamadaṃ dhūpe jīvajātaṃ vivarjayet  Hbhv 
kālikāpurāṇe 
na yakṣadhūpaṃ vitaren madhavaya kadacana  Hbhv 
agnipurāṇe 
na sallakijaṃ na tṛṇam na śalkarasasambhrtaṃ dhūpam 
pratyaṅganirmuktam dadyāt kṛṣṇāya buddhimān  Hbhv 
atha dhūpanamāhātmyam
nārasiṃhe śrīmarkandeyasatanikasamvade
mahiṣākhyaṃ gugguluṃ ca ājyayuktaṃ saśarkaram 
dhūpaṃ dadāti rajendra narasiṃhasya bhaktimān  Hbhv 
sa dhūpitaḥ sarvadikṣu sarvapāpavivarjitaḥ 
apsarogaṇayuktena vimānena virājatā 
vāyulokaṃ samāsādya viṣṇuloke mahīyate  Hbhv 
skānde 
ye kṛṣṇaguruṇā kṛṣṇaṃ dhūpayanti kalau narāḥ 
sakarpūreṇa rājendra kṛṣṇatulyā bhavanti te  Hbhv 
sājyena vai guggulunā sudhūpena janārdanam 
dhūpayitvā naro yāti padaṃ tasya sadāśivaṃ  Hbhv 
aguruṃ tu sakarpūradivyacandanasaurabham 
dattvā nityaṃ harer bhaktyā kulānāṃ tārayec chatam  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottaratrtiyakhaṇḍe 
dhūpanam uttamaṃ tadvat sarvakamaphalapradam 
dhūpaṃ turuṣkakaṃ dattvā vahnistomaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
dattvā tu kṛtrimaṃ mukhyaṃ sarvakāmān avāpnuyāt 
gandhayuktakṛtaṃ dattvā yajñagosavaṃ āpnuyāt  Hbhv 
dattvā karpūraniryāsaṃ vājimedhaphalaṃ labhet 
vasante guggulaṃ dattvā vahnistomaṃ avāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
grīṣme candanasāreṇa rājasūyaphalaṃ labhet 
turuṣkasya pradānena pravṛṣy uttamatāṃ labhet  Hbhv 
karpūradānāc charadi rājasūyaṃ avāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
hemante mrgadarpeṇa vājimedhaphalaṃ labhet 
śiśire 'gurusarena sarvamedhaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
padam uttamaṃ āpnoti dhūpadaḥ puṣṭim aśnute 
dhūpalekha yathāivordhvam nityaṃ eva prasarpati 
tathāivordhvagato nityaṃ dhūpadānād bhaven naraḥ  Hbhv 
prahlādasaṃhitāyāṃ ca
yo dadāti harer dhūpam tulasīkāṣṭhavahninā 
śatakratusamaṃ puṇyaṃ go 'yutaṃ labhate phalaṃ  Hbhv 
iti 
dhūpayec ca tathā samyak śrīmadbhagavadālayaṃ 
dhūpaśeṣaṃ tato bhaktyā svayaṃ seveta vaiṣṇavaḥ  Hbhv 
tathā ca brāhme ambarisaṃ prati gautamapraśne 
dhūpaśeṣaṃ tu kṛṣṇasya bhaktyā bhajasi bhūpate 
kṛtvā cārātrikaṃ viṣṇoḥ svamūrdhnā vandase nṛpa  Hbhv 
atha śrībhagavadalayadhūpanamāhātmyaṃ
kṛṣṇāgurusamutthena dhūpena śrīdharālayam 
dhūpayed vaiṣṇavo yas tu sa mukto narakārṇavat  Hbhv 
dhūpaśeṣasevanamāhātmyam
pādme śrīgautamāmbarīṣasaṃvāde 
tīrthakoṭiśatair dhauto yathā bhavati nirmalaḥ 
karoti nirmalaṃ dehaṃ dhūpaśeṣas tathā hareḥ  Hbhv 
na bhayaṃ vidyate tasya bhaumaṃ divyaṃ rāsātalam 
kṛṣṇadhūpāvaśeṣena yasyāṅgaṃ parivāsitam  Hbhv 
nāpado vipadas tasya bhavanti khalu dehinaḥ 
harer dattāvaśeṣena dhūpayed yas tanuṃ sadā  Hbhv 
nāsaukhyaṃ na bhayaṃ duḥkhaṃ nādhijaṃ naiva rogajam 
yaḥ sevayed dhūpaśeṣaṃ viṣṇor adbhutakarmaṇaḥ  Hbhv 
krūrasattvabhayaṃ naiva na ca caurabhayaṃ kvacit 
sevayitvā harer dhūpaṃ nirmālyaṃ padayor jalam  Hbhv 
haribhaktisudhodaye ca
āghrāṇaṃ yad dharer dattaṃ dhūpocchiṣṭasya sarvataḥ 
tadbhavavyāladaṣṭānāṃ bhavet karmaviṣāpahaṃ  Hbhv 
iti 
darśanād api dhūpasya dhūpadānādijaṃ phalam 
sarvaṃ anye'pi vindanti tac cāgre vyatiṃ eṣyati  Hbhv 
atha dīpanaṃ
tathaiṭa dīpam utsṛjya prāgvad ghaṇṭaṃ ca vādayan 
padābjād adṛgabjāntaṃ mudrayoccaiḥ pradīpayet  Hbhv 
tatra mantraḥ
gautamīye
suprakāśo mahātejah sarvatas timirāpahaḥ 
sabāhyābhyantarajyotir dīpo 'yaṃ pratigṛhyatām  Hbhv 
atha dīpaḥ
dīpaṃ prajvalayet śaktau karpūrena ghṛtena vā 
gavyena tatrāsāmārthye tailenāpi sugandhinā  Hbhv 
tathā ca nāradīyakalpe
saghṛtaṃ guggulaṃ dhūpaṃ dīpaṃ goghṛtadīpitam 
samastaparivārāya haraye śraddhayārpayet  Hbhv 
bhaviṣyottare
ghṛtena dīpo dātavyo rājan tailena vā punaḥ  Hbhv 
mahābhārate ca
haviṣā prathamaḥ kalpo dvitīyaś cauṣadhorasaiḥ  Hbhv 
atha dīpe niṣiddhaṃ
bhaviṣyottare
vasāmajjādibhir dīpo na tu deyaḥ kadācana  Hbhv 
mahābhārate
vasāmajjāsthiniryāsair na kāryaḥ puṣṭiṃ icchata  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare tṛtīyakhaṇḍe
nīlaraktadaśaṃ dīpaṃ prayatnena vivarjayet  Hbhv 
kālikāpurāṇe
dīpavṛkṣaś ca kartavyas taijāsādyaiś ca bhairava 
vṛkṣeṣu dīpo dātavyo na tu bhūmau kadācana  Hbhv 
atha dīpamāhātmyaṃ
skānde brahmanāradasaṃvāde
prajvālya devadevasya karpūrena ca dīpakam 
aśvamedhaṃ avāpnoti kulaṃ caiva samuddharet  Hbhv 
atraivānyatra ca
yo dadāti mahīpāla kṛṣṇasyāgre tu dīpakam 
pātakaṃ tu samutsṛjya jyotīrūpaṃ labhet phalam  Hbhv 
vārāhe
dīpaṃ dadāti yo devi madbhaktyā tu vyavasthitaḥ 
nātrāndhatvaṃ bhavet tasya saptajanmani sundari  Hbhv 
yas tu dadyāt pradīpaṃ me sarvataḥ sraddhayānvitaḥ 
svayamprabheṣu deśeṣu tasyotpattir vidhīyate  Hbhv 
haribhaktisudhodaye
dattaṃ svajyotiṣe jyotir yad vistārayati prabhām 
tadvad dharyati sajjyotir dātuḥ pāpatamo 'pahaṃ  Hbhv 
nārasiṃhe
ghṛtena vātha tailena dīpaṃ prajvalayen naraḥ 
viṣṇave vidhivad bhaktyā tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu  Hbhv 
vihāya pāpaṃ sakalaṃ sahasrādityasaprabhaḥ 
jyotiṣmatā vimānena viṣṇuloke mahīyate  Hbhv 
prahlādasaṃhitāyāṃ
ca tulasīpavakenaiva dīpaṃ yaḥ kurute hareḥ 
dīpalakṣasahasrāṇāṃ puṇyaṃ bhavati daityaja  Hbhv 
iti 
paścād dīpaṃ ca taṃ bhaktyā mūrdhnā vandeta vaiṣṇavaḥ 
dhūpasyevekṣaṇāt tasya labhante'nye'pi tat phalam  Hbhv 
kecic cānena dīpena śrīmūrter mūrdhni vaiṣṇavaḥ 
nīrājanaṃ ihecchanti mahānīrājane yathā  Hbhv 
tathā ca rāmārcanacandrikāyāṃ dhūpānantaraṃ dīpaprasaṅge
ārātrikaṃ tu viṣamabahuvartisamanvitam 
abhyarcya rāmacandrāya vāmamadhyam athārpayet  Hbhv 
namo dīpeśvarāyeti dadyāt puṣpāñjaliṃ tataḥ 
avadhūpyābhyarcya vādyair mūrdhni nīrājayet prabhum  Hbhv 
iti 
ata eveṣyate tasya karābhyāṃ vandanaṃ ca taiḥ 
nāma cārātrikety ādi vartyo 'pi bahulāḥ samāḥ  Hbhv 
prasaṅgāl likhyate'traiva śrīmadbhagavadālaye 
dīpadānasya māhātmyaṃ kārttikīyaṃ ca tad vinā  Hbhv 
atha śrībhagavadālaye dīpapradānamāhātmyam
viṣṇudharmottare prathamakāṇḍe ff mixed up
dīpadānāt paraṃ dānaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati 
keśavāyatane kṛtvā dīpavṛkṣāmanoharam 
atīva bhrājate lakṣmyā divam āsādya sarvataḥ  Hbhv 
dīpamālāṃ prayacchanti ye narāḥ śārṅgiṇo gṛhe 
bhavanti te candrasamāḥ svargam āsādya mānavāḥ  Hbhv 
dīpāgāraṃ naraḥ kṛtvā kūtāgāranibhaṃ śubham 
keśavālayam āsādya loke bhāti sa śakravat  Hbhv 
yathojjvalo bhaved dīpaḥ sampradātāpi yādava 
tathā nityojjvalo loke nākapṛṣṭhe virājate  Hbhv 
sadīpe ca yathā dese cakṣūṃsi phalavanti ca 
tathā dīpasya dataro bhavanti saphalekṣanaḥ  Hbhv 
ekādaśyāṃ ca dvādaśyāṃ pratipakṣaṃ tu yo naraḥ 
dīpaṃ dadāti kṛṣṇāya tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu  Hbhv 
suvarṇamaṇimuktāḍhyam manojñam atisundaram 
dīpamālākulaṃ divyaṃ vimānam adhirohati  Hbhv 
padmasutrodbhavaṃ vartti gandhatailena dīpakān 
virogaḥ subhagaś caiva dattvā bhavati mānavaḥ  Hbhv 
dīpadanaṃ mahāpuṇyam anyadeveṣv api dhruvam 
kiṃ punar vāsudevasyānantasya tu mahātmanaḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva tṛtīyakhaṇḍe
dīpaṃ cakṣuḥpradaṃ dadyāt tathaivordhvagatipradam 
ūrdhvaṃ yathā dīpaśikhā dātā cordhvagatis tathā  Hbhv 
yāvad akṣinimeṣāṇi dīpo devālaye jvalet 
tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi nākapṛṣṭhe mahīyate  Hbhv 
brhannāradīye vitihotraṃ prati yajñadhvajasya pūrvajanmavṛttakathane
pradīpaḥ sthāpitas tatra suratārthaṃ dvijottama 
tenāpi mama duṣkarma nihśeṣaṃ kṣayam agatam  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharme ca
vilīyate svahaste tu svatantre sati dīpakaḥ 
mahāphalo viṣṇugṛhe na datto narakāya saḥ  Hbhv 
nāradīye mohinīṃ prati śrīrukmāṅgadoktau
tiṣṭhantu bahuvittāni dānārthaṃ varavarṇini 
hṛdayāyāsakartṛṇi dīpadānād divaṃ vrajet  Hbhv 
tasyāpy abhāve subhage paradīpaprabodhanam 
kartavyaṃ bhaktibhāvena sarvadānādhikaś ca yat  Hbhv 
iti 
sada kalaviśeṣe'pi bhaktyā bhagavadālaye 
mahādīpapradānasya mahimāpy atra likhyāte  Hbhv 
atha mahādīpamāhātmyam
viṣṇudharmottare prathamakhaṇḍe
mahāvarttiḥ sadā deyā bhūmipāla mahāphalā 
kṛṣṇapakṣe viśeṣeṇa tatrāpi sa viśeṣataḥ  Hbhv 
amāvasyā ca nirdiṣṭā dvādaśī ca mahāphalā 
aśvayujyām atītāyāṃ kṛṣṇapakṣaś ca yo bhavet  Hbhv 
amāvasyā tadā puṇyā dvādaśī ca viśeṣataḥ 
devasya dakṣiṇe pārśve deyā tailatulā nṛpa  Hbhv 
palāṣṭakayutāṃ rājan vartti tatra ca dāpayet 
vāsasā tu samagreṇa sopavāso jitendriyaḥ  Hbhv 
mahāvarttidvayam idaṃ sakṛd dattvā mahāmate 
svarlokaṃ suciraṃ bhuktvā jāyate bhūtale yadā  Hbhv 
tadā bhavati lakṣmīvān jayadraviṇasamyutaḥ 
rāṣṭre ca jāyate svasmin deśe ca nagare tathā  Hbhv 
kule ca rājaśārdūla tatra syād dīpavatprabhaḥ 
pratyujjvalaś ca bhavati yuddheṣu kalaheṣu ca  Hbhv 
khyātiṃ yāti tathā loke sadguṇānāṃ ca sadguṇaiḥ 
ekam apy atha yo dadyād abhīṣṭatamayor dvayoḥ  Hbhv 
manuṣye sarvam āpnoti yad uktaṃ te mahānagha 
svarge tathātvam āpnoti bhogakāle tu yādava  Hbhv 
samānyasya tu dīpasya rājan dānaṃ mahāphalam 
kiṃ punar mahato dīpasyātreyatta na vidyate  Hbhv 
atha sonamalinadivastravarttya dīpadananisedhaḥ
śoṇaṃ vādarakaṃ vastraṃ jīrṇaṃ malinam eva ca 
upabhuktaṃ na vā dadyāt varttikārthaṃ kadācana  Hbhv 
iti 
svayam anyena vā dattaṃ dīpān na śrīharer haret 
nirvāpayen na hiṃsāc ca śubhaṃ icchan kadācana  Hbhv 
atha dīpanirvāpanādidoṣaḥ
viṣṇudharmottare prathamakhaṇḍe
dattvā dīpo na hartavyas tena karma vijānatā 
nirvāpanaṃ ca dīpasya hiṃsanaṃ ca vigarhitam  Hbhv 
yaḥ kuryād dhiṃsanaṃ tena karmaṇā puṣpitekṣaṇaḥ 
dīpahartā bhaved andhaḥ kaṇo nirvāṇakṛd bhavet  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharme ca nārakān prati śrīdharmarājoktau
yuṣmābhir yauvanonmādam uditair avivekibhiḥ 
dyutodyotaya govindagehād dīpaḥ purā hṛtaḥ  Hbhv 
tenādya narake ghore kṣuttṛṣṇāparipīḍitāḥ 
bhavanti patitās tīvre śītavātavidāritāḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrīpulastyoktau ca
tasmād āyātane viṣṇor dadyād dīpān dvijottama 
tāmś ca dattvā na hiṃseta na ca tailaviyojitān  Hbhv 
kurvīta dīpahantā ca mūko 'ndho jāyate mṛtaḥ 
andhe tamasi duṣpare narake pacyate kila  Hbhv 
bhūmau dīpadananisedhaḥ
kālikāpurāṇe
dīpavṛkṣaś ca kartavyas taijāsādyaiś ca bhairava 
vṛkṣeṣu dīpo dātavyo na tu bhūmau kadācana  Hbhv 
atha naivedyaṃ
dattvā puṣpāñjaliṃ pīṭhaṃ padyam ācamanaṃ tathā 
kṛtvā pātreṣu kṛṣṇāyārpayed bhojyaṃ yathāvidhi  Hbhv 
atha naivedyarpanavidhiḥ
astraṃ japtvāmbunā prokṣya naivedyaṃ cakramudrayā 
saṃrakṣya prokṣayed vāyubījajaptajalena ca  Hbhv
