tena saṃśoṣya taddoṣam agnibījaṃ ca dakṣiṇe 
dhyātvā karatale'nyat tat pṛṣṭhe saṃyojya darśyate  Hbhv 
tadutthavahninā tasya śuṣkadoṣaṃ hṛdā dahet 
tataḥ karatale savye'mṛtabījaṃ vicintayet  Hbhv 
tatpṛṣṭhe dakṣiṇaṃ panitalaṃ saṃyojya darśayet 
tadutthayā nivedyaṃ tat siced amṛtadhārayā  Hbhv 
jalena mūlajaptena prokṣya tac cāmṛtātmakam 
sarvaṃ vicintya saṃspṛśya mūlaṃ vārāṣṭakaṃ japet  Hbhv 
amṛtīkṛtya tad dhenumudrayā salilādibhiḥ 
tac ca kṛṣṇaṃ ca sampūjya gṛhitvā kusumāñjalim  Hbhv 
śrīkṛṣṇaṃ prārthya tadvaktrāt tejo dhyātvā vinirgatam 
saṃyojya ca nivedyaitat patraṃ vāmena saṃspṛśan  Hbhv 
dakṣeṇa pāṇinādāya gandhapuṣpānvitaṃ jalam 
svāhāntaṃ mūlam uccārya tajjalaṃ visṛjed bhuvi  Hbhv 
tat pāṇibhyāṃ samutthāya nivedyaṃ tulasīyutam 
patrāḍhyaṃ tasya mantreṇa bhaktyā bhāgavate'rpayet  Hbhv 
nivedanamantraś cayaṃ
nivedayami bhavate jusanedaṃ havir hare  Hbhv 
iti 
amṛtopastaranam asi svāhety uccārayan hareḥ 
dattvātha vidhivad vārigaṇḍūṣaṃ vāmapāṇinā 
darśayed grāsamudrāṃ tu praphullotpalasannibham  Hbhv 
prāṇādimudrāhastena dakṣiṇena tu darśayet 
mantraiś caturthīsvāhāntais tārādyais tattadāhvayaiḥ  Hbhv 
tataḥ spṛśamś ca karayor aṅguṣṭhābhyām anāmike 
pradarśayen nivedyasya mudrāṃ tasya manuṃ japan  Hbhv 
mantraś cāyaṃ kramadīpikāyām  
nandajo 'mbumanubinduyuṅ natiḥ
pārśvarāmarudavātmane ni ca 
ruddhaṅeyutanivedyam ātmabhūr
māsapārśvam anilas tathā'miyuk  Hbhv 
nivedyasya manutvena svābhīṣṭaṃ manum eva te 
ekāntino japantas tu grāsamudrāṃ vitanvate  Hbhv 
na ca dhyāyante te kṛṣṇavaktrāt tejovinirgamam 
mañjulavyavahāreṇa bhojayanti hariṃ mudā  Hbhv 
anyatra ca
śālībhaktaṃ subhaktaṃ śiśirakarasitaṃ pāyasaṃ pūpasūpam
lehyaṃ peyaṃ sucūṣyaṃ sitam amṛtaphalaṃ ghārikādyaṃ sukhādyam 
ājyaṃ prājyaṃ samijyaṃ nayanarucikaraṃ vājikailamarīca
svādiyaḥ śākarājiparikaram amṛtāhārajoṣaṃ juṣasva  Hbhv 
kiṃ cagaruḍapurāṇe
naivedyaṃ parayā bhaktyā ghaṇṭādyair jayanisvanaiḥ 
nīrājanaiś ca haraye dadyād dīpāsanaṃ budhaḥ  Hbhv 
atha naivedyapatrāṇi
skānde śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde
naivedyapātraṃ vakṣyāmi keśavasya mahātmanaḥ 
hairaṇyaṃ rajataṃ tāmraṃ kaṃsyaṃ mṛnmayam eva ca 
palāśaṃ padmapatraṃ ca pātraṃ viṣṇor atipriyam  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare
patrāṇāṃ tu pradānena narakaṃ ca na gacchati  Hbhv 
patraparimanaṃ
devīpurāṇe
ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgulaṃ pātram uttamaṃ parikīrtitam 
madhyamaṃ ca tribhāgonaṃ kanyasaṃ dvādaśāṅgulam 
vasvaṅgulavihīnaṃ tu na pātraṃ kārayet kvacit  Hbhv 
atha bhojyani
ekādaśaskande 
guḍapāyasasarpīṃṣi saṣkulyāpūpamodakān 
saṃyāvadadhisūpāmś ca naivedyaṃ sati kalpayet  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
yad yad iṣṭatamaṃ loke yac cātipriyam ātmanaḥ 
tat tan nivedayen mahyaṃ tad ānantyāya kalpate  Hbhv 
aṣṭamaskānde 
naivedyaṃ cādhiguṇavad dadyāt puruṣatuṣṭidam  Hbhv 
baudhāyanasmṛtau ca
nānāvidhānnapānaiś ca bhakṣanādyair manoharaiḥ 
naivedyaṃ kalpayed viṣṇos tadabhāve ca pāyasaṃ
kevalaṃ ghṛtasaṃyuktaṃ  Hbhv 
vāmanapurāṇe
haviṣā saṃskṛtā ye ca yavagodhūmaśalayaḥ 
tilamudgādayo māṣā vrīhayaś ca priyā hareḥ  Hbhv 
gāruḍe
annaṃ caturvidhaṃ puṇyam guṇāḍhyaṃ cāmṛtopamam 
niṣpaṇṇaṃ svagṛhe yad vā śraddhayā kalpayed dhareḥ  Hbhv 
bhaviṣye
puṣpaṃ dhūpaṃ tathā dīpaṃ naivedyaṃ sumanoharam 
khaṇḍalaḍḍukaśrīvestakāsārāśokavartikāḥ  Hbhv 
svastikollasikadugdhatilaveṣṭakilāṭikāḥ 
phalāni caiva pakvāni nāgaraṅgādikāni ca  Hbhv 
anyāni vidhinā dattvā bhakṣyāṇi vividhāni ca 
evam ādini dāpayed bhaktito nrpa  Hbhv 
vārāhe
yas tu bhāgavato devi annād yena tu prīṇayet 
prīṇitas tiṣṭhate'sau vā bahujanmāni mādhavi  Hbhv 
sarvavrīhimayaṃ gṛhyam śubhaṃ sarvarasānvitam 
mantreṇa me pradīyeta na kiṃcid api saṃspṛśet  Hbhv 
iṅgudiphalabilvāni badarāmalakāni ca 
kharjurāmś cāsanāmś caiva mānavāmś ca parūṣakān  Hbhv 
śāloḍḍambarikāmś caiva tathā plakṣaphalāni ca 
paippalaṃ kaṇṭakīyaṃ ca tumburuṃ ca priyaṅgukam  Hbhv 
marīcaṃ śiṃśapākaṃ ca bhallātakaramardakam 
drākṣāṃ ca dāḍimaṃ caiva piṇḍakharjūram eva ca  Hbhv 
sauvīraṃ kelikaṃ caiva tathā śubhaphalāni ca 
piṇḍārakaphalaṃ caiva punnāgaphalam eva ca  Hbhv 
śamīṃ caiva kavīraṃ ca kharjūrakamahāphalam 
kumudasya phalaṃ caiva vaheḍakaphalaṃ tathā  Hbhv 
ajaṃ karkoṭakaṃ caiva tathā talaphalāni ca 
kadambaḥ kaumudaṃ caiva dvividhaṃ sthalakañjayoḥ  Hbhv 
piṇḍikaṇḍeti vikhyātaṃ vaṃśanīpaṃ tataḥ param 
madhukaṇḍeti vikhyātaṃ māhiṣaṃ kaṇḍam eva ca  Hbhv 
karamardakakandaṃ ca tathā nilotpalasya ca 
mṛṇālaṃ pauṣkaraṃ caiva śālūkasya phalaṃ tathā  Hbhv 
ete cānye ca bahavaḥ kāṇḍamūlaphalāni ca 
etāni copayojyāni ye mayā parikalpitāḥ  Hbhv 
mūlakasya tataḥ śākam ciñcaśākaṃ tathaiva ca 
śākaṃ caiva kalāyasya sarṣapasya tathaiva ca  Hbhv 
vaṃsakasya tu śākaṃ ca śākam eva kalambikam 
ārdrakasya ca śākaṃ vai pālaṅkaṃ śākam eva ca  Hbhv 
ambiloḍakaśākaṃ ca kāśaṃ kaumārakaṃ tathā 
śukamaṇḍalapatraṃ ca dvāv eva taruvānakau  Hbhv 
carasya caiva śākaṃ ca madhukoḍḍumbaraṃ tathā 
ete cānye ca bahavah śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ 
karmaṇyāś caiva sarve vai ye mayā parikīrtitāḥ  Hbhv 
vrīhīṇāṃ ca pravakṣyāmi upayogāmś ca mādhavi 
ekacittaṃ samādhāya tat sarvaṃ śṛṇu sundari  Hbhv 
dharmādhārmikaraktaṃ ca sugandhaṃ raktaśālikam 
dīrghaśūkaṃ mahāśāliṃ varakuṅkumapatrakam  Hbhv 
grāmaśāliṃ samadrāśām saśrīśāṃ kuśaśālikām 
yavāś ca dvividhā jñeyāḥ karmaṇyā mama sundari  Hbhv 
karmaṇyāś caiva mudgāś ca tilāḥ kṛṣṇāḥ kulatthakāḥ 
godhūmakaṃ mahāmudgamudgāṣṭakam avāṭajit  Hbhv 
karmaṇy etāni coktāni vyajanāni priyānvitān 
pratigṛhṇāmy ahaṃ hy etān sarvān bhāgavatān priyān  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
ye mayaivopayojyāni gavyaṃ dadhi payo ghṛtam  Hbhv 
skānde ca brahmanāradasaṃvāde
haviḥ śalyodanaṃ divyam ājyayuktaṃ saśarkaram 
naivedyaṃ devadevāya yāvakaṃ pāyasaṃ tathā  Hbhv 
naivedyānām abhāve tu phalāni vinivedayet 
phalānām apy abhāve tu tṛṇagulmauṣadhīr api  Hbhv 
auṣadhīnām alābhe tu toyaṃ ca vinivedayet 
tadalābhe tu sarvatra mānasaṃ pravaraṃ smṛtam  Hbhv 
skānde mahendraṃ prati śrīnāradavacanaṃ
yacchanti tulasīśākaṃ śrutaṃ ye mādhavāgrataḥ 
kalpāntaṃ viṣṇuloke tu vasanti pitṛbhiḥ saha  Hbhv 
atha naivedyaniṣiddhāni
hāritasmṛtau
nābhakṣyaṃ naivedyārthe bhakṣyesv apy ajāmahiṣīkṣīraṃ pañcanakhā matsyāś ca  Hbhv 
dvārakāmāhātmye
nīlīkṣetraṃ vāpayanti mūlakaṃ bhakṣayanti ye 
naivāsti narakottārah kalpakoṭiśatair api  Hbhv 
vārāhe
māhiṣaṃ cāvikaṃ cājam ayajñīyam udāhṛtam  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
māhiṣaṃ varjayen mahyaṃ kṣīraṃ dadhi ghṛtaṃ yadi  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare tṛtīyakhaṇḍe
abhakṣyaṃ capy ahṛdyaṃ ca naivedyaṃ na nivedayet 
keśakīṭāvapannaṃ ca tathā cāvihitaṃ ca yat  Hbhv 
mūṣikālāṅgulopetam avadhūtam avakṣutam 
uḍḍumbaraṃ kapitthaṃ ca tathā dantaśaṭhaṃ ca yat 
evam ādīni devāya na deyāni kadācana  Hbhv 
athābhakṣyāṇi
kaurme
vṛntākaṃ jālikāśākaṃ kusumbhāśmantakaṃ tathā 
palāṇḍuṃ laśunaṃ śuklam niryāsaṃ caiva varjayet  Hbhv 
gṛñjanaṃ kiṃśukaṃ caiva kukuṇḍaṃ ca tathaiva ca 
uḍumbaram alābuṃ ca jagdhvā patati vai dvijaḥ  Hbhv 
vaiṣṇave
bhuñjītoddhṛtasārāṇi na kadācin nareśvara  Hbhv 
skānde
na bhakṣayati vṛntākaṃ tasya dūrataro hariḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ cānyatra
dorbhyāṃ pādbhyāṃ ca jānubhyām urasā śirasā dṛśā 
manasā vacasā ceti praṇāmo 'ṣṭāṅga īritaḥ  Hbhv  
jānubhyām caiva bāhubhyāṃ śirasā vacasā dhiyā 
pañcāṅgakaḥ praṇāmaḥ syāt pūjāsu pravarāv imau  Hbhv  
ata evoktaṃ yāmale
yatra madyaṃ tathā māṃsam tathā vṛntākamūlake 
nivedayen naiva tatra harer aikāntikī ratiḥ  Hbhv 
atha naivedyarpanamāhātmyaṃ
skānde
naivedyāni manojñāni kṛṣṇasyāgre nivedayet 
kalpāntaṃ tatpitṝṇaṃ tu tṛptir bhavati śāśvatī  Hbhv 
phalāni yacchate yo vai suhṛdyāni nareśvara 
kalpāntaṃ jāyate tasya saphalaṃ ca manorathaḥ  Hbhv 
nārasiṃhe
haviḥ śālyodanaṃ diyyam ājyayuktaṃ saśarkaram 
nivedya narasiṃhāya yāvakaṃ pāyasaṃ tathā  Hbhv 
samās taṇḍulaśaṅkhyāyā yāvatyas tāvatīr nṛpa 
viṣṇuloke mahābhogan bhuñjānas te savaiṣṇavāḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare
annadas tṛptim āpnoti svargalokaṃ ca gacchati 
dattvā ca saṃvibhāgāya tathaivānnam atandritaḥ 
trailokyatarpite puṇyaṃ tatkṣanāt samavāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
akṣayyam annapānaṃ ca pitṛbhyaś copatiṣṭhate 
odanaṃ vyajanopetam dattvā svargam avāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
paramānnaṃ tathā dattvā tṛptim āpnoti śaśvatim 
viṣṇulokam avāpnoti kulam uddharate tathā  Hbhv 
ghṛtaudanapradānena dīrgham āyur avāpnuyāt 
dadhyodanapradānena śriyam āpnoty anuttamām  Hbhv 
kṣīrodanapradānena dīrghajīvitam āpnuyāt 
ikṣūṇāṃ ca pradānena paraṃ saubhāgyam aśnute  Hbhv 
ratnānāṃ caiva bhāgī syāt svargalokaṃ ca gacchati 
phāṇitasya pradānena agnyādhānaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
tathā guḍapradānena kāmitābhīṣṭam āpnuyāt  Hbhv 
nivedyekṣurasaṃ bhaktyā paraṃ saubhāgyam āpnuyāt 
sarvān kāmān avāpnoti kṣaudraṃ yaś ca prayacchati  Hbhv 
tad eva tuhitopetam rājasūyam avāpnuyāt 
vahniṣṭomam avāpnoti yavākasya nivedakaḥ 
atirātram avāpnoti tathā pūpanivedakaḥ  Hbhv 
vaidalānāṃ ca bhakṣyāṇāṃ dānāt kāmān avāpnuyāt 
dīrghajīvitam āpnoti ghṛtapūranivedakaḥ  Hbhv 
modakānāṃ pradānena kāmān āpnoty abhīpsitān  Hbhv 
nānāvidhānāṃ bhakṣyāṇāṃ dānāt svargam avāpnuyāt 
bhojanīyapradānena tṛptim āpnoty anuttamām  Hbhv 
tathā lehyapradānena saubhāgyam adhigacchati 
balavarṇam avāpnoti cūṣyāṇāṃ ca nivedane  Hbhv 
kulmāṣollāsikadātā vahnyādheyaṃ phalaṃ labhet 
tathā kṛṣāradānena vahniṣṭomam avāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
dhanānāṃ kṣaudrayuktānāṃ lājānāṃ ca nivedakaḥ 
mukhyaṃ caiva śaktūnāṃ vahniṣṭomam avāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
vānaprasthāśritaṃ puṇyam labhec chākanivedakaḥ 
dattvā haritakaṃ caiva tad eva phalam āpnuyāt  Hbhv 
dattvā śākāni ramyāṇi viśokas tv abhijāyate 
dattvā ca vyajanārthāya tathopakaraṇāni ca  Hbhv 
sukule labhate janma kandamūlanivedakaḥ 
nīlotpalavidarīṇāṃ taruṭasya tathā dvijaḥ  Hbhv 
kandadānād avāpnoti vānaprasthaphalaṃ śubham 
trapuṣer vārukaṃ dattvā puṇḍarīkaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
karkandhuvadare dattvā tathā pāraivataṃ kalam 
parūṣakaṃ tathābhraṃ ca panasaṃ nārikelakam  Hbhv 
bhavyaṃ mocaṃ tathā cocam kharjūram atha dāḍimam 
āmrātakasruvāmloṭaphalamānapriyālakam  Hbhv 
jambūbilvāmalaṃ caiva jātyaṃ vīṇātakaṃ tathā 
nāraṅgabījapūre ca bījaphalguphalany api  Hbhv 
evam ādīni divyani yaḥ phalāni prayacchati 
tathā kandāni mukhyāni devadevāya bhaktitaḥ  Hbhv 
kriyāsāphalyam āpnoti svargalokaṃ tathaiva ca 
prāpnoti phalam ārogyam mṛdvīkānāṃ nivedakaḥ  Hbhv 
rasān mukhyān avāpnoti saubhāgyam api cottamam 
āmrair abhyarcya deveśam aśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
mocakaṃ panasaṃ jambū tathānyat kumbhāliphalam 
prācīnāmalakaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ madhukoḍḍumbarasya ca 
yatnapakvam api grāhyaṃ kadalīphalam uttamam  Hbhv 
haribhaktisudhodaye ca
yat kiñcid alpaṃ naivedyam bhaktabhaktirasaplutam 
pratibhojayati śrīśas taddātṝn svasukhaṃ drutam iti  Hbhv 
tataḥ prāgvad vicitrāṇi panakāny uttamāni ca 
sugandhi śītalaṃ svacchaṃ jalam apy arpayet tataḥ  Hbhv 
atha panakāni
tanmāhātmyaṃ ca
viṣṇudharmottare
pānakāni sugandhīni śītalāni viśeṣataḥ 
nivedya devadevāya vājimedham avāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
tvagelānāgakusumakarpūrasitasaṃyutaiḥ 
sitākṣaudraguḍopetair gandhavarṇaguṇānvitaiḥ  Hbhv 
bījapūrakanāraṅgasahakārasamanvitaiḥ 
rājasūyam avāpnoti panakair viniveditaiḥ  Hbhv 
nivedya nārikelāmbuvahniṣṭomaphalaṃ labhet 
sarvakāmavahā nadyo nityaṃ yatra manoramāḥ 
tatra pānapradā yānti yatra rāmā guṇānvitāḥ  Hbhv 
iti 
itthaṃ samarpya naivedyam dattvā javanikaṃ tataḥ 
bahirbhūya yathāsakti japaṃ sandhyānam ācaret  Hbhv 
atha dhyānam
brahmeśādyaiḥ parita ṛṣibhiḥ sūpaviṣṭaiḥ sameto
lakṣmyā śiñjadvalayakarayā sādaraṃ vījyamana 
marmakrīḍaprahasitamukho hāsayan paṅktibhoktṝn
bhuṅkte pātre kanakaghaṭite ṣaḍrasaṃ śrīrameśaḥ  Hbhv 
iti 
ekantibhiś cātmakṛtaṃ savayasyasya gokule 
yaśodālālyamānasya dhyeyaṃ kṛṣṇasya bhojanam  Hbhv 
atha homaḥ
nityaṃ cāvaśyakaṃ homaṃ kuryāt śaktyanusārataḥ 
homāśaktau tu kurvīta japaṃ tasya caturguṇam  Hbhv 
ke'py evaṃ manvate'vaśyam nityahomaṃ sadācaret 
puraścaranahomasyāśaktau hi sa vidhir mataḥ  Hbhv 
pūrvaṃ dīkṣāvidhau homavidhiś ca likhitaḥ kiyān 
tadvistāraś ca vijñeyas tattacchāstrāt tadicchubhiḥ  Hbhv 
samāptiṃ bhojane dhyātvā dattvā gaṇḍūṣikaṃ jalam 
amṛtāpidhānam asi svāhety uccārayet sudhīḥ  Hbhv 
visṛjed devavaktre tat tejaḥ saṃhāramudrayā 
naikantī tejasaḥ kuryān niṣkrāntiṃ iva saṅkramam  Hbhv 
atha balidānam
tato javanikā vidvān apasārya yathāvidhi 
viṣvaksenāya bhagavannaivedyāṃśaṃ nivedayet  Hbhv 
tathā ca pañcarātre śrīnāradavacanam
viśvaksenāya dātavyaṃ naivedyaṃ tacchatāṃśakam 
pādodakaṃ prasādaṃ ca liṅge caṇḍeśvarāya ca  Hbhv 
tadvidhiḥ
mukhyād īsānataḥ pātrān naivedyāṃśaṃ samuddharet 
sarvadevasvarupāya parāya parameṣṭhine  Hbhv 
śrīkṛṣṇasevayuktāya viṣvaksenāya te namaḥ 
ity uktvā śrīharer vāme tīrthaklinnaṃ samarpayet  Hbhv 
sataṃsaṃ vā sahasrāṃśam anyathā niṣphalaṃ bhavet  Hbhv 
paścāc ca balir ity ādi ślokāv uccārya vaiṣṇavaḥ 
sarvebhyo vaiṣṇavebhyas tacchatāṃsaṃ vinivedayet  Hbhv 
tau ca ślokau 
balir vibhīṣaṇo bhīṣmaḥ kapilo nārado 'rjunaḥ 
prahlādaś cāmbarīṣaś ca vasur vāyusutaḥ sivaḥ  Hbhv 
viṣvaksenoddhavākrūraḥ sanakādyāḥ śukādayaḥ 
śrīkṛṣṇasya prasādo 'yaṃ sarve gṛhṇantu vaiṣṇavāḥ  Hbhv 
idaṃ yadyapi yujyeta darpaṇārpaṇataḥ param 
tathāpi bhaktavātsalyāt kṛṣṇasyātrāpi sambhavet  Hbhv 
atha balidanamāhātmyaṃ
nārasiṃhe
tatas tadannaśeṣeṇa pārṣadebhyaḥ samantataḥ 
puṣpākṣatair vimiśreṇa baliṃ yas tu prayacchati  Hbhv 
balinā vaiṣṇavenātha tṛptaḥ santo divaukasaḥ 
śāntiṃ tasya prayacchanti śriyam ārogyam eva ca  Hbhv 
atha jalagandusadyarpanaṃ
upalipya tato bhūmiṃ punar gāṇḍūṣikaṃ jalam 
dadyāt trir agre kṛṣṇasya tato 'smai dantasodhanam  Hbhv 
punar ācamanaṃ dattvā śrīpāṇyoḥ śrīmukhasya ca 
mārjanāyāṃśukaṃ dattvā sarvāṇy aṅgāni mārjayet  Hbhv 
paridhāpy apare vastre punar dattvāsanāntaram 
padyam ācamanīyaṃ ca pūrvavat punar arpayet  Hbhv 
candanāgurucūrṇādi pradadyāt karamārjanam 
karpūradyāsyavāsaṃ ca tāmbūlaṃ tulasīm api  Hbhv 
atha mukhavasadimāhātmyaṃ
viṣṇudharmottare trtīyakhaṇḍe
pūgajātiphalaṃ dattvā jātipatraṃ tathaiva ca 
lavaṅgaphalakakkolamelakataphalaṃ tathā  Hbhv 
tāmbūlīnāṃ kiśalayaṃ svargalokam avāpnuyāt 
saubhāgyam atulaṃ loke tathā rūpam anuttamam  Hbhv 
skānde
tāmbūlaṃ ca sakarpūram sapūgaṃ naranāyaka 
kṛṣṇāya yacchati prītyā tasya tuṣṭo hariḥ sadā  Hbhv 
atha punar gandharpanaṃ
divyaṃ gandhaṃ punar dattvā yatheṣṭam anulepanaiḥ 
divyair vicitraiḥ śrīkṛṣṇam bhakticchedena lepayet  Hbhv 
ramyāṇi cordhvapuṇḍrāṇi sadvarṇena yathāspadam 
sugandhinānulepena kṛṣṇasya racayettarām  Hbhv 
tathā cāgame dhyānaprasaṅge
lalāṭe hṛdaye kukṣau kaṇṭhe bahvoś ca pārśvayoḥ 
virājatordhvapuṇḍreṇa sauvarṇena vibhūṣitam  Hbhv 
iti 
divyāni kañcukoṣṇīṣakāñcyādīni parāṇy api 
vastrāṇi suvicitrāṇi śrīkṛṣṇaṃ paridhāpayet  Hbhv 
tato divyakirīṭādibhūṣaṇani yathāruci 
vicitradivyamālyāni paridhāpya vibhūṣayet  Hbhv 
atha mahārajopacararpanaṃ
tataś ca cāmaracchatrapādukādīn parān api 
mahārājopacārāmś ca dattvādarśaṃ pradarśayet  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare
yathādeśaṃ yathākalaṃ rājaliṅgaṃ surālaye 
dattvā bhavati rājaiva nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  Hbhv 
tatra cāmaramāhātmyaṃ
tathā cāmaradānena śrīmān bhavati bhūtale 
mucyate ca tathā pāpaiḥ svargalokaṃ ca gacchati  Hbhv 
chatrasya māhātmyaṃ
tatraiva
chatraṃ bahuśalākaṃ ca jhallarīvastrasaṃyutam 
divyavastraiś ca saṃyuktaṃ hemadaṇḍasamanvitam  Hbhv 
yaḥ prayacchati kṛṣṇasya chatralakṣayutair vṛtaḥ 
prārthyate so 'maraiḥ sarvaiḥ krīḍate pitṛbhiḥ saha  Hbhv 
tatraiva vānyatra
rājā bhavati loke'smin chatraṃ dattvā dvijottamaḥ 
nāpnoti ripujaṃ duḥkhaṃ saṅgrāme ripujid bhayet  Hbhv 
upānatsampradānena vimānam adhirohati 
yatheṣṭaṃ tena lokeṣu vicaraty amaraprabhaḥ  Hbhv 
dhvajasya māhātmyaṃ
tatraiva
lokeṣu dhvajabhūtaḥ syād dattvā viṣṇor varaṃ dhvajam 
śakralokam avāpnoti bahūn abdagaṇān naraḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
yuktaṃ pītapatākābhir nivedya garuḍadhvajam 
keśavāya dvijaśreṣṭhaḥ sarvaloke mahīyate iti  Hbhv 
yatprasāde dhvajāropamāhātmyaṃ likhitaṃ purā 
tad atrāpy akhilaṃ jñeyaṃ tatrātratyaṃ idaṃ tathā  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca bhaviṣye
viṣṇor dhvaje tu sauvarṇam daṇḍaṃ kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ 
patākā cāpi pītā syād garuḍasya samīpagā  Hbhv 
vyajanasya māhātmyaṃ
viṣṇudharmottare
talavrṇtapradānena nirvṛtiṃ prāpnuyāt param  Hbhv 
vitanasya māhātmyaṃ
tatraiva
vitānakapradānena sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate 
paraṃ nirvṛtim āpnoti yatra tatrābhijāyate  Hbhv 
khadgadīnāṃ māhātmyaṃ
dattvā nistriṃśakān mukhyān śatrubhir nābhibhūyate 
dattvā tadbandhanaṃ mukhyam agnyādheyaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
patadgrahaṃ tathā dattvā śubhadas tv abhijāyate 
pādapīṭhapradānena sthānaṃ sarvatra vindati  Hbhv 
darpaṇasya pradānena rūpavān darpavān bhavet 
mārjayitvā tathā taṃ ca śubhagas tv abhijāyate  Hbhv 
yat kiñcid devadevāya dadyād bhaktisamanvitaḥ 
tad evākṣayam āpnoti svargalokaṃ sa gacchati  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca vāmanapurāṇe śrībaliṃ prati śrīprahlādoktau
śraddadhānair bhaktiparair yāny uddiśya janārdanam 
balidānāni dīyante akṣayāni vidur budhaḥ  Hbhv 
atrāpi kecid icchanti dattvā puṣpāñjalitrayam 
pūrvokta daśa śaṅkhādyā mudrāḥ sandarśayet  Hbhv 
iti 
atha gītavadyanṛtyani
tato vicitrair lalitaiḥ kāritair vā svayaṃ kṛtaiḥ 
gītair vādyaiś ca nṛtyaiś ca śrīkṛṣṇaṃ paritoṣayet  Hbhv 
atha tatra niṣiddhaṃ
nṛtyādi kurvato bhaktān nopaviṣṭo 'valokayet 
na ca tiryag vrajet tatra taiḥ sahāntarayan prabhum  Hbhv 
tathā coktaṃ
nṛtyantaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ harsād āsīno yas tu paśyati 
khañjo bhavati rājendra so 'yaṃ janmani janmani  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
nṛtyatāṃ gāyatāṃ madhye bhaktānāṃ keśavasya ca 
tān ṛte yas tiro yāti tiryagyoniṃ sa gacchati  Hbhv 
atha gītadimāhātmyam
adau samanyataḥ
nārasiṃhe
gītavādyādikaṃ nāṭyam śaṅkhaturyādinisvanam 
yaḥ kārayati viṣṇos tu sandhyāyāṃ mandire naraḥ 
sarvakāle viśeṣeṇa kāmagaḥ kāmarūpavān  Hbhv 
susaṅgītavidagdhaiś ca sevyamāno 'psarogaṇaiḥ 
mahārheṇa vimānena vicitreṇa virājatā 
svargāt svargam anuprāpya viṣṇuloke mahīyate  Hbhv 
skānde viṣṇunāradasaṃvāde
gītaṃ vādyaṃ ca nṛtyaṃ ca nāṭyaṃ viṣṇukathāṃ mune 
yaḥ karoti sa puṇyātmā trailokyopari saṃsthitaḥ  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye śrīyamabhagīrathasaṃvāde
devatāyatane yas tu bhaktiyuktaḥ pranṛtyati 
gītāni gāyaty athavā tatphalaṃ śṛṇu bhūpate  Hbhv 
gandharvarājatāṃ gaṇair nṛtyād rudragaṇeśatām 
prāpnoty aṣṭakulair yuktas tataḥ syān mokṣabhāṅ naraḥ  Hbhv 
laiṅge śrīmārkaṇḍeyāmbarīṣasaṃvāde
viṣṇukṣetre tu yo vidvān kārayed bhaktisaṃyutaḥ 
gananṛtyādikaṃ caiva viṣṇvākhyaṃ ca kathāṃ tathā  Hbhv 
jātiṃ smṛtiṃ ca medhāṃ ca tathaiva paramāṃ sthitim 
prāpnoti viṣṇusālokyaṃ satyam etan nārādhipa  Hbhv 
anyatra ca śrībhagavaduktau
visṛjya lajjāṃ yo 'dhīte gāyate nṛtyate'pi ca 
kulakoṭisamāyukto labhate māmakaṃ padam  Hbhv 
ata evoktaṃ
bhārate nṛtyagīte tu kuryāt svābhāvike'pi vā 
svābhāvikena bhagavān prīṇātīty āha śaunakaḥ  Hbhv 
ata eva nāradīye
viṣṇor gītaṃ ca nṛtyaṃ ca naṭānāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ 
brahman brāhmaṇajātīnāṃ kartavyaṃ nityakarmavat  Hbhv 
kintu smṛtau
gītanṛtyāni kurvīta devadvijādituṣṭaye 
na jīvanāya yuñjīta vipro pāpabhiyā kvacit  Hbhv 
evaṃ kṛṣṇaprīṇanatvād gītāder nityatā parā 
saṃsiddhair aviśeṣena jñeyā sā harivasare  Hbhv 
tathā coktaṃ
keśavāgre nṛtyagītaṃ na karoti harer dine 
vahninā kiṃ na dagdho 'sau gataḥ kiṃ na rasātalaṃ  Hbhv 
atha viśeṣato gītasya māhātmyaṃ
dvārakāmāhātmye śrīmarkandeyendradyumnasaṃvāde
kṛṣṇaṃ santoṣayed yas tu sugītair madhurasvanaiḥ 
sarvavedaphalaṃ tasya jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
skānde śrīmahādevoktau
śrutikoṭisamaṃ japyaṃ japakoṭisamaṃ haviḥ 
havihkoṭisamaṃ geyaṃ geyaṃ geyasamaṃ viduḥ  Hbhv 
kasikhaṇḍe viṣṇudūtaśivaśarmasaṃvāde
yadi gītaṃ kvacid gītaṃ śrīmaddhariharāṅkitam 
mokṣaṃ tu tat phalaṃ prāhuh sānnidhyam athavā tayoḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇuśarme śrībhagavaduktau
rāgeṇākṛṣyate ceto gāndharvābhimukhaṃ yadi 
mayi buddhiṃ samāsthāya gāyetha mama satkathāḥ  Hbhv 
haribhaktisudhodaye
yo gāyati sam aniśaṃ bhuvi bhaktā uccaiḥ
sa drāṇ samastajanapāpabhide'lam ekaḥ 
dīpesv asatsv api nanu pratigeham antar
dhvāntaṃ kim atra vilasaty amale dyunāthe  Hbhv 
yad ānandakalaṃ gāyan bhaktaḥ puṇyāśru varṣati 
tat sarvatīrthasalilasnānaṃ svamalaśodhanaṃ  Hbhv 
vārāhe 
brāhmaṇo vāsudevārthaṃ gāyamano 'niśaṃ param 
samyak tālaprayogeṇa sannipātena vā punaḥ  Hbhv 
nava varṣasahasrāṇi nava varṣaśatāni ca 
kuverabhavanaṃ gatvā modate vai yadṛcchayā  Hbhv 
kuverabhavanād bhraṣṭaḥ svacchandagamanālayaḥ 
phalam āpnoti suśroṇi mama karmaparāyaṇaḥ  Hbhv 
nārāyaṇānāṃ vidhinā gānaṃ śreṣṭhatamaṃ smṛtam 
gānenārādhito viṣṇuh svakīrtijanavarcasā dadāti 
tuṣṭaḥ sthānaṃ svaṃ yathāsmai kauśikayā vai  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
eṣa vo muniśārdūlaḥ prokto gītakramo muneḥ 
brāhmaṇo vāsudevākhyaṃ gāyamāno 'niśaṃ param  Hbhv 
hareḥ sālokyam āpnoti rudragānādhiko bhavet 
karmaṇā manasā vācā vāsudevaparāyaṇaḥ 
gāyan nṛtyaṃs tam āpnoti tasmād geyaṃ paraṃ viduḥ  Hbhv 
prathamaskandhe śrīnāradoktau 
pragāyataḥ svavīryāṇi tīrthapadaḥ priyaśravaḥ 
ahuta iva me sighram darśanaṃ yāti cetasi  Hbhv 
dvādaśaskandhe 
śrīsūtoktau
mṛṣā giras tā hy asatīr asatkathā
na kathyate yad bhagavān adhokṣajaḥ 
tad eva satyaṃ tad uhaiva maṅgalaṃ
tad eva puṇyaṃ bhagavadgunodayam  Hbhv 
tad eva ramyaṃ ruciraṃ navaṃ navaṃ
tad eva śaśvan manaso mahotsavam 
tad eva śokārṇavaśoṣaṇaṃ nṝṇāṃ
yad uttamaślokayaśo 'nugīyate  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare
dattvā ca gītaṃ dharmajñā gandharvaiḥ saha modate 
svayaṃ gītena sampūjya tasyaivānucaro bhavet  Hbhv 
pādme śrīkṛṣṇasatyabhāmāsaṃvādīyakārttikamāhātmye śrīpṛthunāradasaṃvāde śrībhagavaduktau
nāhaṃ vasāmi vaikuṇṭhe na yogihṛdayeṣu vā 
madbhaktā yatra gāyanti tatra tiṣṭhāmi nārada  Hbhv 
teṣāṃ pūjādikaṃ gandhapadyādyaiḥ kriyate naraiḥ 
tena prītiṃ parāṃ yāmi na tathā matpūjanāt  Hbhv 
ata evoktaṃ
karmāṇy aupāyikatvena brāhmaṇo 'nya iti smṛtaḥ 
kārikāyām ataḥ proktaṃ vipro gītai ramed iti  Hbhv 
atha nṛtyasya māhātmyaṃ
dvārakāmāhātmye tatraiva
yo nṛtyati prahṛṣṭātmā bhāvair bahusubhaktitaḥ 
sa nirdahati pāpāni janmāntaraśateṣv api  Hbhv 
haribhaktisudhodaya
bahudhotsāryate harṣād viṣṇubhaktasya nṛtyataḥ 
padbhyāṃ bhūmer diśo 'kṣibhyāṃ dorbhyāṃ vāmaṅgalaṃ divaḥ  Hbhv 
vārāhe
yaś ca nṛtyati suśroṇi purāṇoktaṃ samāsataḥ 
triṃśadvarṣasahasrāṇi triṃśadvarṣaśatāni ca 
puṣkaradvīpam āsādya modate vai yadṛcchayā  Hbhv 
puṣkarāc ca paribhraṣṭaḥ svacchandagamanālayaḥ 
phalam āpnoti suśroṇi mama karmaparāyaṇaḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare
nṛtyaṃ dattvā tathāpnoti rudralokam asaṃśayam 
svayaṃ nṛtyena sampūjya tasyaivānucaro bhavet  Hbhv 
anyatra śrīnāradoktau
nṛtyatāṃ śrīpater agre tālikāvādanair bhṛśam 
uḍḍīyante śarīrasthāḥ sarve pātakapakṣiṇaḥ  Hbhv 
saṅgītaśāstre
vīṇāvādanatattvajñah śrutijātiviśāradaḥ 
tālajñaś cāprayāsena mokṣamārgaṃ niyacchati  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare
vādyaṃ dattvā tathā viprah śakralokam avāpnuyāt 
svayaṃ vadyena sampūjya tasyaivanucaro bhavet  Hbhv 
vādyānām api devasya tantrīvādyaṃ sadā priyam 
tena sampūjya varadaṃ gāṇapatyam avāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
ataḥ saktau punaḥ pūja
śaktaś cet saparivāraṃ kṛṣṇaṃ gandhādibhiḥ punaḥ 
pañcopacārair mūlena sampūjyārghyaṃ samarpayet  Hbhv 
atha nīrājanaṃ
tataś ca mūlamantrena dattvā puṣpāñjalitrayam 
mahānīrājanaṃ kuryān mahāvādyajayasvanaiḥ  Hbhv 
prajvalayet tadarthaṃ ca karpūreṇa ghṛtena vā 
ārātrikaṃ śubhe pātre viṣamānekavartikaṃ  Hbhv 
atha nīrājanamāhātmyam
skānde brahmanāradasaṃvāde
bahuvarttisamāyuktaṃ jvalantaṃ keśavopari 
kuryād ārātrikaṃ yas tu kalpakoṭiṃ vased divi  Hbhv 
karpūrena tu yaḥ kuryād bhaktyā keśavamurdhani 
ārātrikaṃ muniśreṣṭha praviśed viṣṇum avyayaṃ  Hbhv 
tatraivanyatra
dīptimantaṃ sakarpūram karoty ārātrikaṃ nṛpa 
kṛṣṇasya vasate loke sapta kalpāni mānavāḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrīsivomasaṃvāde
mantrahīnaṃ kriyāhīnam yat kṛtaṃ pūjanaṃ hareḥ 
sarvaṃ sampūrṇatām eti kṛte nīrājane śive  Hbhv 
haribhaktisudhodaye
kṛtvā nīrājanaṃ viṣṇor dīpāvalyā sudṛśyayā 
tamovikāraṃ jayati jite tasmimś ca ko bhavaḥ  Hbhv 
anyatra ca
koṭayo brahmahatyānām agamyāgamakotayaḥ 
dahaty ālokamātreṇa viṣṇoḥ sārātrikaṃ mukhaṃ  Hbhv 
iti 
yac ca dīpasya māhātmyaṃ pūrvaṃ likhitam asti tat 
drastavyaṃ sarvatrāpi prāyenābhedato 'nayoḥ  Hbhv 
ataḥ sādaram utthāya mahānīrājanaṃ tv idam 
draṣṭavyaṃ dīpavat sarvair vandyam ārātrikaṃ ca yat  Hbhv 
tad uktaṃ śrīpulastyena viṣṇudharme
dhūpaṃ cārātrikaṃ paśyet karābhyāṃ ca pravandate 
kulakoṭiṃ samuddhṛtya yāti viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padaṃ  Hbhv 
mūlāgame ca
nīrājanaṃ ca yaḥ paśyed devadevasya cakriṇaḥ 
sapta janmāni vipraḥ syād ante ca paramaṃ padam  Hbhv 
atha śaṅkhādivādanamāhātmyam
bṛhannāradīye śrīyamabhagīrathasaṃvāde
keśavāyatane rājan kurvan śaṅkharavaṃ naraḥ 
sarvapāpavinirmukto brahmaṇā saha modate  Hbhv 
karaśabdaṃ prakurvanti keśavāyataneṣu ye 
te sarve pāpanirmuktā vimāneśā yugadvayam  Hbhv 
tālādikāṃsyaninadaṃ kurvan viṣṇugṛhe naraḥ 
yat phalaṃ labhate rājan śṛṇuṣva gadato mama  Hbhv 
sarvapāpavinirmukto vimānaśatasaṅkulaḥ 
gīyamānaś ca gandharvair viṣṇunā saha modate  Hbhv 
bherīmṛdaṅgapaṭahamurajaiś ca saḍiṇḍimaiḥ 
saṃprīṇayanti deveśaṃ teṣāṃ puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu  Hbhv 
devastrīgaṇasaṃyuktāḥ sarvakāmaiḥ samarcitāḥ 
svargalokam anuprāpya modante kalpapañcakam  Hbhv 
iti 
atha sajalaśaṅkhanīrājanaṃ
tataś ca sajalaṃ śaṅkhaṃ bhagavanmastakopari 
tri bhrāmayitvā kurvīta punar nīrājanaṃ prabhoḥ  Hbhv 
tanmāhātmyaṃ ca
dvārakāmāhātmye tatraiva
śaṅkhe kṛtvā tu pānīyaṃ bhrāmitaṃ keśavopari 
sannidhau vasate viṣṇoḥ kalpāntaṃ kṣīrasāgare  Hbhv 
iti 
nīrājanadvayaṃ caitat tāmbūlasyārpaṇaṃ param 
kecid icchanti kecic ca darpaṇārpaṇataḥ param  Hbhv 
tathā ca pañcarātre
punar ācamanaṃ dadyāt karodvartanam eva ca 
sakarpūraṃ ca tāmbūlam kuryān nīrājanaṃ tathā  Hbhv 
samarpya mukuṭādīni bhūṣaṇāni vicakṣaṇaḥ 
ādarśayet tathādarśaṃ prakalpya chatracāmare  Hbhv 
gāruḍe ca
atha bhuktavate dattvā jalaiḥ karpūravāsitaiḥ 
ācamanaṃ ca tāmbūlam candanaiḥ karamārjanam  Hbhv 
puṣpāñjaliṃ tataḥ kṛtvā bhaktyādarśaṃ pradarśayet 
nīrājanaṃ punaḥ kāryaṃ karpūraṃ vibhave sati  Hbhv 
ata eva vāyupurāṇe
ārātrikaṃ tu niḥsnehaṃ niḥsnehayati devatām 
ataḥ saṃśamayitvaiva punaḥ pūjanam ācaret  Hbhv 
ata eva dvārakāmāhātmye
tatraiva kṛtvā pūjādikaṃ sarvaṃ jvalantaṃ kṛṣṇamūrdhani 
ārātrikaṃ prakurvāṇo modate kṛṣṇasannidhau  Hbhv 
iti 
kecin nīrājanat paścād icchanti praṇatiṃ tataḥ 
pradakṣiṇaṃ tataḥ stotraṃ gītanṛtyādikaṃ tataḥ  Hbhv 
evaṃ bhagavataḥ svasvasampradāyānusārataḥ 
pravartante prabhor bhaktau bhaktyā sarvaṃ hi śobhanam  Hbhv 
tato nikṣipya devasyopari puspāñjalitrayam 
vicitrair madhuraiḥ stotraih stutiṃ kurvīta bhaktimān  Hbhv 
atha stutividhiḥ
mahābhārate
ārirādhayiṣuḥ kṛṣṇaṃ vācaṃ jigadiṣāmi yam 
tayā vyāsasamāsinyā prīyatāṃ madhusūdanaḥ  Hbhv 
iti 
ārambhe ca stuter etam ślokaṃ stutiparaḥ paṭhet 
satyāṃ tasyāṃ samāptau ca ślokaṃ saṅkīrtayed imam  Hbhv 
iti vidyātapoyonir ayonir viṣṇur īritaḥ 
vagyajñenārcito devaḥ prīyatāṃ me janārdanaḥ  Hbhv 
pūrvatāpanīśrutiṣu GTU  
oṃ namo viśvarūpāya viśvasthityantahetave 
viśveśvarāya viśvāya govindāya namo namaḥ  Hbhv 
namo vijñānarūpāya paramānandarūpiṇe 
kṛṣṇāya gopīnāthāya govindāya namo namaṃ  Hbhv 
namaḥ kamalanetrāya namaḥ kamalamāline 
namaḥ kamalanābhāya kamalāpataye namaḥ  Hbhv 
barhāpīḍābhirāmāya rāmayākuṇṭhamedhase 
ramāmānasahaṃsāya govindāya namo namaṃ  Hbhv 
kaṃsavaṃśavināśāya keśicāṇūraghātine 
vṛṣabhadhvajavandyāya pārthasārathaye namaḥ  Hbhv 
veṇuvādanaśīlāya gopālāyāhimardine 
kālindīkūlalolāya lolakuṇḍaladhāriṇe  Hbhv 
vallavīvadanāmbhojamāline nṛtyaśāline 
namaḥ praṇatapālāya śrīkṛṣṇāya namo namaḥ  Hbhv 
namaḥ pāpapraṇāśāya govardhanadharāya ca 
pūtanājīvitāntāya tṛṇāvārtāsuhāriṇe  Hbhv 
niṣkalāya vimohāya śuddhāyāśuddhavairiṇe 
advitīyāya mahate śrīkṛṣṇāya namo namaḥ  Hbhv 
prasīda paramānanda prasīda parameśvara 
ādhivyādhibhujaṅgena daṣṭaṃ mām uddhara prabho  Hbhv 
śrīkṛṣṇa rukmiṇīkānta gopījanamanohara 
saṃsārasāgare magnaṃ mām uddhara jagad guro  Hbhv 
keśava kleśaharaṇa nārāyaṇa janārdana 
govinda paramānanda māṃ samuddhara mādhava  Hbhv 
ekādaśaskandhe BhP  
dhyeyaṃ sadā paribhavaghnam abhīṣṭadohaṃ
tīrthāspadaṃ śivaviriñcinutaṃ śaraṇyaṃ
bhṛtyārtihaṃ praṇatapāla bhavābdhipotaṃ
vande mahāpuruṣa te caraṇāravindam  Hbhv 
tyaktvā sudustyajasurepsitarājyalakṣmīṃ
dharmiṣṭha āryavacasā yad agād araṇyam 
māyāmṛgaṃ dayitayepsitam anvadhāvad
vande mahāpuruṣa te caraṇāravindam  Hbhv 
atha vadyasya māhātmyaṃ
vaidikānīdṛśāny eva kṛṣṇe paurāṇikāny api 
tāntrikāṇi ca śāstrāṇi stotrāṇy abhinavāny api  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare haṃsagītayaṃ
abhraṣṭalakṣaṇaiḥ kṛtvā svayaṃ viracitākṣaraiḥ 
stavaṃ brāhmaṇaśārdūlas tasmāt kāmān avāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
stutimāhātmyaṃ
viṣṇudharme
sarvadeveṣu yat puṇyaṃ sarvadeveṣu yat phalam 
naras tat phalam āpnoti stutvā devaṃ janārdanam  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare
na vittadānanicayair bahubhir madhusūudanaḥ 
tathā toṣam avāpnoti yathā stotrair dvijottamaḥ  Hbhv 
nārasiṃhe
stotrair japaiś ca devāgre yaḥ stauti madhusūdanam 
sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇulokam avāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
haribhaktisudhodaye
stuvann ameyamāhātmyaṃ bhaktigrathitaramyavāk 
bhaved brahmādidurlabhyaprabhukāruṇyabhājanam  Hbhv 
yathā narasya stuvato bālakasyeva tuṣyati 
mugdhavākyair na hi tathā vibudhānāṃ jagatpitā  Hbhv 
abalaṃ prabhur īpsitonnatiṃ
kṛtayatnaṃ svayaśahstave ghrṇī 
svayam uddharati stanārthinaṃ
padalagnaṃ jananīva bālakam  Hbhv 
skānde amṛtasaroddhare
śrīkṛṣṇastavaratnaughair yeṣāṃ jihvā tv alaṅkṛtā 
namasyā munisiddhānāṃ vandanīyā divaukasām  Hbhv 
tatraiva karttikamāhātmye śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde
stotrāṇāṃ paramaṃ stotraṃ viṣṇor nāmasahasrakam 
hitvā stotrasahasrāṇi paṭhanīyaṃ mahāmune  Hbhv 
tenaikena muniśreṣṭha pathitena sadā hariḥ 
prītim āyāti deveśo yugakoṭiśatāni ca  Hbhv 
iti 
snāne yat stotramāhātmyaṃ likhitaṃ lekhyam agrataḥ 
yac ca kīrtanamāhātmyaṃ sarvaṃ jñeyaṃ ihāpi tat  Hbhv 
tannityata
viṣṇudharme
nūnaṃ tat kaṇṭhaśālūkam athavā pratijihvikā 
rogo vānyo na sā jihvā yā na stauti harer guṇān  Hbhv 
atha vandanaṃ
praṇamed atha sāṣṭāṅgaṃ tanmudrāṃ ca pradarśayet 
paṭhet pratipraṇāmaṃ ca prasīda bhagavann iti  Hbhv 
tad uktam ekādaśe śrībhagavatā BhP 
stavair uccāvacaiḥ stotraiḥ paurāṇaiḥ prākṛtair api 
stutvā prasīda bhagavann iti vandeta daṇḍavat  Hbhv 
atha praṇāmavidhiḥ
tatraiva BhP 
śiro matpādayoḥ kṛtvā bāhubhyāṃ ca parasparam 
prapannaṃ pāhi mām īśa bhītaṃ mṛtyugrahārṇavāt  Hbhv 
kiṃ cāgame
dorbhyāṃ padbhyāṃ ca jānubhyām urasā śirasā dṛśā 
manasā vacasā ceti praṇāmo 'ṣṭāṅga īritaḥ  Hbhv 
jānubhyāṃ caiva bāhubhyāṃ śirasā vacasā dhiyā 
pañcāṅgakaḥ praṇāmaḥ syāt pūjāsu pravarāv imau  Hbhv 
iti 
garudaṃ dakṣine kṛtvā kuryāt tatpṛṣṭhato budhaḥ 
avaśyaṃ ca praṇāmāṃs trīn śaktaś ced adhikādhikān  Hbhv 
tathā ca nāradapañcarātre
sandhiṃ vīkṣya hariṃ cādyaṃ gurūn svagurum eva ca 
dvicaturviṃśad athavā caturviṃśat tadardhakam 
namet tadardham athavā tadardhaṃ sarvathā namet  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare
devārcādarśanād eva praṇamen madhusūdanam 
snānāpekṣā na kartavyā dṛṣṭvārcāṃ dvijasattamaḥ 
devārcādṛṣṭapūtaṃ hi śuci sarvaṃ prakīrtitam  Hbhv 
atha namaskaramāhātmyaṃ
nārasiṃhe
namaskāraḥ smṛto yajñaḥ sarvayajñeṣu cottamaḥ 
namaskāreṇa cakena sāṣṭāṅgena hariṃ vrajet  Hbhv 
skānde
daṇḍapraṇāmaṃ kurute viṣṇave bhaktibhāvitaḥ 
reṇusaṅkhyaṃ vaset svarge manvantaraśataṃ naraḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde
praṇamya daṇḍavad bhūmau namaskāreṇa yo 'rcayet 
sa yāṃ gatim avāpnoti na tāṃ kratuśatair api 
namaskāreṇa caikena naraḥ puto hariṃ vrajet  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrīsivomasaṃvāde
bhūmim āpīḍya jānubhyāṃ śira āropya vai bhuvi 
praṇamed yo hi deveśam so 'śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
tatraivanyatra
tīrthakoṭisahasrāṇi tīrthakoṭiśatāni ca 
nārāyaṇapraṇāmasya kālaṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm  Hbhv 
śāṭhyenāpi namaskāram kurvataḥ śārṅgadhanvane 
śataśan mārjitaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣanād eva naśyati  Hbhv 
reṇumaṇḍitagātrasya kaṇā dehe bhavanti yat 
tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi viṣṇuloke mahīyate  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare
abhivādyaṃ jagannāthaṃ kṛtārthaś ca tathā bhavet 
namaskārakriyā tasya sarvapāpapraṇāśinī  Hbhv 
jānubhyāṃ caiva pāṇibhyāṃ śirasā ca vicakṣaṇaḥ 
kṛtvā praṇāmaṃ devasya sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
viṣṇupurāṇe 
anādinidhanaṃ devaṃ daityadānavadāraṇam 
ye namanti narā nityaṃ na hi paśyanti te yamam  Hbhv 
ye janā jagatāṃ nāthaṃ nityaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ dvijāḥ 
namanti na hi te viṣṇoḥ snānād anyatra gāminaḥ  Hbhv 
nāradīye 
eko 'pi kṛṣṇāya kṛtaḥ praṇāmo
daśāśvamedhāvabhṛthair na tulyaḥ 
daśāśvamedhī punar eti janma
kṛṣṇapraṇāmī na punarbhavāya  Hbhv 
haribhaktisudhodaye
viṣṇor daṇḍapraṇāmārthaṃ bhaktena patito bhuvi 
patitaṃ pātakaṃ kṛtsnaṃ nottiṣṭhati punaḥ saha  Hbhv 
pādme devadūtavikuṇḍalasaṃvāde
tapas taptvā naro ghoram araṇye niyatendriyaḥ 
yat phalaṃ samavāpnoti tan natvā garuḍadhvajam  Hbhv 
kṛtvāpi bahuśaḥ pāpaṃ naro mohasamanvitaḥ 
na yāti narakaṃ natvā sarvapāpaharaṃ harim  Hbhv 
tatraiva vedanidhistutau
api pāpaṃ durācāraṃ naraṃ tat praṇato hareḥ 
nekṣante kiṅkarā yāmyā ulūkās tapanaṃ yathā  Hbhv 
viṣṇupurāṇe śrīyamasya nijabhaṭānuśāsane ViP 
harim amaragaṇārcitāṅghripadmaṃ
praṇamati yaḥ paramārthato hi martyaḥ 
tam apagatasamastapāpabandhaṃ
vraja parihṛtya yathāgnim ājyasiktam  Hbhv 
brahmavaivarte
śaraṇāgatarakṣaṇodyataṃ
harim īśaṃ praṇamanti ye narāḥ 
na patanti bhavāmbudhau sphuṭaṃ
patitānuddharati sma tān asau  Hbhv 
aṣṭamaskandhe ca balivākye BhP  
aho praṇāmāya kṛtaḥ samudyamaḥ
prapannabhaktārthavidhau samāhitaḥ 
yal lokapālais tvadanugraho 'marair
alabdhapūrvo 'pasade 'sure 'rpitaḥ  Hbhv 
ataiva nārāyaṇavyūhastave 
aho bhāgyam aho bhāgyam aho bhāgyaṃ nṝṇām idam 
yeṣāṃ haripadābjāgre śiro nyastaṃ yathā tathā  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca nārasiṃhe śrīyamoktau
tasya vai narasiṃhasya viṣṇor amitatejasaḥ 
praṇāmaṃ ye prakurvanti teṣām api namo namaḥ  Hbhv 
bhaviṣyottare ca
viṣṇor devajagaddhātur janārdanajagatpateḥ 
praṇāmaṃ ye prakurvanti teṣām api namo namaḥ  Hbhv 
iti 
atha praṇāmanityata
bṛhannāradīye lubdhakopākhyānārambhe
sakṛd vā na named yas tu viṣṇave sarmakāriṇe 
śavoparaṃ vijānīyāt kadācid api nālapet  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye yamabrāhmaṇasaṃvāde
paśyanto bhagavaddvāraṃ nāma śāstraparicchadam 
akṛtvā tatpraṇāmādi yānti te narakaukasaḥ  Hbhv 
atha namaskaraniṣiddhani
viṣṇusmṛtau
janmaprabhṛti yat kiñcit pumān vai dharmam ācaret 
sarvaṃ tan niṣphalaṃ yāty ekahastābhivādanāt  Hbhv 
vārāhe
vastraprāvṛtadehas tu yo naraḥ praṇameta mām 
śvitrī sa jāyate mūrkhah sapta janmāni bhāminī  Hbhv 
kiṃ cānyatra
agre pṛṣṭhe vāmabhāge samīpe garbhamandire 
japahomanamaskārān na kuryāt keśavālaye  Hbhv 
api ca
sakṛd bhūmau nipatito na śaktaḥ praṇamen muhuḥ 
utthāyotthāya kartavyaṃ daṇḍavat praṇipātanam  Hbhv 
iti 
atha pradakṣiṇā
tataḥ pradakṣināṃ kuryād bhaktyā bhagavato hareḥ 
nāmāni kīrtayan śaktau tāṃ ca sāṣṭāṅgavandanām  Hbhv 
pradakṣiṇāśaṅkhyā
nārasiṃhe
ekāṃ cāṇḍyāṃ ravau sapta tisro dadyād vināyake 
catasraḥ keśave dadyāt śive tv ardhapradakṣinām  Hbhv 
atha pradakṣiṇāmāhātmyaṃ
vārāhe
pradakṣiṇāṃ ye kurvanti bhaktiyuktena cetasā 
na te yamapuraṃ yānti yānti puṇyakṛtāṃ gatim  Hbhv 
yas triḥ pradakṣiṇāṃ kuryāt sāṣṭāṅgakapraṇāmakam 
daśāśvamedhasya phalaṃ prāpnuyān nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
skānde śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde
viṣṇor vimānaṃ yaḥ kuryāt sakṛd bhaktyā pradakṣiṇām 
aśvamedhasahasrasya phalam āpnoti mānavaḥ  Hbhv 
tatra caturmasyamāhātmye
caturvāraṃ bhramībhis tu jagat sarvaṃ carācaram 
krāntaṃ bhavati viprāgrya tat tīrthagamanādhikam  Hbhv 
tatraivānyatra
pradakṣiṇāṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt hariṃ bhaktyā samanvitaḥ 
haṃsayuktavimānena viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati  Hbhv 
nārasiṃhe
pradakṣiṇena caikena devadevasya mandire 
kṛtena yat phalaṃ nṛṇāṃ tac chṛṇuṣva nṛpātmaja 
pṛthvīpradakṣiṇaphalaṃ yat tat prāpya hariṃ vrajet  Hbhv 
anyatra ca
evaṃ kṛtvā tu kṛṣṇasya yaḥ kuryād dviḥ pradakṣiṇām 
saptadvīpavatīpuṇyaṃ labhate tu pade pade 
paṭhan nāmasahasraṃ tu nāmāny evātha kevalam  Hbhv 
haribhaktisudhodaye
viṣṇuṃ pradakṣiṇīkurvāṇ yas tatrāvartate punaḥ 
tad evāvartanaṃ tasya punar nāvartate bhave  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye yamabhagīrathasaṃvāde
pradakṣiṇātrayaṃ kuryād yo viṣṇor manujeśvara 
sarvapāpavinirmukto devendratvaṃ samaśnute  Hbhv 
tatraiva pradakṣiṇāmāhātmye sudharmopākhyānārambhe
bhaktyā kurvanti ye viṣṇoh pradakṣiṇācatuṣṭayam 
te'pi yanti paraṃ sthānam sarvalokottamottamam  Hbhv 
iti 
tat khyātaṃ yat sudharmasya pūrvasmin gṛdhrajanmani 
kṛṣṇapradakṣiṇābhyāsān mahāsiddhir abhūd iti  Hbhv 
atha pradakṣiṇāyaṃ niṣiddhaṃ
viṣṇusmṛtau
ekahastapraṇāmaś ca ekā caiva pradakṣiṇā 
akāle darśanaṃ viṣṇor hanti puṇyaṃ purākṛtam  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
kṛṣṇasya purato naiva sūryasyaiva pradakṣiṇām 
kuryād bhramarikārūpāṃ vaimukhyapadanīṃ prabhoḥ  Hbhv 
tathā coktaṃ
pradakṣiṇāṃ na kartavyaṃ vimukhatvāc ca kāraṇāt  Hbhv 
atha karmādyarpaṇam
tataḥ śrīkṛṣṇapādābje dāsyenaiva samarpayet 
tribhir mantraiḥ svakarmāṇi sarvāṇy ātmānam apy atha  Hbhv 
mantraś ca
itaḥ pūrvaṃ prāṇabuddhidharmādhikārato jāgratsvapnasuṣuptyavasthāsu manasā vācā
karmaṇā hastābhyāṃ padbhyām udareṇa śiśnā yat smṛtaṃ yad uktaṃ yat kṛtaṃ tat sarvaṃ
śrīkṛṣṇārpaṇaṃ bhavatu svāhā māṃ madīyaṃ ca sakalaṃ haraye samarpayāmīti 
oṃ tat sat  Hbhv 
iti 
atha tatra karmarpanaṃ
bṛhannāradīye
virāgī cet karmaphale na kiñcid api kārayet 
arpayet svakṛtaṃ karma prīyatām iti me hariḥ  Hbhv 
ata eva kūrmapurāṇe
prīṇātu bhagavān īśaḥ karmaṇānena śāśvataḥ 
karoti satataṃ buddhyā brahmārpaṇam idaṃ param  Hbhv 
yad vā phalānāṃ sannyāsaṃ prakuryāt parameśvare 
karmaṇām etad apy āhur brahmārpaṇam anuttamam  Hbhv 
atha karmārpaṇavidhiḥ
dakṣeṇa pāṇinārghyasthaṃ gṛhītvā culukodakam 
nidhāya kṛṣṇapādābjasamīpe prārthayed idam  Hbhv 
pādatrayakramākrānta trailokeśvara keśava 
tvatprasādād idaṃ toyaṃ pādyaṃ te'stu janārdana  Hbhv 
atha karmarpanamāhātmyaṃ
bṛhannāradīye
paralokaphalaprepsuḥ kuryāt karmāṇy atandritaḥ 
harer nivedayet tāni tat sarvaṃ tv akṣayaṃ bhavet  Hbhv 
ata eva nārāyaṇavyūhastave
kṛṣṇārpitaphalāḥ kṛṣṇaṃ svadharmeṇa yajanti ye 
viṣṇubhaktyarthino dhanyās tebhyo 'pīha namo namaḥ  Hbhv 
atha svārpaṇavidhiḥ
ahaṃ bhagavato 'ṃśo 'smi sadā dāso 'smi sarvathā 
tatkṛpāpekṣako nityam i ty ātmānaṃ samarpayet  Hbhv 
tathā coktaṃ śrīśaṅkarācāryapādaiḥ 
saty api bhedāpagame nātha tavāhaṃ na māmakīnas tvam 
sāmudro hi taraṅgaḥ kvacana samudro na tāraṅgaḥ  Hbhv 
athātmārpaṇamāhātmyam
saptamaskandhe śrīprahlādoktau BhP  
dharmārthakāma iti yo 'bhihitas trivarga
īkṣā trayī nayadamau vividhā ca vārtā 
manye tad etad akhilaṃ nigamasya satyaṃ
svātmārpaṇaṃ svasuhṛdaḥ paramasya puṃsaḥ  Hbhv 
ekādaśe śrībhagavaduddhavasaṃvāde BhP  
martyo yadā tyaktasamastakarmā
niveditātmā vicikīrṣito me 
tadāmṛtatvaṃ pratipadyamāno
mayātmabhūyāya ca kalpate vai  Hbhv 
atha japaḥ
japasya purataḥ kṛtvā prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ budhaḥ 
mantrārthasmṛtipūrvaṃ ca japed aṣṭottaraṃ śatam 
mūlaṃ lekhyena vidhinā sadaiva japamālayā  Hbhv 
śaktau'ṣṭādhikasāhasram japet taṃ cārpayan japam 
prāṇāyāmāṃś ca kṛtvā trīn dadyāt kṛṣṇakare jalam  Hbhv 
tatra cāyaṃ mantraḥ
guhyātiguhyagoptā tvaṃ gṛhāṇāsmatkṛtaṃ japam 
siddhir bhavatu me deva tvatprasādāt tvayi sthite  Hbhv 
iti 
japaprakāro yo 'pekṣyo mālādiniyamātmakaḥ 
puraścaryāprasaṅge tu sa vilikhyate'grataḥ  Hbhv 
arpitaṃ taṃ ca sañcintya svīkṛtaṃ prabhuṇākhilam 
punaḥ stutvā yathāśakti praṇamya prārthayed idam  Hbhv  
āgame
mantrahīnaṃ kriyāhīnaṃ bhaktihīnaṃ janārdana 
yat pūjitaṃ mayā deva paripūrṇaṃ tad astu me  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
yad dattaṃ bhaktimātreṇa patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ jalam 
āveditaṃ nivedyaṃ tu tad gṛhāṇānukampayā  Hbhv 
vidhihīnaṃ mantrahīnaṃ yat kiñcid upapāditam 
kriyāmantravihīnaṃ vā tat sarvaṃ kṣantum arhasi  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
ajñānād athavā jñānād aśubhaṃ yan mayā kṛtam 
kṣantum arhasi tat sarvaṃ dāsyenaiva gṛhāṇa mām  Hbhv 
sthitiḥ sevā gatir yātrā smṛtiś cintā stutir vacaḥ 
bhūyāt sarvātmanā viṣṇo madīyaṃ tvayi ceṣṭitam  Hbhv 
api ca
kṛṣṇa rāma mukunda vāmana vāsudeva jagadguro 
matsya kacchapa nārasiṃha varāha rāghava pāhi mām  Hbhv 
devadānavanāradādivandya dayānidhe 
devakīsuta dehi me tava pādabhaktim acalām  Hbhv 
śrīviṣṇupurāṇe ViP  
nātha yonisahasreṣu yeṣu yeṣu vrajāmy aham 
teṣu teṣv acyutā bhaktir acyute'stu sadā tvayi  Hbhv 
yā prītir avivekānāṃ viṣayeṣv anapāyinī 
tvām anusmarataḥ sā me hṛdayān nāpasarpatu  Hbhv 
pāṇḍavagītāyāṃ 
kīṭeṣu pakṣiṣu mṛgeṣu sarīsṛpeṣu
rakṣaḥpiśācamanujeṣv api yatra tatra 
jātasya me bhavatu keśava te prasādāt
tvayy eva bhaktir atulāvyabhicāriṇī ca  Hbhv 
pādme 
yuvatīnāṃ yathā yūni yūnāṃ ca yuvatau yathā 
mano 'bhiramate tadvan mano 'bhiramatāṃ tvayi  Hbhv 
athāparādhakṣamāpaṇam
tato 'parādhān śrīkṛṣṇaṃ kṣamāśīlaṃ kṣamāpayet 
sakāku kīrtayan ślokān uttamān sāmpradāyikān  Hbhv 
tathā hi
aparādhasahasrāṇi kriyante'harniśaṃ mayā 
dāso 'ham iti māṃ matvā kṣamasva madhusūdana  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
pratijñā tava govinda na me bhaktaḥ praṇaśyati 
iti saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya prāṇān saṃdhārayāmy aham  Hbhv 
athāparādhāḥ
āgame 
yānair vā pādukair vāpi gamanaṃ bhagavadgṛhe 
devotsavādyasevā ca apraṇāmas tadagrataḥ  Hbhv 
ucchiṣṭe vāpy aśauce vā bhagavadvandanādikam 
ekahastapraṇāmaś ca tatpurastāt pradakṣiṇam  Hbhv 
pādaprasāraṇaṃ cāgre tathā paryaṅkabandhanam 
śayanaṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ cāpi mithyābhāṣaṇam eva ca  Hbhv 
uccair bhāṣā mitho jalpo rodanāni ca vigrahaḥ 
nigrahānugrahau caiva nṛṣu ca krūrabhāṣaṇam  Hbhv 
kambalāvaraṇaṃ caiva paranindā parastutiḥ 
aślīlabhāṣaṇaṃ caiva adhovāyuvimokṣaṇam  Hbhv 
śaktau gauṇopacāraś ca aniveditabhakṣaṇam 
tattatkālodbhavānāṃ ca phalādīnām anarpaṇam  Hbhv 
viniyuktāvaiśiṣṭhasya pradānaṃ vyañjanādike 
pṛṣṭhīkṛtyāsanaṃ caiva pareṣām abhivādanam  Hbhv 
gurau maunaṃ nijastotraṃ devatānindanaṃ tathā 
aparādhās tathā viṣṇor dvātriṃśat parikīrtitāḥ  Hbhv 
vārāhe
dvātriṃśadaparādhā ye kīrtyante vasudhe mayā 
vaiṣṇavena sadā te tu varjanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ  Hbhv 
ye vai na varjayanty etān aparādhān mayoditān 
sarvadharmaparibhraṣṭāḥ pacyante narake ciram  Hbhv 
rājānnabhakṣaṇaṃ caivam āpady api bhayāvaham 
dhvāntāgāre hareḥ sparśaḥ paraṃ sukṛtanāśanaḥ  Hbhv 
tathaiva vidhim ullaṅghya sahasā sparśanaṃ hareḥ 
dvārodghāṭo vinā vādyaṃ kroḍamāṃsanivedanam  Hbhv 
pādukābhyāṃ tathā viṣṇor mandirāyopasarpaṇam 
kukkurocchiṣṭakalanaṃ maunabhaṅgo 'cyutārcane  Hbhv 
tathā pūjanakāle viḍutsargāya sarpaṇam 
śrāddhādikam akṛtvā ca navānnasya ca bhakṣaṇam  Hbhv 
adattvā gandhamālyādi dhūpanaṃ madhughātinaḥ 
akarmaṇy aprasūnena pūjanaṃ ca hares tathā  Hbhv  
akṛtvā dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca kṛtvā nidhūvanaṃ tathā 
spṛṣṭvā rajasvalāṃ dīpaṃ tathā mṛtakam eva ca  Hbhv 
raktaṃ nīlam adhautaṃ ca pārakyaṃ malinaṃ paṭam 
paridhāya mṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā vimucyāpānamārutam  Hbhv 
krodhaṃ kṛtvā śmaśānaṃ ca gatvā bhuktāpy ajīrṇayuk 
bhakṣayitvā kroḍamāṃsaṃ pinyākaṃ jālapādakam  Hbhv 
tathā kusumbhaśākaṃ ca tailābhyaṅgaṃ vidhāya ca 
hareḥ sparśo hareḥ karmakaraṇaṃ pātakāvaham  Hbhv 
kiṃ tatraiva
mama śāstraṃ bahiṣkṛtya asmākaṃ yaḥ prapadyate 
muktvā ca mama śāstrāṇi śāstram anyat prabhāṣase  Hbhv 
madyapas tu samāsādya praviśed bhavanaṃ mama  Hbhv 
yo me kusumbhaśākena prāpaṇaṃ kurute naraḥ  Hbhv 
api ca
mama dṛṣṭer abhimukhaṃ tāmbūlaṃ carvayet tu yaḥ 
kurūvakaḥ palāśasthaiḥ puṣpaiḥ kuryān mamārcanam  Hbhv 
mamārcām āsure kāle yaḥ karoti vimūḍhadhīḥ 
pīṭhāsanopaviṣṭo yaḥ pūjayed vā nirāsanaḥ  Hbhv 
vāmahastena māṃ dhṛtvā snāpayed vā vimūḍhadhīḥ 
pūjā paryuṣitaiḥ puṣpaiḥ ṣṭhīvanaṃ garvakalpanam  Hbhv 
tiryakpuṇḍradharo bhūtvā yaḥ karoti mamārcanam 
yācitaiḥ patrapuṣpādyair yaḥ karoti mamārcanam  Hbhv 
aprakṣālitapādo yaḥ praviśen mama mandiram 
avaiṣṇavasya pakvānnaṃ yo mahyaṃ vinivedayet  Hbhv 
avaiṣṇaveṣu paśyatsu mama pūjāṃ karoti yaḥ 
apūjayitvā vighneśaṃ sambhāṣya ca kapālinam  Hbhv 
naraḥ pūjāṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt snapanaṃ ca nakhāmbhasā 
amaunī dharmaliptāṅgo mama pūjāṃ karoti yaḥ  Hbhv 
jñeyāḥ pare'pi bahavo 'parādhāḥ sadasammataiḥ 
ācāraiḥ śāstravihitaniṣiddhātikramādibhiḥ 
tatrāpi sarvathā kṛṣṇanirmālyaṃ tu na laṅghayet  Hbhv 
tathā ca nārasiṃhe śantanuṃ prati nāradavākyam 
ataḥ paraṃ tu nirmālyaṃ na laṅghaya mahīpate 
narasiṃhasya devasya tathānyeṣāṃ divaukasām  Hbhv 
kṛṣṇasya paritoṣepsur na tacchapatham ācaret 
nānādevasya nirmālyam upayuñjīta na kvacit  Hbhv 
tathā viṣṇudharmottare
āpādy api ca kaṣṭāyāṃ deveśaśapathaṃ naraḥ 
na karoti hi yo brahmaṃs tasya tuṣyati keśavaḥ  Hbhv 
na dhārayati nirmālyam anyadevadhṛtaṃ tu yaḥ 
bhuṅkte na cānyanaivedyaṃ tasya tuṣyati keśavaḥ  Hbhv 
iti 
athāparādhaśamanam
saṃvatsarasya madhye tu tīrthe śaukarake mama 
kṛtopavāsaḥ snānena gaṅgāyāṃ śuddhim āpnuyāt  Hbhv  
mathurāyāṃ tathāpy evaṃ sāparādhaḥ śuci bhavet  Hbhv  
anayos tīrthayor ekaṃ yaḥ seveta sukṛtī naraḥ 
sahasrajanmajanitān aparādhān jahāti saḥ  Hbhv  
skānde 
ahany ahani yo martyo gītādhyāyaṃ paṭhet tu vai 
dvātriṃśadaparādhāṃs tu kṣamate tasya keśavaḥ  Hbhv  
tatra kārttikamāhātmye 
tulasyā ropaṇaṃ kāryaṃ śrāvaṇeṣu viśeṣataḥ 
aparādhasahasrāṇi kṣamate puruṣottamaḥ  Hbhv  
tatraivānyatra 
dvādaśyāṃ jāgare viṣṇor yaḥ paṭhet tulasīstavam 
dvātriṃśadaparādhāni kṣamate tasya keśavaḥ  Hbhv  
yaḥ karoti hareḥ pūjāṃ kṛṣṇaśatrāṅkito naraḥ 
aparādhasahasrāṇi nityaṃ harati keśavaḥ  Hbhv 
atha śeṣagrahaṇam
tato bhagavatā dattaṃ manyamāno dayālunā 
mahāprasāda ity uktvā śeṣaṃ śirasi dhārayet  Hbhv 
atha nirmālyadhāraṇanityatā
pādme śrīgautamāmbarīṣasaṃvāde
ambarīṣa harer lagnaṃ nīraṃ puṣpaṃ vilepanam 
bhaktyā na dhatte śirasā śvapacād adhiko hi saḥ  Hbhv 
atha śrībhagavannirmālyamāhātmyaṃ
skānde brahmanāradasaṃvāde
kṛṣṇottīrṇaṃ tu nirmālyaṃ yasyāṅgaṃ spṛśate mune 
sarvarogair tathā pāpair mukto bhavati nārada  Hbhv 
viṣṇor nirmālyaśeṣeṇa yo gātraṃ parimārjayet 
duritāni vinaśyanti vyādhayo yānti khaṇḍaśaḥ  Hbhv 
mukhe śirasi dehe tu viṣṇūttirnaṃ tu yo vahet 
tulasīṃ muniśārdūla na tasya spṛśate kaliḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
viṣṇumūrtisthitaṃ puṣpaṃ śirasā yo vahen naraḥ 
aparyūṣitapāpas tu yāvad yugacatuṣṭayam  Hbhv 
kiṃ kariṣyati susnāto gaṅgāyāṃ bhūsurottama 
yo vahet śirasā nityaṃ tulasīṃ viṣṇusevitāṃ  Hbhv 
viṣṇupādābjasaṃlagnām ahorātroṣitāṃ śubhām 
tulasīṃ dhārayed yo vai tasya puṇyam anantakam  Hbhv 
ahoratraṃ śire yasya tulasī viṣṇusevitā 
na sa lipyati pāpena padmapatram ivāmbhasā  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
viṣṇoḥ śiraḥparibhraṣṭam bhaktyā yas tulasīṃ vahet 
sidhyānti sarvakāryāṇi manasā cintitāni ca  Hbhv 
api ca
pramārjayati yo deham tulasyā vaiṣṇavo naraḥ 
sarvatīrthamayaṃ dehaṃ tatkṣanāt dvija jāyate  Hbhv 
gāruḍe
harer mūrtyavaśeṣaṃ tu tulasīkāṣṭhacandanam 
nirmālyaṃ tu vahed yas tu koṭitīrthaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
nāradapañcarātre
bhojananāntaraṃ viṣṇor arpitaṃ tulasīdalam 
tatkṣanāt pāpanirmoktas cāndrāyaṇaśatādhikaḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ cānyatra
kautukaṃ śṛṇu me devi viṣṇor nirmālyavahninā 
tāpitaṃ nāśam āyāti brahmahatyādipātakam  Hbhv 
ekādaśaskandhe 
śrībhagavantaṃ praty uddhavoktau
tvayopayuktasraggandhavāso 'laṅkāracarcitaḥ 
ucchistabhojino dāsās tava māyāṃ jayema hi  Hbhv 
ata eva skānde śrīyamasya dūtānuśāsane
pādodakaratā ye ca harer nirmālyadhārakāḥ 
viṣṇubhaktiratā ye vai te tu tyājyaḥ sudurataḥ  Hbhv 
iti 
visarjanaṃ tu cet kāryaṃ visṛjyavaraṇāni tat 
deve tanmudrayā prārthya devaṃ hṛdi visarjayet  Hbhv 
tathā coktaṃ
pūjito 'si mayā bhaktyā bhagavan kamalapate 
sa lakṣmīko mama svāntaṃ viśa viśrāntihetave  Hbhv 
prārthyaivaṃ pāduke dattvā saṅgam udvāsayed dharim 
prāṇāyāmaṃ ṣaḍaṅgaṃ ca kṛtvā mudrāṃ visarjanīm  Hbhv 
atha pūjavidhivivekaḥ
ayaṃ pūjavidhir mantrasiddhyarthasya japasya hi 
aṅgaṃ bhaktes tu tanniṣṭhair nyāsādīn antareṣyate  Hbhv 
tatra devalaye pūja nityatvena mahāprabhoḥ 
kāmyatvenāpi gehe tu prāyo nityatayā matā  Hbhv 
sevādiniyamo devālaye devasya ceṣyate 
prāyaḥ svagehe svacchandasevā svavratarakṣayā  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca viṣṇudharmottare
ghṛtena snapitaṃ devaṃ candanenānulepayet 
sitajātyāś ca kusumaih pūjayet tadanantaram  Hbhv 
śvetena vastrayugmena tathā muktāphalaiḥ śubhaiḥ 
mukhyakarpūradhūpena payasā pāyasena ca  Hbhv 
padmasūtrasya varttyā ca ghṛtadhūpena cāpy atha 
pūjayet sarvathā yatnāt sarvakāmapradārcanam  Hbhv 
kṛtvemaṃ mucyate rogī rogāt śīghram asaṃśayam 
duḥkhārto mucyate duḥkhād baddho mucyeta bandhanāt  Hbhv 
rājagrastaś ca mucyeta tathā rājabhayān naraḥ 
kṣemeṇa gacched adhvānam sarvānarthavivarjitaḥ  Hbhv 
iti 
iti śrīgopālabhaṭṭavilikhite śrībhagavadbhaktivilāse
prātararcāsamāpano nāmāṣṭamo vilāsaḥ  
 MahaprasadaVilasa
navamavilāsaḥ
mahāprasādaḥ
sa prasṚdatu caitanyadevo yasya prasādataḥ 
mahāprasādajātārhaḥ sadyaḥ syād adhamo 'py aham  Hbhv 
atha śaŚkhodakaṃ tac ca kṛṣñadṛṣṭisudhokṣitam 
vaiṣñavebhyaḥ pradāyābhivandya mūrdhani dhārayet  Hbhv 
śaŚkhodakamāhātmyaṃ
skānde brahmanāradasaṃvāde
śaŚkhodakaṃ harer bhaktir nirmālyaṃ pādayor jalaṃ 
candanaṃ dhūpaśeṣaṃ tu brahmahatyāpahārakam  Hbhv 
tatraiva śaŚkhamāhātmye
śaŚkhasthitaṃ tu yat toyaṃ bhrāmitaṃ keśavopari 
vandate śirasā nityaṃ gaŚgāsnānena tasya kim  Hbhv 
na dāho na klamo nārtir narakāgnibhayaṃ na hi 
yasya śaŚkhodakaṃ mūrdhni kṛṣñadṛṣṭyavalokitam  Hbhv 
na grahā na ca kuṣmāñḍāḥ piśācoragarakṣasāḥ 
dṛṣṭvā śaŚkhodakaṃ mūrdhni vidravanti diśo daśa  Hbhv 
kṛṣñamūrdhni bhrāmitaṃ tu jalaṃ tacchaŚkhasaṃsthitam 
kṛtvā mūrdhany avāpnoti muktiṃ viṣñoḥ prasādataḥ  Hbhv 
bhrāmayitvā harer mūrdhni mandiraṃ śaŚkhavāriñā 
prokṣayed vaiṣñavo yas tu nāśubhaṃ tadgṛhe bhavet  Hbhv 
nṚrājanajalaṃ yatra yatra pādodakaṃ hareḥ 
tiṣṭhate muniśārdūla vardhante tatra sampadaḥ  Hbhv 
tatraivāgre
nṚrājanajalaṃ viṣñor yasya gātrāñi saṃspṛśet 
yajñāvabhṛtalakṣañaṃ snānajaṃ labhate phalam  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrṚśivoktau
pādodakena devasya hatyāyutasamanvitaḥ 
śudhyate nātra sandehas tathā śaŚkhodakena hi  Hbhv 
bṛhadviṣñupurāñe ca
tṚrthādhikaṃ yajñaśatāc ca pāvanaṃ
jalaṃ sadā keśavadṛṣṭisaṃsthitam 
chinatti pāpaṃ tulasṚvimiśritaṃ
viśeṣataś cakraśilāvinirmitam  Hbhv 
atha tṚrthadhārānaṃ
kṛṣñapadabjatṚrthaṃ ca vaiṣñavebhyaḥ pradāya hi 
svayaṃ bhaktyabhivandyādau pṚtvā śirasi dhārayet  Hbhv 
tasya mantravidhiś ca prāk prātaḥsnānaprasaŚgataḥ 
likhito hy adhunā pāne viśeṣo likhyate kiyān  Hbhv 
sa coktaḥ
oṃ carañaṃ pavitraṃ vitataṃ purāñaṃ
yena pūtas tarati duṣkṛtāni 
tena pavitreña śuddhena pūtā
api pāpmānam arātiṃ tarema  Hbhv 
 lokasya dvāram ārcayat pavitraṃ jyotiṣmat vibhrājamānaṃ mahas tad amṛtasya dhārā bahudhā dohamānaṃ carañaṃ loke sudhitaṃ dadhatu  Hbhv  
 iti  
imaṃ mantraṃ samuccārya sarvaduṣṭagrahāpaham 
prāśnṚyāt prokṣayed dehaṃ putramitraparigraham  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
viṣñoḥ pādodakaṃ pṚtaṃ koṭihatyāghanāśanam 
tad evaṣṭagunaṃ pāpaṃ bhumau bindunipatanat  Hbhv 
atha śrṚcaranodakapanamāhātmyaṃ
pādme gautamāmbarṚṣasaṃvāde
hareḥ snānāvaśeṣas tu jalaṃ yasyodare sthitam 
ambarṚṣa prañamyoccaiḥ pādapāṃśuḥ pragṛhyatām  Hbhv 
tatraiva devadūtavikuñḍalasaṃvāde
ye pibanti narā nityaṃ śālagrāmaśilājalam 
pañcagavyasahasrais tu sevitaiḥ kiṃ prayojanam  Hbhv 
koṭitṚrthasahasrais tu sevitaiḥ kiṃ prayojanam 
nityaṃ yadi pibet puñyaṃ śālagrāmaśilājalam  Hbhv 
śālagrāmaśilātoyaṃ yaḥ pibed bindunā samam 
mātuḥ stanyaṃ punar naiva na pibed bhaktibhāŚ naraḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
dahanti narakān sarvān garbhavāsaṃ ca dāruñam 
pṚtaṃ yais tu sadā nityaṃ śālagrāmaśilājalam  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrṚyamadhumraketusaṃvāde
śālagrāmaśilātoyaṃ bindumātraṃ tu yaḥ pibet 
sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyeta bhaktimārge kṛtodyamaḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva pulastyabhagṚrathasaṃvāde
pādodakasya māhātmyaṃ bhagṚratha vadāmi te 
pāvanaṃ sarvatṚrthebhyo hatyākoṭivināśakam  Hbhv 
dhṛte śirasi pṚte ca sarvās tusyanti devatāḥ 
prāyaścittaṃ tu pāpānāṃ kalau pādodakaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
tribhiḥ sārasvataṃ toyaṃ saptāhena tu nārmadam 
sadyaḥ punāti gāŚgeyaṃ darśanād eva yāmunam  Hbhv 
punanty etāni toyāni snānadarśanakṚrtanaiḥ 
punāti smarañād eva kalau pādodakaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
arcitaiḥ koṭibhir liŚgair nityaṃ yat kriyate phalam 
tat phalaṃ śatasahasraṃ pite pādodake hareḥ  Hbhv 
aśucir vā durācāro mahāpātakasaṃyutaḥ 
spṛṣṭvā pādodakaṃ viṣñoḥ sadā śudhyati mānavaḥ  Hbhv 
pāpakoṭiyuto yas tu mṛtyukāle śiromukhe 
dehe pādodakaṃ tasya na prayāti yamālayam  Hbhv 
na dānaṃ na havir yeṣāṃ svādhyāyo na surārcanam 
te 'pi pādodakaṃ pṚtvā prayanti paramāṃ gatim  Hbhv 
kārttike kārttikṚyoge kiṃ kariṣyati puṣkare 
nityaṃ ca puṣkaraṃ tasya yasya pādodakaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv 
viśākhāṛkṣasaṃyukta vaiśākhṚ hi kariṣyati 
piñḍārake mahātṚrthe ujjāyinyāṃ bhagṚratha  Hbhv 
māghamāse prayāge tu snānaṃ kiṃ kariṣyati 
prayāgaṃ satataṃ tasya yasya pādodakaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv 
prabodhavāsare prāpte mathurāyāṃ ca tasya kim 
nityaṃ ca yāmunaṃ snānaṃ yasya pādodakaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv 
kasyām uttaravāhinyāṃ gaŚgāyāṃ tu mṛtasya kim 
yasya pādodakaṃ viṣñor mukhe caivāvatiṣṭhate  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
hitvā pādodakaṃ viṣñor yo 'nyatṚrthāni gacchati 
anarghaṃ ratnam utsṛjya loṣṭraṃ vāñchati durmatiḥ  Hbhv 
kurukṣetrasamo deśo binduḥ pādodakaṃ mataḥ  Hbhv 
pated yatrākṣayaṃ puñyaṃ nityaṃ bhavati tadgṛhe 
gayāpiñḍasamaṃ puñyaṃ putrāñām api jāyate  Hbhv 
pādodakena devasya ye kuryuḥ pitṛtarpañam 
nāsurāñāṃ bhayaṃ tasya pretajanyaṃ ca rākṣasam  Hbhv 
na rogasya bhayaṃ caiva nāsti vighnakṛtaṃ bhayam 
na duṣṭā naiva ghorākṣāḥ svāpadotthabhayaṃ na hi  Hbhv 
grahāḥ pṚdāṃ na kurvanti caurā naśyanti dāruñāḥ 
kiṃ tasya tṚrthagamane devarṣṚñāṃ ca darśane  Hbhv 
yasya pādodakaṃ mūrdhni śālagrāmaśilodbhavam 
prṚto bhavati mārtañḍaḥ prṚto bhavati keśavaḥ 
brahmā bhavati suprṚtaḥ prṚto bhavati saŚkaraḥ  Hbhv 
pādodakasya māhātmyaṃ yaḥ paṭhet keśavagrataḥ 
sa yāti paramaṃ sthānaṃ yatra devo janardanaḥ  Hbhv 
brahmāñḍapurāñe śrṚbrahmanāradasaṃvāde
prāyaścittaṃ yadi prāptaṃ kṛcchraṃ vā tv aghamarṣañam 
so 'pi pādodakaṃ pṚtvā śuddhiṃ prāpnoti tatkṣañāt  Hbhv 
aśaucaṃ naiva vidyeta sūtake mṛtake 'pi ca 
yeṣāṃ pādodakaṃ mūrdhni prāśanaṃ ye ca kurvate  Hbhv 
antakāle 'pi yasyeha dṚyate pādayor jalam 
so 'pi sadgatim āpnoti sadācārair bahiṣkṛtaḥ  Hbhv 
apeyaṃ pibate yas tu bhuŚkte yaś cāpy abhojanam 
agamyāgamanā ye vai pāpācārāś ca ye narāḥ 
te 'pi pūjyā bhavanty āśu sadyaḥ pādāmbusevanāt  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
apavitraṃ yadannaṃ syāt pānṚyaṃ cāpi pāpinām 
bhuktvā pṚtvā viśuddhaḥ syāt pṚtvā pādodakaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv 
taptakṛcchrāt pañcagavyān mahākṛcchrād viśiṣyate 
cāndrāyañāt pārakṛcchrāt parākād api suvrata 
kāyaśuddhir bhavaty āśu pṚtvā pādodakaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv 
aguruṃ kuŚkumaṃ cāpi karpūraṃ cānulepanam 
viṣñupādāmbusaṃlagnaṃ tad vai pāvanapāvanam  Hbhv 
dṛṣṭipūtaṃ tu yat toyaṃ viṣñunā prabhaviṣñunā 
tad vai pāpaharaṃ putra kiṃ punaḥ pādayor jalam  Hbhv 
etadartham ahaṃ putra śirasā viṣñutatparaḥ 
dhārāyāmi pibāmy adya māhātmyaṃ viditaṃ mama  Hbhv 
priyas tvam agrajaḥ putras tadarthaṃ gaditaṃ mayā 
rahasyaṃ me tv anarhasya na vaktavyaṃ kadācana  Hbhv 
dhārayasva sadā mūrdhni prāśanaṃ kuru nityaśaḥ 
janmamṛtyujarāduḥkhair mokṣaṃ yāsyasi putraka  Hbhv 
viṣñudharmottare
sadyaḥ phalapradaṃ puñyaṃ sarvapāpavināśanam 
sarvamaŚgalamaŚgalyaṃ sarvaduḥkhavināśanam  Hbhv 
duḥsvapnanāśanaṃ puñyaṃ viṣñupādodakaṃ śubham 
sarvopadravahantāraṃ sarvavyādhivināśanam  Hbhv 
sarvotpātapraśamanaṃ sarvapāpanivārañam 
sarvakalyāñasukhadaṃ sarvakāmaphalapradam  Hbhv 
sarvasiddhipradaṃ dhanyaṃ sarvadharmavivardhanam 
sarvaśatrupraśamanaṃ sarvabhogapradāyakam  Hbhv 
sarvatṚrthasya phaladam mūrdhni pādāmbudhārañam 
prayāgasya prabhāsasya puṣkarasya ca sevane 
pṛthūdakasya tṚrthasya ācānto labhate phalam  Hbhv 
cakratṚrthaṃ phalaṃ yādṛk tādṛñ pādāmbudhārañāt 
sarasvatyāṃ gayāyāṃ ca gatvā yat prāpnuyāt phalam 
tat phalaṃ labhate śreṣṭhaṃ mūrdhni pādāmbudhārañāt  Hbhv 
skānde
pādodakasya māhātmyaṃ devo jānāti śaŚkaraḥ 
viṣñupādacyutā gaŚgā śirasā yena dhāritā 
sthānaṃ naivāsti pāpasya dehināṃ dehamadhyataḥ  Hbhv 
sabāhyābhyantaraṃ yasya vyāptaṃ pādodakena vai 
pādodaṃ viṣñunaivedyam udare yasya tiṣṭhati  Hbhv 
nāśrayaṃ labhate pāpaṃ svayam eva vinaśyati 
mahāpāpagrahagrasto vyāpto rogaśatair yadi  Hbhv 
hareḥ pādodakaṃ pṚtvā mucyate nātra saṃsayaḥ 
śirasā tiṣṭhate yeṣāṃ nityaṃ pādodakaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ kariṣyati te loke tṚrthakoṭimanorathaiḥ 
ayam eva paro dharma idam eva paraṃ tapaḥ 
idam eva paraṃ tṚrthaṃ viṣñupādāmbu yat pibet  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrṚśivomāsaṃvāde
vilayaṃ yānti pāpāni pṚte pādodake hareḥ 
kiṃ punar viṣñupādodaṃ śālagrāmaśilācyutam  Hbhv 
viśeṣena haret pāpaṃ brahmahatyādikaṃ priye 
pṚte pādodake viṣñor yadi prāñair vimucyate 
hatvā yamabhaṭān sarvān vaiṣñavaṃ lokam āpnuyāt  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrṚśivakārttikeyasaṃvāde śrṚśālagrāmaśilāmāhātmye
chinnas tena mahāsena garbhāvāsaḥ sudāruñaḥ 
pṚtaṃ yena sadā viṣñoḥ śālagrāmaśilājalam  Hbhv 
ye pibanti narā nityaṃ śālagrāmaśilājalam 
pañcagavyasahasrais tu prāśitaiḥ kiṃ prayojanam  Hbhv 
prāyaścitte samutpanne kiṃ dānaiḥ kim upoṣañaiḥ 
cāndrāyañaiś ca tṚrthaiś ca pṚtvā pādodakaṃ śuci  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradiye lubdhakopākhyānārambhe
haripādodakaṃ yas tu kṣañamātraṃ ca dhārayet 
sa snātaḥ sarvatṚrthesu viṣñoḥ priyataras tathā  Hbhv 
akālamṛtyuśamanaṃ sarvavyādhivināśanam 
sarvaduḥkhopaśamanaṃ haripādodakaṃ śubham  Hbhv 
tatraiva tadupākhyānānte
haripādodakasparśāl lubdhako vṚtakalmaṣaḥ 
divyaṃ vimānam āruhya munim enam athābravṚt  Hbhv 
haripādodakaṃ yasmān mayi tvaṃ kṣiptavān mune 
prāpito 'smi tvayā tasmāt tad viṣñoḥ paramaṃ padam  Hbhv 
haribhaktisudhodaye
pādaṃ pūrvaṃ kila spṛṣṭvā gaŚgābhūt smartṛmokṣadā 
viṣñoḥ sadyas tu satsaŚgi pādāmbu katham Ṛḍyate  Hbhv 
tāpatrayānalo yo 'sau na śāmyet sakalābdhibhiḥ 
drutaṃ śāmyati so 'lpena śrṚmadviṣñupadāmbunā  Hbhv 
yuddhāstrābhedyakavacaṃ bhavāgnistambhanauṣadham 
sarvāŚgaiḥ sarvathā dhāryaṃ pādyaṃ śucipadaḥ sadā  Hbhv 
amṛtatvāvahaṃ nityaṃ viṣñupādāmbu yaḥ pibet 
sa pibaty amṛtaṃ nityaṃ māse māse tu devatāḥ  Hbhv 
māhātmyam iyad ity asya vaktā yo 'pi sa nirbhayaḥ 
nanv anarghamañer mūlyaṃ kalpayann agham aśnute  Hbhv 
anyatrapi
sa brahmacārṚ sa vratṚ āśramṚ ca sadāśuciḥ 
viṣñupādodakaṃ yasya mukhe śirasi vigrahe  Hbhv 
janmaprabhṛtipāpānāṃ prāyaścittaṃ yadṚcchati 
śālagrāmaśilāvari pāpahāri niṣevyatām  Hbhv 
ata eva tejodravinapañcaratre śrṚbrahmañoktam
pṚṭhaprañālād udakaṃ pṛthag ādāya putraka 
siñcayen mūrdhni bhaktānāṃ sarvatṚrthamayaṃ hi tat  Hbhv  iti 
pādodakasya māhātmyaṃ vikhyātaṃ sarvaśāstrataḥ 
likhituṃ śaknuyat ko hi sindhūrmṚn gañayann api  Hbhv 
viśeṣataś ca pādodaṃ tulasṚdalasaṃyutam 
śaŚkhe kṛtvā vaiṣñavebhyo dattvā prāgvat pibet svayam  Hbhv 
atha śaŚkhakṛtapādodakamāhātmyaṃ
skānde śrṚbrahmanāradasaṃvāde
kṛtvā pādodakaṃ śaŚkhe vaiṣñavānāṃ mahātmanām 
yo dadyāt tulasṚmiśraṃ cāndrāyañaśataṃ labhet  Hbhv 
gṛhṚtvā kṛṣñapādāmbu śaŚkhe kṛtvā tu vaiṣñavaḥ 
yo vahet śirasā nityaṃ sa munis tapasottamaḥ  Hbhv 
pādme devadūtavikuñḍalasaṃvāde
śālagrāmaśilātoyaṃ yadi śaŚkhabhṛtaṃ pibet 
hatyākoṭivināśaṃ ca kurute nātra saṃsayaḥ  Hbhv 
agastyasaṃhitāyām
śālagrāmaśilātoyaṃ tulasṚdalavāsitam 
ye pibanti punas teṣāṃ stanyapānaṃ na vidyate  Hbhv  iti 
śrṚviṣñor vaiṣñavānāṃ ca pāvanaṃ carañodakam 
sarvatṚrthamayaṃ pṚtvā kuryād ācamanaṃ na hi  Hbhv 
tad uktaṃ skānde śivena
viṣñoḥ pādodakaṃ pṚtvā paścād aśuciśaŚkayā 
ācamati ca yo mohād brahmahā sa nigadyate  Hbhv 
srutiś ca
bhagavān pavitraṃ bhagavatpādau pavitraṃ
bhagavatpādodakaṃ pavitraṃ
na tatpāna ācamanṚyam 
yathā hi soma iti  Hbhv 
sauparñe ca
viṣñupādodakaṃ pṚtvā bhaktapādodakaṃ tathā 
ya ācamati saṃmohād brahmahā sa nigadyate  Hbhv  iti 
tataḥ śuddhaṃ payaḥpūrñaṃ gandhapuṣpākṣatānvitam 
adharopari sannyasec chaŚkhaṃ bhagavadagrataḥ  Hbhv 
atha śrṚbhagavadagrataḥ śaŚkhasthapanamahatamyaṃ
skānde brahmanāradasaṃvāde śaŚkhamāhātmye
purato vāsudevasya sapuṣpaṃ sajalākṣatam 
śaŚkham abhyarcitaṃ paśyet tasya lakṣmṚr na durlabhā  Hbhv 
sapuṣpaṃ vārijaṃ yasya durvākṣatasamanvitam 
purato vāsudevasya tasya śrṚḥ sarvatomukhṚ  Hbhv  iti 
bhūtvātha bhaktimān śrṚmattulasyā kānane prabhum 
sampūjyābhyarcayet taṃ ca śrṚkṛṣñacarañapriyam  Hbhv 
atha śrṚtulasṚvanapūjā
prāg dattvārghyaṃ tato 'vyarcya gandhapuṣpākṣatādinā 
stutvā bhagavatṚṃ tāṃ ca prañamet prārhtya dañḍavat  Hbhv 
athārghyamantraḥ
śriyaḥ śriye śriyāvāse nityaṃ śrṚdhārāsatkṛte 
bhaktyā dattaṃ mayā devi arghyaṃ gṛhña namo 'stu te  Hbhv 
pūjā mantraḥ
nirmitā tvaṃ purā devair arcitā tvaṃ surāsuraiḥ 
tulasṚ hara me pāpaṃ pūjāṃ gṛhña namo 'stu te  Hbhv 
stutiś ca
mahāprasādajananṚ sarvasaubhāgyavardhinṚ 
ādhivyādhiharo nityaṃ tulasṚ tvaṃ namo 'stu te  Hbhv 
prārthanā
śrṚyaṃ dehi yaśo dehi kṚrtim āyus tathā sukham 
balaṃ puṣṭiṃ tathā dharmaṃ tulasṚ tvaṃ prasṚda me  Hbhv 
prañāmavākyam
avantṚkhañḍe
yā dṛṣṭā nikhilāghasaŚghaśamanṚ spṛṣṭā vapuḥpāvanṚ
rogāñām abhivanditā nirasinṚ siktāntakatrāsinṚ 
pratyāsattividhāyinṚ bhagavataḥ kṛṣñasya saṃropitā
nyastā taccarañe vimuktiphaladā tasyai tulasyai namaḥ  Hbhv 
bhagavatyās tulasyās tu māhātmyāmṛtasāgare 
lobhāt kūrditum icchāmi kṣudras tat kṣamyatāṃ tvayā  Hbhv 
atha tulasivanapujamahatmyam
skānde
śrāvañadvādaśṚyoge śālagrāmaśilārcane 
yat phalaṃ saŚgame proktaṃ tulasṚpūjanena tat  Hbhv 
gāruḍe
dhātrṚphalena yat puñyaṃ jayantyāṃ samupoṣañe 
khagendra bhavate nṛñāṃ tulasṚpūjanena tat  Hbhv 
prayāgasnānaniratau kasyāṃ prāñavimokṣañe 
yat phalaṃ vihitaṃ devais tulasṚpūjanena tat  Hbhv 
agastyasaṃhitāyām
caturñām api varñānām āśramāñām viśeṣataḥ 
strṚñāṃ ca puruṣāñāṃ ca pūjiteṣṭaṃ dadāti hi  Hbhv 
tulasṚ ropitā siktā dṛṣṭā spṛṣṭā ca pāvayet 
ārādhitā prayatnena sarvakāmaphalapradā  Hbhv 
atha tulasṚvanapūjamāhātmyaṃ
pradakṣiñaṃ bhramitvā ye namaskurvanti nityaśaḥ 
na teṣāṃ duritaṃ kiñcid akṣṚñam avaśiṣyate  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradiye yajñadhvajopākhyānānte
pūjyamānā ca tulasṚ yasya veśmani tiṣṭhati 
tasya sarvāñi śreyāṃsi vardhante 'harahar dvijāḥ  Hbhv 
ata eva pādme devadūtavikuñḍalasaṃvāde
pakṣe pakṣe tu samprāpte dvādaśyāṃ vaiśyasattama 
brahmādayo 'pi kurvanti tulasṚvanapūjanam  Hbhv 
ata eva śrṚtulasṚstutimahimā
ananyamanasā nityaṃ tulasṚṃ stauti yo naraḥ 
pitṛdevamanuṣyāñāṃ priyo bhavati sarvadā  Hbhv 
atha tulasṚvanamāhātmyaṃ
skānde
ratiṃ badhnāti nānyatra tulasṚkānanam vinā 
devadevo jagatsvāmṚ kalikāle viśeṣataḥ  Hbhv 
hitvā tṚrthasahasrāñi sarvān api śiloccayan 
tulasṚkānane nityaṃ kalau tiṣṭhati keśavaḥ  Hbhv 
nirṚkṣitā narair yais tu tulasṚvanavāṭikā 
ropitā yaiś ca vidhinā samprāptaṃ paramaṃ padam  Hbhv 
na dhātrṚ saphalā yatra na viṣñus tulasṚvanam 
tat śmaśānasamaṃ sthānaṃ santi yatra na vaiṣñavāḥ  Hbhv 
keśavārthe kalau ye tu ropayantṚha bhūtale 
kiṃ kariṣyaty asantuṣṭo yamo 'pi saha kiŚkaraiḥ  Hbhv 
tulasyā ropañaṃ kāryaṃ śravañena viśeṣataḥ 
aparādhasahasrāñi kṣamate puruṣottamaḥ  Hbhv 
devālayeṣu sarveṣu puñyakṣetreṣu yo naraḥ 
vāpayet tulasṚṃ puñyāṃ tat tṚrthaṃ cakrapāñinaḥ  Hbhv 
ghaṭair yantraghaṭṚbhiś ca siñcitaṃ tulasṚvanam 
jaladhārābhir viprendra prṚñitaṃ bhuvanatrayam  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrṚbrahmanāradasaṃvāde
tulasṚgandham ādāya yatra gacchati mārutaḥ 
diśo daśa ca pūtāḥ syur bhūtagrāmāś caturvidhāḥ  Hbhv 
tulasṚkānanodbhūtā chāyā yatra bhaved dvija 
tatra śrāddhaṃ pradātavyam pitṄñāṃ tṛptihetave  Hbhv 
tulasṚbṚjanikarāḥ patate yatra nārada 
piñḍadānaṃ kṛtaṃ tatra pitṄñāṃ dattam akṣayam  Hbhv 
tatraivāgre
dṛṣṭā spṛṣṭā tathā dhyātā kṚrtitā namitā śrutā 
ropitā sevitā nityaṃ pūjitā tulasṚ śubhā  Hbhv 
navadhā tulasṚṃ nityaṃ ye bhajanti dine dine 
yugakoṭisahasrāñi te vasanti harer gṛhe  Hbhv 
ropitā tulasṚ yāvat kurute mūlavistaraṃ 
tāvat koṭisahasraṃ tu tanoti sukṛtaṃ kalau  Hbhv 
yāvac chākhāpraśākhābhir bṚjapuṣpaiḥ phalair mune 
ropitā tulasṚ pumbhir vardhate vasudhātale  Hbhv 
kule teṣāṃ tu ye jātā ye bhaviṣyanti ye mṛtaḥ 
ākalpaṃ yugasāhasraṃ teṣāṃ vāso harer gṛhe  Hbhv 
tatraiva cāvantṚkhañḍe
tulasṚṃ ye vicinvanti dhanyās tatkarapallavāḥ 
keśavārthe kalau ye ca ropayantṚha bhūtale  Hbhv 
snāne dāne tathā dhyāne prāśane keśavārcane 
tulasṚ dahate pāpaṃ ropañe kṚrtane kalau  Hbhv 
kāśṚkhañḍe svadūtān prati śrṚyamānuśāsane
tulasyalaŚkṛtā ye ye tulasṚnāmajāpakāḥ 
tulasṚvanapālā ye te tyājyā dūrato bhaṭāḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva dhruvacarite
tulasṚ yasya bhavane pratyahaṃ paripūjyate 
tadgṛhe nopasarpanti kadācid yamakiŚkarāḥ  Hbhv 
pādme devadūtavikuñḍalasaṃvāde
na paśyanti yamaṃ vaiśya tulasṚvanaropañāt 
sarvapāpaharaṃ sarvakāmadaṃ tulasṚvanam  Hbhv 
tulasṚkānanaṃ vaiśya gṛhe yasmiṃs tu tiṣṭhate 
tadgṛhaṃ tṚrthṚbhūtaṃ hi no yānti yamakiŚkarāḥ  Hbhv 
tāvad varṣasahasrāñi yāvad bṚjadalāni ca 
vasanti devaloke tu tulasṚṃ ropayanti ye  Hbhv 
tulasṚgandham āghrāya pitaras tuṣṭamānasāḥ 
prayānti garuḍārūḍhās tat padaṃ cakrapāñinaḥ  Hbhv 
darśanaṃ narmadāyās tu gaŚgāsnānaṃ viśāṃ vara 
tulasṚdalasaṃsparsaḥ samam etat trayaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv 
ropañāt pālanāt sekād darśanāt sparśanān nṛñām 
tulasṚ dahate pāpaṃ vāŚmanaḥkāyasañcitam  Hbhv 
āmravṛkṣasahasreña pippalānāṃ śatena ca 
yat phalaṃ hi tad ekena tulasṚvitapena tu  Hbhv 
viṣñupūjanasaṃyuktas tulasṚṃ yas tu ropayet 
yugāyutadaśaikaṃ sa ropako ramate divi  Hbhv 
tatraiva vaiśākhamāhātmye
puṣkarādṚni tṚrthāni gaŚgādyāḥ saritas tathā 
vāsudevādayo devā vasanti tulasṚdale  Hbhv 
dāridryaduḥkharogārtipāpāni subahūny api 
tulasṚ harati kṣipraṃ rogān iva harṚtakṚ  Hbhv 
tatraiva kārttikamāhātmye
yadgṛhe tulasṚ bhāti rakṣābhir jalasecanaiḥ 
tadgṛhe yamadūtāś ca dūrato varjayanti hi  Hbhv 
tulasyās tarpañaṃ ye ca pitṄn uddiśya mānavāḥ 
kurvanti teṣāṃ pitaras tṛptā varṣayutaṃ jalaiḥ  Hbhv 
paricaryāṃ ca ye tasya rakṣayābālabandhanaiḥ 
śuśrūṣito haris tais tu nātra kāryā vicārañā  Hbhv 
nāvajñā jātu kāryāsyā vṛkṣabhāvān manṚṣibhiḥ 
yathā hi vāsudevasya vaikuñṭhabhogavigrahaḥ  Hbhv 
śālagrāmaśilārūpam sthāvaraṃ bhuvi dṛśyate 
tathā lakṣmyaikyam āpannā tulasṚ bhogavigrahā  Hbhv 
aparaṃ sthāvaraṃ rūpaṃ bhuvi lokahitāya vai 
spṛṣṭā dṛṣṭā rakṣitā ca mahāpātakanāśinṚ  Hbhv 
agastyasaṃhitāyām
viṣños trailokyanāthasya rāmasya janakātmajā 
priyā tathaiva tulasṚ sarvalokaikapāvanṚ  Hbhv 
tulasṚvāṭikā yatra puṣpāntaraśatāvṛtā 
śobhate rāghavas tatra sṚtayā sahitaṃ svayam  Hbhv 
tulasṚvipinasyāpi samantāt pāvanaṃ sthalam 
krośamātraṃ bhavaty eva gāŚgeyasyaiva pāthasaḥ  Hbhv 
tulasṚsannidhau prāñān ye tyajanti munṚśvara 
na teṣāṃ narakakleśah prayānti paramaṃ padam  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
ananyadarśanāḥ prātar ye paśyanti tapodhana 
ahorātrakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣañāt praharanti te  Hbhv 
gāruḍe
kṛtaṃ yena mahābhāga tulasṚvanaropañam 
muktis tena bhaved dattā prāñināṃ vinatāsuta  Hbhv 
tulasṚ vāpitā yena puñyārāme vane gṛhe 
pakṣṚndra tena satyoktaṃ lokāḥ sapta pratiṣṭhitāḥ  Hbhv 
tulasṚkānane yas tu muhūrtam api viśramet 
janmakoṭikṛtāt pāpān mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
pradakṣiñāṃ yaḥ kurute paṭhan nāmasahasrakam 
tulasṚkānane nityaṃ yajñāyutaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
haribhaktisudhodaye
nityaṃ sannihito viṣñuḥ saspṛhas tulasṚvane 
api me'kṣatapatraikaṃ kaścid dhanyo 'rpayed iti  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradṚye gaŚgāprasaŚge
saṃsārapāpavicchedi gaŚgānāma prakṚrtitam 
tathā tulasyā bhaktiś ca harikṚrtipravaktari  Hbhv 
tulasṚkānanaṃ yatra yatra padmavanāni ca 
purāñapaṭhanaṃ yatra tatra sannihito hariḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrṚyamabhagṚrathasaṃvāde
tulasṚropañaṃ ye tu kurvate manujeśvara 
teṣāṃ puñyaphalaṃ vakṣye vadatas tvaṃ niśāmaya  Hbhv 
saptakoṭikulair yukto mātṛtaḥ pitṛtas tathā 
vaset kalpaśataṃ sāgraṃ nārāyañasamṚpagaḥ  Hbhv 
tṛñāni tulasṚmūlāt yāvanty apahinoti vai 
tāvatṚr brahmahatyā hi chinnatty eva na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
tulasyā siñcayed yas tu culukodakamātrakam 
kṣṚrodaśāyinā sārdhaṃ vased ācandratārakam  Hbhv 
kañṭakāvarañaṃ vāpi vṛtiṃ kāṣṭhaiḥ karoti yaḥ 
tulasyāḥ śṛñu rājendra tasya puñyaphalaṃ mahat  Hbhv 
yāvad dināni santiṣṭhet kañṭakāvarañaṃ prabho 
kulatrayayutas tāvat tiṣṭhed brahmapade yugam  Hbhv 
prākārakalpako yas tu tulasyā manujeśvara 
kulatrayeña sahito viṣñoḥ sārūpyatāṃ vrajet  Hbhv 
ataiva tatraiva yajñadhvajopākhyānānte
durlabhā tulasṚsevā durlabhā saŚgatiḥ satām 
durlabhā haribhaktiś ca saṃsārārñavapātinām  Hbhv 
purāñāntareṣu
yat phalaṃ kratubhiḥ sviṣṭaiḥ samāptavaradakṣiñaiḥ 
tat phalaṃ koṭiguñitaṃ ropayitvā hareḥ priyām  Hbhv 
tulasṚṃ ye prayacchanti surāñām arcanāya vai 
ropayanti śucau deśe teṣāṃ loko 'kṣayaḥ smṛtaḥ  Hbhv 
ropitāṃ tulasṚṃ dṛṣṭvā nareña bhuvi bhūmipa 
vivarñavadano bhūtvā tallipiṃ mārjayed yamaḥ  Hbhv 
tulasṚti ca yo brūyāt trikālaṃ vadane yadi 
nityaṃ sa gosahasrasya phalam āpnoti bhūsura  Hbhv 
tena dattaṃ hutaṃ japtaṃ kṛtaṃ śrāddhaṃ gayāśire 
tapas taptaṃ khagaśreṣṭha tulasṚ yena ropitā  Hbhv 
śrutābhilaṣitā dṛṣṭā ropitā siñcitā natā 
tulasṚ dahate pāpaṃ yugāntāgnir ivākhilam  Hbhv 
keśavāyatane yas tu kārayet tulasṚvanam 
labhate cākṣayaṃ sthānaṃ pitṛbhiḥ saha vaiṣñavaḥ  Hbhv 
anyatrāpi
tulasṚkānane śrāddhaṃ pitṄñāṃ kurute tu yaḥ 
gayāśrāddhaṃ kṛtaṃ tena bhāṣitaṃ viṣñunā purā  Hbhv 
tulasṚgahanaṃ dṛṣṭvā vimukto yāti pātakāt 
sarvathā muniśārdūla brahmahā puñyabhāg bhavet  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca skānde vaśiṣṭhamāndhātṛsaṃvāde
śuklapakṣe yadā rājan tṛtṚyā budhasaṃyutā 
śravañena mahābhāga tulasṚ cātipuñyadā  Hbhv  iti 
prasaŚgāt śrṚtulasyā hi mṛdaḥ kāṣṭhasya cādhunā 
māhātmyaṃ likhyate kṛṣñe arpitasya dalasya ca  Hbhv 
atha śrṚtulasṚmṛttikākāṣṭhādimāhātmyam
skānde śrṚbrahmanāradasaṃvāde
bhūgatais tulasṚmūlair mṛttikā sparśitā tu yā 
tṚrthakoṭisamā jñeyā dhāryā yatnena sā gṛhe  Hbhv 
yasmin gṛhe dvijaśreṣṭha tulasṚmūlamṛttikā 
sarvadā tiṣṭhate dehe devatā na sa mānuṣaḥ  Hbhv 
tulasṚmṛttikālipto yadi prāñān parityajet 
yamena nekṣituṃ śakto yuktaḥ pāpaśatair api  Hbhv 
śirasi kriyate yais tu tulasṚmūlamṛttikā 
vighnāni tasya naśyanti sānukūlā grahās tathā  Hbhv 
tulasṚmṛttikā yatra kāṣṭhaṃ patraṃ ca veśmani 
tiṣṭhate muniśārdūla niścalaṃ vaiṣñavaṃ padam  Hbhv 
atha vṛttisampadānaṃ
tatraivānyatra
maŚgalārthaṃ ca doṣaghnaṃ pavitrārthaṃ dvijottama 
tulasṚmūlasaṃlagnāṃ mṛttikām āvahed budhaḥ  Hbhv 
tanmūlamṛttikāṃ yo vai dhārayiṣyati mastake 
tasya tuṣṭo varān kāmān pradadāti janārdanaḥ  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradiye gaŚgāprasaŚge
tulasṚmūlasambhūtā haribhaktapadodbhavā 
gaŚgodbhavā ca mṛllekhā nayaty acyutarūpatām  Hbhv 
gāruḍe
yadgṛhe tulasṚkāṣṭham patraṃ śuṣkam athārdrakam 
bhavate naiva pāpaṃ tadgṛhe saŚkramate kalau  Hbhv 
śrṚprahlādasaṃhitāyāṃ tathā viṣñudharmottare'pi
patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ kāṣṭhaṃ tvakśākhāpallavāŚkuram 
tulasṚsambhavaṃ mūlaṃ pāvanaṃ mṛttikādy api  Hbhv 
homaṃ kurvanti ye viprās tulasṚkāṣṭhavahninā 
lave lave bhavet puñyam agniṣṭomaśatodbhavam  Hbhv 
naivedyaṃ pacate yas tu tulasṚkāṣṭhavahninā 
merutulyaṃ bhaved annaṃ tad dattaṃ keśavāya hi  Hbhv 
śarṚraṃ dahyate yeṣāṃ tulasṚkāṣṭhavahninā 
na teṣāṃ punar āvṛttir viṣñulokāt kathañcana  Hbhv 
grasto yadi mahāpāpair agamyāgamanādikaiḥ 
mṛtaḥ śudhyati dāhena tulasṚkāṣṭhavahninā  Hbhv 
tṚrthaṃ yadi na samprāptaṃ smṛtir vā kṚrtanam hareḥ 
tulasṚkāṣṭhadagdhasya mṛtasya na punar bhavaḥ  Hbhv 
yady ekaṃ tulasṚkāṣṭhaṃ madhye kāṣṭhacayasya hi 
dahakāle bhaven muktih pāpakoṭiyutasya ca  Hbhv 
janmakoṭisahasrais tu toṣito yair janārdanaḥ 
dahyante te janā loke tulasṚkāṣṭhavahninā  Hbhv 
agastyasaṃhitāyām
yaḥ kuryāt tulasṚkāṣṭhair akṣamālāṃ surūpiñṚm 
kañṭhamālāṃ ca yatnena kṛtaṃ tasyākṣayaṃ bhavet  Hbhv 
atha tulasṚpatradhārañamāhātmyam
skānde śrṚbrahmanāradasaṃvāde
yasya nābhisthitaṃ patraṃ mukhe śirasi karñayoḥ 
tulasṚsambhavaṃ nityaṃ tṚrthais tasya makhaiś ca kim  Hbhv 
tatraivānyatra
śatrughnaṃ ca supuñyaṃ ca śrṚkaraṃ roganāśanam 
kṛtvā dharmam avāpnoti śirasā tulasṚdalam  Hbhv 
yaḥ kaścid vaiṣñavo loke mithyācāro 'py anāśramṚ 
punāti sakalān lokān śirasā tulasṚṃ vahan  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradiye śrṚyamabhagṚrathasaṃvāde
karñena dhārayed yas tu tulasṚṃ satataṃ naraḥ 
tatkāṣṭhaṃ vāpi rājendra tasya nāsty upapātakam  Hbhv 
haribhaktisudhodaye vaiṣñavavipraṃ prati yamadūtanam uktau
kasmād iti na jānṚmas tulasyā hi priyo hariḥ 
gacchantaṃ tulasṚhastam rakṣañn evanugacchati  Hbhv 
purāñāntare ca
yaḥ kṛtvā tulasṚpatram śirasā viṣñutatparaḥ 
karoti dharmakāryāñi phalam āpnoti cākṣayam  Hbhv 
garuḍapurāñe
mukhe tu tulasṚpatram dṛṣṭvā śirasi karñayoḥ 
kurute bhaskaris tasya duṣkṛtasya tu mārjanam  Hbhv 
trikālaṃ vinatāputra prāśayet tulasṚṃ yadi viśiṣyate 
kāyaśuddhiś cāndrāyañaśataṃ vinā  Hbhv 
skānde śrṚvaśiṣthamandhatṛsaṃvāde
cāndrāyañat taptakṛcchrāt brahmakūrcāt kuśodakāt 
viśiṣyate kāyaśuddhis tulasṚpatrabhakṣañāt  Hbhv 
tathā ca tulasṚpatrabhakṣañād bhāvavarjitaḥ 
pāpo 'pi sadgatiṃ prāpta ity etad api viśrutam  Hbhv 
tathā ca skānde śrṚbrahma nāradaṃ prati kathite amṛtasaroddhare lubdhakopākhyānānte yamadūtan prati śrṚviṣñudūtanaṃ vacanaṃ
kṣṚrābdhau mathyamāne hi tulasṚ kāmarūpiñṚ 
utpāditā mahābhāga lokoddhārañahetave  Hbhv 
yasyāḥ smarañamātreña darśanāt kṚrtanād api 
vilayaṃ yānti pāpāni kiṃ punar viṣñupūjanāt  Hbhv 
jātarūpamayaṃ puṣpam padmarāgamayaṃ śubham 
hitvā tu ratnajātāni gṛhñāti tulasṚdalam  Hbhv 
bhakṣitaṃ lubdhakenāpi patraṃ tulasṚsambhavam 
paścād diṣṭāntam āpanno bhasmṚbhūtaṃ kalevaram  Hbhv 
sitāsitaṃ yathā nṚraṃ sarvapāpakṣayāvaham 
tathā ca tulasṚpatram prāśitaṃ sarvakāmadam  Hbhv 
yathā jātabalo vahnir dahate kānanādikam 
prāśitaṃ tulasṚpatraṃ yathā dahati pātakam  Hbhv 
yathā bhaktirato nityaṃ naro dahati pātakam 
tulasṚbhakṣañāt tat tad dahate pāpasañcayam  Hbhv 
cāndrāyañasahasrasya parakāñāṃ śatasya ca 
na tulyaṃ jāyate puñyaṃ tulasṚpatrabhakṣañāt  Hbhv 
kṛtvā pāpasahasrāñi pūrve vayasi mānavaḥ 
tulasṚbhakṣañān mucyet śrutam etat purā hareḥ  Hbhv 
tāvat tiṣṭhanti pāpāni dehināṃ yamakiŚkarāḥ 
yāvan na tulasṚpatraṃ mukhe śirasi tiṣṭhati  Hbhv 
amṛtād utthitā dhātrṚ tulasṚ viṣñuvallabhā 
smṛtā saŚkṚrtitā dhyātā prāśitā sarvakāmadā  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrṚyamaṃ prati śrṚbhagavadvakyaṃ
dhātrṚphalaṃ ca tulasṚ mṛtyukāle bhaved yadi 
mukhe yasya śire dehe durgatir nāsti tasya vai  Hbhv 
yukto yadi mahāpāpaiḥ sukṛtaṃ nārjitaṃ kvacit 
tathāpi dṚyate mokṣas tulasṚ bhakṣitā yadi  Hbhv 
lubdhakenātmadehena bhakṣitaṃ tulasṚdalam 
samprāpto matpadaṃ nūnaṃ kṛtvā prāñasya saṃkṣayam  Hbhv 
purāñāntare ca
upoṣya dvādaśṚṃ śuddhāṃ parāñe tulasṚdalam 
prāśayed yadi viprendra aśvamedhāṣṭakaṃ labhet  Hbhv  iti 
tathaiva tulasṚsparsat kṛṣñacakreña rakṣitaḥ 
brahmabandhur iti khyāto haribhaktisudhodaye  Hbhv 
ata evoktam
kiṃ citram asyāḥ patitaṃ tulasyā
dalaṃ jalaṃ vā patitaṃ punṚte 
lagnādhibhālasthalam ālavāla
mṛtsnāpi kṛtsnāghavināśanāya  Hbhv  iti 
śrṚmattulasyāḥ patrasya māhātmyaṃ yady apṚdṛśam 
tathāpi vaiṣñavais tan na grāhyaṃ kṛṣñārpañaṃ vinā  Hbhv 
kṛṣñapriyatvāt sarvatra śrṚtulasyāḥ prasaŚgataḥ 
saŚkṚrtyamānaṃ dhātryāś ca māhātmyaṃ likhyate 'dhunā  Hbhv 
atha dhātrṚmāhātmyaṃ skānde brahmanāradasaṃvāde
dhātrṚcchāyāṃ samāśritya yo 'rcayec cakrapāñinām 
puṣpe puṣpe 'śvamedhasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ  Hbhv 
tatraivāgre
dhātrṚcchāyāṃ tu saṃspṛśya kuryāt piñḍaṃ tu yo mune 
muktiṃ prayānti pitaraḥ prasādān mādhavasya ca  Hbhv 
mūrdhni ghrāñe mukhe caiva dehe ca munisattama 
dhatte dhātrṚphalaṃ yas tu sa mahātmā sudurlabhaḥ  Hbhv 
dhātrṚphalaviliptāŚgo dhātrṚphalavibhūṣitaḥ 
dhātrṚphalakṛtāhāro naro nārāyaño bhavet  Hbhv 
yaḥ kaścid vaiṣñavo loke dhatte dhātrṚphalaṃ mune 
priyo bhavati devānāṃ manuṣyāñāṃ tu kā kathā  Hbhv 
yaḥ kaścid vaiṣñavo loke mithyācāro 'pi duṣṭadhṚḥ 
punāti sakalān lokān dhātrṚphaladalānvitaḥ  Hbhv 
dhātrṚphalāni yo nityaṃ vahate karasampuṭe 
tasya nārāyaño devo varam ekaṃ prayacchati  Hbhv 
dhatrṚphalaṃ ca bhoktavyaṃ kadācit karasampuṭāt 
yaśaḥ śriyam avāpnoti prasādāc cakrapāñinaḥ  Hbhv 
dhātrṚphalaṃ ca tulasṚ mṛttikā dvārakodbhavā 
saphalaṃ jṚvitaṃ tasya tritayaṃ yasya veśmani  Hbhv 
dhātrṚphalais tu saṃmiśraṃ tulasṚdalavāsitam 
pibate vahate yas tu tṚrthakoṭiphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
yasmin gṛhe bhavet toyaṃ tulasṚdalavāsitam 
dhātrṚphalaiś ca viprendra gāŚgeyaiḥ kiṃ prayojanam  Hbhv 
tulasṚdalanaivedyaṃ dhātryā yasya phalaṃ gṛhe 
kavacaṃ vaiṣñavaṃ tasya sarvapāpavināśanam  Hbhv 
brahmapurāñe ca
dhātrṚphalāni tulasṚ hy antakāle bhaved yadi 
mukhe caiva śirasy aŚge pātakaṃ nāsti tasya vai  Hbhv 
kṛtvā tu bhagavatpūjāṃ na tṚrthaṃ snānam ācaret 
na ca devālayopetāspṛśyasaṃsparśanādinā  Hbhv 
atha snānaviśeṣakalaḥ
smṛtyarthasāre
na snāyād utsave tṚrthe māŚgalyaṃ vinivartya ca 
anuvrajya suhṛdbandhūn arcayitveṣṭadevatām  Hbhv 
viṣñusmṛtau ca
viṣñvālayasamṚpasthān viṣñusevārtham āgatān 
cāñḍālān patitān vāpi spṛṣṭvā na snānam ācaret  Hbhv 
devayatravivāheṣu yajñopakarañeṣu ca 
utsaveṣu ca sarveṣu spṛṣṭāspṛṣṭir na vidyate  Hbhv 
evaṃ prātaḥ samabhyarcya śrṚkṛṣñaṃ tadanantaram 
śāstrābhyāsaṃ dvijaḥ śaktyā kuryād vipro viśeṣataḥ  Hbhv 
yad uktam
śrutismṛtṚ ubhe netre viprāñaṃ parikṚrtite 
ekena vikalaḥ kāño dvābhyām andhaḥ prakṚrtitaḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca kaurme vyasagṚtāyām
yo 'nyatra kurute yatnaṃ anādhṚtya śrutiṃ dvijaḥ 
sa samūḍho na sambhāṣyo vedabāhyo dvijātibhiḥ  Hbhv 
na vedapathamātreña santusyed esa vai dvijaḥ 
yathoktācārahinas tu paŚke gaur iva sidati  Hbhv 
yo 'dhṚtya vidhivad vedaṃ vedārthaṃ na vicārayet 
sa cāndhaḥ śūdrakalpas tu padārthaṃ na prapadyate  Hbhv  iti 
ato 'dhṚtyānvahaṃ vidvān athādhyāpya ca vaiṣñavaḥ 
samarpya tac ca kṛṣñāya yateta nijavṛttaye  Hbhv 
vṛttau satyāṃ ca śṛñuyāt sādhūn saŚgatya satkathām  Hbhv 
saptamaskandhe BhP 
ṛtāmṛtābhyāṃ jṚveta mṛtena pramṛtena vā 
satyānrtābhyām api vā na svavṛttyā kadācana  Hbhv 
ṛtam uñchaśilaṃ proktaṃ amṛtaṃ syād ayācitam 
mṛtaṃ tu nityaṃ yācñā syāt pramṛtaṃ karṣañaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv 
satyānṛtaṃ tu vāñijyaṃ śvavṛttir nṚcasevanam  Hbhv 
ātmano nṚcalokānāṃ sevanaṃ vṛttisiddhaye 
nitarāṃ nindyate sadbhir vaiṣñavasya viśeṣataḥ  Hbhv 
tad uktaṃ
sevā śvavṛttir yair uktā na samyak tair udāhṛtam 
svacchandacaritaḥ kva śvā vikrṚtāsuḥ kva sevakaḥ  Hbhv 
pañṚkṛtyātmanaḥ prāñān ye vartante dvijādhamāḥ 
teṣāṃ durātmanām annaṃ bhuktvā cāndrāyañaṃ caret  Hbhv  iti 
śuklavṛtter asiddhau ca bhojyānnān śūdravargataḥ 
tathaiva grāhyāgrāhyāñi jānṚyāc chāstrato budhaḥ  Hbhv 
śuklavṛttiś ca
śrṚviṣñudharmottare trtiyakhañḍe
pratigraheña yal labdhaṃ yajyataḥ śiṣyatas tathā 
gunānvitebhyo viprasya śuklaṃ tat trividhaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv 
yuddhopakārāl labdhaṃ ca dañḍāc ca vyavahārataḥ 
kṣatriyasya dhanaṃ śuklaṃ trividhaṃ parikṚrtitam  Hbhv 
kṛṣivāñijyagorakṣaḥ kṛtvā śuklaṃ tathā viśaḥ 
dvijaśuśrūṣayā labdhaṃ śuklaṃ śūdrasya kṚrtitam  Hbhv 
kramāgataṃ prṚtidānaṃ prāptaṃ ca saha bhāryayā 
aviśeṣena sarveṣāṃ dhanaṃ śuklaṃ prakṚrtitam  Hbhv 
atha grāhyāgrāhyāñi
kaurme tatraiva
nādyāc chūdrasya vipro 'nnaṃ mohād vā yadi kāmataḥ 
na śūdrayoniṃ vrajati yas tu bhuŚkte hy anāpadi  Hbhv 
duṣkṛtaṃ hi manuṣyasya sarvam anne pratiṣṭhitam 
yo yasyānnaṃ samaśnāti sa tasyāśnāti kilbiṣam  Hbhv 
ārdhikaḥ kulamitraś ca svagopālaś ca nāpitaḥ 
ete śūdreṣu bhojyānnā dattvā svalpapañaṃ budhaiḥ  Hbhv 
pāyasaṃ snehapakvaṃ yad gorasaṃ caiva śaktavaḥ 
piñyākaṃ caiva tailaṃ ca śūdrād grāhyaṃ tathaiva ca  Hbhv 
aŚgirāḥ
gorasaṃ caiva śaktūṃś ca tailapiñyākam eva ca 
apūpān bhakṣayec chūdrāt yat kiñcit payasā kṛtam  Hbhv 
atrismṛtau
svasutāyāś ca yo bhuŚkte sa bhuŚkte pṛthivṚmalam 
narendrabhavane bhuktvā viṣṭhāyāṃ jāyate kṛmiḥ  Hbhv 
dāsanāpitagopāla kulamitrārdhasṚriñaḥ 
bhojyānnāḥ śūdravarge 'mṚ tathātmavinivedakaḥ  Hbhv 
madhūdakaṃ phalaṃ mūlam edhāṃsyabhayadakṣiñā 
abhyudyatāni tv etāni grāhyāñy api nikṛṣṭataḥ  Hbhv 
khalakṣetragataṃ dhanyaṃ kūpavāpisu yaj jalam 
agrāhyād api tadgrāhyaṃ yac ca goṣṭhagataṃ payaḥ  Hbhv 
pānṚyaṃ pāyasaṃ bhakṣyaṃ ghṛtaṃ lavañam eva ca 
hastadattaṃ na gṛhñṚyāt tulyaṃ gomāṃsabhakṣañaiḥ  Hbhv 
manusmṛtau
samudraṃ saindhavaṃ caiva lavañe paramādbhute 
pratyakṣe api tu grāhye niṣedhas tv anyagocaraḥ  Hbhv 
āyasenaiva pātreña yad annam upanṚyate 
bhoktā tad viṭsamaṃ bhuŚkte dātā ca narakaṃ vrajet  Hbhv 
gorakṣakān vāñijakān tathā kārukaśṚlinaḥ 
proṣyān vārdhūṣikāṃś caiva viprān śūdravad ācaret  Hbhv 
kaurme ca tatraiva
tṛñaṃ kāṣṭhaṃ phalaṃ puṣpaṃ prakāśaṃ vai harer budhaḥ 
dharmārthaṃ kevalaṃ vipra hy anyathā patito bhavet  Hbhv 
tilamudgayavādṚnāṃ muṣṭir grāhyā pathi sthitaiḥ 
kṣudhārthair nānyathā vipra dharmavidbhir iti sthitiḥ  Hbhv 
vaiṣñavānāṃ hi bhoktavyaṃ prārthyānnaṃ vaiṣñavaiḥ sadā

tathā ca pādme devadūtavikuñḍalasaṃvāde

nāradiye

yācayed annam amṛtaṃ tadabhāve jalaṃ pibet  Hbhv 
viṣñusmṛtau
śrotriyānnaṃ vaiṣñavānnaṃ hutaśeṣaṃ ca yaddhaviḥ 
ānakhāt śodhayet pāpaṃ tuṣāgniḥ kanakaṃ yathā  Hbhv 
skānde mārkañḍeyabhagṚrathasaṃvāde
śuddhaṃ bhāgavatasyānnaṃ śuddhaṃ bhagṚrathijalam

avaiṣñavagṛhe bhuktvā pṚtvā vā jānato 'pi vā 
śuddhiś cāndrāyañe prokta iṣṭāpūrtaṃ vṛthā sadā  Hbhv 
śrṚprahlādavākye ca
keśavārcā gṛhe yasya na tiṣṭhati mahṚpate 
tasyānnaṃ naiva bhoktavyam abhakṣyeña samaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv 
kecid vṛttyanapekṣasya japaśraddhāvataḥ prabho 
viśvastasyādiśanty asmin kāle 'pi kṛtino japam  Hbhv 
atha madhyāhnikakṛtyāni
madhyāhne snānataḥ pūrvaṃ puṣpādy āhṛtya vā svayam 
bhṛtyādinā vā sampādya kuryān madhyāhnikṚḥ kriyāḥ  Hbhv 
snānāśaktau ca madhyāhne snānam ācārya māntrikam 
yathoktaṃ bhagavatpūjāṃ śaktaś cet prāgvad ācaret  Hbhv 
atha vaiṣñavavaisvadevadividhiḥ
tataḥ kṛṣñārpitenaiva śuddhenānena vaiṣñavaḥ 
vaiśvadevādikaṃ daivaṃ karma paitraṃ ca sādhayet  Hbhv 
tad uktaṃ ṣaṣṭhe dinavibhāge tu kuryāt pañca mahāmakhān 
daivo homena yajñaḥ syāt bhautas tu balidānatah  Hbhv 
paitro viprānnadānena paitreña balināthavā 
kiñcid annapradānād vā tarpañād vā caturvidhaḥ  Hbhv 
nṛyajño 'tithisatkārāt hantakāreña cāmbunā 
brahmayajño vedajapāt purāñapaṭhanena vā  Hbhv

kaurme
akṛtvā tu dvijaḥ pañca mahāyajñān dvijottamaḥ 
bhuñjṚta cet sumūḍhātmā tiryagyoniṃ sa gacchati  Hbhv

candanena tu piñḍanam kartavyaṃ pitṛtṛptaye

evaṃ kṛte mahṚpala mā bhavet saṃśayaḥ kvacit  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrṚpurusottamakhañḍe

tulasṚdalamiśreña salilenābhiṣiñcayet  Hbhv

tatraiva śrṚbrahmanāradasaṃvāde
pitṄn uddiśya yaiḥ pūjā keśavasya kṛtā naraih

dhanyās te mānavā loke kalikāle viśeṣatah 
ye kurvanti harer nityaṃ pitrarthaṃ pūjanaṃ mune  Hbhv 
kiṃ dattair bahubhir piñḍair gayāśrāddhādibhir mune 
yair arcito harir bhaktyā pitrarthaṃ ca dine dine  Hbhv 
yam uddiśya hareḥ pūjā kriyate munipuŚgava 
uddhṛtya narakāvāsāt taṃ nayet paramaṃ padam  Hbhv 
yo dadāti hareḥ sthānaṃ pitṄn uddiśya nārada

pitṛśeṣaṃ tu you dadyād dharaye paramātmane 
retodāḥ pitaras tasya bhavanti kleśabhāginaḥ  Hbhv 
śrṚ viṣñudharme
hariśeṣaṃ havir dadyāt pitṄñām akṣayaṃ bhavet

anyatra ca
dakṣādayaś ca pitaro bhṛtyā indrādayaḥ surāḥ 
atas tadbhaktaśeṣaṃ tu viṣñor naiva nivedayet  Hbhv  iti 
evam āvaśyakaṃ kṛtvā vaiṣñavebhyo vibhajya ca

avaiṣñave devadhṛtaṃ nirmālyaṃ na prayacchati

atha pūjāvyatiriktabhojanadoṣāḥ

kiṃ ca

brahmāñḍapurāñe

 aurvasagarasaṃvāde
