nirmālyaśeṣaṃ vratadānatulyam  Hbhv 
naivedyaśeṣaṃ tulasṚvimiśraṃ
viśeṣataḥ pādajalena siktam 
yo 'śnāti nityaṃ purato murāreḥ
prāpnoti yajñāyutakoṭipuñyam  Hbhv 
ṣaḍbhir māsopavāsais tu yat phalaṃ parikṚrtitam 
viṣñor naivedyaśeṣe yat phalaṃ tad bhuñjatāṃ kalau  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca tatra śrṚśālagrāmaśilāmāhātmye
bhaktyā bhunakti naivedyaṃ śālagrāmaśilārpitam 
koṭiṃ makhasya labhate phalaṃ śatasahasraśaḥ  Hbhv 
brahmavārigṛhasthaiś ca vānaprasthaiś ca bhikṣubhiḥ 
bhoktavyaṃ viṣñunaivedyaṃ nātra kāryā vicārañā  Hbhv 
bhuktvānyadevanaivedyaṃ dvijaś cāndrāyañaṃ caret 
bhuktvā keśavanaivedyaṃ yajñakoṭiphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrṚbrahmanāradasaṃvāde
agniṣṭomasahasrais tu vājapeyaśatair api 
tat phalaṃ prāpyate nūnaṃ viṣñor naivedyabhakṣañāt  Hbhv 
hṛdi rūpaṃ mukhe nāma naivedyam udare hareḥ 
pādodakaṃ ca nirmālyaṃ mastake yasya so 'cyutaḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
pāvanaṃ viṣñunaivedyaṃ surasiddharṣibhiḥ smṛtam 
anyadevasya naivedyaṃ bhuvattvācāndrāyañaṃ caret  Hbhv 
koṭiyajñais tu yat puñyaṃ māsopoṣañakoṭibhiḥ 
tat phalaṃ prāpyate pumbhir viṣñor naivedyabhakṣañāt  Hbhv 
tulasyāś ca rajojuṣṭaṃ naivedyasya ca bhakṣañam 
nirmālyaṃ ca dhṛtaṃ yena mahāpātakanāśanam  Hbhv 
bṛhadviṣñupurāñe 
naivedyaṃ jagadṚśasya annapānādikaṃ ca yat 
brahmavan nirvikāraṃ hi yathā viṣñus tathaiva tat  Hbhv 
vikāraṃ ye prakurvanti bhakṣañe tad dvijātayaḥ  Hbhv 
kuṣṭhavyādhisamāyuktāḥ putradāravivarjitāḥ 
nirayaṃ yānti te viprā yasmān nāvartate punaḥ  Hbhv 
viṣñudharmottare
navam annaṃ phalaṃ puṣpaṃ nivedya madhusūdane 
paścād bhuŚkte svayaṃ yaś ca tasya tuṣyati keśavaḥ  Hbhv 
brahmāñḍapurāñe
mukundāśanaśeṣaṃ tu yo hi bhuŚkte dine dine 
sikthe sikthe bhavet puñyaṃ cāndrāyañaśatādhikam  Hbhv 
anyatrāpi
ekādaśṚsahasrais tu māsopoṣañakoṭibhiḥ 
tat phalaṃ prāpyate pumbhir viṣñor naivedyabhakṣañāt  Hbhv  iti 
tato yathoktam ācamya tāmbūlādi vibhajya ca 
mahāprasādaṃ dāsyena gṛhñṚyāt prayataḥ svayam  Hbhv 
tathā ca navamaskandhe śrṚmadambarṚṣacarite BhP 
kāmaṃ ca dāsye na tu kāmakāmyayā
yathottamaślokajanāśrayā ratiḥ  Hbhv 
naivedyabhakṣañe yac ca nirmālyagrahañe ca yat 
māhātmyam ādau likhitaṃ jñeyaṃ sarvam ihāpi tat  Hbhv 
iti śrṚgopālabhaṭṭavilikhite śrṚbhagavadbhaktivilāse
mahāprasādo nāma navamo vilāsaḥ  
 SatsamgamaVilasa
daśamavilāsaḥ
śrīkṛṣṇacaraṇāmbhojamadhupebhyo namo namaḥ 
kathañcid āśrayād yeṣāṃ śvāpi tadgandhabhāg bhavet  Hbhv 
atha śrīkṛṣṇabhaktānāṃ sabhāṃ savinayaṃ śubhām 
gacched vaiṣṇavacihnāḍhyaḥ pātuṃ kṛṣṇakathāsudhām  Hbhv 
tathā ca smṛtiḥ 
itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ ṣaṣṭhasaptamakau nayet  Hbhv 
atha śrībhagavadbhaktānāṃ lakṣaṇāni 
sāmānyataḥ laiṅge 
viṣṇur eva hi yasyaiṣa devatā vaiṣṇavaḥ smṛtaḥ  Hbhv 
atra viśeṣaḥ 
vratakarmaguṇajñānabhogajanmādimatsv api 
śaiveṣv api ca kṛṣṇasya bhaktāḥ santi tathā tathā  Hbhv 
atra vratiṣu madhye bhagavadbhaktihetuvrataparatā bhagavadbhaktalakṣaṇam
tathā skānde śrīmārkaṇḍeyabhagīrathasaṃvāde 
daśamīśeṣasaṃyuktaṃ dinaṃ vaiṣṇavavallabham 
nopāsate mahīpāla te vai bhāgavatā narāḥ  Hbhv 
prāṇātyaye na cāśnanti dinaṃ prāpya harer narāḥ 
kurvanti jāgaraṃ rātrau sadā bhāgavatā hi te  Hbhv 
upoṣya dvādaśīṃ śuddhāṃ rātrau jāgaraṇānvitām 
alpāṃ tu sādhayed yas tu sa vai bhāgavato naraḥ  Hbhv 
bhaktir na vicyutā yeṣāṃ na cyutāni vratāni ca 
supriyaḥ śrīpatir yeṣāṃ te syur bhāgavatā narāḥ  Hbhv 
karmiṣu bhagavadarpaṇādinā tadājñābuddhyā vā bhaktihetuḥ sadācāraparatā 
dharmārthaṃ jīvitaṃ yeṣāṃ santānārthaṃ ca maithunam 
pacanaṃ vipramukhyārthaṃ jñeyās te vaiṣṇavā narāḥ  Hbhv 
adhvagaṃ tu pathi śrāntaṃ kāle'tra gṛham āgatam 
yo 'tithiṃ pūjayed bhaktyā vaiṣṇavaḥ sa na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
sadācāraratāḥ śiṣṭāḥ sarvabhūtānukampakāḥ 
śucayas tyaktarāgā ye sadā bhāgavatā hi te  Hbhv 
pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye śrīnāradāmbarīṣasaṃvāde  
jīvitaṃ yasya dharmārthaṃ dharmo haryartham eva ca 
ahorātrāṇi puṇyārthaṃ taṃ manye vaiṣṇavaṃ bhuvi  Hbhv 
laiṅge ca 
viṣṇubhaktisamāyuktān śrautasmārtapravartakān 
prīto bhavati yo dṛṣṭvā vaiṣṇavo 'sau prakīrtitaḥ  Hbhv 
guṇavatsu bhaktihetuḥ kṛpālutvādisadguṇaśīlatā 
skānde tatraiva 
paraduḥkhenātmaduḥkhaṃ manyante ye nṛpottama 
bhagavaddharmaniratās te narā vaiṣṇavā nṛpa  Hbhv 
tṛtīyaskandhe śrīkapiladevahūtisaṃvāde  
titikṣavaḥ kāruṇikāḥ suhṛdaḥ sarvadehinām 
ajātaśatravaḥ śāntāḥ sādhavaḥ sādhubhūṣaṇāḥ  Hbhv 
pañcamaskandhe ṛṣabhadevasya putrānuśāsane y 
mahatsevāṃ dvāram āhur vimuktes
tamodvāraṃ yoṣitāṃ saṅgisaṅgam 
mahāntas te samacittāḥ praśāntā
vimanyavaḥ suhṛdaḥ sādhavo ye  Hbhv 
ekādaśaskandhe bhagavatpradattoddhavapraśnottare  
kṛpālur akṛtadrohas titikṣuḥ sarvadehinām 
satyasāro 'navadyātmā samaḥ sarvopakārakaḥ  Hbhv 
kāmair ahatadhīr dānto mṛduḥ śucir akiñcanaḥ 
anīho mitabhuk śāntaḥ sthiro maccharaṇo muniḥ  Hbhv 
apramatto gabhīrātmā dhṛtimāñ jitaṣaḍguṇaḥ 
amānī mānadaḥ kalyo maitraḥ kāruṇikaḥ kaviḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇupurāṇe yamatadbhaṭasaṃvāde ViP  
na calati nijavarṇadharmato yaḥ
samamatir ātmasuhṛdvipakṣapakṣe 
na harati na hanti kiñcid uccaiḥ
sthitamanasaṃ tam avehi viṣṇubhaktam  Hbhv 
jñāniṣu bhaktihetur jñānavattā 
ekādaśe haviyogeśvarottare BhP  
sarvabhūteṣu yaḥ paśyed bhagavadbhāvam ātmanaḥ 
bhūtāni bhagavaty ātmany eṣa bhāgavatottamaḥ  Hbhv 
na yasya svaḥ para iti vitteṣv ātmani vā bhidā 
sarvabhūtasamaḥ śāntaḥ sa vai bhāgavatottamaḥ  Hbhv 
ekādaśe śrībhagavaduktau BhP  
jñātvājñātvātha ye vai māṃ yāvān yaś cāsmi yādṛśaḥ 
bhajanty ananyabhāvena te me bhaktatamā matāḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva haviyogeśvarottare BhP 
īśvare tadadhīneṣu bāliśeṣu dviṣatsu ca 
premamaitrīkṛpopekṣā yaḥ karoti sa madhyamaḥ  Hbhv 
arcāyām eva haraye pūjāṃ yaḥ śraddhayehate 
na tadbhakteṣu cānyeṣu sa bhaktaḥ prākṛtaḥ smṛtaḥ  Hbhv 
bhogavatsu bhaktihetur bhogānāsaktatā 
haviyogeśvarottare BhP 
gṛhītvāpīndriyair arthān yo na dveṣṭi na hṛṣyati 
viṣṇor māyām idaṃ paśyan sa vai bhāgavatottamaḥ  Hbhv 
sajjanmavidyādimatsu bhaktihetur nirabhimānitā  tatraiva BhP  
na yasya janmakarmabhyāṃ na varṇāśramajātibhiḥ 
sajjate 'sminn ahambhāvo dehe vai sa hareḥ priyaḥ  Hbhv 
bhāvāḥ kathañcid bhaktaiva jñānānāsaktyamānitā 
bhaktiniṣṭhāpakā jātās tato hy uttamatoditā  Hbhv 
śaiveṣu śrīśivakṛṣṇabhedakāḥ 
bṛhannāradīye NārP  
śive ca parameśāne viṣṇau ca paramātmani 
samabuddhyā pravarttante te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ  Hbhv 
anyac ca teṣāṃ bhagavacchāstrārthaparatādikam 
sākṣādbhaktyātmakaṃ mukhyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ likhyate'dhunā  Hbhv 
skānde 
yeṣāṃ bhāgavataṃ śāstraṃ sadā tiṣṭhati sannidhau 
pūjayanti ca ye nityaṃ te syur bhāgavatā narāḥ  Hbhv 
yeṣāṃ bhāgavataṃ śāstraṃ jīvitād adhikaṃ bhavet 
mahābhāgavatāḥ śreṣṭhā viṣṇunā kathitā narāḥ  Hbhv 
vaiṣṇavasammānaniṣṭhā  laiṅge 
viṣṇubhaktam athāyātaṃ yo dṛṣṭvā sumukhaḥ priyaḥ 
praṇāmādi karoty eva vāsudeve yathā tathā 
sa vai bhakta iti jñeyaḥ sa punāti jagat trayam  Hbhv 
rukṣākṣarā giraḥ śṛṇvan tathā bhāgavateritāḥ 
praṇāmapūrvakaṃ kṣāntvā yo vaded vaiṣṇavo hi saḥ  Hbhv 
bhojanācchādanaṃ sarvaṃ yathāśaktyā karoti yaḥ 
viṣṇubhaktasya satataṃ sa vai bhāgavataḥ smṛtaḥ  Hbhv 
gāruḍe 
yena sarvātmanā viṣṇubhaktyā bhāvo niveśitaḥ 
vaiṣṇaveṣu kṛtātmatvān mahābhāgavato hi saḥ  Hbhv 
śrītulasīsevāniṣṭhā NārP  
tulasīkānanaṃ dṛṣṭvā ye namaskurvate narāḥ 
tatkāṣṭhāṅkitakarṇā ye te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ  Hbhv 
tulasīgandham āghrāya santoṣaṃ kurvate tu ye 
tanmūlam ṛddhūtā yaiś ca te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ  Hbhv 
śrībhagavataḥ kathāparatā
bṛhannāradīye  śrībhagavanmārkaṇḍeyasaṃvāde 
matkathāśravaṇe yeṣāṃ vartate sāttvikī matiḥ 
tadbhaktaviṣṇubhaktāś ca te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ  Hbhv 
skānde śrībhagavadarjunasaṃvāde 
matkathāṃ kurute yas tu matkathāṃ ca śṛṇoti yaḥ 
hṛṣyate matkathāyāṃ ca sa vai bhāgavatottamaḥ  Hbhv 
tṛtīyaskandhe BhP  tatraiva 
madāśrayāḥ kathā mṛṣṭāḥ śṛṇvanti kathayanti ca 
tapanti vividhās tāpā naitān madgatacetasaḥ  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye  tatraiva 
manmānasāś ca madbhaktā madbhaktajanalolupāḥ 
mannāmaśravaṇāsaktās te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ  Hbhv 
ye'bhinandanti nāmāni hareḥ śrutvā'tiharṣitāḥ 
romāñcitaśarīrāśca te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ  Hbhv 
tatraivānyatra  
anyeṣām udayaṃ dṛṣṭvā ye'bhinandanti mānavāḥ 
harināmaparā ye ca te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ  Hbhv 
smaraṇaparatā tatra svadharmaniṣṭhayā rāgadveṣanivṛttyā smaraṇam
śrīviṣṇupurāṇe yamatadbhaṭasaṃvāde ViP  
na calati ya uccaiḥ śrībhagavatpadāravinde 
sitamanās tam avehi viṣṇubhaktam  Hbhv 
kalikaluṣamalena yasya nātmā
vimalamater malinīkṛtas tam enam 
manasi kṛtajanārdanaṃ manuṣyaṃ
satatam avehi harer atīvabhaktam  Hbhv 
kanakam api rahasy avekṣya buddhyā
tṛṇam iva yaḥ samavaiti parasvam 
bhavati ca bhagavaty ananyacetāḥ
puruṣavaraṃ tam avehi viṣṇubhaktam  Hbhv 
sphaṭikagiriśilāmalaḥ kva viṣṇur
manasi nṝṇāṃ kva ca matsarādidoṣaḥ 
na hi tuhinamayūkharaśmipuñje
bhavati hutāśanadīptijaḥ pratāpaḥ  Hbhv 
vimalamatir amatsaraḥ praśāntaḥ
śucicarito 'khilasattvamitrabhūtaḥ 
priyahitavacano 'stumānamāyo
vasati sadā hṛdi tasya vāsudevaḥ  Hbhv 
vasati hṛdi sanātane ca tasmin
bhavati pumān jagato 'sya saukhyarūpaḥ 
kṣitirasam atiramyam ātmano 'ntaḥ
kathayati cārutayaiva śālapotaḥ  Hbhv 
anyavijaye vairāgyādinā ca smaraṇam
ekādaśaskandhe haviyogeśvarottare BhP  
dehendriyaprāṇamanodhiyāṃ yo
janmāpyayakṣudbhayatarṣakṛcchraiḥ 
saṃsāradharmair avimuhyamānaḥ
smṛtyā harer bhāgavatapradhānaḥ  Hbhv 
tribhuvanavibhavahetave 'py akuṇṭha
smṛtir ajitātmasurādibhir vimṛgyāt 
na calati bhagavatpadāravindāl
lavanimiṣārdham api yaḥ sa vaiṣṇavāgryaḥ  Hbhv 
bhagavata uruvikramāṅghriśākhā
nakhamaṇicandrikayā nirastatāpe 
hṛdi katham upasīdatāṃ punaḥ sa
prabhavati candra ivodite 'rkatāpaḥ  Hbhv 
skānde tatraiva 
ye'rcayanti sadā viṣṇuṃ yajñeśaṃ varadaṃ harim 
dehinaḥ puṇyakarmāṇaḥ sadā bhāgavatā hi te  Hbhv 
laiṅge 
viṣṇukṣetre śubhāny eva karoti snehasaṃyutaḥ 
pratimāṃ ca harer nityaṃ pūjayet pratayāmavān  Hbhv 
viṣṇubhaktaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ karmaṇā manasā girā 
nārāyaṇaparo nityaṃ bhūpa bhāgavato hi saḥ  Hbhv 
atha vaiṣṇavadharmaniṣṭhādi
pādmottarakhaṇḍe 
tāpādipañcasaṃskārī navejyākarmakārakaḥ 
arthapañcakavid vipro mahābhāgavataḥ smṛtaḥ  Hbhv 
ekāntikatā
gāruḍe 
ekāntena sadā viṣṇau yasmād deve parāyaṇāḥ 
tasmād ekāntinaḥ proktās tadbhāgavatacetasaḥ  Hbhv 
tadvijñānenānanyaparatā
ekādaśe BhP  uddhavapraśnottare

ekādaśaskandhe BhP  
na kāmakarmabījānāṃ yasya cetasi sambhavaḥ 
vāsudevaikanilayaḥ sa vai bhāgavatottamaḥ  Hbhv 
sā ca ekāntitā caturdhā
tatra dharmānādareṇa śrīmaduddhavapraśnottara eva BhP  
ājñāyaivaṃ guṇān doṣān mayādiṣṭān api svakān 
dharmān santyajya yaḥ sarvān māṃ bhajeta sa tu sattamaḥ  Hbhv 
śrībhagavadgītāyām Gītā  
sarvadharmān parityajya mām ekaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraja 
ahaṃ tvā sarvapāpebhyo mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ  Hbhv 
caturthaskandhe BhP  
yadā yasyānugṛhṇāti bhagavān atmabhāvitaḥ 
na jahāti matiṃ loke vede ca pariniṣṭhitām  Hbhv 
anyasarvanirapekṣatā
śrībhagavaduddhavasaṃvāde BhP  ailopākhyāne 
santo 'napekṣā maccittāḥ praśāntāḥ samadarśinaḥ 
nirmamā nirahaṅkārā nirdvandvā niṣparigrahāḥ  Hbhv 
ataeva śrīkapiladevahūtisaṃvāde  
ta ete sādhavaḥ sādhvi sarvasaṅgavivarjitāḥ 
saṅgas teṣv atha te prārthyaḥ saṅgadoṣaharā hi te  Hbhv 
vighnākulatve'pi manoratiparatā 
skānde tatraiva 
yasya kṛcchragatasyāpi keśave ramate manaḥ 
na vicyutā ca bhaktir vai sa vai bhāgavato naraḥ  Hbhv 
āpadgatasya yasyeha bhakir avyabhicāriṇī 
nānyatra ramate cittaṃ sa vai bhāgavato naraḥ  Hbhv 
premaikarasatā 
śrīṛṣabhadevasya putrānuśāsane BhP  
ye vā mayīśe kṛtasauhṛdārthā
janeṣu dehambharavārtikeṣu 
gṛheṣu jāyātmajarātimatsu
na prītiyuktā yāvadarthāś ca loke  Hbhv 
tridhā premaikaparatā premṇaḥ syāt tāratamyataḥ 
uttamā madhyamā cāsau kaniṣṭhā ceti bhedataḥ  Hbhv 
tatrottamā 
yathā ekādaśe haviyogeśvarottare BhP  
sarvabhūteṣu yaḥ paśyed bhagavadbhāvam ātmanaḥ 
bhūtāni bhagavaty ātmany eṣa bhāgavatottamaḥ  Hbhv 
sveṣṭadevasya bhāvaṃ yaḥ sarvabhūteṣu paśyati 
bhāvayanti ca tāny asminn ity arthaḥ sammataḥ satām  Hbhv 
śrīkapiladevahūtisaṃvāde  
mayy ananyena bhāvena bhaktiṃ kurvanti ye dṛḍhām 
matkṛte tyaktakarmāṇas tyaktasvajanabāndhavāḥ  Hbhv 
śrīhaviyogeśvarottare BhP  
visṛjati hṛdayaṃ na yasya sākṣād
dharir avaśābhihito 'py aghaughanāśaḥ 
praṇayarasanayā dhṛtāṅghripadmaḥ
sa bhavati bhāgavatapradhāna uktaḥ  Hbhv 
tatra madhyamā 
śrīhaviyogeśvarottare BhP  
īśvare tadadhīneṣu bāliśeṣu dviṣatsu ca 
premamaitrīkṛpopekṣā yaḥ karoti sa madhyamaḥ  Hbhv 
tatra kaniṣṭhā 
tatraiva BhP  
arcāyām eva haraye pūjāṃ yaḥ śraddhayehate 
na tadbhakteṣu cānyeṣu sa bhaktaḥ prākṛtaḥ smṛtaḥ  Hbhv 
śraddhayā pūjanaṃ premabodhakaṃ bhakta ity api 
lakṣaṇāni ca yāny agre bhakter lekhyāni tāny api  Hbhv 
vandanādīni vidyante yeṣu bhāgavatā hi te 
etāni lakṣaṇānītthaṃ gauṇamukhyādibhedataḥ  Hbhv 
ūhyāni lakṣaṇāny evaṃ vivecyāni parāṇy api  Hbhv 
īdṛglakṣaṇavantaḥ syur durlabhā bahavo janāḥ 
divyā hi maṇayo vyaktaṃ na varterann itas tataḥ  Hbhv 
ataevoktaṃ mokṣadharme nārāyaṇīye Mbh  
jāyamānaṃ hi puruṣaṃ yaṃ paśyen madhusūdanaḥ 
sāttvikas tu sa vijñeyo bhaven mokṣe ca niścitaḥ  Hbhv 
evaṃ saṅkṣipya likhitād vaiṣṇavānāṃ tu lakṣaṇāt 
māhātmyam api vijñeyaṃ likhyate'nyac ca tat kiyat  Hbhv 
atha bhagavadbhaktānāṃ māhātmyam 
sauparṇe śrīśakroktau 
kalau bhāgavataṃ nāma yasya puṃsaḥ prajāyate 
jananī putriṇī tena pitṝṇāṃ tu dhurandharaḥ  Hbhv 
kalau bhāgavataṃ nāma durlabhaṃ naiva labhyate 
brahmarudrapadotkṛṣṭaṃ guruṇā kathitaṃ mama  Hbhv 
yasya bhāgavataṃ cihnaṃ dṛśyate tu harir mune 
gīyate ca kalau devā jñeyās te nāsti saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
śrīmārkaṇḍeyoktau 
samīpe tiṣṭhate yasya ha antakāle'pi vaiṣṇavaḥ 
gacchate paramaṃ sthānaṃ yadyapi brahmahā bhavet  Hbhv 
nāradīye śrīvāmadevarukmāṅgadasaṃvāde NārP  
śvapaco 'pi mahīpāla viṣṇubhakto dvijādhikaḥ 
viṣṇubhaktivihīnas tu dvijo 'pi śvapacādhikaḥ  Hbhv 
skānde revākhaṇḍe śrībrahmoktau 
indro maheśvaro brahmā paraṃ brahma tadaiva hi 
śvapaco 'pi bhavaty eva yadā tuṣṭā'si keśava  Hbhv 
śvapacād api kaṣṭatvaṃ brahmeśānādayaḥ surāḥ 
tadaivācyuta yānty ete yadaiva tvaṃ parāṅmukhaḥ  Hbhv 
sa kartā sarvadharmāṇāṃ bhakto yas tava keśava 
sa kartā sarvapāpānāṃ yo na bhaktas tavācyuta  Hbhv 
dharmo bhavaty adharmo 'pi kṛto bhaktais tavācyuta 
pāpaṃ bhavati dharmo 'pi tavābhaktaiḥ kṛto hareḥ  Hbhv 
niḥśeṣadharmakartā vāpy abhakto narake hare 
sadā tiṣṭhati bhaktas te brahmahāpi viśudhyati  Hbhv 
niścalā tvayi bhaktir yā saiva muktir janārdana 
muktā eva hi bhaktās te tava viṣṇo yato hare  Hbhv 
tatraiva durvāsonāradasaṃvāde 
nūnaṃ bhāgavatā loke lokarakṣāviśāradāḥ 
vrajanti viṣṇunādiṣṭā hṛdisthena mahāmune  Hbhv 
bhagavān eva sarvatra bhūtānāṃ kṛpayā hariḥ 
rakṣaṇāya caran lokān bhaktarūpeṇa nārada  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde 
yas tu viṣṇuparo nityaṃ dṛḍhabhaktir jitendriyaḥ 
svagṛhe'pi vasan yāti tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam  Hbhv 
aśvamedhasahasrāṇāṃ sahasraṃ yaḥ karoti vai 
nāsau tatphalam āpnoti tadbhaktair yad avāpyate  Hbhv 
tatraivāmṛtasāroddhāre śrīyamatadbhaṭasaṃvāde 
sarvatra vaiṣṇavāḥ pūjyāḥ svarge martye rasātale 
devatānāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ tathaivoragarakṣasām  Hbhv 
yeṣāṃ smaraṇamātreṇa pāpalakṣaśatāni ca 
dahyante nātra sandeho vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahātmanām  Hbhv 
yeṣāṃ pādarajenaiva prāpyate jāhnavījalam 
nārmadaṃ yāmunaṃ caiva kiṃ punaḥ pādayor jalam  Hbhv 
yeṣāṃ vākyajalaughena vinā gaṅgājalair api 
vinā tīrthasahasreṇa snāto bhavati mānavaḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva cāturmāsyamāhātmye 
tāvad bhramanti saṃsāre pitaraḥ piṇḍatatparaḥ 
yāvat kule bhaktiyuktaḥ suto naiva prajāyate  Hbhv 
sa eva jñānavān loke yogināṃ prathamo hi saḥ 
mahākratūnām āhartā haribhaktiyuto hi yaḥ  Hbhv 
kāśīkhaṇḍe dhruvacarite 
na cyavante hi yadbhaktyā mahatyāṃ pralayāpadi 
ato 'cyuto 'khile loke sa ekaḥ sarvago 'vyayaḥ  Hbhv 
na tasmād bhagavadbhaktād bhetavyaṃ kenacit kvacit 
niyataṃ viṣṇubhaktā yena te syuḥ paratāpinaḥ  Hbhv 
tatraivāgre 
brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ vaiśyaḥ śūdro vā yadi vetaraḥ 
viṣṇubhaktisamāyukto jñeyaḥ sarvottamottamaḥ  Hbhv 
śaṅkhacakrāṅkitatanuḥ śirasā mañjarīdharaḥ 
gopīcandanaliptāṅgo dṛṣṭaś ced tadaghaṃ kutaḥ  Hbhv 
mahābhārate rājadharme
īśvaraṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ jagataḥ prabhavāpyayam 
bhaktā nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ durgāṇy atitaranti te  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare
śayanād utthito yas tu kīrtayen madhusūdanam 
kīrtanāt tasya pāpāni nāśam āyānty aśeṣataḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva
yasyāpy anante jagatām adhīśe
bhaktiḥ parā yādavadevadeve 
tasmāt paraṃ nāparam asti kiñcit
pātraṃ triloke puruṣapravīra  Hbhv 
dvārakāmāhātmye śrīprahlādabalisaṃvāde
nityaṃ ye prātar utthāya vaiṣṇavānāṃ tu kīrtanam 
kurvanti te bhāgavatāḥ kṛṣṇatulyāḥ kalau bale  Hbhv 
haribhaktisudhodaye
svadarśanasparśanapūjanaiḥ kṛtī
tamāṃsi viṣṇupratimeva vaiṣṇavaḥ 
dhunvan vasaty atra janasya yan na tat
svārthaṃ paraṃ lokahitāya dīpavat  Hbhv 
itihāsasamuccaye śrīlomaśavākye
ye bhajanti jagadyoniṃ vāsudevaṃ sanātanam 
na tebhyo vidyate tīrtham adhikaṃ rājasattama  Hbhv 
yatra bhāgavatāḥ snānaṃ kurvanti vimalāśrayāḥ 
tattīrtham adhikaṃ viddhi sarvapāpaviśodhanam  Hbhv 
yatra rāgādirahitā vāsudevaparāyaṇāḥ 
tatra sannihito viṣṇur nṛpate nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
na gandhair na tathā toyair na puṣpaiś ca manoharaiḥ 
sānnidhyaṃ kurute devo yatra santi na vaiṣṇavāḥ  Hbhv 
balibhiś copavāsaiś ca nṛtyagītādibhis tathā 
nityam ārādhyamāno 'pi tatra viṣṇur na tṛpyati  Hbhv 
tasmād ete mahābhāgā vaiṣṇavā vītakalmaṣāḥ 
punanti sakalān lokāṃs tat tīrtham adhikaṃ tataḥ  Hbhv 
śūdraṃ vā bhagavadbhaktaṃ niṣādaṃ śvapacaṃ tathā 
vīkṣataṃ jātisāmānyāt sa yāti narakaṃ dhruvam  Hbhv 
tasmād viṣṇuprasādāya vaiṣṇavān paritoṣayet 
prasādasumukho viṣṇus tenaiva syān na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrīnāradapuṇḍarīkasaṃvāde 
ye nṛśaṃsā durātmānaḥ pāpācāraratāḥ sadā 
te'pi yānti paraṃ dhāma nārāyaṇaparāśrayāḥ  Hbhv 
lipyante na ca pāpena vaiṣṇavā viṣṇutatparāḥ 
punanti sakalān lokān sahasrāṃśur ivoditaḥ  Hbhv 
janmāntarasahasreṣu yasya syād buddhir īdṛśī 
dāso 'haṃ vāsudevasya sarvān lokān samuddharet  Hbhv 
sa yāti viṣṇusālokyaṃ puruṣo nātra saṃśayaḥ 
kiṃ punas tadgataprāṇāḥ puruṣāḥ saṃyatendriyāḥ  Hbhv 
smṛtaḥ sambhāṣito vāpi pūjito vā dvijottamāḥ 
punāti bhagavadbhaktaś cāṇḍālo 'pi yadṛcchayā  Hbhv 
śrīvyāsavākye 
janmāntarasahasreṣu viṣṇubhakto na lipyate 
yasya sandarśanād eva bhasmībhavati pātakam  Hbhv 
itihāsasamuccaye śrībhagavadvākye 
na me priyaś caturvedī madbhaktaḥ śvapacaḥ priyaḥ 
tasmai deyaṃ tato grāhyaṃ sa ca pūjyo yathā hy aham  Hbhv 
tatraiva brahmavākye 
sabhartṛkā vā vidhavā viṣṇubhaktiṃ karoti yā 
samuddharati cātmānaṃ kulam ekottaraṃ śatam  Hbhv 
dvārakāmāhātmye prahlādabalisaṃvāde 
saṅkīrṇayonayaḥ pūtā ye bhaktā madhusūdane 
mlecchatulyāḥ kulīnās te ye na bhaktā janārdane  Hbhv 
ādipurāṇe śrīkṛṣṇārjunasaṃvāde 
vaiṣṇavān bhaja kaunteya mā bhajasvānyadevatāḥ 
punanti vaiṣṇavāḥ sarve sarvadevam idaṃ jagat 
madbhakto durlabho yasya sa eva mama durlabhaḥ  Hbhv 
tatparo durlabho nāsti satyaṃ satyaṃ dhanañjaya 
jagatāṃ guravo bhaktā bhaktānāṃ guravo vayam 
sarvatra guravo bhaktā vayaṃ ca guravo yathā 
asmākaṃ bāndhavā bhaktā bhaktānāṃ bāndhavā vayam  Hbhv 
asmākaṃ guravo bhaktā bhaktānāṃ guravo vayam 
madbhaktā yatra gacchanti tatra gacchāmi pārthiva 
bhaktānām anugacchanti muktayaḥ śrutibhiḥ saha  Hbhv 
ye me bhaktajanāḥ pārtha na me bhaktāś ca te janāḥ 
madbhaktānāṃ ca ye bhaktās te me bhaktatamā matāḥ  Hbhv 
ye kecit prāṇino bhaktā madarthe tyaktabāndhavāḥ 
teṣām ahaṃ parikrīto nānyakrīto dhanañjaya  Hbhv 
eṣāṃ bhakṣyaṃ sunirṇītaṃ śrūyatāṃ niścitaṃ mama 
ucchiṣṭam avaśiṣṭaṃ ca bhaktānāṃ bhojanadvayam  Hbhv 
nāmayuktajanāḥ kecij jātyantarasamanvitāḥ 
kurvanti me yathā prītiṃ na tathā vedapāragāḥ  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye mārkaṇḍeyaṃ prati śrībhagavaduktau  
viṣṇur bhaktakuṭumbīti vadanti vibudhāḥ sadā 
tad eva pālayiṣyāmi majjano nānṛtaṃ vadet  Hbhv 
mama janma kule yasya tat kulaṃ mokṣagāmi vai 
mayi tuṣṭe muniśreṣṭha kim asādhyaṃ jagattraye  Hbhv 
mayi bhaktiparo yas tu madyājī matkathāparaḥ 
maddhyānī svakulaṃ sarvaṃ nayaty acyutarūpatām  Hbhv 
madarthaṃ karma kurvāṇo matpraṇāmaparo naraḥ 
manmanāḥ svakulaṃ sarvaṃ nayaty acyutarūpatām  Hbhv 
aham eva dvijaśreṣṭha nityaṃ pracchannavigrahaḥ 
bhagavadbhaktarūpeṇa lokān rakṣāmi sarvadā  Hbhv 
tatraivāditimāhātmye śrīsūtoktau 
viprāḥ śṛṇudhvaṃ māhātmyaṃ haribhaktiratātmanām 
haridhyānaparāṇāṃ tu kaḥ samarthaḥ prabādhitum  Hbhv 
haribhaktiparo yatra tatra brahmā hariḥ śivaḥ 
tatra devāś ca siddhādyā nityaṃ tiṣṭhanti sattamāḥ  Hbhv 
nimiṣaṃ nimṣārdhaṃ vā yatra tiṣṭhanti sattamāḥ 
tatraiva sarvaśreyāṃsi tat tīrthaṃ tat tapovanam  Hbhv 
tatraivāditiṃ prati śrībhagavaduttare NārP 
rāgadveṣavihīnā ye madbhaktā matparāyaṇāḥ 
vadanti satataṃ te māṃ gatāsūyā adāmbhikāḥ  Hbhv 
paropatāpavimukhāḥ śivabhaktiparāyaṇāḥ 
matkathāśravaṇāsaktā vahanti satataṃ hi mām  Hbhv 
tatraiva dhvajāropaṇamāhātmye śrīviṣṇudūtoktau NārP  
yatīnāṃ viṣṇubhaktānāṃ paricaryāparāyaṇāḥ 
īkṣitā api gacchanti pāpino 'pi parāṃ gatim  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrībhagavattoṣaprakārapraśnottare NārP  
ripavas taṃ na hiṃsanti na bādhante grahāś ca tam 
rākṣasāś ca na cekṣante naraṃ viṣṇuparāyaṇam  Hbhv 
bhaktir dṛḍhā bhaved yasya devadeve janārdane 
śreyāṃsi tasya sidhyanti bhaktimanto 'dhikās tataḥ  Hbhv 
tatraivāgre NārP  
adyāpi ca muniśreṣṭha brahmādyā api devatāḥ 
prabhāvaṃ na vijānanti viṣṇubhaktiratātmanām  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca NārP  
dharmārthakāmamokṣākhyāḥ puruṣārthā dvijottamāḥ 
haribhaktiparāṇāṃ vai sampadyante na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva lubdhakopākhyānasyādau NārP  
ye viṣṇuniratāḥ śāntā lokānugrahatatparāḥ 
sarvabhūtadayāyuktā viṣṇurūpāḥ parikīrtitāḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇubhaktivihīnā ye caṇḍālāḥ parikīrtitāḥ 
caṇḍālā api vai śreṣṭhā haribhaktiparāyaṇāḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva yajñadhvajopākhyānasyādau śrīsūtavākyam NārP  
haribhaktirasāsvādamuditā ye narottamāḥ 
namaskaromy ahaṃ tebhyo yatsaṅgān muktibhāg naraḥ  Hbhv 
haribhaktiparā ye tu harināmaparāyaṇāḥ 
durvṛttā vā suvṛttā vā tebhyo nityaṃ namo namaḥ  Hbhv 
aho bhāgyam aho bhāgyaṃ viṣṇubhaktiratātmanām 
yasmān muktiḥ karasthaiva yoginām api durlabhā  Hbhv 
tatraiva kaliprasaṅge NārP 
ghore kaliyuge prāpte sarvadharmavivarjite 
vāsudevaparā martyāḥ kṛtārthā nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
asty antar durlabhā proktā haribhaktiḥ kalau yuge 
haribhaktiratānāṃ vai pāpabandho na jāyate  Hbhv 
vedavādaratāḥ sarve tathā tīrthaniṣeviṇaḥ 
haribhaktirataiḥ sārdhaṃ kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm  Hbhv 
ataevoktaṃ devais tatraiva bhāratavarṣaprasaṅge NārP  
harikīrtanaśīlo vā tadbhaktānāṃ priyo 'pi vā 
śuśrūṣur vāpi mahatāṃ sa vandyo 'smābhir uttamaḥ  Hbhv 
pādme śrībhagavadbrahmasaṃvāde 
darśanadhyānasaṃsparśair martyakūrmavihaṅgamāḥ 
puṣṇanti svāny apatyāni tathāham api padmaja  Hbhv 
muhūrtenāpi saṃhartuṃ śaktau yadyapi dānavāt 
madbhaktānāṃ vinodārthaṃ karomi vividhāḥ kriyāḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva māghamāhātmye devadūtavikuṇḍalasaṃvāde 
na vayaṃ yamaṃ yamalokaṃ na na dūtān ghoradarśanāt 
paśyanti vaiṣṇavā nūnaṃ satyaṃ satyaṃ mayoditam  Hbhv 
śvapākam iva nekṣeta loke vipram avaiṣṇavam 
vaiṣṇavo varṇabāhyo 'pi punāti bhuvanatrayam  Hbhv 
na śūdrā bhagavadbhaktās te tu bhāvanā matāḥ 
sarvavarṇeṣu te śūdrā ye na bhaktā janārdana  Hbhv 
viṣṇubhaktasya ye dāsā vaiṣṇavānnabhujaś ca ye 
te'pi kratubhujāṃ gvaiśya gatiṃ yānti nirākulāḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva vaiśākhamāhātmye pañcapuruṣāṇām uktau 
bhavyāni bhūtāni janārdanasya
paropakārāya caranti viśvam  Hbhv 
tathā 
santaḥ pratiṣṭhā dīnānāṃ daivād udbhūtapāpmanām 
ārtānām ārtihantāro darśanād eva sādhavaḥ  Hbhv 
tatraivottarakhaṇḍe śivapārvatīsaṃvāde PadmaP 
na karmabandhanaṃ janma vaiṣṇavānāṃ ca vidyate 
viṣṇor anucaratvaṃ hi mokṣayāhur manīṣiṇaḥ  Hbhv 
na dāsyam amareśasya bandhanaṃ parikīrtitam 
sarvabandhananirmuktā haridāsā nirāmayāḥ  Hbhv 
brahmāṇḍapurāṇe janmāṣṭamīvratamāhātmye śrīcitraguptoktau 
darśanasparśanālāpasahavāsādibhiḥ kṣaṇāt 
bhaktāḥ punanti kṛṣṇasya sākṣād api ca pukkaśam  Hbhv 
tyaktasarvakulācāro mahāpātakavān api 
viṣṇor bhaktaṃ samāśritya naro nārhati yātanām  Hbhv 
vāśiṣṭhe 
yasmin deśe marau tajjño nāsti sajjanapādapaḥ 
saphalaḥ śītalacchāyo na tatra divasaṃ vaset  Hbhv 
sadā santo 'bhigantavyā yadyapy upadiśanti na 
yā hi svairakathās teṣām upadeśā bhavanti te  Hbhv 
gāruḍe 
satrayājisahasrebhyaḥ sarvavedāntapāragaḥ 
sarvavedāntavitkoṭyā viṣṇubhakto viśiṣyate  Hbhv 
vaiṣṇavānāṃ sahasrebhya ekānty eko viśiṣyate 
ekāntinas tu puruṣā gacchanti paramaṃ padam  Hbhv 
śrībhagavadgītāsu Gītā  
api cet sudurācāro bhajate mām ananyabhāk 
sādhur eva sa mantavyaḥ samyag vyavasito hi saḥ  Hbhv 
kṣipraṃ bhavati dharmātmā śaśvacchāntiṃ nigacchati 
kaunteya pratijānīhi na me bhaktaḥ praṇaśyati  Hbhv 
māṃ hi pārtha vyapāśritya ye 'pi syuḥ pāpayonayaḥ 
striyo vaiśyās tathā śūdrās te 'pi yānti parāṃ gatim 
kiṃ punar brāhmaṇāḥ puṇyā bhaktā rājarṣayas tathā  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca tatraiva Gītā  
yoginām api sarveṣāṃ madgatenāntarātmanā 
śraddhāvān bhajate yo māṃ sa me yuktatamo mataḥ  Hbhv 
śrībhāgavatasya prathamaskandhe śrīparīkṣitoktau BhP  
yeṣāṃ saṃsmaraṇāt puṃsāṃ sadyaḥ śuddhyanti vai gṛhāḥ 
kiṃ punar darśanasparśa pādaśaucāsanādibhiḥ  Hbhv 
tṛtīyaskandhe śrīvidurasya BhP  
śrutasya puṃsāṃ suciraśramasya
nanv añjasā sūribhir īḍito 'rthaḥ 
tattadguṇānuśravaṇaṃ mukunda
pādāravindaṃ hṛdayeṣu yeṣām  Hbhv 
devahūtiṃ prati kapiladevasya BhP  
na karhicin matparāḥ śāntarūpe
naṅkṣyanti no me 'nimiṣo leḍhi hetiḥ 
yeṣām ahaṃ priya ātmā sutaś ca
sakhā guruḥ suhṛdo daivam iṣṭam  Hbhv 
caturthe śrīdhruvasya BhP  
yā nirvṛtis tanubhṛtāṃ tava pādapadma
dhyānād bhavajjanakathāśravaṇena vā syāt 
sā brahmaṇi svamahimany api nātha mā bhūt
kiṃ tv antakāsilulitāt patatāṃ vimānāt  Hbhv 
śrīrudrasya BhP 
svadharmaniṣṭhaḥ śatajanmabhiḥ pumān
viriñcatām eti tataḥ paraṃ hi mām 
avyākṛtaṃ bhāgavato 'tha vaiṣṇavaṃ
padaṃ yathāhaṃ vibudhāḥ kalātyaye  Hbhv 
pañcame śrījaḍabharatasya BhP  
rahūgaṇaitat tapasā na yāti
na cejyayā nirvapaṇād gṛhād vā 
na cchandasā naiva jalāgnisūryair
vinā mahatpādarajo'bhiṣekam  Hbhv 
ṣaṣṭhe śrīparīkṣitaḥ BhP  
rajobhiḥ samasaṅkhyātāḥ pārthivair iha jantavaḥ 
teṣāṃ ye kecanehante śreyo vai manujādayaḥ  Hbhv 
prāyo mumukṣavas teṣāṃ kecanaiva dvijottama 
mumukṣūṇāṃ sahasreṣu kaścin mucyeta sidhyati  Hbhv 
muktānām api siddhānāṃ nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ 
sudurlabhaḥ praśāntātmā koṭiṣv api mahāmune  Hbhv 
śrīśivasya BhP  
nārāyaṇaparāḥ sarve na kutaścana bibhyati 
svargāpavarganarakeṣv api tulyārthadarśinaḥ  Hbhv 
saptame śrīprahlādasya BhP  
naiṣāṃ matis tāvad urukramāṅghriṃ
spṛśaty anarthāpagamo yadarthaḥ 
mahīyasāṃ pādarajo'bhiṣekaṃ
niṣkiñcanānāṃ na vṛṇīta yāvat  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca BhP  
viprād dviṣaḍguṇayutād aravindanābha
pādāravindavimukhāt śvapacaṃ variṣṭham 
manye tadarpitamanovacanehitārtha
prāṇaṃ punāti sa kulaṃ na tu bhūrimānaḥ  Hbhv 
aṣṭame śrīgajendrasya BhP  
ekāntino yasya na kañcanārthaṃ
vāñchanti ye vai bhagavatprapannāḥ 
atyadbhutaṃ taccaritaṃ sumaṅgalaṃ
gāyanta ānandasamudramagnāḥ  Hbhv 
navame śrībhagavataḥ BhP   
ahaṃ bhaktaparādhīno hy asvatantra iva dvija 
sādhubhir grastahṛdayo bhaktair bhaktajanapriyaḥ  Hbhv 
nāham ātmānam āśāse madbhaktaiḥ sādhubhir vinā 
śriyaṃ cātyantikīṃ brahman yeṣāṃ gatir ahaṃ parā  Hbhv 
ye dārāgāraputrāpta prāṇān vittam imaṃ param 
hitvā māṃ śaraṇaṃ yātāḥ kathaṃ tāṃs tyaktum utsahe  Hbhv 
mayi nirbaddhahṛdayāḥ sādhavaḥ samadarśanāḥ 
vaśe kurvanti māṃ bhaktyā satstriyaḥ satpatiṃ yathā  Hbhv 
sādhavo hṛdayaṃ mahyaṃ sādhūnāṃ hṛdayaṃ tv aham 
madanyat te na jānanti nāhaṃ tebhyo manāg api  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrīdurvāsasaḥ BhP  
duṣkaraḥ ko nu sādhūnāṃ dustyajo vā mahātmanām 
yaiḥ saṅgṛhīto bhagavān sātvatām ṛṣabho hariḥ  Hbhv 
yannāmaśrutimātreṇa pumān bhavati nirmalaḥ 
tasya tīrthapadaḥ kiṃ vā dāsānām avaśiṣyate  Hbhv 
daśame devastutau BhP  
tathā na te mādhava tāvakāḥ kvacid
bhraśyanti mārgāt tvayi baddhasauhṛdāḥ 
tvayābhiguptā vicaranti nirbhayā
vināyakānīkapamūrdhasu prabho  Hbhv 
śrībādarāyaṇeḥ BhP  
nāyaṃ sukhāpo bhagavān dehināṃ gopikāsutaḥ 
jñānināṃ cātmabhūtānāṃ yathā bhaktimatām iha  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrībhagavataḥ BhP  
sādhūnāṃ samacittānāṃ mukundacaraṇaiṣiṇām 
upekṣyaiḥ kiṃ dhanastambhair asadbhir asadāśrayaiḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca BhP  
na hy ammayāni tīrthāni na devā mṛcchilāmayāḥ 
te punanty urukālena darśanād eva sādhavaḥ  Hbhv 
api ca BhP  
nāgnir na sūryo na ca candratārakā
na bhūr jalaṃ khaṃ śvasano 'tha vāṅ manaḥ 
upāsitā bhedakṛto haranty aghaṃ
vipaścito ghnanti muhūrtasevayā  Hbhv 
yasyātmabuddhiḥ kuṇape tridhātuke
svadhīḥ kalatrādiṣu bhauma ijyadhīḥ 
yattīrthabuddhiḥ salile na karhicij
janeṣv abhijñeṣu sa eva gokharaḥ  Hbhv 
śrutistutau BhP  
tava pari ye caranty akhilasattvaniketatayā
ta uta padākramanty avigaṇayya śiro nirṛteḥ 
parivayase paśūn iva girā vibudhān api tāṃs
tvayi kṛtasauhṛdāḥ khalu punanti na ye vimukhāḥ  Hbhv 
ekādaśe śrīvasudevasya BhP  
bhūtānāṃ devacaritaṃ duḥkhāya ca sukhāya ca 
sukhāyaiva hi sādhūnāṃ tvādṛśām acyutātmanām  Hbhv 
bhajanti ye yathā devān devā api tathaiva tān 
chāyeva karmasacivāḥ sādhavo dīnavatsalāḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrībhagavataḥ BhP  
na mayy ekāntabhaktānāṃ guṇadoṣodbhavā guṇāḥ 
sādhūnāṃ samacittānāṃ buddheḥ param upeyuṣām  Hbhv 
evam etān mayā diṣṭān anutiṣṭhanti me pathaḥ 
kṣemaṃ vindanti matsthānaṃ yad brahma paramaṃ viduḥ  Hbhv 
nimajjyonmajjatāṃ ghore bhavābdhau paramāyaṇam 
santo brahmavidaḥ śāntā nor dṛḍhevāpsu majjatām  Hbhv 
annaṃ hi prāṇināṃ prāṇā ārtānāṃ śaraṇaṃ tv aham 
dharmā vittaṃ nṝṇāṃ pretya santo 'rvāgbibhyato 'raṇam  Hbhv 
santo diśanti cakṣūṃṣi bahir arkaḥ samutthitaḥ 
devatā bāndhavāḥ santaḥ santa ātmāham eva ca  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca BhP  
na kiñcit sādhavo dhīrā bhaktā hy ekāntino mama 
vāñchanty api mayā dattaṃ kaivalyam apunarbhavam  Hbhv 
dvādaśe ca śrīparīkṣitaḥ BhP  
nātyadbhutam ahaṃ manye mahatām acyutātmanām 
ajñeṣu tāpatapteṣu bhūteṣu yad anugrahaḥ  Hbhv 
śrīrudrasya ca mārkaṇḍeyam adhikṛtya BhP  
śravaṇād darśanād vāpi mahāpātakino 'pi vaḥ 
śudhyerann antyajāś cāpi kim u sambhāṣaṇādibhiḥ  Hbhv 
ataeva śrīdharmarājasya svadūtānuśāsane ṣaṣṭhaskandhe BhP  
te devasiddhaparigītapavitragāthā
ye sādhavaḥ samadṛśo bhagavatprapannāḥ 
tān nopasīdata harer gadayābhiguptān
naiṣāṃ vayaṃ na ca vayaḥ prabhavāma daṇḍe  Hbhv 
tathā śrīviṣṇupurāṇe ViP  
yamaniyamavidhūtakalmaṣāṇām
anudinam acyutasaktamānasānām 
apagatam adamānamatsarāṇāṃ
vraja bhaṭa dūratareṇa mānavānām  Hbhv 
sakalam idam ahaṃ ca vāsudevaḥ
paramapumān parameśvaraḥ sa ekaḥ 
iti matir acalā bhavaty anante
hṛdayagate vraja tān vihāya dūrāt  Hbhv 
kamalanayana vāsudeva viṣṇo
dharaṇidharācyuta śaṅkhacakrapāṇe 
bhava śaraṇam itīrayanti ye vai
tyaja bhaṭa dūratareṇa tān apāpān  Hbhv 
vasati manasi yasya so 'vyayātmā 
puruṣavarasya na tasya dṛṣṭipāte 
tava gatir atha vā mamāsti cakra
pratihatavīryabalasya so 'nyalokyaḥ  Hbhv 
nārasiṃhe viṣṇupurāṇe ca ViP 
aham amarārcitena dhātrā
yama iti lokahitāhite niyuktaḥ 
hariguruvaśago 'smi na svatantraḥ
prabhavati saṃyamane mamāpi viṣṇuḥ  Hbhv 
sugatim abhilaṣāmi vāsudevā
vaham api bhāgavatasthitāntarātmā 
madhuvara vaśago 'smi na svatantraḥ
prabhavati saṃyamane mamāpi kṛṣṇaḥ  Hbhv 
na hi śaśakaluṣacchaviḥ kadācit
timiraparābhavatām upaiti candraḥ 
bhagavati ca harāv ananyacetā
bhṛśamalino 'pi virājate manuṣyaḥ  Hbhv 
pādme devadyūtivikuṇḍalasaṃvāde PadmaP  
prāhāsmān yamunā bhrātā sadaiva hi punaḥ punaḥ 
bhavadbhir vaiṣṇavās tyājyā na te syur mama gocarāḥ  Hbhv 
durācāro duṣkṛto 'pi sadācārarato 'pi yaḥ 
bhavadbhiḥ sa sadā tyājyo viṣṇuṃ ca bhajate naraḥ  Hbhv 
vaiṣṇavo yadgṛhe bhuṅkte yeṣāṃ vaiṣṇavasaṅgatiḥ 
te'pi vaḥ parivāryāḥ syus tatsaṅgahatakilbiṣāḥ  Hbhv 
skānde amṛtasāroddhāre 
ekādaśyām abhuñjānā yuktāḥ pāpaśatair api 
bhavadbhiḥ parihartavyā hitā me yadi sarvadā  Hbhv 
ye smaranti jagannāthaṃ mṛtyukāle janārdanam 
pāpakoṭiśatair yuktā na te grāhyā mamājñayā  Hbhv 
na brahmā na śivāgnīndrā nāhaṃ nānye divaukasaḥ 
śaktā na nigrahaṃ kartuṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahātmanām  Hbhv 
ato 'haṃ sarvakālaṃ ca vaiṣṇavānāṃ bibhemi vai 
bhavadbhiḥ parihartavyā vaiṣṇavā ye sadaiva hi  Hbhv 
vaiṣṇavā viṣṇuvat pūjyā mama mānyā viśeṣataḥ 
teṣāṃ kṛte'pamāne'pi vināśo jāyate dhruvam  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca 
yeṣāṃ smaraṇamātreṇa pāpalakṣaśatāni ca 
dahyante nātra sandeho vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahātmanām  Hbhv 
yeṣāṃ pādarajenaiva prāpyate jāhnavījalam 
nārmadaṃ yāmunaṃ caiva kiṃ punaḥ pādayor jalam  Hbhv 
yeṣāṃ vākyajalaughena vinā gaṅgājalair api 
vinā tīrthasahasreṇa snāto bhavati mānavaḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca 
brahmaloke na me vāso na me vāso harālaye 
nālaye lokapālānāṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ parābhave  Hbhv 
na devā na ca gandharvā na yakṣoragarākṣasāḥ 
trātuṃ samarthā ṛṣayo vaiṣṇavānāṃ parābhave  Hbhv 
karomi karmaṇā vācā manasāpi na vipriyam 
vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahābhāgāḥ sudarśanabhayād api  Hbhv 
ekato dhāvate cakram ekato harivāhanam 
ekato viṣṇudūtāś ca vaiṣṇave cārdite mayā  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye caikādaśīmāhātmye NārP   
ye viṣṇupūjanaratāḥ prayatāḥ kṛtajñāś
caikādaśīvrataparā vijitendriyāś ca 
nārāyaṇācyuta hare śaraṇaṃ bhaveti
śāntā vadanti satataṃ tarasā tyajadhvam  Hbhv 
nārāyaṇārpitadhiyo haribhaktabhaktān
svācāramārganiratān gurusevakāṃś ca 
satpātradānaniratān harikīrtibhaktān
dūtās tyajadhvam aniśaṃ harināmasaktān  Hbhv 
pāṣaṇḍasaṅgarahitān haribhaktituṣṭān
satsaṅgalolupatarāṃś ca tathātipuṇyān 
śambhor hareś ca samabuddhimatas tathaiva
dūtās tyajadhvam upakāraparāñ narāṇām  Hbhv 
ye vīkṣitā harikathāmṛtasevakaiś ca
nārāyaṇasmṛtiparāyaṇamānasaiś ca 
viprendrapādajalasevanasamprahṛṣṭais
tān pāpino 'pi ca bhaṭā satataṃ tyajadhvam  Hbhv 
ataevoktaṃ śrīnāradena caturthaskandhaśeṣe BhP 
śriyam anucaratīṃ tadarthinaś ca
dvipadapatīn vibudhāṃś ca yat svapūrṇaḥ 
na bhajati nijabhṛtyavargatantraḥ
katham amum udvisṛjet pumān kṛtajñaḥ  Hbhv 
ataeva prārthanam 
nārāyaṇavyūhastave 
nāhaṃ brahmāpi bhuyāsaṃ tvadbhaktirahito hare 
tvayi bhaktas tu kīṭo 'pi bhūyāsaṃ janmajanmasu  Hbhv 
śrībrahmastutau ca daśamaskandhe BhP  
tad astu me nātha sa bhūribhāgo
bhave'tra vānyatra tu vā tiraścām 
yenāham eko 'pi bhavajjanānāṃ
bhūtvā niṣeve tava pādapallavam  Hbhv 
ataevoktaṃ śrīnārāyaṇavyūhastave 
ye tyaktalokadharmārthā viṣṇubhaktivaśaṃ gatāḥ 
bhajanti paramātmānaṃ tebhyo nityaṃ namo namaḥ  Hbhv 
evaṃ śrībhagavadbhaktamāhātmyāmṛtavāridheḥ 
vicitrabhaṅgalekhārho lobhalolaṃ vināsti kaḥ  Hbhv 
ataḥ śrībhagavadbhaktajanānāṃ saṅgatiḥ sadā 
kāryā sarvaprayatnena dvau lokau vijigīṣubhiḥ  Hbhv 
atha śrībhagavadbhaktasaṅgamāhātmyam
bhagavadbhaktapādābjapādukābhyo namo 'stu me 
yatsaṅgamaḥ sādhanaṃ ca sādhyaṃ cākhilam uttamam  Hbhv 
tatra sarvapātakamocakatā
bṛhannāradīye NārP  yajñamālyupākhyānānte 
haribhaktiparāṇāṃ tu saṅgināṃ saṅgamātrataḥ 
mucyate sarvapāpebhyo mahāpātakavān api  Hbhv 
sāmānyato 'narthanivartakatāarthaprāpakatā ca 
pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye PadmaP  śrīmuniśarmāṇaṃ prati pretānām uktau 
vināśayaty apayaśo buddhiṃ viśadayaty api 
pratiṣṭhāpayati prāyo nṛṇāṃ vaiṣṇavadarśanam  Hbhv 
tatra  śrīyamabrāhmaṇasaṃvāde mahārathanṛpoktau 
yathā prapadyamānasya bhagavantaṃ vibhāvasum 
śītaṃ bhayaṃ tamo 'py eti sādhūn saṃsevataḥ sadā  Hbhv 
tatraiva pretopākhyāne pretoktau PadmaP  
apākaroti duritaṃ śreyaḥ saṃyojayaty api 
yaśo vistārayaty āśu nṝṇāṃ vaiṣṇavasaṅgamaḥ  Hbhv 
atha sarvatīrthādhikatā
tatraiva PadmaP  
gaṅgādipuṇyatīrtheṣu yo naraḥ snātum icchati 
yaḥ karoti satāṃ saṅgāṃ tayoḥ satsaṅgamo varaḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva bhagīrathanṛpoktau PadmaP  
yaḥ snātaḥ śāntisitayā sādhusaṅgatigaṅgayā 
kiṃ tasya dānaiḥ kiṃ tīrthaiḥ kiṃ tapobhiḥ kim adhvaraiḥ  Hbhv 
atha sarveṣṭasādhakatā
yāni yāni durāpāṇi vāñchitāni mahītale 
prāpyante tāni tāny eva sādhūnām eva saṅgamāt  Hbhv 
atha anarthasyāpy arthatvāpādakatā
vāśiṣṭhe 
śūnyam āpūrṇatām eti mṛtir apy amṛtāyate 
āpat sampad iva bhāti vidvajjanasamāgame  Hbhv 
tṛtīyaskandhe BhP  
saṅgo yaḥ saṃsṛter hetur asatsu vihito 'dhiyā 
sa eva sādhuṣu kṛto niḥsaṅgatvāya kalpate  Hbhv 
śrīkapiladevoktau BhP  
prasaṅgam ajaraṃ pāśam ātmanaḥ kavayo viduḥ 
sa eva sādhuṣu kṛto mokṣadvāram apāvṛtam  Hbhv 
yataḥ 
arir mitraṃ viṣaṃ pathyam adharmo dharmatāṃ vrajet 
prasanne puṇḍarīkākṣe viparīte viparyayaḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca śrībhagavadvākyaṃ BhaktiS  attributed to PadmaP 
mannimittaṃ kṛtaṃ pāpam api dharmāya kalpate 
mām anādṛtya dharmo 'pi pāpaṃ syān matprabhāvataḥ  Hbhv 
caturthaskandhe śrīdhruvoktau BhP  
te na smaranty atitarāṃ priyam īśa martyaṃ
ye cānv adaḥ sutasuhṛdgṛhavittadārāḥ 
ye tv abjanābha bhavadīyapadāravinda
saugandhyalubdhahṛdayeṣu kṛtaprasaṅgāḥ  Hbhv 
pādme tatraiva pretoktau PadmaP  
rasāyanamayī śītā paramānandadāyinī 
nānandayati kaṃ nāma vaiṣṇavāśrayacandrikā  Hbhv 
atha mokṣadatvam 
daśamaskandhe śrīmucukundastutau BhP  
bhavāpavargo bhramato yadā bhavej
janasya tarhy acuta satsamāgamaḥ 
satsaṅgamo yarhi tadaiva sadgatau
parāvareśe tvayi jāyate matiḥ  Hbhv 
ataevoktaṃ śrīpracetobhiś caturthaskandhe BhP 
yatreḍyante kathā mṛṣṭās tṛṣṇāyāḥ praśamo yataḥ 
nirvairaṃ yatra bhūteṣu nodvego yatra kaścana  Hbhv 
yatra nārāyaṇaḥ sākṣād bhagavān nyāsināṃ gatiḥ 
saṃstūyate satkathāsu muktasaṅgaiḥ punaḥ punaḥ  Hbhv 
teṣāṃ vicaratāṃ padbhyāṃ tīrthānāṃ pāvanecchayā 
bhītasya kiṃ na roceta tāvakānāṃ samāgamaḥ  Hbhv 
atha sarvasāratā 
bṛhannāradīye śrīnāradasanatkumārasaṃvāde NārP  
asārabhūte saṃsāre sāram etad ajātmaja 
bhagavadbhaktasaṅgaś ca haribhaktis titikṣutā  Hbhv 
pādme tatraiva mahārathanṛpoktau 
asāgarotthaṃ pīyūṣam adravyaṃ vyasanauṣadham 
harṣaś cālokaparyantaḥ satāṃ kila samāgamaḥ  Hbhv 
atha bhagavatkathāmṛtapānaikahetutā 
pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye śrīnāradoktau PadmaP 
prasaṅgena satām ātmamanaḥ śrutirasāyanāḥ 
bhavanti kīrtanīyasya kathāḥ kṛṣṇasya nirmalāḥ  Hbhv 
tṛtīyaskandhe BhP  śrīkapiladevoktau 
satāṃ prasaṅgān mama vīryasaṃvido
bhavanti hṛtkarṇarasāyanāḥ kathāḥ 
tajjoṣaṇād āśv apavargavartmani
śraddhā ratir bhaktir anukramiṣyati  Hbhv 
caturthe śrīnāradoktau BhP  
yatra bhāgavatā rājan sādhavo viśadāśayāḥ 
bhagavadguṇānukathana śravaṇavyagracetasaḥ  Hbhv 
tasmin mahanmukharitā madhubhic
caritrapīyūṣaśeṣasaritaḥ paritaḥ sravanti 
tā ye pibanty avitṛṣo nṛpa gāḍhakarṇais
tān na spṛśanty aśanatṛḍbhayaśokamohāḥ  Hbhv 
pañcame BhP  śrībrāhmaṇarahūgaṇasaṃvāde 
yatrottamaślokaguṇānuvādaḥ
prastūyate grāmyakathāvighātaḥ 
niṣevyamāṇo 'nudinaṃ mumukṣor
matiṃ satīṃ yacchati vāsudeve  Hbhv 
ekādaśe śrībhagavaduddhavasaṃvāde śrīailopākhyānānte BhP  
teṣu nityaṃ mahābhāga mahābhāgeṣu matkathāḥ 
sambhavanti hi tā nṇāṃ juṣatāṃ prapunanty agham  Hbhv 
tā ye śṛṇvanti gāyanti hy anumodanti cādṛtāḥ 
matparāḥ śraddadhānāś ca bhaktiṃ vindanti te mayi  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye tatraiva  
bhaktis tu bhagavadbhaktasaṅgena parijāyate 
satsaṅgaḥ prāpyate pumbhiḥ sukṛtaiḥ pūrvasañcitaiḥ  Hbhv 
ekādaśe śrībhagavaduddhavasaṃvāde BhP  
athaitat paramaṃ guhyaṃ śṛṇvato yadunandana
sugopyam api vakṣyāmi tvaṃ me bhṛtyaḥ suhṛt sakhā  Hbhv 
no rodhayati māṃ yogo na sāṅkhyaṃ dharma eva ca 
na svādhyāyas tapas tyāgo neṣṭāpūrtaṃ na dakṣiṇā  Hbhv 
vratāni yajñaś chandāṃsi tīrthāni niyamā yamāḥ 
yathāvarundhe satsaṅgaḥ sarvasaṅgāpaho hi mām  Hbhv 
ataevoktaṃ vidureṇa tṛtīyaskandhe BhP  
yatsevayā bhagavataḥ kūṭasthasya madhudviṣaḥ 
ratirāso bhavet tīvraḥ pādayor vyasanārdanaḥ  Hbhv 
prathamaskandhe śrīśaunakādīnāṃ BhP 
caturthe ca śrīpracetasām uktau BhP  
tulayāma lavenāpi na svargaṃ nāpunarbhavam 
bhagavatsaṅgisaṅgasya martyānāṃ kim utāśiṣaḥ  Hbhv 
caturthe ca śrīpracetasaḥ prati śrīśivopadeśaḥ BhP  
kṣaṇārdhenāpi tulaye na svargaṃ nāpunarbhavam 
bhagavatsaṅgisaṅgasya martyānāṃ kim utāśiṣaḥ  Hbhv 
dvādaśe śrīmārkaṇḍeyopākhyāne śrīśivasya BhP  
athāpi saṃvadiṣyāmo bhavāny etena sādhunā 
ayaṃ hi paramo lābho nṛṇāṃ sādhusamāgamaḥ  Hbhv 
ataeva śrīprahlādaṃ prati śrīdharaṇyoktaṃ haribhaktisudhodaye 
akṣṇoḥ phalaṃ tvādṛśadarśanaṃ hi
tanvāḥ phalaṃ tvādṛśagātrasaṅgaḥ 
jihvāphalaṃ tvādṛśakīrtanaṃ hi
sudurlabhā bhāgavatā hi loke  Hbhv 
ataeva vidureṇa tṛtīyaskandhe BhP  
durāpā hy alpatapasaḥ sevā vaikuṇṭhavartmasu 
yatropagīyate nityaṃ devadevo janārdanaḥ  Hbhv 
śrīvidehenāpy ekādaśaskandhe BhP  
durlabho mānuṣo deho dehināṃ kṣaṇabhaṅguraḥ 
tatrāpi durlabhaṃ manye vaikuṇṭhapriyadarśanam  Hbhv 
ataeva hi prārthitaṃ śrīdhruveṇa caturthaskandhe BhP  
bhaktiṃ muhuḥ pravahatāṃ tvayi me prasaṅgo
bhūyād ananta mahatām amalāśayānām 
yenāñjasolbaṇam uruvyasanaṃ bhavābdhiṃ
neṣye bhavadguṇakathāmṛtapānamattaḥ  Hbhv 
pracetasaḥ pratyupadeśe śrīśivena ca BhP  
athānaghāṅghres tava kīrtitīrthayor
antarbahiḥsnānavidhūtapāpmanām 
bhūteṣv anukrośasusattvaśīlināṃ
syāt saṅgamo 'nugraha eṣa nas tava  Hbhv 
śrīpracetobhiś ca BhP  
yāvat te māyayā spṛṣṭā bhramāma iha karmabhiḥ 
tāvad bhavatprasaṅgānāṃ saṅgaḥ syān no bhave bhave  Hbhv 
śrīprahlādenāpi saptamaskandhe BhP  
tasmād amūs tanubhṛtām aham āśiṣo jña
āyuḥ śriyaṃ vibhavam aindriyam āviriñcyāt 
necchāmi te vilulitān uruvikrameṇa
kālātmanopanaya māṃ nijabhṛtyapārśvam  Hbhv  iti 
athāsatsaṅgadoṣāḥ 
śrīkātyāyanavākye 
varaṃ hutavahajvālāpañjarāntarvyavasthitiḥ 
na śauricintāvimukhajanasaṃvāsavaiśasam  Hbhv 
pādme uttarakhaṇḍe śrīumāmaheśvarasaṃvāde 
avaiṣṇavās tu ye viprāś cāṇḍālād adhamāḥ smṛtāḥ 
teṣāṃ sambhāṣaṇaṃ sparśaṃ somapānādi varjayet  Hbhv 
tṛtīyaskandhe śrīkapiladevahūtisaṃvāde BhP 
satyaṃ śaucaṃ dayā maunaṃ buddhiḥ śrīr hrīr yaśaḥ kṣamā 
śamo damo bhagaś ceti yatsaṅgād yāti saṅkṣayam  Hbhv 
teṣv aśānteṣu mūḍheṣu khaṇḍitātmasv asādhuṣu 
saṅgaṃ na kuryāc chocyeṣu yoṣitkrīḍāmṛgeṣu ca  Hbhv 
na tathāsya bhaven moho bandhaś cānyaprasaṅgataḥ 
yoṣitsaṅgād yathā puṃso yathā tatsaṅgisaṅgataḥ  Hbhv 
ekādaśe ca śrībhagavaduddhavasaṃvāde BhP  
saṅgaṃ na kuryād asatāṃ śiśnodaratṛpāṃ kvacit 
tasyānugas tamasy andhe pataty andhānugāndhavat  Hbhv 
bhagavadbhaktihīnā ye mukhyā'santas ta eva hi 
teṣāṃ niṣṭhā śubhā kvāpi na syāt saccaritair api  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye prāyaścittaprakaraṇānte 
kiṃ vedaiḥ kim u vā śāstraiḥ kim u tīrthaniṣevaṇaiḥ 
viṣṇubhaktivihīnānāṃ kiṃ tapobhiḥ kim adhvaraiḥ  Hbhv 
śrīgāruḍe 
antaṃ gato 'pi vedānāṃ sarvaśāstrārthavedy api 
yo na sarveśvare bhaktas taṃ vidyāt puruṣādhamam  Hbhv 
tṛtīyaskandhe BhP  
ahny āpṛtārtakaraṇā niśi niḥśayānā
nānāmanorathadhiyā kṣaṇabhagnanidrāḥ 
daivāhatārtharacanā ṛṣayo 'pi deva
yuṣmatprasaṅgavimukhā iha saṃsaranti  Hbhv 
ataevoktaṃ ṣaṣṭhe BhP  
prāyaścittāni cīrṇāni nārāyaṇaparāṅmukham 
na niṣpunanti rājendra surākumbham ivāpagāḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare 
kutaḥ pāpakṣayas teṣāṃ kutas teṣāṃ ca maṅgalam 
yeṣāṃ naiva hṛdistho 'yaṃ maṅgalāyatano hariḥ  Hbhv 
ataeva bṛhannāradīye lubdhakopākhyānārambhe 
haripūjāvihīnāś ca vedavidveṣiṇas tathā 
dvijagodveṣiṇaś cāpi rākṣasāḥ parikīrtitāḥ  Hbhv 
ataeva nijadūtān prati dharmarājasyānuśāsanaṃ ṣaṣṭhaskandhe BhP  
tān ānayadhvam asato vimukhān mukunda
pādāravindamakarandarasād ajasram 
niṣkiñcanaiḥ paramahaṃsakulair asaṅgair
juṣṭād gṛhe nirayavartmani baddhatṛṣṇān  Hbhv 
jihvā na vakti bhagavadguṇanāmadheyaṃ
cetaś ca na smarati taccaraṇāravindam 
kṛṣṇāya no namati yacchira ekadāpi
tān ānayadhvam asato 'kṛtaviṣṇukṛtyān  Hbhv 
skānde mārkaṇḍeyabhagīrathasaṃvāde 
yo hi bhāgavataṃ lokam upahāsaṃ nṛpottama 
karoti tasya naśyanti arthadharmayaśaḥsutā  Hbhv 
nindāṃ kurvanti ye mūḍhā vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahātmanām 
patanti pitṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ mahārauravasaṃjñite  Hbhv 
hanti nindati vai dveṣṭi vaiṣṇavān nābhinandati 
krudhyate yāti no harṣaṃ darśane patanāni ṣaṭ  Hbhv 
tatraivāmṛtasāroddhāre śrīyamoktau 
janmaprabhṛti yat kiñcit sukṛtaṃ samupārjitam 
nāśam āyāti tat sarvaṃ pīḍayed yadi vaiṣṇavān  Hbhv 
dvārakāmāhātmye prahlādabalisaṃvāde 
karapatraiś ca phālyante sutīvrair yamaśāsanaiḥ 
nindāṃ kurvanti ye pāpā vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahātmanām  Hbhv 
pūjito bhagavān viṣṇur janmāntaraśatair api 
prasīdati na viśvātmā vaiṣṇave cāpamānite  Hbhv 
daśamaskandhe ca BhP  
nindāṃ bhagavataḥ śṛṇvaṃs tatparasya janasya vā 
tato nāpaiti yaḥ so 'pi yāty adhaḥ sukṛtāc cyutaḥ  Hbhv 
ataevoktaṃ viṣṇudharmottare 
jīvitaṃ viṣṇubhaktasya varaṃ pañcadināni ca 
na tu kalpasahasrāṇi bhaktihīnasya keśave  Hbhv 
ataevoktaṃ śrībhāgavate ailopākhyānānte BhP  
tato duḥsaṅgam utsṛjya satsu sajjeta buddhimān 
santa evāsya chindanti manovyāsaṅgam uktibhiḥ  Hbhv 
atha śrīvaiṣṇavasamāgamavidhiḥ
atha śrībhagavadbhaktān sallakṣaṇavibhūṣitān 
gatvā tān dūrato dṛṣṭvā daṇḍavat praṇamen mudā  Hbhv 
tejodraviṇapañcarātre 
vaiṣṇavo vaiṣṇavaṃ dṛṣṭvā daṇḍavat praṇamed bhuvi 
ubhayor antarā viṣṇuḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ  Hbhv 
tatra ca viśeṣo bṛhannāradīye  
sabhāyāṃ yajñaśālāyāṃ devatāyataneṣv api 
pratyekaṃ tu namaskāro hanti puṇyaṃ purākṛtam  Hbhv 
puṇyakṣetre puṇyatīrthe svādhyāyasamaye tathā 
pratyekaṃ tu namaskāro hanti puṇyaṃ purākṛtam  Hbhv 
vaiṣṇavaṃ cāgataṃ vīkṣyābhigamyāliṅga vaiṣṇavam 
vaideśikaṃ prīṇayeyur darśayantaḥ svavaiṣṇavān  Hbhv 
tathā coktaṃ śrībrahmaṇā tejodraviṇapañcarātre 
nārāyaṇāśrayaṃ bhaktaṃ deśāntarasamāgatam 
prīṇayed darśayaṃs tasya bhaktyā nārāyaṇāśrayān  Hbhv  iti
tataś ca vaiṣṇavaḥ prāptaḥ santarpya vacanāmṛtaiḥ 
sadbandhur iva sammānyo 'nyathā doṣo mahān smṛtaḥ  Hbhv 
atha vaiṣṇavasammānananityatā
skānde śrīmārkaṇḍeyabhagīrathasaṃvāde 
dṛṣṭvā bhāgavataṃ daivāt sammukhe yo na yāti hi 
na gṛhṇāti haris tasya pūjāṃ dvādaśavārṣikīm  Hbhv 
yo na gṛhṇāti bhūpāla vaiṣṇavaṃ gṛham āgatam 
tadgṛhaṃ pitṛbhis tyaktaṃ śmaśānam iva bhīṣaṇam  Hbhv 
athavābhyagataṃ dūrād yo nārcayanti vaiṣṇavam 
svaśaktyā nṛpaśārdūla nānyaḥ pāparatas tataḥ  Hbhv 
śrāntaṃ bhāgavataṃ dṛṣṭvā kaṭhinaṃ yasya mānasam 
prasīdati na duṣṭātmā śvapacād adhiko hi saḥ  Hbhv 
vipraṃ bhāgavataṃ dṛṣṭvā dīnam āturamānasam 
na karoti paritrāṇaṃ keśavo na prasīdati  Hbhv 
dṛṣṭvā bhāgavataṃ vipraṃ namaskāreṇa nārcayet 
dehinas tasya pāpasya na ca vai kṣamate hariḥ  Hbhv 
apūjito yadā gacchad vaiṣṇavo gṛhamedhinaḥ 
śatajanmārjitaṃ bhūpa puṇyam ādāya gacchati  Hbhv 
anabhyarcya pitṝn devān bhuñjate harivāsare 
tat pāpaṃ jāyate bhūpa vaiṣṇavānām atikrame  Hbhv 
pūrvaṃ kṛtvā tu sammānam avajñāṃ kurute tu yaḥ 
vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahīpāla sānvayo yāti saṅkṣayam  Hbhv 
pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye yamabrāhmaṇasaṃvāde PadmaP 
vaiṣṇavaṃ janam ālokya nābhyutthānaṃ karoti yaḥ 
praṇayādarato vipra sa naro narakātithiḥ  Hbhv 
caturthaskandhe BhP  ca 
vyālālayadrumā vai teṣv ariktākhilasampadaḥ 
yadgṛhās tīrthapādīya pādatīrthavivarjitāḥ  Hbhv 
atha vaiṣṇavastutiḥ
skānde 
dahnyo 'haṃ kṛtakṛtyo 'haṃ yad yūyaṃ gṛham āgatāḥ 
durlabhaṃ darśanaṃ nūnaṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ yathā hareḥ  Hbhv 
merumandaratulyā vai puṇyapuñjā mayā kṛtāḥ 
samprāptaṃ darśanaṃ yad vai vaiṣṇavānāṃ mahātmanām  Hbhv 
daśamaskandhe śrīgargācāryaṃ prati śrīnandasya vākyam BhP  
mahadvicalanaṃ nṝṇāṃ gṛhiṇāṃ dīnacetasām 
niḥśreyasāya bhagavan kalpate nānyathā kvacit  Hbhv 
caturthaskandhe BhP   
aho ācaritaṃ kiṃ me maṅgalaṃ maṅgalāyanāḥ 
yasya vo darśanaṃ hy āsīd durdarśānāṃ ca yogibhiḥ  Hbhv 
adhanā api te dhanyāḥ sādhavo gṛhamedhinaḥ 
yadgṛhā hy arhavaryāmbu tṛṇabhūmīśvarāvarāḥ  Hbhv 
kaccin naḥ kuśalaṃ nāthā indriyārthārthavedinām 
vyasanāvāpa etasmin patitānāṃ svakarmabhiḥ  Hbhv 
bhavatsu kuśalapraśna ātmārāmeṣu neṣyate 
kuśalākuśalā yatra na santi mativṛttayaḥ  Hbhv 
atha vaiṣṇavābhigamanamāhātmyam
skānde śrīmārkaṇḍeyabhagīrathasaṃvāde
sammukhaṃ vrajamānasya vaiṣṇavānāṃ narādhipa 
pade pade yajñaphalaṃ prāhuḥ paurāṇikā dvijāḥ  Hbhv 
atha vaiṣṇavastutimāhātmyam  tatraiva
pratyakṣaṃ vā parokṣaṃ vā yaḥ praśaṃsati vaiṣṇavam 
brahmahā madyapaḥ steyī gurugāmī sadā nṝṇām 
mucyate pātakāt sadyo viṣṇur āha nṛpottama  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
pratyakṣaṃ vā parokṣaṃ vā ye praśaṃsanti vaiṣṇavam 
prasādād vāsudevasya te taranti bhavārṇavam  Hbhv 
atha vaiṣṇavasammānamāhātmyam 
tatraivāmṛtasāroddhāre
śraddhayā dattam annaṃ ca vaiṣṇavāgniṣu jīryati 
tadannaṃ meruṇā tulyaṃ bhavate ca dine dine  Hbhv 
daive paitre ca yo dadyād vārimātraṃ tu vaiṣṇave 
saptodadhisamaṃ bhūtvā pitṝṇām upatiṣṭhati  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharme
kiṃ dānaiḥ kiṃ tapobhir vā yajñaiś ca vividhaiḥ kṛtaiḥ 
sarvaṃ sampadyate puṃsāṃ viṣṇubhaktābhipūjanāt  Hbhv 
pūjayed vaiṣṇavān etān prayatnena vicakṣaṇaḥ 
svaśaktyā vaiṣṇavebhyo yad dattaṃ syād akṣayaṃ bhavet  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye yajñamālyupākhyāne NārP 
haribhaktiratān yas tu haribuddhyā prapūjayet 
tasya tuṣyanti viprendra brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ  Hbhv 
haripūjāparāṇāṃ ca harināmaratātmanām 
śuśrūṣāniratā yānti pāpino 'pi parāṃ gatim  Hbhv 
tatraiva yajñadhvajopākhyānasyārambhe NārP 
saṃsārasāgaraṃ tartuṃ ya icchen munipuṅgava 
sa bhajed dharibhaktānāṃ bhaktān vai pāpahāriṇaḥ  Hbhv 
tadante ca NārP  
yo viṣṇubhaktān niṣkāmān bhojayet śraddhayānvitaḥ 
triḥsaptakulasaṃyuktās te yānti harimandiram  Hbhv 
viṣṇubhaktāya yo dadyān niṣkāmāya mahātmane 
pānīyaṃ vā phalaṃ vāpi sa eva bhagavatpriyaḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇubhaktiparāṇāṃ tu śuśrūṣāṃ kurvate tu ye 
te yānti viṣṇubhavanaṃ yāvadābhūtasamplavam  Hbhv 
devapūjāparo yasya gṛhe vasati sarvadā 
tatraiva sarvadevāś ca tiṣṭhanti śrīharis tathā  Hbhv 
laiṅge
nārāyaṇaparo vidvān yasyānnaṃ prītamānasaḥ 
aśnāti taddharer āsyaṃ gatam annaṃ na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
sarvārcanād api viśvātmā prīto bhavati mādhavaḥ 
dṛṣṭvā bhāgavatasyānnaṃ sa bhuṅkte bhaktavatsalaḥ  Hbhv 
brāhme śrībhagavadvākyam
naivedyaṃ purato nyastaṃ dṛṣṭvaiva svīkṛtaṃ mayā 
bhaktasya rasanāgreṇa rasam aśnāmi padmaja  Hbhv 
pādmottarakhaṇḍe 
śrīśivomāsaṃvāde 
ārādhanānāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣṇor ārādhanaṃ param 
tasmāt parataraṃ devi tadīyānāṃ samarcanam  Hbhv 
arcayitvāpi govindaṃ tadīyān nārcayet punaḥ 
na sa bhāgavato jñeyaḥ kevalaṃ dāmbhikaḥ smṛtaḥ  Hbhv 
pumāṃs tasmāt prayatnena vaiṣṇavān pūjayet sadā 
sarvaṃ tarati duḥkhaughaṃ mahābhāgavatārcanāt  Hbhv 
ekādaśe śrībhagavadvākyam BhP   
vaiṣṇave bandhusatkṛtyā  Hbhv 
madbhaktapūjābhyadhikā  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca skānde śrīmārkaṇḍeyabhagīrathasaṃvāde 
karmaṇā manasā vācā ye'rcayanti sadā harim 
teṣāṃ vākyaṃ naraiḥ kāryaṃ te hi viṣṇusamā narāḥ  Hbhv 
ity ādṛto 'nuśṛṇuyād bhaktiśāstrāṇi tatra ca 
śrībhāgavatam atrāpi kṛṣṇalīlākathāṃ muhuḥ  Hbhv 
atha vaiṣṇavaśāstramāhātmyam 
skānde śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde 
vaiṣṇavāni tu śāstrāṇī ye śṛṇvanti paṭhanti ca 
dhanyās te mānavā loke tesāṃ kṛṣṇaḥ prasīdati  Hbhv 
vaiṣṇavāni tu śāstrāṇī ye rcayanti gṛhe narāḥ 
sarvapāpavinirmuktā bhavanti suravanditāḥ  Hbhv 
sarvasvenāpi viprendra kartavyaḥ śāstrasaṅgrahaḥ 
vaiṣṇavais tu mahābhaktyā tuṣṭyarthaṃ cakrapāṇinaḥ  Hbhv 
tiṣṭhate vaiṣṇavaṃ śāstraṃ likhitaṃ yasya mandire 
tatra nārāyaṇo devaḥ svayaṃ vasati nārada  Hbhv 
paurāṇaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ ślokaṃ ślokārdham athavāpi ca 
ślokapādaṃ paṭhed yas tu gosahasraphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
devatānām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca yoginām api durlabham 
viprendra vaiṣṇavaṃ śāstraṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ ca kā kathā  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrīkṛṣṇārjunasaṃvāde 
mama śāstrāṇi ye nityaṃ pūjayanti paṭhanti ca 
te narāḥ kuruśārdūla mamātithyaṃ gatāḥ sadā  Hbhv 
mama śākhyapravaktāraṃ mama śāstrānucintakam 
cintayāmi na sandeho naraṃ taṃ cātmavat sadā  Hbhv 
atha śrīmadbhāgavatamāhātmyam
tatraiva 
jīvitād adhikaṃ yeṣāṃ śāstraṃ bhāgavataṃ kalau 
na teṣāṃ bhavati kleśo yāmyaḥ kalpaśatair api  Hbhv 
dhārayanti gṛhe nityaṃ śāstraṃ bhāgavataṃ hi ye 
āsphoṭayanti valganti teṣāṃ prītāḥ pitāmahāḥ  Hbhv 
yāvad dināni viprarṣe śāstraṃ bhāgavataṃ gṛhe 
tāvat pibanti pitaraḥ kṣīraṃ sarpir madhūdakam  Hbhv 
ye'rcayanti sadā gehe śāstraṃ bhāgavataṃ narāḥ 
prīṇitās taiś ca vibudhā yāvad āhūtasamplavam  Hbhv 
yaccanti vaiṣṇave bhaktyā śāstraṃ bhāgavataṃ hi ye 
kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi viṣṇuloke vasanti te  Hbhv 
ślokārdhaṃ ślokapādaṃ vā varaṃ bhāgavataṃ gṛhe 
śataśo 'tha sahasraiś ca kim anyaiḥ śāstrasaṅgrahaiḥ  Hbhv 
na yasya tiṣṭhate gehe śāstraṃ bhāgavataṃ kalau 
na tasya punar āvṛttir yāmyāt pāśāt kadācana  Hbhv 
kathaṃ sa vaiṣṇavo jñeyaḥ śāstraṃ bhāgavataṃ kalau 
gṛhe na tiṣṭhate yasya sa vipraḥ śvapacādhamaḥ  Hbhv 
yatra yatra bhaved vipra śāstraṃ bhāgavataṃ kalau 
tatra tatra harir yāti tridaśaiḥ saha nārada  Hbhv 
tatra sarvāṇi tīrthāni nadīnadasarāṃsi ca 
yatra bhāgavataṃ śāstraṃ tiṣṭhate munisattama  Hbhv 
tatra sarvāṇi tīrthāni sarve yajñāḥ sudakṣiṇāḥ 
yatra bhāgavataṃ śāstraṃ pūjitaṃ tiṣṭhate gṛhe  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca 
nityaṃ bhāgavataṃ yas tu purāṇaṃ paṭhate naraḥ 
pratyakṣaraṃ bhavet tasya kapilādānajaṃ phalam  Hbhv 
ślokārdhaṃ ślokapādaṃ vā nityaṃ bhāgavatodbhavam 
paṭhet śṛṇoti vā bhaktyā gosahasraṃ phalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
yaḥ paṭhet prayato nityaṃ ślokaṃ bhāgavataṃ mune 
aṣṭādaśapurāṇānāṃ phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva mārkaṇḍeyabhagīrathasaṃvāde 
yo hi bhāgavate śāstre vighnam ācarate pumān 
nābhinandati duṣṭātmā kulānāṃ pātayec chatam  Hbhv 
pādme gautamāmbarīṣasaṃvāde 
ambarīṣa śukaproktaṃ nityaṃ bhāgavataṃ śṛṇu 
paṭhasva svamukhenāpi yadīcchasi bhavakṣayam  Hbhv 
ślokaṃ bhāgavataṃ vāpi ślokardhapādam eva vā 
likhitaṃ tiṣṭhate yasya gṛhe tasya sadā hariḥ 
vasate nātra sandeho devadevo janārdanaḥ  Hbhv 
dvārakāmāhātmye śrīmārkaṇḍeyendradyumnasaṃvāde 
śrīmadbhāgavataṃ śāstraṃ paṭhate kṛṣṇasannidhau 
kulakoṭiśatair yuktaḥ krīḍate yogibhiḥ saha  Hbhv 
gāruḍe
artho 'yaṃ brahmasūtrāṇāṃ bhāratārthavinirṇayaḥ 
gāyatrībhāṣyarūpo 'sau vedārthaparibṛṃhitaḥ  Hbhv 
purāṇānāṃ sāmarūpaḥ sākṣādbhagavatoditaḥ 
dvādaśaskandhayukto 'yaṃ śatavicchedasaṃyutaḥ 
grantho 'ṣṭādaśasāhasraḥ śrīmadbhāgavatābhidhaḥ  Hbhv 
tasminn eva śrībhāgavate prathamaskandhe BhP  
dharmaḥ projjhitakaitavo 'tra paramo nirmatsarāṇāṃ satāṃ
vedyaṃ vāstavam atra vastu śivadaṃ tāpatrayonmūlanam 
śrīmadbhāgavate mahāmunikṛte kiṃ vā parair īśvaraḥ
sadyo hṛdy avarudhyate 'tra kṛtibhiḥ śuśrūṣubhis tatkṣaṇāt  Hbhv 
idaṃ bhāgavataṃ nāma purāṇaṃ brahmasammitam 
uttamaślokacaritaṃ cakāra bhagavān ṛṣiḥ  Hbhv 
niḥśreyasāya lokasya dhanyaṃ svastyayanaṃ mahat 
tad idaṃ grāhayām āsasutam ātmavatāṃ varam 
sarvavedetihāsānāṃ sāraṃ sāraṃ samuddhṛtam  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca BhP  
kṛṣṇe svadhāmopagate dharmajñānādibhiḥ saha 
kalau naṣṭadṛśām eṣa purāṇārko 'dhunoditaḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca BhP 
anarthopaśamaṃ sākṣād bhaktiyogam adhokṣaje 
lokasyājānato vidvāṃś cakre sātvatasaṃhitām  Hbhv 
yasyāṃ vai śrūyamāṇāyāṃ kṛṣṇe paramapūruṣe 
bhaktir utpadyate puṃsaḥ śokamohabhayāpahā  Hbhv 
dvitīye śrīśukoktau BhP  
pariniṣṭhito 'pi nairguṇya uttamaślokalīlayā 
gṛhītacetā rājarṣe ākhyānaṃ yad adhītavān  Hbhv 
rājante tāvad anyāni purāṇāni satāṃ gaṇe 
yāvad bhāgavataṃ naiva śrūyate 'mṛtasāgaram  Hbhv 
dvādaśe ca BhP    
rājante tāvad anyāni purāṇāni satāṃ gaṇe 
yāvad bhāgavataṃ naiva śrūyate'mṛtasāgaraḥ  Hbhv 
sarvavedāntasāraṃ hi śrībhāgavatam iṣyate 
tadrasāmṛtatṛptasya nānyatra syād ratiḥ kvacit  Hbhv 
nimnagānāṃ yathā gaṅgā devānām acyuto yathā 
vaiṣṇavānāṃ yathā śambhuḥ purāṇānām idaṃ tathā  Hbhv 
śrīmadbhāgavataṃ purāṇam amalaṃ yad vaiṣṇavānāṃ priyaṃ
yasmin pāramahaṃsyam ekam amalaṃ jñānaṃ paraṃ gīyate 
tatra jñānavirāgabhaktisahitaṃ naiṣkarmyam āviṣkṛtaṃ
tac chṛṇvan supaṭhan vicāraṇaparo bhaktyā vimucyen naraḥ  Hbhv 
ataevoktaṃ BhP  
nigamakalpataror galitaṃ phalaṃ
śukamukhād amṛtadravasaṃyutam 
pibata bhāgavataṃ rasam ālayaṃ
muhur aho rasikā bhuvi bhāvukāḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca BhP  
yaḥ svānubhāvam akhilaśrutisāram ekam
adhyātmadīpam atititīrṣatāṃ tamo 'ndham

taṃ vyāsasūnum upayāmi guruṃ munīnām  Hbhv 
atha śrībhagavacchāstravaktṛmāhātmyam
bhagavaddharmavaktāraṃ bhagavacchāstravācakam

nāradapañcarātre ṛṣīn prati śrīśāṇḍilyoktau 
vaiṣṇavaṃ jñānavaktāraṃ yo vidyād viṣṇuvad gurum 
pūjayed vāṅmanaḥkāyaiḥ sa śāstrajñaḥ sa vaiṣṇavaḥ  Hbhv 
ślokapādasya vaktāpi yaḥ pūjyaḥ sa sadaiva hi 
kiṃ punar bhagavadviṣṇoḥ svarūpaṃ vitanoti yaḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca 
nārāyaṇaḥ paraṃ brahma tajjñānenātha gamyate 
jñānasya sādhanaṃ śāstraṃ śāstraṃ ca guruvaktṛgam  Hbhv 
brahma prāptir ato hetor gurvadhīnā sadaiva hi 
hetunānena vai viprā gurur gurutaraḥ smṛtaḥ  Hbhv 
yasmād devo jagannāthaḥ kṛtvā maryamayīṃ tanum 
magnān uddharate lokān kāruṇyāc chāstrapāṇinā  Hbhv 
tasmād bhaktir gurau kāryā saṃsārabhayabhīruṇā 
śāstrajñānena yo 'jñānaṃ timiraṃ vinipātayet  Hbhv 
śāstraṃ pāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ pavitraṃ bhogamokṣadam 
śāntidaṃ ca mahārthaṃ ca vakti yaḥ sa jagadguruḥ  Hbhv 
atha śrīkṛṣṇalīlākathāśravaṇamāhātmyam
tatra pāpādiśodhakatvam
skānde brahmanāradasaṃvāde 
teṣāṃ kṣīṇaṃ mahat pāpaṃ varṣakoṭiśatodbhavam 
viprendra nāsti sandeho ye śṛṇvanti hareḥ kathām  Hbhv 
tatraivānyatra 
sarvāśramābhigamanaṃ sarvatīrthāvagāhanam 
na tathā pāraṇaṃ nṝṇāṃ nārāyaṇakathā yathā  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye  yajñadhvajopākhyānānte 
aho harikathā loke pāpaghnī puṇyadāyinī 
śṛṇvatāṃ vadatāṃ caiva tadbhaktānāṃ viśeṣataḥ  Hbhv 
prathamaskandhe BhP

hṛdy antaḥstho hy abhadrāṇi vidhunoti suhṛtsatām  Hbhv

vidyāśrutādhyayanadānatapaḥkriyābhiḥ

tatraiva 
śrotavyaṃ sādhucaritaṃ yaśodharmajayārthibhiḥ

kuṭumbavṛddhiṃ vijayaṃ śatrunāśaṃ balam 
karoti viṣṇucaritaṃ sarvakālaphalapradam  Hbhv 
prathamaskandhe BhP  
dharmaḥ svanuṣṭhitaḥ puṃsāṃ viṣvaksenakathāsu yaḥ 
notpādayed yadi ratiṃ śrama eva hi kevalam  Hbhv 
tṛtīye śrīviduramaitreyasaṃvāde BhP

suślokamauler guṇavādam āhuḥ

kathāsudhāyām upasamprayogam  Hbhv

viraktim anyatra karoti puṃsaḥ

ekādaśe ca śrībhagavantaṃ praty uddhavavākye BhP  
tava vikrīḍitaṃ kṛṣṇa nṛṇāṃ paramamaṅgalam

caturthe pracetasaḥ prati śrībhagavaduktau BhP  
gṛheṣv āviśatāṃ cāpi puṃsāṃ kuśalakarmaṇām 
madvārtāyātayāmānāṃ na bandhāya gṛhā matāḥ  Hbhv 
skānde tatraiva 
dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ yad iṣṭaṃ ca nṝṇām iha 
tat sarvaṃ labhate vatsa kathāṃ śrutvā hareḥ sadā  Hbhv

dvārakāmāhātmye

dvitīyaskandhe BhP 
jñānaṃ yad āpratinivṛttaguṇormicakram
ātmaprasāda uta yatra guṇeṣv asaṅgaḥ 
kaivalyasammatapathas tv atha bhaktiyogaḥ
ko nirvṛto harikathāsu ratiṃ na kuryāt  Hbhv 
daśamaskandhe śrutistutau BhP

na parilaṣanti kecid apavargam apīśvara te

tṛtīyaskandhe śrīkapiladevahūtisaṃvāde BhP

vrajanti taccaraṇasaroruhāntikam  Hbhv

pravṛddhabhaktyā viśadāśayā ye 
vairāgyasāraṃ pratilabhya bodhaṃ
yathāñjasānvīyur akuṇṭhadhiṣṇyam  Hbhv

kalāyutaṃ nāvalokyaṃ gatās te brahma śāśvatam  Hbhv

tasya na cyavate lakṣmīs tatpadaṃ ca kare sthitam  Hbhv

yat tūttamaḥślokaguṇānuvādaḥ

skānde 
yatra yatra mahīpāla vaiṣṇavī vartate kathā

kiṃ ca BhP

suślokamauleś caritāmṛtāni  Hbhv 
daśamaskandhe ca śrīparīkṣitā BhP  
brahman kṛṣṇakathāḥ puṇyā mādhvīr lokamalāpahāḥ 
ko nu tṛpyeta śṛṇvānaḥ śrutajño nityanūtanaḥ  Hbhv 
ato hi śrīpṛthurājena prārthitaṃ BhP  
na kāmaye nātha tad apy ahaṃ kvacin

mahattamāntarhṛdayān mukhacyuto

nātaḥ paraṃ paramatoṣaviśeṣapoṣaṃ
paśyāmi puṇyam ucitaṃ ca paraspareṇa 
santaḥ prasahya yad anantaguṇān ananta
śreyonidhīn adhikabhāvabhujo bhajanti  Hbhv 
prathamaskandhe śrīsūtena BhP  
yā yāḥ kathā bhagavataḥ kathanīyorukarmaṇaḥ 
guṇakarmāśrayāḥ pumbhiḥ saṃsevyās tā bubhūṣubhiḥ  Hbhv 
daśamaskandhaśeṣe ca śrībādarāyaṇinā BhP  
itthaṃ parasya nijavartmarirakṣayātta
līlātanos tadanurūpaviḍambanāni 
karmāṇi karmakaṣaṇāni yadūttamasya
śrūyād amuṣya padayor anuvṛttim icchan  Hbhv 
atha śrībhagavatkathātyāgādidoṣaḥ
ataḥ kṛṣṇakathāyāṃ tu satyām anyakathāśrutim 
tad aśrutiṃ ca vaimukhyaṃ tasyāṃ tṛptim api tyajet  Hbhv 
tṛtīyaskandhe kapiladevahūtisaṃvāde BhP  
nūnaṃ daivena vihatā ye cācyutakathāsudhām 
hitvā śṛṇvanty asadgāthāḥ purīṣam iva viḍbhujaḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrīvaikuṇṭhavarṇane BhP  
yan na vrajanty aghabhido racanānuvādāc
chṛṇvanti ye 'nyaviṣayāḥ kukathā matighnīḥ 
yās tu śrutā hatabhagair nṛbhir āttasārās
tāṃs tān kṣipanty aśaraṇeṣu tamaḥsu hanta  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca skānde brahmanāradasaṃvāde 
vācyamānaṃ tu ye śāstraṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ puruṣādhamāḥ 
na śṛṇvanti muniśreṣṭha teṣāṃ svāmī sadā yamaḥ  Hbhv 
na śṛṇvanti na hṛṣyanti vaiṣṇavīṃ prāpya ye kathām 
dhama āyur yaśo dharmaḥ santānaś caiva naśyati  Hbhv 
na śṛṇoti harer yas tu kathāṃ pāpapraṇāśinīm 
acirād eva devarṣe samūlaṃ tu vinaśyati  Hbhv 
dvitīyaskandhe śrīśaunakoktau BhP  
bile batorukramavikramān ye
na śṛṇvataḥ karṇapuṭe narasya 
jihvāsatī dārdurikeva sūta
na copagāyaty urugāyagāthāḥ  Hbhv

lobhābhibhūtamanaso 'kuśalāni śaśvat  Hbhv 
BhP  
tāñ chocyaśocyān avido 'nuśoce
hareḥ kathāyāṃ vimukhān aghena

āyur vṛthāvādagatismṛtīnām  Hbhv 
śrīmaitreyoktau ca BhP  
ko nāma loke puruṣārthasāravit
purākathānāṃ bhagavatkathāsudhām 
āpīya karṇāñjalibhir bhavāpahām
aho virajyeta vinā naretaram  Hbhv 
caturthe śrīpṛthustutau BhP 
yaśaḥ śivaṃ suśrava āryasaṅgame
yadṛcchayā copaśṛṇoti te sakṛt 
kathaṃ guṇajño viramed vinā paśuṃ
śrīr yat pravavre guṇasaṅgrahecchayā  Hbhv 
daśamārambhe śrīparīkṣitpraśne BhP  
nivṛttatarṣair upagīyamānād
bhavauṣadhāc chrotramano'bhirāmāt 
ka uttamaślokaguṇānuvādāt

ataevoktaṃ devaiḥ pañcamaskandhe BhP  
na yatra vaikuṇṭhakathāsudhāpagā

na yatra yajñeśamakhā mahotsavāḥ
sureśaloko 'pi na vai sa sevyatām  Hbhv 
atha bhagavatkathāsaktiḥ
ato niṣevyamāṇāṃ ca sarvathā bhagavatkathām 
muhus tadrasikān pṛcchen mitho modavivṛddhaye  Hbhv 
daśamaskandhe BhP  
satām ayaṃ sārabhṛtāṃ nisargo
yadarthavāṇīśruticetasām api 
pratikṣaṇaṃ navyavad acyutasya yat
striyā viṭānām iva sādhu vārtā  Hbhv 
ataeva tatraiva BhP 
tulyaśrutatapaḥśīlās tulyasvīyārimadhyamāḥ 
api cakruḥ pravacanam ekaṃ śuśrūṣavo 'pare  Hbhv  iti 
atha śrībhagavaddharmapratipādanamāhātmyam
tathā vaiṣṇavadharmāṃś ca kriyamānām api svayam 
sampṛcchet tadvidaḥ sādhūn anyonyaprītivṛddhaye  Hbhv 
śraddhayā bhagavaddharmān vaiṣṇavāyānupṛcchate 
avaśyaṃ kathayed vidvān anyathā doṣabhāg bhavet  Hbhv 
tad uktam
nākhyāti vaiṣṇavaṃ dharmaṃ viṣṇubhaktasya pṛcchataḥ 
kalau bhāgavato bhūtvā puṇyaṃ yāti śatābdikam  Hbhv 
skānde brahmanāradasaṃvāde
vaiṣṇave vaiṣṇavaṃ dharmaṃ yo dadāti dvijottamaḥ 
sasāgaramahīdāne yat phalaṃ labhate'dhikam  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca tatraiva 
ajñānāya ca yo jñānaṃ dadyād dharmopadeśanam 
kṛtsnāṃ vā pṛthivīṃ dadyāt tena tulyaṃ hi tat smṛtam  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare  
tat kathāṃ śrāvayed yas tu tadbhaktān mānavottamaḥ 
godānaphalam āpnoti sa naras tena karmaṇā  Hbhv 
pādme devadūtavikuṇḍalasaṃvāde PadmaP

api devās tam arcanti bhavabandhavidārakam  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye NārP 
satsaṅgadevārcanasatkathāsu
hitopadeśe nirato manuṣyaḥ 
prayāti viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ yad
dehāvasāne'cyutatulyatejāḥ  Hbhv 
atha bhagavaddharmāḥ
te ca śrībhagavaddharmā bhagavadbhaktalakṣaṇaiḥ 
vyañjitāḥ katicin mukhyā likhyante'tra pare'pi te  Hbhv 
te tu yadyapi vikhyātāḥ śrīmadbhāgavatādiṣu 
tathāpi yatnād ekatra saṅgṛhyante samādhanāḥ  Hbhv 
te coktāḥ kāśīkhaṇḍe dvārakāmāhātmye candraśarmaṇā 
adya prabhṛti kartavyaṃ yan mayā kṛṣṇa tac chṛṇu 
ekādaśyāṃ na bhoktavyaṃ kartavyo jāgaraḥ sadā  Hbhv 
mahotsavaḥ prakartavyaḥ pratyahapūjanaṃ tava 
palārdhenāpi biddhaṃ tu bhoktavyaṃ vāsarāntare  Hbhv 
tvatprītyāṣṭau mayā kāryā dvādaśyo vratasaṃyutā 
bhaktir bhāgavatī kāryā prāṇair api dhanair api  Hbhv 
nityaṃ nāmasahasraṃ tu paṭhanīyaṃ tava priyam 
pūjā tu tulasīpatrair mayā kāryā sadaiva hi  Hbhv 
tulasīkāṣṭhāsambhūtā mālā kāryā sadā mayā 
nṛtyagītaṃ prakartavyaṃ samprāpte jāgare tava  Hbhv 
tulasīkāṣṭhāsambhūtacandanena vilepanam 
kariṣyāmi tavāgre ca guṇānāṃ tava kīrtanam  Hbhv 
mathurāyāṃ prakartavyaṃ pratyabdaṃ gamanaṃ mayā 
tatkathāśravaṇaṃ kāryaṃ tathā pustakavācanam  Hbhv 
nityaṃ pādodakaṃ mūrdhnā mayā dhāryaṃ prayatnataḥ 
naivedyabhakṣaṇaṃ cāpi kariṣyāmi yatavrataḥ  Hbhv 
nirmālyaṃ śirasā dhāryaṃ tvadīyaṃ sādaraṃ mayā 
tava dattvā yad iṣṭaṃ tu bhakṣaṇīyaṃ mudā mayā  Hbhv 
tathā tathā prakartavyaṃ tava tuṣṭiḥ prajāyate 
satyam etan mayā kṛṣṇa tavāgre parikīrtanam  Hbhv 
saptamaskandhe śrīprahlādena BhP  
guruśuśrūṣayā bhaktyā sarvalabdhārpaṇena ca 
śraddhayā tatkathāyāṃ ca kīrtanair guṇakarmaṇām 
tatpādāmburuhadhyānāt talliṅgekṣārhaṇādibhiḥ  Hbhv 
hariḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu bhagavān āsta īśvaraḥ 
iti bhūtāni manasā kāmais taiḥ sādhu mānayet  Hbhv 
ekādaśe ca śrīkaviyogeśvareṇa BhP 
ye vai bhagavatā proktā upāyā hy ātmalabdhaye 
añjaḥ puṃsām aviduṣāṃ viddhi bhāgavatān hi tān  Hbhv 
tatraiva prabuddhayogeśvareṇa BhP  
sarvato manaso 'saṅgam ādau saṅgaṃ ca sādhuṣu 
dayāṃ maitrīṃ praśrayaṃ ca bhūteṣv addhā yathocitam  Hbhv 
śaucaṃ tapas titikṣāṃ ca maunaṃ svādhyāyam ārjavam 
brahmacaryam ahiṃsāṃ ca samatvaṃ dvandvasaṃjñayoḥ  Hbhv 
sarvatrātmeśvarānvīkṣāṃ kaivalyam aniketatām 
viviktacīravasanaṃ santoṣaṃ yena kenacit  Hbhv 
śraddhāṃ bhāgavate śāstre 'nindām anyatra cāpi hi 
manovākkarmadaṇḍaṃ ca satyaṃ śamadamāv api  Hbhv 
śravaṇaṃ kīrtanaṃ dhyānaṃ harer adbhutakarmaṇaḥ 
janmakarmaguṇānāṃ ca tadarthe 'khilaceṣṭitam  Hbhv 
iṣṭaṃ dattaṃ tapo japtaṃ vṛttaṃ yac cātmanaḥ priyam 
dārān sutān gṛhān prāṇān yat parasmai nivedanam  Hbhv 
evaṃ kṛṣṇātmanātheṣu manuṣyeṣu ca sauhṛdam 
paricaryāṃ cobhayatra mahatsu nṛṣu sādhuṣu  Hbhv 
parasparānukathanaṃ pāvanaṃ bhagavadyaśaḥ
mitho ratir mithas tuṣṭir nivṛttir mitha ātmanaḥ  Hbhv 
śrībhagavatā ca BhP  
malliṅgamadbhaktajana darśanasparśanārcanam 
paricaryā stutiḥ prahva guṇakarmānukīrtanam  Hbhv 
matkathāśravaṇe śraddhā madanudhyānam uddhava 
sarvalābhopaharaṇaṃ dāsyenātmanivedanam  Hbhv 
majjanmakarmakathanaṃ mama parvānumodanam 
gītatāṇḍavavāditra goṣṭhībhir madgṛhotsavaḥ  Hbhv 
yātrā balividhānaṃ ca sarvavārṣikaparvasu 
vaidikī tāntrikī dīkṣā madīyavratadhāraṇam  Hbhv 
mamārcāsthāpane śraddhā svataḥ saṃhatya codyamaḥ 
udyānopavanākrīḍa puramandirakarmaṇi  Hbhv 
sammārjanopalepābhyāṃ sekamaṇḍalavartanaiḥ 
gṛhaśuśrūṣaṇaṃ mahyaṃ dāsavad yad amāyayā  Hbhv 
amānitvam adambhitvaṃ kṛtasyāparikīrtanam 
api dīpāvalokaṃ me nopayuñjyān niveditam  Hbhv 
yad yad iṣṭatamaṃ loke yac cātipriyam ātmanaḥ 
tat tan nivedayen mahyaṃ tad ānantyāya kalpate  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca BhP 
śraddhāmṛtakathāyāṃ me śaśvan madanukīrtanam 
pariniṣṭhā ca pūjāyāṃ stutibhiḥ stavanaṃ mama  Hbhv 
ādaraḥ paricaryāyāṃ sarvāṅgair abhivandanam 
madbhaktapūjābhyadhikā sarvabhūteṣu manmatiḥ  Hbhv 
madartheṣv aṅgaceṣṭā ca vacasā madguṇeraṇam 
mayy arpaṇaṃ ca manasaḥ sarvakāmavivarjanam  Hbhv 
madarthe 'rthaparityāgo bhogasya ca sukhasya ca 
iṣṭaṃ dattaṃ hutaṃ japtaṃ madarthaṃ yad vrataṃ tapaḥ  Hbhv 
api cāgre BhP  
kuryāt sarvāṇi karmāṇi madarthaṃ śanakaiḥ smaran 
mayy arpitamanaścitto maddharmātmamanoratiḥ  Hbhv 
deśān puṇyān āśrayeta madbhaktaiḥ sādhubhiḥ śritān 
devāsuramanuṣyeṣu madbhaktācaritāni ca  Hbhv 
pṛthak satreṇa vā mahyaṃ parvayātrāmahotsavān 
kārayed gītanṛtyādyair mahārājavibhūtibhiḥ  Hbhv 
mām eva sarvabhūteṣu bahir antar apāvṛtam 
īkṣetātmani cātmānaṃ yathā kham amalāśayaḥ  Hbhv 
atha śrībhagavaddharmamāhātmyam
uktaṃ ca saptamaskandhe śrīprahlādena BhP  
evaṃ nirjitaṣaḍvargaiḥ kriyate bhaktir īśvare 
vāsudeve bhagavati yayā saṃlabhyate ratiḥ  Hbhv 
ekādaśe śrīnāradena BhP  
śruto 'nupaṭhito dhyāta ādṛto vānumoditaḥ
sadyaḥ punāti saddharmo devaviśvadruho 'pi hi  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrīkaviyogeśvareṇa BhP  
yān āsthāya naro rājan na pramādyeta karhicit 
dhāvan nimīlya vā netre na skhalen na pated iha  Hbhv 
śrīprabuddhayogeśvareṇa BhP  
iti bhāgavatān dharmān śikṣan bhaktyā tadutthayā 
nārāyaṇaparo māyām añjas tarati dustarām  Hbhv 
śrībhagavatā ca BhP  
evaṃ dharmair manuṣyāṇām uddhavātmanivedinām 
mayi sañjāyate bhaktiḥ ko 'nyo 'rtho 'syāvaśiṣyate  Hbhv 
kiṃ cāgre BhP  
na hy aṅgopakrame dhvaṃso maddharmasyoddhavāṇv api
mayā vyavasitaḥ samyaṅ nirguṇatvād anāśiṣaḥ  Hbhv  iti
alābhe satsabhāyās tu śuśrūṣuṃ ca nijālaye 
devālaye vā śāstrajñaḥ kīrtayed bhagavatkathām  Hbhv 
atha śrībhagavallīlākathākīrtanamāhātmyam 
uktaṃ ca skānde śrībhagavatā arjunaṃ prati 
matkathā kurute yas tu vaiṣṇavānāṃ sadāgrataḥ 
iha bhogān avāpnoti tathā mokṣaṃ na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
prathamaskandhe BhP  śrīnāradena
idaṃ hi puṃsas tapasaḥ śrutasya vā
sviṣṭasya sūktasya ca buddhidattayoḥ 
avicyuto 'rthaḥ kavibhir nirūpito
yaduttamaślokaguṇānuvarṇanam  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca BhP  
etad dhy āturacittānāṃ mātrāsparśecchayā muhuḥ 
bhavasindhuplavo dṛṣṭo haricaryānuvarṇanam  Hbhv 
ekādaśe śrīśukenāpi BhP  
itthaṃ harer bhagavato rucirāvatāra
vīryāṇi bālacaritāni ca śantamāni 
anyatra ceha ca śrutāni gṛṇan manuṣyo
bhaktiṃ parāṃ paramahaṃsagatau labheta  Hbhv 
ataeva śrīprahlādena nṛsiṃhastutāv uktam BhP  
so 'haṃ priyasya suhṛdaḥ paradevatāyā
līlākathās tava nṛsiṃha viriñcagītāḥ 
añjas titarmy anugṛṇan guṇavipramukto
durgāṇi te padayugālayahaṃsasaṅgaḥ  Hbhv 
gopikābhir api gītam BhP  
tava kathāmṛtaṃ taptajīvanaṃ
kavibhir īḍitaṃ kalmaṣāpaham 
śravaṇamaṅgalaṃ śrīmadātataṃ
bhuvi grṇanti te bhuridā janāḥ  Hbhv 
kirtane'py atra taj jñeyaṃ māhātmyaṃ śravaṇe'sya yat 
sidhyati śravaṇam nūnaṃ kīrtanāt svayam eva hi  Hbhv 
śāstrābhyāsasya cābhāve pūrveṣāṃ lokaviśrutām 
satām ādhunikānāṃ ca kathāṃ bandhuṣu kīrtayet  Hbhv 
iti śrīgopālabhaṭṭavilikhite śrībhagavadbhaktivilāse
satsaṅgamo nāma
daśamo vilāsaḥ 
 NityakrtyasamapanaVilasa
ekādaśavilāsaḥ
nityakṛtyasamāpanaḥ
śrīcaitanyaṃ prapadye taṃ mahāścaryaprabhāvakam 
prasāde yasya duṣṭo 'pi bhagavadbhaktimān bhavet  Hbhv 
tato dināntyabhāgeṣu bāhyeṣu surasadmasu 
yātrāṃ kṛtvā dvijaḥ sandhyām upāsīta yathāvidhi  Hbhv 
śrīviṣṇupurāṇe aurvasagarasaṃvāde ViP   
dināntasandhyāṃ sūryeṇa pūrvā mṛkṣair yutāṃ budhaḥ 
upatiṣṭhed yathānyāyaṃ samyag ācamya pārthiva  Hbhv 
sarvakālam upasthānaṃ sandhyāyāḥ pārthiveṣyate 
anyatra sūtikāśaucavibhramāturabhītitaḥ  Hbhv 
upatiṣṭhanti vai sandhyāṃ ye na pūrvāṃ na paścimām 
vrajanti te durātmānas tāmisraṃ narakaṃ nṛpa  Hbhv 
iti 
tato yathāśramācāraṃ karma sāyantanaṃ kṛtī 
nirvartya pūrvavat kuryād bhaktyā bhagavadarcanam  Hbhv 
śrīkṛṣṇabhaktyāsaktyā tu sandhyopāsyādikaṃ yadi 
patet karma na pātityadoṣaśaṅkā kathañcana  Hbhv 
atha śrībhagavadbhaktānāṃ karmapātityaparihāraḥ
pādme  śrībhagavaduktau 
matkarma kurvatāṃ puṃsāṃ kriyālopo bhaved yadi 
teṣāṃ karmāṇi kurvanti tisraḥ koṭyo maharṣayaḥ  Hbhv 
ādipurāṇe ca 
smaranti mama nāmāni ye tyaktvā karma cākhilam 
teṣāṃ karmāṇi kurvanti ṛṣayo bhagavatparāḥ  Hbhv 
iti 
mṛduśraddhasya bhaktasya prauḍhatām anupeyuṣaḥ 
kiṃcit karmādhikāritvāt karmāsyaitat prapañcitam  Hbhv 
prauḍhaśraddhasya bhaktasyakarmasv anadhikārataḥ 
pātityaṃ na bhavaty eva lekhanīyaṃ tadagrataḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃcid dhyānādibhedena trisandhyaṃ ca pṛthak pṛthak 
proktaḥ pūjāvidhiḥ prājñais tattatkāmāśusiddhaye  Hbhv 
atha trikālārcanavidhiviśeṣataḥ
śrīgautamīyatantre 
ārādhanavidhiṃ vakṣye prātaḥkāle viśeṣataḥ 
varaṃ vṛndāvanaṃ dhyāyet puṇyavṛkṣādisevitam  Hbhv 
punnāgair nāgavṛkṣaiś ca panasaiś caiva kāñcanaiḥ 
bakulaiś caiva bilvaiś ca vanyaiḥ kurvakair api  Hbhv 
sarvartukusumopetaiḥ puṣpāvanataśākhibhiḥ 
tanmadhye pulinaṃ dhyāyed bahupuṣpakacampakam  Hbhv 
dhūpadipair vitānena puṣpamālāvibhūṣitam 
muktādāmapatākābhir vanyapuṣpair alaṅkṛtam  Hbhv 
tanmadhye kalpavṛkṣasya cchāyāyāṃ paṅkajāsane 
susthitaṃ veṇugītāḍhyaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam  Hbhv 
vanamālāparivṛtaṃ gopikāśataveṣṭitam 
devāsuraiś ca siddhaiś ca gandharvair apsarogaṇaiḥ  Hbhv 
yakṣair vidyādharagaṇair vihagair bhuvi saṃsthitaiḥ 
brahmarṣibhiḥ stūyamānaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ caiva śucismitam  Hbhv 
nānāvidhaiś ca gopālair mṛgapakṣivibhūṣitam 
lelihyamānaṃ praṇayāt paśūnāṃ śatakoṭibhiḥ  Hbhv 
indīvaranibhaṃ divyaṃ sundaraṃ tv indirālayam 
sampūrṇacandravadanaṃ padmapatranibhekṣaṇam  Hbhv 
padmābhapāṇipādaṃ ca padmarāgavarārcitam 
śaraṇyaṃ sarvalokānāṃ gopīnāṃ prāṇavallabham  Hbhv 
evaṃ dhyātvārcayen nityaṃ ṣoḍaśenopacārataḥ 
dugdhaṃ ca dadhikhaṇḍena sahitaṃ saṃnivedayet  Hbhv 
sauvarṇapātre gopānāṃ grāsaṃ kāṃsye nivedayet 
evaṃ samarcayed bhaktyā japan mantraṃ samāhitaḥ  Hbhv 
madhyāhne sampravakṣyāmi pūjāṃ sarvārthasiddhidām 
sauvarṇaparvate mūle dhātubhiḥ samalaṅkṛte  Hbhv 
puṇyavṛkṣasamākīrṇe puṇyapakṣininādite 
padmotpalādisaṅkīrṇe vāpībhiḥ samalaṅkṛte  Hbhv 
tasmin satpuline ramye chāyāyāṃ paṅkajāsane 
sauvarṇamaṇḍape samyagvitānādivibhūṣite  Hbhv 
mālādiracite ramye maṇibhiḥ puṣpaśobhitaiḥ 
suvarṇaratnasandohair antarāntaraśobhite  Hbhv 
siṃhāsane samāsīnaṃ viśrāntaṃ kaṃsasūdanam 
muktāmayaiḥ surucirair hārair dāmavibhūṣitam  Hbhv 
dhyātvā samyag viśuddhātmā jātīpuṣpaiḥ samarcayet 
mahārajatapātre tu naivedyānnaṃ nivedayet  Hbhv 
dadyād grāsaṃ sakhīnāṃ ca gopīnāṃ vijitendriyaḥ 
devakīparamānandam evaṃ dhyāyet sukhāsanam  Hbhv 
rātripūjāvidhiṃ vakṣye rukmiṇīvallabhasya ca 
adhastāt kalpavṛkṣasya sarvapuṣpaphalasya ca  Hbhv 
ratnamaṇḍapamadhyasthaṃ divyapītāmbaraṃ harim 
divyacandanaliptāṅgaṃ divyābharaṇabhūṣitam  Hbhv 
anekadivyamālābhir maṇḍitaṃ paṅkajekṣaṇam 
ratnamaṇḍapamadhyasthaṃ sundaraṃ sundarasmitam  Hbhv 
śobhayantaṃ svavapuṣā sarvalokān nijaśriyā 
gopījanānāṃ hṛdayavallabhaṃ proktavarcasam  Hbhv 
sugandhipuṣpair ārādhyaṃ śrīkṛṣṇaṃ sarvanāyakam 
rājate tu payaḥ śuddhaṃ pakvaṃ pātre nivedayet  Hbhv 
evam abhyarcya manasā japen mantraṃ samāhitaḥ 
kālatrayārcane caiva sahasraṃ sāṣṭakaṃ japet 
eṣa nityakramaḥ proktaḥ kṛṣṇamantrasya sūribhiḥ  Hbhv 
tatraivādau saṃkṣiptatrikālapūjoktyanantaram
manasā vā samabhyarcya triṣu sandhyāsu saṃyamī 
pratyahaṃ tu japen mantram aṣṭottarasahasrakam 
asāmarthye japen mantraṃ nityam aṣṭaśataṃ tathā  Hbhv 
iti 
atha naktaṃ kṛtyāni
tato yathāsampradāyaṃ homaṃ niṣpādya vaiṣṇavaḥ 
gītanṛtyādikaṃ bhaktyā vidhāya prārthayet prabhum  Hbhv 
tathā coktam
balīyasā padā svāmin padavīm avadhāraya 
āgaccha śayanasthānaṃ priyābhiḥ saha keśava  Hbhv 
iti 
evaṃ prārthya samarpyāsmai pāduke śayanālayam 
ānīya devaṃ tatratyān upacārān prakalpayet  Hbhv 
viśeṣato 'rpayet tatra ghanaṃ dugdhaṃ saśarkaram 
tāmbūlaṃ ca sakarpūraṃ divyamālyānulepanam  Hbhv 
itthaṃ bhaktyā samārādhyaṃ bhagavantaṃ svaśaktitaḥ 
tatprītyai sarvakarmāṇi tat phalaṃ vārpayet kṛtī  Hbhv 
athāhorātrākhilakarmārpaṇavidhiḥ
ekādaśaskandhe BhP  
kāyena vācā manasendriyair vā
buddhyātmanā vānusṛtasvabhāvāt 
karoti yad yat sakalaṃ parasmai
nārāyaṇāyeti samarpayet tat  Hbhv 
kiṃ cātra 
sādhu vāsādhu vā karma yad yad ācaritaṃ mayā 
tat sarvaṃ bhagavan viṣṇo gṛhāṇārādhanaṃ param  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
apāṃ samīpe śayanāsane gṛhe
divā ca rātrau ca yathā ca gacchatā 
yad asti kiṃcit sukṛtaṃ kṛtaṃ mayā
janārdanas tena kṛtena tuṣyatu  Hbhv 
ataivoktaṃ tṛtīyaskandhe brahmāṇaṃ prati śrībhagavatā BhP  
pūrtena tapasā yajñair dānair yogasamādhinā 
rāddhaṃ niḥśreyasaṃ puṃsāṃ matprītis tattvavinmatam  Hbhv 
iti 
ittham ārādhayen nityaṃ bhagavantaṃ yathā vidhi 
nyāyārjitāptavittena samagraphalasiddhaye  Hbhv 
atha pūjāphalasamprāptyupāyaḥ
daśamaskandhe BhP  
ayaṃ svastyayanaḥ panthā dvijāter gṛhamedhinaḥ 
yac chraddhayāptavittena śuklenejyeta pūruṣaḥ  Hbhv 
agastyasaṃhitāyāṃ ca
nyāyāj jitaiḥ sādhanaiś ca dānahomārcanādikam 
kuryān na ced adho yāti bhaktyā kurvann api dvija  Hbhv 
iti 
yatnāt siddhair nijaiḥ śuddhair dravyair dhanyo 'rcayet prabhum 
pūjādravyāṇy aśaktaś ced dahyād īkṣeta vārcanam  Hbhv 
athāśaktasya pūjāprāptyupāyaḥ
agastyasaṃhitāyāṃ
ārādhanāsamarthyaś ced dadyād arcanasādhanam 
yo dātuṃ naiva śaknoti kuryād arcanadarśanam  Hbhv 
nistārāya tad evālaṃ bhavābdher munisattama 
naikaṃ ca yasya vidyeta so 'dho yāty eva nānyathā  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca tatraiva
yas tu bhaktyā prayatnena svayaṃ sampādya cākhilam 
sādhanaṃ cārcayed vidvān samagraṃ labhate phalam  Hbhv 
yo 'rcayed vidhivad bhaktyā parānītaiś ca sādhanaiḥ 
pūjāphalārdham eva syān na samagraṃ phalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca pādme śrīkṛṣṇasatyabhāmāsaṃvādīyakārttikamāhātmye 
dharmoddeśena yo dravyam aparaṃ yācate naraḥ 
tatpuṇyakarmajaṃ tasya dhanadas tv āpnuyāt phalam  Hbhv 
atha darśanamāhātmyam
pādme śrīpulastyabhagīrathasaṃvāde
pūjitaṃ pūjyamānaṃ ca ye paśyanti janārdanam 
kapilāśatadānasya nityaṃ bhavati tat phalam  Hbhv 
āgneye
pūjitaṃ pūjyamānaṃ vā yo paśyed bhaktito harim 
śraddhayā modayed yas tu so 'pi yāgaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
sampūjyamānaṃ vidhinā yaḥ paśyet śraddhayā harim 
so 'pi yāgaphalaṃ kṛtsnaṃ prāpnuyāt nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
dṛṣṭvā sampūjitaṃ devaṃ nṛtyamāno 'numodayet 
asaṃśayamatiḥ śuddhaḥ paraṃ brahmādhigacchati  Hbhv 
atha śrībhagavanmūrtidarśananityatā
viṣṇudharmottare
tāvad bhramanti saṃsāre manuṣyā mandabuddhayaḥ 
yāvad rūpaṃ na paśyanti keśavasya mahātmanaḥ  Hbhv 
pādme ca tatraiva
pūjyamānaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ ye na paśyanti vaiṣṇavāḥ 
teṣāṃ dattaṃ hutaṃ japtaṃ daiteyāyopatiṣṭhati  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca tatraiva nārāyaṇanāradasaṃvāde pūjāvidhikathane
yatra kutrāpi pratimāṃ vedadharmasamanvitām 
na paśyanti janā gatvā te daṇḍyā yamakiṅkaraiḥ  Hbhv 
atha bhagavadarthe dravyadānamāhātmyam
skānde
viṣṇum uddiśya yat kiñcid viṣṇubhaktāya dīyate 
dānaṃ tad vimalaṃ proktaṃ kevalaṃ mokṣasādhanam  Hbhv 
kaurme
yat kiñcid deyam īśānam uddiśya brāhmaṇāya ca 
prabhave viṣṇave cātha tad anantaphalaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare not found
anugraheṇa mahatā pretasya patitasya ca 
nārāyaṇabaliḥ kāryas tenāsyānugraho bhavet  Hbhv 
anādinidhano devaḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ 
akṣayaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣas tatra dattaṃ na naśyati  Hbhv 
yathā kathañcid yad dattaṃ devadeve janārdane 
avināśi tu tad viddhi pātram eko janārdanaḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva tṛtīyakāṇḍe not found
sāmānyabhaktyā yad dattaṃ tad dhi padbhyāṃ pratīcchati 
ekāntabhāvopagamair mūrdhnā divjavarottamāḥ  Hbhv 
ananto bhagavān viṣṇus tasya kāmavivarjitaiḥ 
yad eva dīyate kiñcit tad evākṣayam ucyate  Hbhv 
padbhyāṃ pratīcchate devaḥ sakāmena niveditam 
mūrdhnā pratīcchate dattam akāmena dvijottamāḥ  Hbhv 
tathaivoktaṃ mokṣadharme śrīnāradena not found
brahmā yad ṛṣayaś caiva svayaṃ paśupatiś ca yat 
anye ca vibudhaśreṣṭhā daityadānavarākṣasāḥ  Hbhv 
nāgāḥ suvarṇāḥ gandharvāḥ siddhā rājarṣayas tathā 
havyaṃ kravyaṃ ca satataṃ vidhiyuktaṃ prabhuñjate 
kṛtsnaṃ tu tasya devasya caraṇāv upatiṣṭhati  Hbhv 
yāḥ kriyāḥ saṃprayuktās tu ekāntagatabuddhibhiḥ 
tāḥ sarvāḥ śirasā devaḥ pratigṛhṇāti vai svayam  Hbhv 
brahmavaivarte
ekām api naro dhenuṃ savatsāṃ vidhipūrvakam 
dattvoddeśena kṛṣṇasya prāpnoty evābhivāñchitam  Hbhv 
nārasiṃhe
yo gāṃ payasvinīṃ viṣṇoḥ kṛṣṇavarṇāṃ prayacchati 
aśvamedhasya yajñasya phalaṃ prāpya hariṃ vrajet  Hbhv 
sarvapāpair virahitaḥ sarvabhūṣaṇabhūṣitaḥ 
gavāṃ sahasradānasya prāpyaṃ divyaṃ vrajet  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare 
gavāṃ lokam avāpnoti dhenuṃ dattvā payasvinīm 
dadhikṣīraghṛtārthāya vāsudevasya cālaye 
dattvā gāṃ madhuparkāya mahat phalam avāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
jalāśayaṃ tathā kṛtvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  Hbhv 
sapuṣpaiḥ saphalair vṛkṣair yutaṃ kṛtvā jalāśayam 
udyānaiḥ padminīṣaṇḍair āśramaiś ca manoharaiḥ 
śvedadvīpam avāpnoti punar nāvartate tataḥ  Hbhv 
devāgre kārayed yas tu ramyām āpaṇavīthikām 
rājā bhavati lokeṣu vijitārir mahāśayāḥ  Hbhv 
nagaraṃ ca tathā kṛtvā sāmrājyam adhigacchati 
śivikāṃ ye prayacchanti te prayānty amarāvatīm  Hbhv 
aśvadāḥ svargalokasthā rājante divi sūryavat 
kavīndradānāc chakrasya cirāl lokācyuto naraḥ  Hbhv 
rājā bhavati dharmātmā pṛthivyāṃ pṛthivīpatiḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇor āyatane dattvā tatkathāpustakaṃ naraḥ 
brahmalokam avāpnoti bahukālasthiraṃ dvijāḥ  Hbhv 
pustakāṃś ca tathaivānyān yaḥ pradadyān naras tv iha 
sārasvatam avāpnoti lokaṃ kālaṃ tathā bahum  Hbhv 
svabhṛtaṃ vācakaṃ kṛtvā devāgāre naraḥ sadā 
vidyādānaphalaṃ prāpya brahmaloke mahīyate  Hbhv 
viṣṇoḥ śaṅkhapradānena vāruṇaṃ lokam aśnute 
mānuṣyam āsādya tathā khyātaśabdaś ca jāyate  Hbhv 
ghaṇṭāpradānena tathā mahadyaśa upāśnute 
kūṭāgāraṃ tathā dattvā nagarādhipatir bhavet  Hbhv 
dattvā tu devakarmārthaṃ navāṃ vedīṃ dṛḍhāṃ śubhām 
pārthivatvam avāpnoti vedī hi pṛthivī yataḥ  Hbhv 
toraṇaṃ kārayed yas tu devadevālaye naraḥ 
lokeṣu tasya dvārāṇi bhavanti vivṛtāni vai  Hbhv 
devaveśmopayogyāni śilpabhāṇḍāni yo naraḥ 
dadyād vā vādyabhāṇḍāni gaṇeśatvam avāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
yaḥ kumbhaṃ devakarmārthaṃ naro dadyān navaṃ śubham 
vāruṇaṃ lokam āpnoti sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  Hbhv 
caturaḥ kalasān dadyād yas tu devagṛhe naraḥ 
catuḥsamudravalayāṃ sa hi bhuṅkte vasundharām  Hbhv 
dattvaikam api viprendrāḥ kalasaṃ susamāhitaḥ 
rājā bhavati dharmātmā bhūtale nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
vāridhānīṃ tathā dattvā vāruṇaṃ lokam aśnute 
kamaṇḍalupradānena yajñasya phalam āpnuyāt  Hbhv 
mātrāṃ tu paricaryārthaṃ nivedya haraye tathā 
sarvakāmasamṛddhasya yajñasya phalam aśnute  Hbhv 
tālavṛntapradānena nirvṛtiṃ prāpnuyāt parām 
mālyādhāraṃ tathā dattvā dhūpādhāraṃ tathaiva ca 
gandhādhāraṃ tathā pātraṃ kāmānāṃ pātratāṃ vrajet  Hbhv 
saumdrajāni pātrāṇi dattvā vai taijasāni vā 
pātraṃ bhavati kāmānāṃ vidyānāṃ ca dhanasya ca  Hbhv 
śayanāsanadānena sthitiṃ vindati śāśvatīm 
uttaracchadadānena sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
naraḥ suvarṇadānena sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt 
rūpyado rūpam āpnoti viśeṣād bhuvi durlabham  Hbhv 
ratnadānena lokeṣu prāmāṇyam upagacchati 
anaḍvāhapradānena daśadhenuphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
ājñāvimahiṣoṣṭrāṇāṃ dānam aśvatarasya ca 
sahasraguṇitaṃ dānāt pūrvaproktāt prakīrtitam  Hbhv 
vāruṇaṃ lokam āpnoti dattvā vastuṃ dvijottamāḥ 
avipradānāc ca tathā tam enaṃ lokam aśnute  Hbhv 
uṣṭraṃ vā gardabhaṃ vāpi kharaṃ vā yaḥ prayacchati 
alakāṃ sa samāsādya yakṣendraiḥ saha modate  Hbhv 
āraṇyamṛgajātīnāṃ tathā dānāc ca pakṣiṇām 
agniṣṭomam avāpnoti subhagaś ca tathā bhavet  Hbhv 
dāsaṃ dattvā sukhe loke neṣṭabhraṣṭo vijāyate 
dāsīṃ dattvā tathā viprā nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  Hbhv 
gaṇikāṃ ye prayacchanti nṛtyagītaviśāradām 
sarvaduḥkhavinirmuktās te prayānty amarāvatīm  Hbhv 
nṛtyaṃ dattvā tathāpnoti rudralokam asaṃśayam  Hbhv 
prekṣaṇīyapradānena śakraloke mahīyate 
gītaṃ dattvā tathāpnoti brahmalokam asaṃśayam  Hbhv 
dundubhiṃ ye prayacchanti kīrtimanto bhavanti te  Hbhv 
dattvā dhānyāni bījāni śasyāni vividhāni ca 
rūpakāni ca tāny eva prāpnuyāt surapūjyatām  Hbhv 
dattvā śākāni ramyāni viśokas tv abhijāyate 
dattvā ca vyañjanārthāya tathopakaraṇāni ca  Hbhv 
puṣpavṛkṣaṃ tathā dattvā deśasyādhipatir bhavet 
phalavṛkṣaṃ tathā nagarādhipatir bhavet  Hbhv 
tathā
sugandhasādhanānīha paṭavāsāni yo naraḥ 
dadāti devadevasya so 'śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
kaṅkatasya pradānena viromas tv abhijāyate 
kūrcaprasādhanaṃ kṛtvā paraṃ maṅgalam aśnute  Hbhv 
vismāpanīyaṃ yat kiñcid dattvātyantaṃ sukhaṃ labhet  Hbhv 
vastrālaṅkaraṇādīnāṃ kṛṣṇārpaṇaphalaṃ ca yat 
upacāraprayoge prāk tatra tatra vyalekhi tat  Hbhv 
upacārāś ca vividhāḥ śrīmadbhagavadarcane 
śakyaśaktyādibhedena tāntrikair vaiṣṇavir matāḥ  Hbhv 
atha vividhopacārāḥ
āgame
āsanasvāgate sārghye pādyam ācamanīyakam 
madhuparkācamasnānavasanābharaṇāni ca  Hbhv 
sugandhasumanodhūpadīpanaivedyavandanam 
prayojayed aracanājñām upacārāṃs tu ṣoḍaśa  Hbhv 
arghyaṃ ca pādyācamanamadhuparkācamāny api 
gandhādayo nivedyāntā upacārā daśa kramāt  Hbhv 
gandhādibhir nivedyāntaiḥ pūjā pañcopacārikī 
saparyās trividhāḥ proktās tāsām ekāṃ samācaret  Hbhv 
kvacic ca
āsanāvāhanaṃ caiva pādyārghyācamanīyakam
