snānaṃ vāso bhūṣaṇaṃ ca gandhaḥ puṣpaṃ ca dhūpakaḥ  Hbhv 
pradīpaś caiva naivedyaṃ puṣpāñjalir ataḥ param 
pradakṣiṇaṃ namaskāro visargaś caiva ṣoḍaśa  Hbhv 
kecic cāhuś catuḥṣaṣṭim upacārān mamārcane 
teṣv anekaprakāreṣu prakāraiko 'tra likhyate  Hbhv 
sukhasuptasya kṛṣṇasya prātar ādau prabodhanam 
vedaghoṣaṇavīṇāvivādyair vandistavair api  Hbhv 
jayaśabdā namaskārā maṅgalārātrikaṃ tataḥ 
āsanaṃ dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca pādyārghyācamanāny api  Hbhv 
tataś ca madhuparkāḍhyācamanaṃ pādukārpaṇam 
aṅgamārjanam abhyaṅgodvartane snapanaṃ jalaḥ  Hbhv 
kṣīreṇa dadhnā haviṣā madhunā sitayā tathā 
mantrapūtaiḥ punar vārbhir aṅgavāso 'tha vāsasī  Hbhv 
upavītaṃ punaāc cācamanīyaṃ cānulepanam 
bhūṣaṇaṃ kusumaṃ dhūpo dīpo dṛṣṭyapasāraṇam  Hbhv 
naivedyaṃ mukhavāsas tu tāmbūlaṃ śayanottamam 
keśaprasādhanaṃ divyavastrāṇi mukuṭaṃ mahat  Hbhv 
divyagandhānulepaś ca kaustubhādivibhūṣaṇam 
vicitradivyapuṣpāṇi maṅgalārātrikaṃ tataḥ  Hbhv 
ādarśaḥ sukhayānena maṇḍapāgamanotsavaḥ 
siṃhāsanopaveśaś ca pādyādyaiḥ punar arcanam  Hbhv 
punar dhūpādyarpaṇena prāgvan naivedyam uttamam 
tataś ca divyatāmbūlamahānīrājanaṃ punaḥ  Hbhv 
cāmaravyajanacchatraṃ gītaṃ vādyaṃ ca nartanam 
pradakṣiṇaṃ namaskāraḥ stutiḥ śrīcaraṇābjayoḥ  Hbhv 
tayoś ca sthāpanaṃ mūrdhni tīrthanirmālyadhāraṇam 
ucchiṣṭabhojanaṃ pādasevoddeśopaveśanam  Hbhv 
naktaṃ śayyāvinirmāṇaṃ divyair vividhasādhanaiḥ 
hastapradānaṃ śayanasthānāgamamahotsavaḥ  Hbhv 
śayyopaveśanaṃ śrīmatpādakṣālanapūrvakam 
gandhaprasūnatāmbūlārpaṇanīrājanotsavaḥ  Hbhv 
śeṣaparyaṅkaśayanapādasaṃvāhanādikam 
krameṇaite catuḥṣaṣṭhir upacārāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  Hbhv 
sadācārānusāreṇa yad yad ācaryate svayam 
nityakarmādikaṃ tat tat śrīkṛṣṇasyāpi kārayet  Hbhv 
ato 'trālikhitaṃ yad yad upacārādikaṃ param 
sarvaṃ tat tac ca jānīyāl lokarītyanusārataḥ  Hbhv 
uktānāṃ copacārāṇām abhāve bhagavān sadā 
bhaktenārcyo yathālabdhais tair antarbhāvitair api  Hbhv 
athālabdhasamādhānam
tantre
upacāroktavastūnām upasaṅgrahaṇe vidhiḥ 
dravyāṇām apy abhāve tu puṣpākṣatayavaiḥ kriyāḥ  Hbhv 
arcopacāravastūnām abhāve samupasthite 
nirmalenodakenaiva dravyasampūrṇatā bhavet  Hbhv 
upacāreṣu dravyeṣu yat kiñcid duṣkaraṃ budhaḥ 
tat sarvaṃ manasā buddhyā puṣpakṣepeṇa kalpayet  Hbhv 
eteṣu copacāreṣu vittaśāṭhyavivarjitam 
yad asampannam eteṣāṃ manasā tu prakalpayet  Hbhv 
agastyasaṃhitāyāṃ śrītulasīmāhātmye
yad yan nyūnaṃ bhavaty eva rāmārādhanasādhanam 
tulasīdalamātreṇa yuktaṃ tat paripūryate  Hbhv 
ekādaśaskandhe ca śrībhagavaduddhavasaṃvāde 
dravyaiḥ prasiddhair madyāgaḥ pratimādiṣv amāyinaḥ 
bhaktasya ca yathālabdhair hṛdi bhāvena caiva hi  Hbhv 
tato 'nujñāṃ prabhoḥ prārthya daṇḍavat taṃ praṇamya ca 
sāyaṃ bhuktvā yathānyāyaṃ sukhaṃ svapyāt prabhuṃ smaret  Hbhv 
atha śayanavidhiḥ
āgame
nirguṇo niṣkalaś caiva viśvamūrtidharo 'vyayaḥ 
anādyante sadānante phaṇāmaṇiviśobhite 
kṣīrābdhimadhye yaḥ śete sa māṃ rakṣatu mādhavaḥ  Hbhv 
sabāhyābhyantaraṃ deham āpādatalamastakam 
sarvātmā sarvaśaktiś ca pātu māṃ garuḍadhvajaḥ  Hbhv 
iti rakṣāṃ puraskṛtya svaped viṣṇum anusmaran  Hbhv 
kiṃ cānyatra
adbhiḥ śaucavidhiṃ vidhāya caraṇau prakṣāly copaspṛśed
dviḥ saṃsmṛtya jagatpatiṃ vrajapatiṃ śrīvallabhīvallabham 
rādhāyāḥ suciraṃ pibantam amṛtāsārāyamāṇāṃ giraṃ
vastreṇāṅghriyugaṃ pramṛjyaa śayanaṃ tv āpādya sadyaḥ svapet  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
rāmaṃ skandaṃ hanumantaṃ vainateyaṃ vṛkodaram 
śayane yaḥ smaren nityaṃ duḥsvapnas tasya naśyati  Hbhv 
api ca skāndapādmayoḥ PadmaP 
ṛtukālābhigāmī yaḥ svadāranirataś ca yaḥ 
sarvadā brahmacārīha vijñeyaḥ sa gṛhāśramī  Hbhv 
ṛtuḥ ṣoḍaśayāminyaś catasras tāsu garhitāḥ 
putradās tāsu yā yugmā ayugmāḥ kanyakāpradāḥ  Hbhv 
tyaktvā candramasaṃ duṣṭaṃ maghāṃ mūlaṃ vihāya ca 
śuciḥ sannirviśet patnīṃ puṃnāmarkṣe viśeṣataḥ 
śuciṃ putraṃ prasūyeta puruṣārthaprasādhanam  Hbhv 
viṣṇupurāṇe aurvasagarasaṃvāde 
kṛtapādādiśaucaś ca bhuktvā sāyaṃ tato gṛhī 
gacchec chayyām asphuṭitām ekadārumayīṃ nṛpa  Hbhv 
nāviśālāṃ na vai bhagnāṃ nāsamāṃ malināṃ na ca 
na ca jantumayīṃ śayyām adhitiṣṭhed anāstṛtām  Hbhv 
prācyāṃ diśi śiraḥ śastaṃ yāmyāyām athavā nṛpa 
sadaiva svapataḥ puṃso viparītaṃ tu rogadam  Hbhv 
ṛtāv upagamaḥ śastaḥ svapatnyām avanīpate 
punnāmarkṣe śubhe kāle jyeṣṭhayugmāsu rātriṣu  Hbhv 
nāsnātāṃ tu striyaṃ gacchen nāturāṃ na rajasvalām 
nāniṣṭāṃ na prakupitāṃ nāpraśastāṃ na gurviṇīm  Hbhv 
nādakṣiṇāṃ nānyakāmāṃ nākāmāṃ nānyayoṣitam 
kṣutkṣāmām atibhuktāṃ vā svayaṃ caibhir guṇair yutaḥ  Hbhv 
snātaḥ sraggandhadhṛkprīto nādhyātaḥ kṣudhito 'pi vā 
sakāmaḥ sānurāgaś ca vyavāyaṃ puruṣo vrajet  Hbhv 
caturdaśyaṣṭamī caiva amāvasyātha pūrṇimā 
parvāṇy etāni rājendra ravisaṅkrāntir eva ca  Hbhv 
tailastrīmāṃsasambhogī parvasv eteṣu vai pumān 
viṇmūtrabhojanaṃ nāma prayāti narakaṃ nṛpa  Hbhv 
nānyayonāv ayonau vā nopayuktauṣadhas tathā 
devadvijagurūṇāṃ ca vyavāyī nāśramī bhavet  Hbhv 
caityacatvaratīrtheṣu naiva goṣṭhe catuṣpathe 
naiva śmaśānopavane salileṣu mahīpate  Hbhv 
proktaparvasvaśeṣeṣu naiva bhūpāla sandhyayoḥ 
gacched vyavāyaṃ matimān na mūtroccārapīḍitaḥ  Hbhv 
paradārān na gaccheta manasāpi kadācana 
kim u vācāsthibandho 'pi nāsti teṣu vyavāyinām  Hbhv 
mṛto narakam abhyeti hīyate cātra cāyuṣaḥ 
paradāraratiḥ puṃsām ubhayatrāpi bhītidā  Hbhv 
iti matvā svadāreṣu ṛtumatsu budho vrajet 
yathoktadoṣahīneṣu sakāmeṣv anṛtāv api  Hbhv 
iti 
teṣāṃ bhaktyupayogitvaṃ na syād yadyapi karmaṇām 
tathāpi kṛta ullekho gṛhiṣv āvaśyakaṃ tataḥ  Hbhv 
itthaṃ hi prātaru tthānāt pratyahaṃ śayanāvadhi 
śrīkṛṣṇaṃ pūjayan siddhasarvārtho 'sya priyo bhavet  Hbhv 
atha śrībhagavadarcanamāhātmyam
śrīkūrmapurāṇe
na viṣṇvārādhanāt puṇyaṃ vidyate karma vaidikam 
tasmād anādimadhyāntaṃ nityam ārādhayed dharim  Hbhv 
tatraiva bhṛgvādīn prati sākṣāt śrībhagavaduktau
ye'rcayiṣyanti māṃ bhaktyā nityaṃ kaliyuge dvijāḥ 
vidhinā vedadṛṣṭena te gamiṣyanti tatpadam  Hbhv 
viṣṇurahasye
śrīviṣṇor arcanaṃ ye tu prakurvanti narā bhuvi 
te yānti śāśvataṃ viṣṇor ānandaṃ paramaṃ padam  Hbhv 
iti 
tatraiva śrībhagavaduktau
na me dhyānaratāḥ samyagyoginaḥ parituṣṭaye 
tathā bhavanti devarṣe kriyāyogaratā yathā  Hbhv 
kriyāyogo hi me'bhīṣṭaḥ parayogāt svanuṣṭhitāt 
tuṣṭir me sambhavet pumbhir bhaktimadbhir amatsaraiḥ  Hbhv 
ye'rcayanti narā nityaṃ kriyāyogaratāḥ svayam 
dhyāyanti ye ca māṃ nityaṃ teṣāṃ śreṣṭhāḥ kriyā matāḥ  Hbhv 
kriyāhīnasya devarṣe tathā dhyānaṃ na muktidam 
na tathā māṃ vidur viprā dhyāninas tattvato vinā 
kriyāyogaratāḥ samyag labhante māṃ samādhinā  Hbhv 
yathā hi kāmadaṃ nṝṇāṃ mama tuṣṭikaraṃ param 
bhaktiyogaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ bhuktimuktipradaṃ śubham  Hbhv 
saṃvatsareṇa yat puṇyaṃ labhante dhyānino mama 
prāpyante tad ihaikāhāt kriyāyogaparair naraiḥ  Hbhv 
ādipurāṇe
na karmasadṛśaṃ dhyānaṃ na karmasadṛśaṃ phalam 
na karmasadṛśas tyāgo na karmasadṛśaṃ tapaḥ 
na karmasadṛśaṃ puṇyaṃ na karmasadṛśī gatiḥ  Hbhv 
nāradīye NārP 
bhaktigrāhyo hṛṣīkeśo na dhanair dharaṇīdhara 
bhaktyā saṃpūjito viṣṇuḥ pradadāti manoratham  Hbhv 
tasmād viprāḥ sadā bhaktiḥ kartavyā cakrapāṇinaḥ 
janenāpi jagannāthaḥ pūjitaḥ kleśahā bhavet  Hbhv 
haribhaktisudhodaye 
kṛtāpi dambhahāsyārthe sevā tārayate janān 
viphalā nānyakarmeva kṛpāluḥ ko nv ataḥ paraḥ  Hbhv 
brahmavaivarte 
sa samārādhito devo muktikṛt syād yathā tathā 
anicchayāpi hutabhuk saṃspṛṣṭo dahati dvija  Hbhv 
dhanavān putravān bhogī yaśasvī bhayavarjitaḥ 
medhāvī matimān prājño bhavaty ārādhanād dhareḥ  Hbhv 
skānde sanatkumāramarkaṇḍeyasaṃvāde 
viśiṣṭaḥ sarvadharmāc ca dharmo viṣṇvarcanaṃ nṝṇām 
sarvayajñatapohomas tīrthasnānaiś ca yat phalam  Hbhv 
tat phalaṃ koṭiguṇitaṃ viṣṇuṃ sampūjya cāpnuyāt 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena nārāyaṇam ihārcayet  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrīśivomāsaṃvāde 
yaḥ pradadyad dvijendraya sarvaṃ bhumiṃ sasagaram 
arcayed yaḥ sakṛd viṣṇuṃ tat phalaṃ labhate naraḥ  Hbhv 
masardham api yo viṣṇuṃ nairantaryena pūjayet 
puruṣottamaḥ sa vijñeyo viṣṇubhakto na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
madhyandinagate surye yo viṣṇuṃ paripūjayet 
vasupūrṇamahidatur yat punyaṃ tad avāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
prātar utthaya yo viṣṇuṃ satataṃ paripūjayet 
agnistomasahasrasya labhate phalam uttamam  Hbhv 
yo viṣṇuṃ prayato bhūtvā sayaṃkale samarcayet 
gavaṃ medhasya yajñasya phalam āpnoti durlabham  Hbhv 
evaṃ sarvāsu velāsu avelāsu ca keśavam 
sampūjayan naro bhaktyā sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
kiṃ punar yo 'rcayen nityaṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtam 
dhanyaḥ saḥ kṛtakṛtyaś ca viṣṇulokam avāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca 
dīkṣāmātreṇa kṛṣṇasya narā mokṣaṃ labhanti vai 
kiṃ punar ye sadā bhaktyā pūjayanty acyutaṃ naraḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrībrahmanaradasaṃvāde
saṃsāre'smin mahāghore janmamṛtyubhayākule 
pūjanaṃ vāsudevasya tārakaṃ vādibhiḥ smrtam  Hbhv 
sa nāma sukṛti loke kulaṃ tena hy alaṅkṛtam 
ādhāraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ yena viṣṇuḥ prasaditaḥ  Hbhv 
yajñānāṃ tapasāṃ caiva śubhānām api karmaṇām 
tad viśiṣṭaphalaṃ nṝṇāṃ sadaivārādhanaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv 
kalau kalimalākrāntā na jānanti hariṃ param 
ye'rcayanti tam īśānaṃ kṛtakṛtyas ta eva hi 
nāsti śreyottamaṃ nṝṇāṃ viṣṇor ārādhanat param  Hbhv 
yuge'smin tamase tasmāt satataṃ harim arcayet 
arcite devadevese śaṅkhacakragadādhare  Hbhv 
arcitaḥ sarvadevāḥ syur yataḥ sarvagato hariḥ 
arcite sarvalokeśe surāsuranamaskṛte 
keśave keśikaṃsaghne na yāti narakaṃ naraḥ  Hbhv 
sakṛd abhyarcito yena helayāpi namaskṛtaḥ 
sa yāti paramaṃ sthānaṃ yat surair api pūjitam  Hbhv 
samastalokanāthasya devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ 
sākṣād bhagavato nityaṃ pūjanaṃ janmanaḥ phalam  Hbhv 
tatraivagre 
asāre khalu saṃsāre sāram etan nirūpitam 
samastalokanāthasya śraddhayārādhanaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca 
yatra viṣṇukathā nityaṃ yatra tiṣṭhanti vaiṣṇavāḥ 
kalibāhyā narās te vai ye'rcayanti sadā harim  Hbhv 
kāśīkhaṇḍe
harer ārādhanaṃ puṃsāṃ kiṃ kiṃ na kurute bata 
putramitrakalatrārthaṃ rājyasvargāpavargadam  Hbhv 
haraty aghaṃ dhvamsayati vyādhīn ādhīn nirasyati 
dharmaṃ vivardhayet kṣipraṃ prayacchanti manoratham  Hbhv 
ata eva skānde dhruvaṃ prati markaṇḍeyasya vacanaṃ 
sakṛd abhyarcito yena devadevo janārdanaḥ 
sa prāpnoti paraṃ sthānaṃ satyam etan mayoditam  Hbhv 
tathāṅgīrasaḥ 
yasyāntaḥ sarvam evedaṃ yasya nānto mahātmanaḥ 
tam ārādhaya govindaṃ sthānam āgryaṃ yad icchasi  Hbhv 
pulastasya 
paraṃ brahma paraṃ dhāma yo 'sau sasvatapūruṣaḥ 
tam ārādhya hariṃ yāti muktim apy atidurlabham  Hbhv 
pulahasya 
aindram indraḥ paraṃ sthānaṃ yam ārādhya jagatpatim 
prāpa yajñapatiṃ viṣṇuṃ tam ārādhaya suvrata  Hbhv 
vasiṣṭhasya 
prāpnoty ārādhite viṣṇau manasā yad yad icchati 
trailokyāntargataṃ sthānaṃ kim u sarvottamottamam  Hbhv 
yan yan kāmayate kāmān nārī vā puruṣo 'pi vā 
tan samāpnoti vipulān samārādhya janārdanam  Hbhv 
agastyasaṃhitāyāṃ 
ārādhyaiva naro viṣṇuṃ manasā yad yad icchati 
phalaṃ prāpnoty avihataṃ bhūri svalpam athāpi vā  Hbhv 
idrsaṃ viṣṇupurane'pi kiṃcid adhikaṃ cedaṃ
śrīmarīceḥ
anārādhitagovindair narair sthānaṃ nṛpātmaja 
na hi samprāpyate śreṣṭhaṃ tasmād ārādhayācyutam  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca tatraiva
bhaumān manorathān svargaṃ svargavandyaṃ tathāspadam 
prāpnoty ārādhite viṣṇau nirvāṇam api cottamam  Hbhv 
tathā brahmavaivarte
yatpādodakam ādhāya śivaḥ śirasi nṛtyati 
yannābhinalinād āsīd brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ  Hbhv 
yadicchāśaktivikṣobhād brahmaṇḍodbhavasaṅkṣayau 
tam ārādhaya govindaṃ sthānam agryaṃ yadīcchasi  Hbhv 
nārasiṃhe markaṇḍeyasahasranikasaṃvāde
yas tu sampūjayen nityaṃ narasiṃha nareśvara 
sa svargamokṣabhāgī syān nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  Hbhv 
tasmād ekamanā bhūtvā yāvajjīvaṃ pratijñayā 
arcanān narasiṃhasya samprāpnoty abhivāñchitam  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrīvyāsaśukasaṃvāde śrīmārkaṇḍeyamṛtyuñjayasaṃvādānantaraṃ
narake pacyamānas tu yamena paribhāṣitaḥ 
kiṃ tvayā nārcito devaḥ keśavaḥ kleśanāśanaḥ  Hbhv 
udakenāpy alābhe tu dravyāṇāṃ pūjitaḥ prabhuḥ 
yo dadāti svakaṃ lokaṃ sa tvayā kiṃ na pūjitaḥ  Hbhv 
narasiṃho hṛṣīkeśaḥ puṇḍarīkanibhekṣaṇaḥ 
smaranān muktido nṛṇāṃ sa tvayā kiṃ na pūjitaḥ  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye'ditimāhātmye śrīsūtoktau
yatra pūjāparo viṣṇos tatra vighno na bādhate 
rājā ca taskaraś cāpi vyādhayaś ca na santi hi  Hbhv 
pretāḥ piśācāḥ kuṣmāṇḍā grahā bālagrahās tathā 
ḍākinyo rākṣasāś caiva na bādhante'cyutarcakam  Hbhv 
tatraiva yamabhagīrathasaṃvāde
patraiḥ puṣpaiḥ phalair vārcya pūjārahitam acyutam 
sa yāti viṣṇusālokyaṃ kulasaptatisaṃyutaḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva dhvajāropaṇamāhātmye śrīviṣṇudūtānām uktau
utkrāntikāle yannāma śrutavanto 'pi vai sakṛt 
labhante paramaṃ sthānaṃ kim u śuśrūṣaṇe rataḥ  Hbhv 
muhūrtaṃ vā muhūrtārdhaṃ yas tiṣṭhed dharimandire 
sa yāti paramaṃ sthānaṃ kim u śuśrūṣaṇe rataḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva vibhāṇḍakamuneḥ sumatinṛpaṃ prati 
avaśenāpi yat karma kṛtaṃ tu sumahat phalam 
dadāti nṝṇāṃ rājendra kiṃ punaḥ samyagarcanā  Hbhv 
prāyaścittaprakāraṇānte 
samparkād yadi vā mohād yas tu pūjayate harim 
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sa yāti paramaṃ padam  Hbhv 
sarvāntarāyā naśyanti manaḥsuddhiś ca jāyate 
paraṃ mokṣaṃ labhec caiva pūjyamāne janārdane  Hbhv 
dharmārthakāmamokṣākhyā puruṣārthāḥ sanātanāḥ 
haripūjāparāṇāṃ tu sidhyante nātra saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
sarvatīrthāni yajñāś ca sāṅgā vedāś ca sattamāḥ 
nārāyaṇarcanasyaite kālaṃ narhanti sodasim  Hbhv 
śrīviṣṇutoṣavidhipraśnottare
satyaṃ vacmi hitaṃ vacmi sāraṃ vacmi punaḥ punaḥ 
asārodagrasaṃsāre sāraṃ yad viṣṇupūjanam  Hbhv 
upalepanamāhātmyante
akāmād api ye viṣṇoḥ sakṛt pūjāṃ prakurvate na teṣām 
bhavabandhas tu kadācid api jāyate  Hbhv 
yajñadhvajopākhyānānte
tasmāt śṛṇuta viprendra devo nārāyaṇo 'vyayaḥ 
jānato 'jānato vāpi pūjakānāṃ vimuktidaḥ  Hbhv 
te vandyās te prapūjyāś ca namaskāryā viśeṣataḥ 
ye'rcayanti mahāviṣṇuṃ prapannārtipraṇāśanam  Hbhv 
ye yajanti spṛhāśūnyā hariṃ vā haram eva vā 
ta eva bhuvanaṃ sarvaṃ punanti vibudharṣabhāḥ  Hbhv 
pādme śrīnārāyaṇanāradasaṃvāde pūjavidhiprasaṅge
madbhakto yo madarcāṃ ca karoti vidhidṛṣṭaye 
tasyāntarāyaḥ svapne'pi na bhavaty abhayo hi saḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva vaiśākhamāhātmye nāradāmbarīṣasaṃvāde
putrān kalatrān dīrghāyū rājyaṃ svargāpavargakam 
sa dadyād īpsitaṃ sarvaṃ bhaktyā sampūjito 'jitaḥ  Hbhv 
narake'pi ciraṃ magnāḥ pūrvajā ye kuladvaye 
tatraiva yānti te svargaṃ yadārceta sūto harim  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrīyamabrahmasaṃvāde
anārādhya hariṃ bhaktyā ko lokān prāpnuyād budhaḥ 
ārādhite harau kāmāḥ sarve karatalasthitāḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare śrīkṛṣṇāmṛtastotre
so 'pi dhanyatamo loke yo 'rcayed acutyaṃ sakṛt 
kiṃ punaḥ śraddhayā yuktaḥ sapuṣpaiḥ prativāsaram  Hbhv 
vaiṣṇavān api ye nityaṃ prapaśyanty arcayanti ca 
te'pi viṣṇupadaṃ yānti kiṃ punar viṣṇusevakāḥ  Hbhv 
sa yogī sa viśuddhātmā sa śāntaḥ sa mahāmatiḥ 
sa śuddhaḥ sa ca sampūrṇaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ seveta yo naraḥ  Hbhv 
agastyasaṃhitāyām
ananyamanasaḥ śaśvad gaṇayanto 'kṣamālayā 
japanto rāmarāmeti sukhāmṛtanidhau manaḥ 
pravilāpyāmṛtībhūya sukhaṃ tiṣṭhanti kecana  Hbhv 
paricaryāparāḥ kecit prāsādādiṣu śerate 
manuṣyam iva taṃ draṣṭuṃ vyavahartuṃ ca bandhuvat  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
yathā vidhiniṣedhau tu muktaṃ naviopasarpataḥ 
tathā na spṛśato rāmopāsakaṃ vidhipūrvakam  Hbhv 
śrībhagavadgītāsu 
evaṃ satatayuktā ye bhaktās tvāṃ paryupāsate 
ye cāpy akṣaram avyaktaṃ teṣāṃ ke yogavittamāḥ  Hbhv 
ity arjunena pṛṣṭaḥ śrībhagavān uvāca 
mayy āveśya mano ye māṃ nityayuktā upāsate 
śraddhayā parayopetās te me yuktatamā matāḥ  Hbhv 
caturthaskandhe BhP 
yatpādasevābhirucis tapasvinām
aśeṣajanmopacitaṃ malaṃ dhiyaḥ 
sadyaḥ kṣiṇoty anvaham edhatī satī
yathā padāṅguṣṭhaviniḥsṛtā sarit  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca nāradoktau BhP 
yathā taror mūlaniṣecanena
tṛpyanti tatskandhabhujopaśākhāḥ 
prāṇopahārāc ca yathendriyāṇāṃ
tathaiva sarvārhaṇam acyutejyā  Hbhv 
ekādaśaskandhe ca kaviyogeśvarasya vākyaṃ BhP 
manye'kutaścidbhayam acyutasya
pādāmbujopāsanam atra nityam 
udvignabuddher asadātmabhāvād
viśvātmanā yatra nivartate bhīḥ  Hbhv 
śrībhagavataś ca BhP 
evaṃ kriyāyogapathaiḥ pumān vaidikatāntrikaiḥ 
arcann ubhayataḥ siddhiṃ matto vindaty abhīpsitām  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca BhP 
mām eva nairapekṣyeṇa bhaktiyogena vindati 
bhaktiyogaṃ sa labhata evaṃ yaḥ pūjayeta mām  Hbhv 
gautamīyatantre śrīnāradasya
tulasīdalamātreṇa jalasya culukena ca 
vikrīṇīte svam ātmānaṃ bhaktebhyo bhaktavatsalaḥ  Hbhv 
atha pūjānityatā
mahābhārate
mātṛvat parirakṣantaṃ sṛṣṭisaṃhārakārakam 
yo nārcayati deveśaṃ taṃ vidyād brahmaghātakam  Hbhv 
ata evoktaṃ bṛhannāradīye pādodakamāhātmyākhyānārambhe
haripūjāvidhānaṃ tu yasya veśmani no dvijaḥ 
śmaśānasadṛśaṃ vidyān na kadāpi viśec ca tat  Hbhv 
ata evoktaṃ viṣṇudharmottare 
puṣpair vā yadi vā patraih phalair vā yadi vāmbubhiḥ 
yaṣṭavyaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣas tyaktvā kāryaśatāni ca  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca nāradīye
nimitteṣu ca sarveṣu tattatkālaviśeṣataḥ 
pūjayed devadeveśaṃ dravyaṃ sampādya yatnataḥ  Hbhv 
ata evoktaṃ bhagavatā hāyagrīveṇa hāyaśīrṣapañcarātre
pratiṣṭhitārcā na tyājyā yāvajjīvaṃ samarcayet 
varaṃ prāṇasya vā tyāgaḥ śiraso vāpi karttanam  Hbhv 
pūjayā nityatālekhi prāk ca naivedyabhakṣaṇe 
māhātmyaṃ ca paraṃ śālagrāmacakraprasaṅgataḥ  Hbhv 
pūjāṅgānāṃ ca māhātmyaṃ yad yad vilikhitaṃ purā 
tat sarvam iha pūjāyāṃ paryavasyati hi svataḥ  Hbhv 
pūjāmahimamattebhāh śāstrāraṇyavihāriṇaḥ 
kīṭena kati saṅgrāhyāḥ prabhāvam śrīharer vinā  Hbhv 
atha śrībhagavannāma sadā seveta sarvataḥ 
tanmāhātmyaṃ ca vikhyātaṃ saṅkṣepenātra likhyate  Hbhv 
atha śrībhagavannāmamāhātmyam
tatra śrībhagavannāmaviśeṣasya ca sevanam 
ṛṣibhiḥ kṛpayādiṣṭaṃ tattatkāmahatātmanām  Hbhv 
atha kāmaviśeṣeṇa śrībhagavannāmaviśeṣasevāmāhātmyam
tatra pāpakṣayārthaṃ
śrīkaurme
śrīśabdapūrvaṃ jayaśabdamadhyaṃ
jayadvayād uttaratas tathā hi 
triḥsaptakṛtvo narasiṃhanāma
japtaṃ nihanyād api viprahatyām  Hbhv 
mahābhayanivaranartham
tatraiva
śrīpūrvo narasiṃho dvir jayād uttaratas tu saḥ 
triḥsaptakṛtvo japato mahābhayanivāraṇaḥ  Hbhv 
kālaviśeṣe tu maṅgalārthaṃ
viṣṇudharmottare mārkaṇḍeyavajrasaṃvāde
puruṣaṃ vāsudevaṃ ca tathā saṅkarṣaṇaṃ vibhum 
pradyumnam aniruddhaṃ ca kramād abdeṣu kīrtayet  Hbhv 
balabhadraṃ tathā kṛṣṇaṃ kīrtayed ayanadvaye 
madhavaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ tathā vai bhogasayinam  Hbhv 
padmanābhaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ tathā devaṃ trivikramam 
kramena rajasardula vasantadisu kīrtayet  Hbhv 
viṣṇuṃ ca madhuhantāraṃ tathā devaṃ trivikramam 
vāmanaṃ śrīdharaṃ caiva hṛṣīkeśaṃ tathāiva ca  Hbhv 
dāmodaraṃ padmanābhaṃ keśavaṃ ca yadūttamam 
nārāyaṇaṃ mādhavaṃ ca govindaṃ ca tathā kramāt  Hbhv 
caitrādiṣu ca māseṣu devadevam anusmaret 
pradyumnam aniruddhaṃ ca pakṣayoḥ kṛṣṇaśuklayoḥ  Hbhv 
sarvaḥ śarvaḥ sivaḥ sthāṇur bhūtādir nidhir avyayaḥ 
adityādiṣu vareṣu kramād evam anusmaret  Hbhv 
viśvaṃ viṣṇur vaṣaṭkāro bhūtabhavyabhavatprabhuḥ 
bhūtabhṛd bhūtakṛd bhavo bhūtātmā bhūtabhavanaḥ  Hbhv 
avyaktaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣo visvakarma sucisravaḥ 
sadbhavo bhavano bharta prabhavaḥ prabhur isvaraḥ  Hbhv 
aprameyo hṛṣīkeśah padmanabho 'maraprabhuḥ 
agrahyaḥ sasvato dhata kṛṣṇaś caitany anusmaret 
devadevasya nāmāni kṛttikadisu yadava  Hbhv 
brahmāṇaṃ śrīpatiṃ viṣṇuṃ kapilaṃ śrīdharaṃ prabhum 
dāmodaraṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ govindaṃ madhusūdanam  Hbhv 
bhūdharaṃ gadinaṃ devaṃ saṅkhinaṃ padminaṃ tathā 
cakriṇaṃ ca mahārāja prathamādiṣu saṃsmaret  Hbhv 
sarvaṃ vā sarvadā nāma devadevasya yādava  Hbhv 
nāmāni sarvāṇi janārdanasya
kālaś ca sarvaḥ puruṣapravīrāḥ 
tasmāt sadā sarvagatasya nāma
grāhyaṃ yatheṣṭaṃ varadasya rājan  Hbhv 
vividhakāmasiddhaye ca
pulastyoktau
kāmaḥ kāmapradaḥ kāntaḥ kāmapālas tathā hariḥ 
ānando mādhavaś caiva kāmasaṃsiddhaye japet  Hbhv 
rāmaḥ paraśurāmaś ca nṛsiṃho viṣṇur eva ca 
vikramaś caivam ādīni japyāny arijigīṣubhiḥ  Hbhv 
vidyām abhyastatā nityaṃ japtavyaḥ puruṣottamaḥ 
dāmodaraṃ bandhagato nityam eva japen naraḥ  Hbhv 
keśavaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣam aniśaṃ hi tathā japet 
netrabādhāsu sarvāsu hṛṣīkeśaṃ bhayeṣu ca  Hbhv 
acyutaṃ cāmṛtaṃ caiva japed auṣadhakarmāṇi 
saṅgrāmābhimukho gacchan saṃsmared aparājitam  Hbhv 
cakriṇaṃ gadinaṃ caiva śārṅgiṇaṃ khaḍginaṃ tathā 
kṣemārthī pravasan nityaṃ dikṣu pracyādiṣu smaret  Hbhv 
ajitaṃ cādhipaṃ caiva sarvaṃ sarveśvaraṃ tathā 
saṃsmaret puruṣo bhaktyā vyavahāreṣu sarvadā  Hbhv 
nārāyaṇaṃ sarvakālaṃ kṣutapraskhalanādiṣu 
grahanakṣatrapīḍāsu devabādhāsu sarvataḥ  Hbhv 
dasyuvairinirodheṣu vyāghrasiṃhādisaṅkaṭe 
andhākāre tamastīvre narasiṃham anusmaret  Hbhv 
agnidāhe samutpanne saṃsmarej jalaśāyinam 
garuḍadhvajānusmaranād viṣavīryaṃ vyapohati  Hbhv 
snāne devārcane home praṇipāte pradakṣine 
kīrtayed bhagavannāma vāsudeveti tatparaḥ  Hbhv 
sthāpane vittadhānyāder apadhyāne ca duṣṭaje 
kurvīta tanmanā bhūtvā anantācyutakīrtanam  Hbhv 
nārāyaṇam śārṅgadharaṃ śrīdharaṃ puruṣottamam 
vāmanaṃ khaḍginaṃ caiva duṣṭasvapne sadā smaret  Hbhv 
mahārṇavādau paryaṅkaśāyinaṃ ca naraḥ smaret 
balabhadraṃ samṛddhyarthaṃ sarvakarmāṇi saṃsmaret  Hbhv 
jagatpatim apatyārthaṃ stuvān bhaktyā na sīdati 
śrīśaṃ sarvābhyudayike karmany āśu prakīrtayet  Hbhv 
ariṣṭeṣu hy aśeṣeṣu viśokaṃ ca sadā japet 
maruprapātāgnijalabandhanādiṣu mṛtyuṣu 
svatantraparatantreṣu vāsudevaṃ japed budhaḥ  Hbhv 
sarvārthaśaktiyuktasya devadevasya cakriṇaḥ 
yathābhirocate nāma tat sarvārtheṣu kīrtayet  Hbhv 
sarvārthasiddhim āpnoti nāmnām ekārthatā yathā 
sarvāṇy etāni nāmāni parasya brahmaṇo hareḥ  Hbhv 
evaṃ viṣṇudharmottare ca mārkaṇḍeyavajrasaṃvāde kiṃ ca
kūrmaṃ varāhaṃ matsyaṃ vā jalaprataraṇe smaret 
bhrājiṣṇum agnijanane japen nāma tv akhaṇḍitam  Hbhv 
garuḍadhvajānusmaraṇād āpado mucyate naraḥ 
jvarajuṣṭaśirorogaviṣavīryaṃ ca śamyati  Hbhv 
balabhadraṃ tu yuddhārthī kṛśyārambhe halāyudham 
uttarānāṃ vāṇijyārthī rāmam abhyudaye nṛpa  Hbhv 
maṅgalyaṃ maṅgalaṃ viṣṇum maṅgalyeṣu ca kīrtayet 
uttiṣṭhan kīrtayed viṣṇum prasvapan madhavaṃ naraḥ 
bhojane caiva govindaṃ sarvatra madhusūdanam  Hbhv 
tatraivānyatra
auṣadhe cintayed viṣṇum bhojane ca janārdanam 
śayane padmanābhaṃ ca maithune ca prajāpatim  Hbhv 
saṅgrāme cakriṇaṃ kruddham sthānabhraṃśe trivikramam 
nārāyaṇaṃ vṛṣotsarge śrīdharaṃ priyasaṅgame 
jalamadhye ca vārāhaṃ pāvake jalaśāyinam  Hbhv 
kānane narasiṃhaṃ ca parvate raghunandanam 
duḥsvapne smara govindaṃ viśuddhau madhusūdanam 
māyāsu vāmanaṃ devaṃ sarvakāryeṣu mādhavam  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
kīrtayed vāsudevaṃ ca anukteṣv api yādava 
kāryārambhe tathā rājan yatheṣṭaṃ nāma kīrtayet  Hbhv 
sarvāṇi nāmāni hi tasya rājan
sarvārthasiddhyai tu bhavanti pumsaḥ 
tasmād yatheṣṭaṃ khalu kṛṣṇanāma
sarveṣu kāryeṣu japeta bhaktyā  Hbhv 
tatrākhilapāponmūlanatvam
atha sāmānyataḥ śrībhagavannāmakīrtanamāhātmyam
viṣṇudharme haribhaktisudhodaye coktaṃ nāradena
aho sunirmala yūyam rāgo hi harikīrtane 
avidhūya tamaḥ kṛtsnaṃ nṛṇām udeti sūryavat  Hbhv 
garude
pāpānalasya dīptasya mā kurvantu bhayaṃ narāḥ 
govindanāmameghaughair naśyate nīrabindubhiḥ  Hbhv 
avaśenāpi yannāmni kīrtane sarvapātakaiḥ 
pumān vimucyate sadyaḥ siṃhatrastair mṛgair iva  Hbhv 
yannāmakīrtanaṃ bhaktyā vilāpanam anuttamam 
maitreyāśeṣapāpānāṃ dhātūnām iva pāvakaḥ  Hbhv 
yasmin nyastamatir na yāti narakaṃ svargo 'pi yaccintane
vighno yatra niveśitātmamanaso brāhmo 'pi loko 'lpakaḥ 
muktiṃ cetasi yaḥ sthito 'maladhiyāṃ puṃsāṃ dadāty avyayaḥ
kiṃ citraṃ yadaghaṃ prayāti vilayaṃ tatrācyute kīrtite  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare 
sāyaṃ prātas tathā kṛtvā devadevasya kīrtanam 
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ svargaloke mahīyate  Hbhv 
vāmane
nārāyaṇo nāma naro narāṇāṃ
prasiddhacauraḥ kathitaḥ pṛthivyām 
anekajanmārjitapāpasañcayam
haraty aśeṣaṃ śrutamātra eva  Hbhv 
skānde
govindeti tathā proktaṃ bhaktyā vā bhaktivarjitaiḥ 
dahate sarvapāpāni yugāntāgnir ivotthitaḥ  Hbhv 
govindanāmnā yaḥ kaścin naro bhavati bhūtale 
kīrtanād eva tasyāpi pāpaṃ yāti sahasradhā  Hbhv 
kāśīkhaṇḍe
pramādād api saṃspṛṣṭo yathānalakaṇo dahet 
tathauṣṭhapuṭasaṃspṛṣṭaṃ harināma dahed agham  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye lubdhakopakhyānānte
narāṇāṃ viṣayāndhānām mamatākulacetasām 
ekam eva harer nāma sarvapāpavināśanam  Hbhv 
ata eva tatraiva yamenoktam
hari hari sakṛd uccāritam
dasyucchalena yair manuṣyaiḥ 
jananījaṭharamārgaluptā
na mama paṭalipiṃ viśanti martyāḥ  Hbhv 
pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye devaśarmopākhyānānte śrīnāradoktau
hatyāyutaṃ pānasahasram ugram
gurvaṅganākoṭiniṣevanaṃ ca 
steyāny anekāni haripriyeṇa
govindanāmnā nihatāni sadyaḥ  Hbhv 
anicchayāpi dahati spṛṣṭo hutavaho yathā 
tathā dahati govindanāma vyājād apīritam  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrīyamabrāhmaṇasaṃvāde
kīrtanād eva kṛṣṇasya viṣṇor amitatejasaḥ 
duritāni vilīyante tamāṃsīva dinodaye  Hbhv 
nānyat paśyāmi jantūnām vihāya karikīrtanam 
sarvapāpapraśamanam prāyaścittam dvijottama  Hbhv 
ṣaṣṭhaskandhe BhP 
ayaṃ hi kṛtanirveśo janmakoṭyaṃhasām api 
yad vyājahāra vivaśo nāma svastyayanaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv 
stenaḥ surāpo mitradhrug brahmahā gurutalpagaḥ 
strīrājapitṛgohantā ye ca pātakino 'pare  Hbhv 
sarveṣām apy aghavatām idam eva suniṣkṛtam 
nāmavyāharaṇaṃ viṣṇor yatas tadviṣayā matiḥ  Hbhv 
na niṣkṛtair uditair brahmavādibhis
tathā viśuddhyaty aghavān vratādibhiḥ 
yathā harer nāmapadair udāhṛtais
tad uttamaślokaguṇopalambhakam  Hbhv 
BhP 
sāṅketyaṃ pārihāsyaṃ vā stobhaṃ helanam eva vā 
vaikuṇṭhanāmagrahaṇam aśeṣāghaharaṃ viduḥ  Hbhv 
patitaḥ skhalito bhagnaḥ sandaṣṭas tapta āhataḥ 
harir ity avaśenāha pumān nārhati yātanāḥ  Hbhv 
BhP 
ajñānād athavā jñānād uttamaślokanāma yat 
saṅkīrtitam aghaṃ puṃso dahed edho yathānalaḥ  Hbhv 
BhP 
brahmahā pitṛhā goghno mātṛhācāryahāghavān 
śvādaḥ pulkasako vāpi śuddhyeran yasya kīrtanāt  Hbhv 
laghubhāgavate
vartamānaṃ tu yat pāpaṃ yad bhūtaṃ yad bhaviṣyati 
tat sarvaṃ nirdahaty āśu govindānalakīrtanāt  Hbhv 
sadā drohaparo yas tu sajjanānāṃ mahītale 
jāyate pāvano dhanyo harer nāmānukīrtanāt  Hbhv 
kaurme
vasanti yāni koṭis tu pāvanāni mahītale 
na tāni tattulāṃ yānti kṛṣṇanāmānukīrtane  Hbhv 
bṛhadviṣṇupurāṇe 
nāmno 'sya yāvatī śaktiḥ pāpanirharaṇe hareḥ 
tāvat kartuṃ na śaknoti pātakaṃ pātakī janaḥ  Hbhv 
itihāsottame
svādo 'pi na hi śaknoti kartuṃ pāpāni yatnataḥ 
tāvantī yāvatī śaktir viṣṇor nāmno 'subhakṣaye  Hbhv 
viśeṣataḥ kalau skānde
tan nāsti karmajaṃ loke vāgjaṃ mānasam eva vā 
yan na kṣapayate pāpaṃ kalau govindakīrtanam  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare 
śamāyālaṃ jalaṃ vahnes tamaso bhaskarodayaḥ 
śāntyai kaler aghaughasya nāmasaṅkīrtanaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv 
nāmnāṃ hareḥ kīrtanataḥ prayāti
saṃsārapāraṃ duritaughamuktaḥ 
naraḥ sa satyaṃ kalidoṣajanma
pāpaṃ nihaty āśu kim atra citram  Hbhv 
brahmāṇḍapurāṇe
varākacāndrāyaṇataptakṛcchrair
na dehiśuddhir bhavatīha tādṛk 
kalau sakṛn mādhavakīrtanena
govindanāmnā bhavatīha yādṛk  Hbhv 
kīrtanakartrkulasaṅgyādipavanatvaṃ
tatraiva
mahāpātakayukto 'pi kīrtayenn aniśaṃ harim 
śuddhāntaḥkaraṇo bhūtvā jāyate paṅktipāvanaḥ  Hbhv 
laghubhāgavate
govindeti mudā yuktaḥ kīrtayed yas tv ananyadhīḥ 
pāvanena ca dhanyena teneyaṃ pṛthivī dhṛtā  Hbhv 
haribhaktisudhodaye
na caivam ekaṃ vaktāraṃ jihvā rakṣati vaiṣṇavī 
āśrāvya bhagavatkhyātiṃ jagat kṛtsnaṃ punāti hi  Hbhv 
daśamaskandhe  
yannāma gṛhṇann akhilan śrotṝn ātmānam eva ca 
sadyaḥ punāti kiṃ bhūyas tasya spṛṣṭaḥ padā hi te  Hbhv 
ata evoktaṃ prahlādena nārasiṃhe
te santaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ nirupādhikabāndhavāḥ 
ye nṛsiṃha bhavannāma gāyanty uccair mudānvitāḥ  Hbhv 
sarvavyadhinasitvaṃ
bṛhannāradīye bhagavattoṣaprasaṅge
acyutānandagovindanāmoccaraṇabhīṣitaḥ 
naśyanti sakalā rogāḥ satyaṃ satyaṃ vadāmy aham  Hbhv 
parāśarasaṃhitāyāṃ sāmbaṃ prati vyāsoktau
na sāmba vyādhijaṃ duḥkhaṃ heyaṃ nānyauṣadhair api 
harināmauṣadhaṃ pītvā vyādhis tyājyo na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
skānde
ādhayo vyādhayo yasya smaraṇān nāmakīrtanāt 
tadaiva vilayaṃ yānti tam anantaṃ namāmy aham  Hbhv 
vahnipurāṇe
mahāvyādhisamācchanno rājavadhopāpiditaḥ 
nārāyaṇeti saṅkīrtya nirāṭaṅko bhaven naraḥ  Hbhv 
sarvaduḥkhopaśamanatvam
brhadviṣṇupurāṇe
sarvarogopaśamanaṃ sarvopadravanāśanam 
śāntidaṃ sarvāriṣṭānāṃ harer nāmānukīrtanam  Hbhv 
brahmavaivarte
sarvapāpapraśamanaṃ sarvopadravanāśanam 
sarvaduḥkhakṣayakāraṃ harināmānukīrtanam  Hbhv 
dvādaśaskandhe 
saṅkīrtyamāno bhagavān anantaḥ
śrutanubhāvo vyasanaṃ hi puṃsām 
praviśya cittaṃ vidhunoty aśeṣaṃ
yathā tamo 'rko 'bhram ivātivātaḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare
ārtā viṣaṇṇāḥ śithilāś ca bhītā
ghoreṣu ca vyādhiṣu vartamānāḥ 
saṅkīrtya nārāyaṇaśabdam ekaṃ
vimuktaduḥkhāḥ sukhino bhavanti  Hbhv 
kīrtanad devadevasya viṣṇor amitatejasaḥ 
yakṣarakṣasavetalabhūtapretavinayakaḥ  Hbhv 
dakinyo vidravanti sma ye tathānye ca siṃhakaḥ 
sarvānarthaharaṃ tasya nāmasaṅkīrtanaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
nāmasaṅkīrtanaṃ kṛtvā kṣuṭtṛṭpraskhalitādiṣu 
viyogaṃ śīghram āpnoti sarvānarthair na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
pādme devahutistutau
mohanalollasajjvālajvalallokeṣu sarvadā 
yannāmāmbhodharacchāyāṃ praviṣṭo naiva dahyate  Hbhv 
kalibadhapaharitvam
skānde
kalikalakusarpasya tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrasya mā bhayam 
govindanāmadāvena dagdho yāsyati bhasmatām  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye kalidharmaprasaṅge
harināmaparā ye ca ghore kaliyuge narāḥ 
ta eva kṛtakṛtyāś ca na kalir bādhate hi tān  Hbhv 
hare keśava govinda vāsudeva jaganmaya 
itīrayanti te nityaṃ na hi tān bādhate kaliḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare
ye'harniśaṃ jagaddhātur vāsudevasya kīrtanam 
kurvanti tān naravyāghra na kalir bādhate narān  Hbhv 
nārakyuddhārakatvam
nārasiṃhe
yathā yathā harer nāma kīrtayanti sma nārakāḥ 
tathā tathā harau bhaktim udvahanto divaṃ yayuḥ  Hbhv 
itihāsottame
narake pacyamānānāṃ narāṇāṃ pāpakarmaṇām 
muktiḥ sañjāyate tasmān nāmasaṅkīrtanād dhareḥ  Hbhv 
prārabdhavināśitvam
ṣaṣṭhaskandhe 
nātaḥ paraṃ karmanibandhakṛntanaṃ
mumukṣatāṃ tīrthapadānukīrtanāt 
na yat punaḥ karmasu sajjate mano
rajastamobhyāṃ kalilaṃ tato 'nyathā  Hbhv 
dvādaśe  ca
yannāmadheyaṃ mriyamāṇa āturaḥ
patan skhalan vā vivaśo gṛṇan pumān 
vimuktakarmārgala uttamāṃ gatiṃ
prāpnoti yakṣyanti na taṃ kalau janāḥ  Hbhv 
uktya karmanibandheti tathā karmārgaleti ca 
avaśyabhogyatāpatteḥ prārabdhe paryavasyati  Hbhv 
ata eva bṛhannāradīye
govindeti japan jantuḥ pratyahaṃ niyatendriyaḥ 
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ suravad bhāsate naraḥ  Hbhv 
sarvapārādhabhajanatvam
viṣṇuyāmale śrībhagavaduktau
mama nāmāni loke'smin śraddhayā yas tu kīrtayet 
tasyāparādhakoṭis tu kṣamāmy eva na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
sarvasampūrtikāritvam
aṣṭamaskandhe 
śrībhagavantaṃ prati śrīśukroktau
mantratas tantrataś chidraṃ deśakālārhavastutaḥ 
sarvaṃ karoti niśchidram anusaṅkīrtanaṃ tava  Hbhv 
skānde ca
yasya smṛtyā ca nāmoktyā tapoyajñakriyādiṣu 
nyūnaṃ sampūrṇatām eti sadyo vande tam acyutam  Hbhv 
sarvavedādhikatvam
viṣṇudharmottare śrīprahlādoktau
rgvedo hi yajurvedaḥ sāmavedo 'py atharvaṇaḥ 
adhītas tena yenoktaṃ harir ity akṣaradvayam  Hbhv 
skānde śrīparvatyuktau
mā ṛco mā yajus tāta mā sāma paṭha kiṃcana 
govindeti harer nāma geyaṃ gāyasva nityaśaḥ  Hbhv 
pādme ca śrīrāmāṣṭottaraśatanāmastotre
viṣṇor ekaikanāmāpi sarvavedādhikaṃ matam 
tadṛṅnāmasahasreṇa rāmanāma samaṃ smṛtam  Hbhv 
sarvatīrthādhikatvam
skānde
kurukṣetreṇa kiṃ tasya kiṃ kasya puskareṇa vā 
jihvāgre vasate yasya harir ity akṣaradvayam  Hbhv 
vāmane
tīrthakoṭisahasrāṇi tīrthakoṭiśatāni ca 
tani sarvāṇy avāpnoti viṣṇor nāmānukīrtanāt  Hbhv 
viśvāmitrasaṃhitāyām
viśrutāṇi bahūny eva tīrthāni bahudhāni ca 
kotyaṃśenāpi tulyāni nāmakīrtanato hareḥ  Hbhv 
laghubhāgavate
kiṃ tata vedāgamaśāstravistarais
tīrthair anekair api kiṃ prayojanam 
yady ātmano vāñchasi muktikāraṇaṃ
govinda govinda iti sphutaṃ raṭa  Hbhv 
sarvasatkarmādhikatvam
gokoṭidānaṃ grahaṇe khagasya
prayāgagaṅgodakakalpavāsaḥ 
yajñāyutaṃ merusuvarṇadānaṃ
govindakīrter na samaṃ śatāṃśaiḥ  Hbhv 
baudhayanasaṃhitāyām
iṣṭapūrtāni karmāṇi subahūni kṛtāny api 
bhavahetūni tāny eva harer nāma tu muktidam  Hbhv 
gāruḍe śrīśaunakāmbarīṣasaṃvāde
vājapeyasahasrāṇāṃ nityaṃ phalam abhīpsasi 
prātar utthāya bhūpāla kuru govindakīrtanam  Hbhv 
kiṃ kariṣyati sāṅkhyena kiṃ yogair naranāyaka 
muktim icchasi rājendra kuru govindakīrtanam  Hbhv 
tṛtīyaskandhe 
śrīkapiladevaṃ prati devahūtyuktau
aho bata śvapaco 'to garīyān
yajjihvāgre vartate nāma tubhyam 
tepus tapas te juhuvur sasnur aryā
brahmānūcur nāma gṛhṇanti ye te  Hbhv 
sarvatīrthapradatvaṃ
skānde brahmanāradasaṃvāde caturmāsyamāhātmye
etat sadvargaharaṇaṃ ripunigrahaṇaṃ param 
adhyātmamūlam etad dhi viṣṇor nāmānukīrtanam  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare 
hṛdi kṛtvā tathā kāmam abhīṣṭaṃ dvijapuṅgavaḥ 
ekaṃ nāma japed yas tu śataṃ kāmān avāpnuyāt  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrīkṛṣṇāmṛtastotre
sarvamaṅgalamaṅgalyam āyuṣyaṃ vyādhināśanam 
bhuktimuktipradaṃ divyaṃ vāsudevasya kīrtanam  Hbhv 
śrīnārāyaṇavyūhastave
parihāsopahāsādyair viṣṇor gṛhṇanti nāma te 
kṛtārthās te'pi manujās tebhyo 'pīha namo namaḥ  Hbhv 
vārāhe ca
te dhanyās te kṛtārthāś ca tair eva sukṛtaṃ kṛtam 
tair āptaṃ janmanaḥ prāpyaṃ ye kāle kīrtayanti mām  Hbhv 
viśeṣataḥ kalau
sakṛd uccārayanty etad durlabhaṃ cākṛtātmanām 
kalau yuge harer nāma te kṛtārthā na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
ekādaśaskandhe  ca
kaliṃ sabhājayanty āryā guṇajāḥ sārabhāginaḥ 
yatra saṅkīrtanenaiva sarvaḥ svartho 'bhilabhyate  Hbhv 
skānde tatraiva
tathā caivottamaṃ loke tapaḥ śrīharikīrtanam 
kalau yuge viśeṣeṇa viṣṇuprītyai samācaret  Hbhv 
sarvaśaktimattvam
yathā skānde
dānavratatapastīrthayātrādīnāṃ ca yāḥ sthitāḥ 
śaktayo devamahatāṃ sarvapāpaharāḥ śubhāḥ  Hbhv 
rājasūyāśvamedhānāṃ jñānasyādhyātmavastunaḥ 
ākṛṣya hariṇā sarvāḥ sthāpitāḥ sveṣu nāmasu  Hbhv 
vāto 'py ato harer nāmna ugrāṇām api duḥsahaḥ 
sarveṣāṃ pāparāśīnāṃ yathaiva tamasāṃ raviḥ  Hbhv 
ataiva brahmāṇḍe
sarvārthaśaktiyuktasya devadevasya cakriṇaḥ 
yac cābhirucitaṃ nāma tat sarvārtheṣu yojayet  Hbhv 
jagadānandakatvam
śrīmadbhagavadgītāsu 
sthāne hṛṣīkeśa tava prakīrtyā
jagat prahṛṣyaty anurajyate ca 
rakṣāṃsi bhītāni diśo dravanti
sarve namasyanti ca siddhasaṃghāḥ  Hbhv 
jagadvandyatāpādakatvam
bṛhannāradīye
nārāyaṇa jagannātha vāsudeva janārdana 
itīrayanti ye nityaṃ te vai sarvatra vanditāḥ  Hbhv 
śrīsūtenoktaṃ tatraiva yajñadhvajopākhyānānte
svapan bhuñjan vrajaṃs tiṣṭhaṃś ca vadaṃs tathā 
ye vadanti harer nāma tebhyo nityaṃ namo namaḥ  Hbhv 
śrīnārāyaṇavyūhastave
strī śūdraḥ pukkaśo vāpi ye cānye pāpayonayaḥ 
kīrtayanti hariṃ bhaktyā tebhyo 'pīha namo namaḥ  Hbhv 
agatyekagatitvam
pādme bṛhatsahasranāmakathanārambhe
ananyagatayo martyā bhogino 'pi parantapāḥ 
jñānavairāgyarahitā brahmacaryādivarjitāḥ  Hbhv 
sarvadharmojjhitā viṣṇor nāmamātraikajalpakāḥ 
sukhena yāṃ gatiṃ yānti na tāṃ sarve'pi dhārmikāḥ  Hbhv 
sadā sarvatra sevyatvam
viṣṇudharme kṣatrabandhūpākhyāne
na deśaniyamas tasmin na kālaniyamas tathā 
nocchiṣṭhādau niṣedho 'sti śrīharer nāmni lubdhaka  Hbhv 
skānde pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye
viṣṇudharmottare ca
cakrāyudhasya nāmāni sadā sarvatra kīrtayet 
nāśaucaṃ kīrtane tasya sa pavitrakaro yataḥ  Hbhv 
punaḥ skandhe
na deśakālāvasthāsu śuddhyādikam apekṣate 
kintu svatantram evaitan nāma kāmitakāmadam  Hbhv 
vaiśvānarasaṃhitāyām
na deśakālaniyamo na śaucāśaucanirṇayaḥ 
paraṃ saṅkīrtanād eva rāma rāmeti mucyate  Hbhv 
vaiṣṇavacintāmaṇau śrīyudhiṣṭhiraṃ prati śrīnāradavākyaṃ
na deśaniyamo rājan na kālaniyamas tathā 
vidyate nātra sandeho viṣṇor nāmānukīrtane  Hbhv 
kālo 'sti dāne yajñe ca sthāne kālo 'sti sajjape 
viṣṇusaṅkīrtane kālo nāsty atra pṛthivītale  Hbhv 
dvitīyaskandhe BhP 
etan nirvidyamānānām icchatām akutobhayam 
yogināṃ nṛpa nirṇītaṃ harer nāmānukīrtanam  Hbhv 
muktipradatvam
vārāhe
nārāyaṇācyutānanta vāsudeveti yo naraḥ 
satataṃ kīrtayed bhūmi yāti mallayatāṃ sa hi  Hbhv 
gāruḍe
kiṃ kariṣyati sāṅkhyena kiṃ yogair naranāyaka 
muktim icchasi rājendra kuru govindakīrtanam  Hbhv 
yathā padmapurāṇe uttarakhaṇḍe
sakṛd uccāritaṃ yena harir ity akṣaradvayam 
baddhaḥ parikaras tena mokṣāya gamanaṃ prati  Hbhv 
brahmapurāṇe
apy anyacitto 'śuddho vā yaḥ sadā kīrtayed dharim 
so 'pi doṣakṣayān muktiṃ labhec cedipatir yathā  Hbhv 
pādme devahūtistutau
sakṛd uccārayed yas tu nārāyaṇam atandritaḥ 
śuddhāntaḥkaraṇo bhūtvā virvāṇam adhigacchati  Hbhv 
mātsye
paradārarato vāpi parāpakṛtikārakaḥ 
sa śuddho muktim āpnoti harer nāmānukīrtanāt  Hbhv 
vaiśampāyanasaṃhitāyām
sarvadharmabahirbhūtaḥ sarvapāparatas tathā 
mucyate nātra sandeho viṣṇor nāmānukīrtanāt  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye 
yathā kathañcit yan nāsti kīrtite vā śrute'pi vā 
pāpino 'pi viśuddhāḥ syuḥ śuddhā mokṣam avāpnuyuḥ  Hbhv 
bhāratavibhāge
prāṇaprayāṇapātheyaṃ saṃsāravyādhibheṣajam 
duḥkhaśokaparitrāṇaṃ harir ity akṣaradvayam  Hbhv 
nāradīye
navyaṃ navyaṃ nāmadheyaṃ murārer
yad yac caitad geyapīyūṣapuṣṭam 
ye gāyanti tyaktalajjāḥ saharṣaṃ
jīvanmuktāḥ saṃśayo nāsti tatra  Hbhv 
prathamaskandhe BhP 
āpannaḥ saṃsṛtiṃ ghorāṃ yannāma vivaśo gṛṇan 
tataḥ sadyo vimucyeta yad bibheti svayaṃ bhayam  Hbhv 
tṛtīye BhP  brahmastutau
yasyāvatāraguṇakarmaviḍambanāni
nāmāni ye'suvigame vivaśā gṛṇanti 
te'naikajanmaśamalaṃ sahasaiva hitvā
saṃyānty apāvṛtāmṛtaṃ tam ajaṃ prapadye  Hbhv 
ṣaṣṭhe BhP 
etāvatālam aghanirharaṇāya puṃsāṃ
saṅkīrtanaṃ bhagavato guṇakarmanāmnām 
vikruśya putram aghavān yad ajāmilo 'pi
nārāyaṇeti mriyamāṇa iyāya muktim  Hbhv 
śrīvaikuṇṭhalokaprāpakatvam
uktaṃ ca laiṅge śrīnāradaṃ prati śrīśivena
vrajaṃs tiṣṭhan svapann aśnan śvasan vākyaprapūraṇe 
nāmasaṅkīrtanaṃ viṣṇor helayā kalimardanam 
kṛtvā svarūpatāṃ yāti bhaktiyuktaṃ paraṃ vrajet  Hbhv 
nāradīye śrībrahmaṇā
brāhmaṇaḥ śvapacīṃ bhuñjan viśeṣeṇa rajasvalām 
aśnāti surayā pakvaṃ maraṇe harim uccaran  Hbhv 
abhakṣyāgamyayor jātaṃ vihāyāghaughasañcayam 
prayāti viṣṇusālokyaṃ vimukto bhavabandhanaiḥ  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye  śukraṃ prati śrībalinā
jihvāgre vartate yasya harir ity akṣaradvayam 
viṣṇor lokam avāpnoti punar āvṛttidurlabham  Hbhv 
pādme
yatra tatra sthito vāpi kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇeti kīrtayet 
sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā sa gacchet paramāṃ gatim  Hbhv 
tatraiva vaiśākhamāhātmye ambarīṣaṃ prati nāradena
tad eva puṇyaṃ paramaṃ pavitraṃ
govindagehe gamanāya patram 
tad eva loke sukṛtaikasatraṃ
yad ucyate keśavanāmamātram  Hbhv 
brahmavaivarte
evaṃ saṅgrahaṇīputrābhidhānavyājato harim 
samuccāryāntakāle'gād dhāma tat paramaṃ hareḥ  Hbhv 
nārāyaṇam iti vyājād uccārya kaluṣāśrayaḥ 
ajāmilo 'py agād dhāma kim uta śraddhayā gṛṇan  Hbhv 
ṣaṣṭhaskandhe BhP 
mriyamāṇo harer nāma gṛṇan putropacāritam 
ajāmilo 'py agād dhāma kim uta śraddhayā gṛṇan  Hbhv 
vāmane 
ye kīrtayanti varadaṃ varapadmanābhaṃ
śaṅkhābjacakraśaracāpagadāsihastam 
padmālayāvadanapaṅkajaṣaṭpadākṣaṃ
nūnaṃ prayānti sadanaṃ madhughātinas te  Hbhv 
āṅgirasapurāṇe
vāsudeveti manuja uccārya bhavabhītitaḥ 
tanmuktaḥ padam āpnoti viṣṇor eva na saṃśayaḥ  Hbhv 
nandipurāṇe
sarvadā sarvakāleṣu ye'pi kurvanti pātakam 
nāmasaṅkīrtanaṃ kṛtvā yānti viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam  Hbhv 
viśeṣataḥ kalau
dvādaśaskandhe BhP 
kaler doṣanidhe rājann asti hy eko mahān guṇaḥ 
kīrtanād eva kṛṣṇasya muktasaṅgaḥ paraṃ vrajet  Hbhv 
yathā gāruḍe
yad icchasi paraṃ jñānaṃ jñānād yat paramaṃ padam 
tadādareṇa rājendra kuru govindakīrtanam  Hbhv 
śrībhagavatprīṇanatvam
vārāhe
vāsudevasya saṅkīrtyā surāpo vyādhito 'pi vā 
mukto jāyeta niyataṃ mahāviṣṇuḥ prasīdati  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye 
nāmasaṅkīrtanaṃ viṣṇoḥ kṣuttṛṭpraskhalitādiṣu 
karoti satataṃ viprās tasya prīto hy adhokṣajaḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare
nāmasaṅkīrtanaṃ viṣṇoḥ kṣuttṛṭpraskhalitādiṣu 
yaḥ karoti mahābhāga tasya tuṣyati keśavaḥ  Hbhv 
atha śrībhagavadvaśīkāritvam
viṣṇurahasye 
yad abhyarcya hariṃ bhaktyā kṛte kratuśatair api 
phalaṃ prāpnoty avikalaṃ kalau govindakīrtanāt  Hbhv 
ādipurāṇe
gītvā ca mama nāmāni vicaren mama sannidhau 
idaṃ bravīmi te satyaṃ krīto 'haṃ tasya cārjuna  Hbhv 
gītvā ca mama nāmāni vicaren mama sannidhau 
iti bravīmi te satyaṃ krīto 'haṃ tasya cārjuna  Hbhv 
iti 
evaṃ ca śrutvā ca mama nāmāni ity ādi  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharme prahlādena
jitaṃ tena jitaṃ tena jitaṃ teneti niścitam 
jihvāgre vartate yasya harir ity akṣaradvayam  Hbhv 
svataḥ paramapuruṣārthatvam
skānde kāśīkhaṇḍe
pādme ca vaiśākhamāhātmye
idam eva hi māṅgalyam etad eva dhanārjanam 
jīvitasya phalaṃ caitad yad dāmodarakīrtanam  Hbhv 
prabhāsakhaṇḍe
madhuramadhuram etan maṅgalaṃ maṅgalānāṃ
sakalanigamavallīsatphalaṃ citsvarūpam 
sakṛd api parigītaṃ śraddhayā helayā vā
bhṛguvara naramātraṃ tārayet kṛṣṇanāma  Hbhv 
viṣṇurahasye
etad eva paraṃ jñānam etad eva paraṃ tapaḥ 
etad eva paraṃ tattvaṃ vāsudevasya kīrtanam  Hbhv 
vaiṣṇavacintāmaṇau śrīśivomāsaṃvāde
aghacchitsmaraṇaṃ viṣṇor bahvāyāsena sādhyate 
oṣṭhaspandanamātreṇa kīrtanaṃ tu tato varam  Hbhv 
anyatra ca
yena janmaśataiḥ pūrvaṃ vāsudevaḥ samarcitaḥ 
tanmukhe harināmāni sadā tiṣṭhanti bhārata  Hbhv 
viśeṣataḥ kalau rahasye
yad abhyarcya hariṃ bhaktyā kṛte kratuśatair api 
phalaṃ prāpnoty avikalaṃ kalau govindakīrtanāt  Hbhv 
viṣṇupurāṇe ViP 
dhyāyan kṛte yajan yajñais tretāyāṃ dvāpare'rcayan 
yad āpnoti tad āpnoti kalau saṅkīrtya keśavam  Hbhv 
dvādaśaskandhe BhP 
kṛte yad dhyāyato viṣṇuṃ tretāyāṃ yajato makhaiḥ 
dvāpare paricaryāyāṃ kalau tad dharikīrtanāt  Hbhv 
ekādaśe BhP 
kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ tviṣākṛṣṇaṃ sāṅgopāṅgāstrapārṣadam 
yajñaiḥ saṅkīrtanaprāyair yajanti hi sumedhasaḥ  Hbhv 
skānde ca
mahābhāgavatā nityaṃ kalau kurvanti kīrtanam  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye  nāradoktaṃ 
harer nāmaiva nāmaiva nāmaiva mama jīvanam 
kalau nāsty eva nāsty eva nāsty eva gatir anyathā  Hbhv 
ataivoktam
sakṛd uccārayanty eva harer nāma cidātmakam 
phalaṃ nāsya kṣamo vaktuṃ sahasravadano vidhiḥ  Hbhv 
pādmottarakhaṇḍe śrīrāmāṣṭottaraśatanāmastotre śrīśivena
rakārādīni nāmāni śṛṇvato devi jāyate 
prītir me manaso nityaṃ rāmanāmaviśaṅkayā  Hbhv 
vaiṣṇavacintāmaṇau
īśo 'haṃ sarvajagatāṃ nāmnāṃ viṣṇor hi jāpakaḥ 
satyaṃ satyaṃ vadāmy eṣa harer nāma gatir nṝṇām  Hbhv 
ādipurāṇe ca śrīkṛṣṇārjunasaṃvāde
śraddhayā helayā nāma raṭanti mama jantavaḥ 
teṣāṃ nāma sadā pārtha vartate hṛdaye mama  Hbhv 
na nāma sadṛśaṃ jñānaṃ na nāma sadṛśaṃ vratam 
na nāma sadṛśaṃ dhyānaṃ na nāma sadṛśaṃ phalam  Hbhv 
na nāma sadṛśas tyāgo na nāma sadṛśaḥ śamaḥ 
na nāma sadṛśaṃ puṇyaṃ na nāma sadṛśī gatiḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
nāmaiva paramā muktir nāmaiva paramā gatiḥ 
nāmaiva paramā śāntir nāmaiva paramā sthitiḥ  Hbhv 
nāmaiva paramā bhaktir nāmaiva paramā matiḥ 
nāmaiva paramā prītir nāmaiva paramā smṛtiḥ  Hbhv 
nāmaiva kāraṇaṃ jantor nāmaiva prabhur eva ca 
nāmaiva paramārādhyo nāmaiva paramo guruḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
nāmayuktān janān dṛṣṭvā snigdho bhavati yo naraḥ 
sa yāti paramaṃ sthānaṃ viṣṇunā saha modate  Hbhv 
tasmān nāmāni kaunteya bhajasva dṛḍhamānasaḥ 
nāmayuktaḥ priyo 'smākaṃ nāmayukto bhavārjuna  Hbhv 
atha śrībhagavannāmajapasya smaraṇasya ca 
śravaṇasyāpi māhātmyam īṣad bhedād vilikhyate  Hbhv 
atha śrīmannāmajapamāhātmyam
viṣṇurahasye śrībhagavaduktau
satyaṃ bravīmi manujāḥ svayam ūrdvabāhur
yo māṃ mukunda narasiṃha janārdaneti 
jīvan japaty anudinaṃ maraṇe ṛṇīva
pāṣāṇakāṣṭhasadṛśāya dadāmy abhīṣṭam  Hbhv 
kāśīkāṇḍe agnibindustutau
nārāyaṇeti narakārṇavatāraṇeti
dāmodareti madhuheti caturbhujeti 
viśvambhareti virajeti janārdaneti
kvāstīha janma japatāṃ kva kṛtāntabhītiḥ  Hbhv 
pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye  yamabrāhmaṇasaṃvāde
vāsudevajapāsaktān api pāpakṛto janān 
nopasarpanti tān vipra yamadūtāś ca dāruṇāḥ  Hbhv 
bṛhadviṣṇupurāṇe
kva nākapṛṣṭhagamanaṃ punarāvṛttilakṣaṇam 
kva japo vāsudeveti muktibījam anuttamam  Hbhv 
śrīmannāmasmaraṇamāhātmyam
itihāsottame
svapne'pi nāmasmṛtir ādipuṃsaḥ
kṣayaṃ karoty āhitapāparāśeḥ 
prayatnataḥ kiṃ punar ādipuṃsaḥ
prakīrtite nāgnir janārdanasya  Hbhv 
laghubhāgavate
te sabhāgyā manuṣyeṣu kṛtārthā nṛpa niścitam 
smaranti ye smārayanti harer nāma kalau yuge  Hbhv 
pādme devahūtistutau
prayāṇe cāprayāṇe ca yannāmasmaraṇān nṝṇām 
sadyo naśyati pāpaugho namas tasmai cidātmane  Hbhv 
tatraivottarakhaṇḍe
yannāmasmaraṇād eva pāpinām api satvaram 
muktir bhavati jātūnāṃ brahmādīnāṃ sudurlabhā  Hbhv 
brahmavaivarte
yadanudhyānadāvāgnidagdhakarmatṛṇaḥ pumān 
viśuddhaḥ paśyati vyaktam avyaktam api keśavam  Hbhv 
tad asya nāma jīvasya patitasya bhavāmbudhau 
hastāvalambadānāya pravīṇo nāparo hareḥ  Hbhv 
jāvālisaṃhitāyām
harer nāma paraṃ japyaṃ dhyeyaṃ geyaṃ nirantaram 
kīrtanīyaṃ ca bahudhā nirvṛtīr bahudhecchatā  Hbhv 
atha śrībhagavannāmamāhātmyam
bṛhannāradīye śrīnāradoktau
yannāmaśravaṇenāpi mahāpātakino 'pi ye 
pāvanatvaṃ prapadyante kathaṃ stoṣyāmi khinnadhīḥ  Hbhv 
itihāsottame
śrutaṃ saṅkīrtitaṃ vāpi harer āścaryakarmaṇaḥ 
dahaty enāṃsi sarvāṇi prasaṅgāt kim u bhaktitaḥ  Hbhv 
ṣaṣṭhaskandhe BhP  citraketūktau 
na hi bhagavann aghaṭitam idaṃ
tvaddarśanān nṛṇām akhilapāpakṣayaḥ 
yannāma sakṛc chravaṇāt
pukkaśo 'pi vimucyate saṃsārāt  Hbhv 
iti 
śrīmannāmnāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ māhātmyeṣu sameṣv api 
kṛṣṇasyaivāvatāreṣu viśeṣaḥ ko 'pi kasyacit  Hbhv 
atha viśeṣataḥ śrīkṛṣṇāvatāramāhātmyam
brahmāṇḍapurāṇe śrīkṛṣṇāṣṭottaraśatanāmamāhātmye
sahasranāmnāṃ puṇyānāṃ trirāvṛttyā tu yat phalam 
ekāvṛttyā tu kṛṣṇasya nāmaikaṃ tat prayacchati  Hbhv 
idaṃ kirīṭī saṃjapya jayī pāśupatāstrabhāk 
kṛṣṇasya prāṇabhūtaḥ san kṛṣṇaṃ sārathim āptavān  Hbhv 
kim idaṃ bahunā śaṃsan mānuṣānandanirbharaḥ 
brahmānandam avāpyānte kṛṣṇasāyujyam āpnuyāt  Hbhv 
vārāhe ca śrīmāthuramāhātmye
tatra guhyāni nāmāni bhaviṣyanti mama priye 
puṇyāni ca pavitrāṇi saṃsāracchedanāni ca  Hbhv 
tatraiva viśeṣataḥ śrīkṛṣṇeti nāmamāhātmyam
dvārakāmāhātmye prahlādabalisaṃvāde
atītāḥ puruṣāḥ sapta bhaviṣāś ca caturdaśa 
naras tārayate sarvān kalau kṛṣṇeti kīrtanāt  Hbhv 
kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇeti kṛṣṇeti svapan jāgrad vrajaṃs tathā 
yo jalpati kalau nityaṃ kṛṣṇarūpī bhaved dhi saḥ  Hbhv 
brahmavaivarte
hanan brāhmaṇam atyantaṃ kāmato vā surāṃ piban 
kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇety ahorātraṃ saṅkīrtya śucitām iyāt  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharme
kṛṣṇeti maṅgalaṃ nāma yasya vāci pravartate 
bhasmībhavanti rājendra mahāpātakakoṭayaḥ  Hbhv 
nārasiṃhe śrībhagavaduktau
kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇeti kṛṣṇeti yo māṃ smarati nityaśaḥ 
jalaṃ bhittvā yathā padmaṃ narakād uddharāmy aham  Hbhv 
gāruḍe pādme ca
saṃsārasarpasaṃdaṣṭaṃ naṣṭaceṣṭaikabheṣajam 
kṛṣṇeti vaiṣṇavaṃ mantraṃ śrutvā mukto bhaven naraḥ  Hbhv 
prabhāsapurāṇe
nāmnāṃ mukhyataraṃ nāma kṛṣṇākhyaṃ me parantapa 
prāyaścittam aśeṣāṇāṃ pāpānāṃ mocakaṃ param  Hbhv 
pādme
yatra yatra sthito vāpi kṛṣṇakṛṣṇeti kīrtayet 
sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā sa gacchet paramāṃ gatim  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare śrīkṛṣṇasahasranāmastotre
ballavīkānta kiṃ tais tair upāyaiḥ kṛṣṇanāma te 
kintu jihvāgragaṃ jāgran nirundhe hi mahābhayam  Hbhv 
tatraivānyatra
satyaṃ bravīmi te śambho gopanīyam idaṃ mama 
mṛtyusaṃjīvanīṃ nāma kṛṣṇākhyām avadhāraya  Hbhv 
bhāratavibhāge
kṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇa ity antakāle
jalpan jantur jīvitaṃ yo jahāti 
ādyaḥ śabdaḥ kalpate tasya muktyai
vrīḍānamrau tiṣṭhato 'nyāvṛṇasthau  Hbhv 
anyatrāpi
nāma cintāmaṇiḥ kṛṣṇaś caitanyarasavigrahaḥ 
pūrṇaḥ śuddho nityamukto bhinnatvān nāmanāminoḥ  Hbhv 
ataivoktam
tebhyo namo 'stu bhavavāridhijīrṇapaṅka
saṃmagnamokṣaṇavicakṣaṇapādukebhyaḥ 
kṛṣṇeti varṇayugalaṃ śravaṇena yeṣāṃ
ānandathūrbhavati nartitaromavṛndaḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca dvitīyaskandhe BhP  
tad aśmasāraṃ hṛdayaṃ batedaṃ
yad gṛhyamāṇair harināmadheyaiḥ 
na vikriyetātha yadā vikāro
netre jalaṃ gātraruheṣu harṣaḥ  Hbhv 
itihāsottame ca
nāmni saṅkīrtite viṣṇor yasya puṃso na jāyate 
saromapulakaṃ gātraṃ sa bhavet kuliśopamaḥ  Hbhv 
kātyāyanasaṃhitāyām
nāmasaṅkīrtanāj jātaṃ puṇyaṃ nopacayanti ye 
nānāvyādhisamāyuktāḥ śatajanmasu te narāḥ  Hbhv 
sā hānis tan mahac chidraṃ sa mohaḥ sa ca vibhramaḥ 
yanmuhūrtaṃ kṣaṇaṃ vāpi vāsudevo na cintyate  Hbhv 
pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye yamabrāhmaṇasaṃvāde
avamatya ca ye yānti bhagavatkīrtanaṃ narāḥ 
te yānti narakaṃ ghoraṃ tena pāpena karmaṇā  Hbhv 
śrutayaḥ
om āsya jānanto nāma cid viviktan
mahas te viṣṇo sumatiṃ bhajāmahe  Hbhv 
oṃ tat sat oṃ padaṃ devasya namasā
vyantaḥ śravasy avaśrava āpannaṃ ṛktam 
nāmāni cid dadhire yajñiyanti
bhadrāyānte raṇayantaḥ sandṛṣṭau  Hbhv 
oṃ tam u stotāraḥ pūrvaṃ yathāvida
ṛtasya garbhaṃ januṣā pipartana 
āsya jānanto nāma cid viviktan
mahas te viṣṇo sumatiṃ bhajāmahe  Hbhv 
ity ādyā iti 
īdṛśe nāmamāhātmye śrutismṛtiviniścite 
kalpayanty arthavādaṃ ye yānti ghorayātanām  Hbhv 
atha śrībhagavannāmārthavādakalpanādūṣaṇam
śrīkātyāyanasaṃhitāyām
arthavādaṃ harer nāmni sambhāvayati yo naraḥ 
sa pāpiṣṭho manuṣyāṇāṃ niraye patanti sphuṭam  Hbhv 
brahmasaṃhitāyāṃ baudhāyanaṃ prati śrībhagavaduktau
yannāmakīrtanaphalaṃ vividhaṃ niśamya
na śraddadhāti manute yad utārthavādam 
yo mānuṣas tam iha duḥkhacaye kṣipāmi
saṃsāraghoravividhārtinipīḍitāṅgam  Hbhv 
jaiminisaṃhitāyāṃ ca
śrutismṛtipurāṇeṣu nāmamāhātmyavāciṣu 
ye'rthavāda iti brūyur na teṣāṃ nirayakṣayaḥ  Hbhv 
tasmiṃś ca bhagavannāmni jagadekopakāriṇi 
viśvaikasevye matimān aparādhān vivarjayet  Hbhv 
yata uktaṃ pādme śrīnāradaṃ prati sanatkumāreṇa 
sarvāparādhakṛd api mucyate harisaṃśrayāt  Hbhv 
harer apy aparādhān yaḥ kuryād dvipadapāṃsavaḥ 
nāmāśrayaḥ kadācit syāt taraty eva sa nāmataḥ  Hbhv 
nāmno 'pi sarvasuhṛdo hy aparādhāt pataty adhaḥ  Hbhv 
atha nāmāparādhāḥ
taṃ prati tenaivoktāḥ 
satāṃ nindā nāmnaḥ paramam aparādhaṃ vitanute
yataḥ khyātiṃ yātaṃ katham u sahate tadvigarhām 
śivasya śrīviṣṇor ya iha guṇanāmādisakalaṃ
dhiyā bhinnaṃ paśyet sa khalu harināmāhitakaraḥ  Hbhv 
guror avajñā śrutiśāstranindanaṃ
tathārthavādo harināmni kalpanam 
nāmno balād yasya hi pāpabuddhir
na vidyate tasya yamair hi śuddhiḥ  Hbhv 
dharmavratatyāgahutādisarva
śubhakriyāsāmyam api pramādaḥ 
aśraddadhāne vimukhe'py aśṛṇvati
yaś copadeśaḥ śivanāmāparādhaḥ  Hbhv 
śrute'pi nāmamāhātmye yaḥ prītirahito 'dhamaḥ 
ahaṃmamādiparamo nāmni so 'py aparādhakṛt  Hbhv 
jāte nāmāparādhe'pi pramādena kathañcana 
sadā saṅkīrtayan nāma tadekaśaraṇo bhavet  Hbhv 
aparādhabhañjanaṃ
uktaṃ ca tenaiva tatra 
nāmāparādhayuktānāṃ nāmāny eva haranty agham 
aviśrāntaprayuktāni tāny evārthakarāṇi ca  Hbhv 
nāmaikaṃ yasya vāci smaraṇapathagataṃ śrotramūlaṃ gataṃ vā
śuddhaṃ vāśuddhavarṇaṃ vyavahitarahitaṃ tārayaty eva satyam 
tac ced dehadraviṇajanatālobhapāṣaṇḍamadhye
nikṣiptaṃ syān na phalajanakaṃ śīghram evātra vipra  Hbhv 
ataivoktaṃ śrīnāradena bṛhannāradīye 
mahminām api yannāmnaḥ pāraṃ gantum anīśvaraḥ 
manavo 'pi munīdrāś ca kathaṃ kṣuṇṇadhīr bhaje  Hbhv 
iti 
itthaṃ śrīkṛṣṇapādābje bhaktiḥ kāryā sadā budhaiḥ 
sā ca tasya prasādena mahāpuṇyāt prajāyate  Hbhv 
atha śrīmadbhakter durlabhatvam
skānde śrīparāśaroktau
na hy apuṇyavatāṃ loke mūḍhānāṃ kuṭilātmanām 
bhaktir bhavati govinde smaraṇaṃ kīrtanaṃ tathā  Hbhv 
tatraiva śrībrahmoktau
nimiṣaṃ nimiṣārdhaṃ vā martyānām iha nārada 
nādagdhāśeṣapāpānāṃ bhaktir bhavati keśave  Hbhv 
yogavāśiṣṭhe
janmāntarasahasreṣu tapojñānasamādhibhiḥ 
narāṇāṃ kṣīṇapāpānāṃ kṛṣṇe bhaktiḥ prajāyate  Hbhv 
ādivārāhe
janmāntarasahasreṣu samārādhya vṛṣadhvajam 
vaiṣṇavatvaṃ labhed dhīmān sarvapāpakṣaye sati  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye  yajñadhvajanṛpopākhyānānte
janmakoṭisahasreṣu puṇyaṃ yaiḥ samupārjitam 
teṣāṃ bhaktir bhavec chuddhā devadeve janārdane  Hbhv 
sulabhaṃ jāhnavīsnānaṃ tathaivātithipūjanam 
sulabhāḥ sarvayajñāś ca viṣṇubhaktiḥ sudurlabhā  Hbhv 
itihāsasamuccaye śiloñchavṛttivākye
gaṅgāyāṃ maraṇaṃ caiva dṛḍhā bhaktiś ca keśave 
brahmavidyāprabodhaś ca nālpasya tapasaḥ phalam  Hbhv 
agastyasaṃhitāyām
vratopavāsaniyamair janmakoṭyāpy aniṣṭhiteḥ 
yajñaiś ca vividhaiḥ samyag bhaktir bhavati keśave  Hbhv 
viṣṇudharmottare
divasaṃ divasārdhaṃ vā muhūrtaṃ caikam eva vā 
nāśāc cāśeṣapāpasya bhaktir bhavati keśave  Hbhv 
anekajanmasāhasrair nānāyonyantareṣu ca 
jantoḥ kaluṣahīnasya bhaktir bhavati keśave  Hbhv 
daśamaskandhe gopīḥ prati uddhavoktau BhP 
dānavrātatapohoma japasvādhyāyasaṃyamaiḥ 
śreyobhir vividhaiś cānyaiḥ kṛṣṇe bhaktir hi sādhyate  Hbhv 
śrībhagavadgītāsu 
yeṣāṃ tv antagataṃ pāpaṃ janānāṃ puṇyakarmaṇām 
te dvandvamohanirmuktā bhajante māṃ dṛḍhavratāḥ  Hbhv 
pañcamaskandhe parīkṣitaṃ prati śrībādarāyaṇinā BhP 
rājan patir gurur alaṃ bhavatāṃ yadūnāṃ
daivaṃ priyaḥ kulapatiḥ kva ca kiṅkaro vaḥ 
astv evam aṅga bhagavān bhajatāṃ mukundo
muktiṃ dadāti karhicit sma na bhaktiyogam  Hbhv 
ṣaṣṭhaskandhe vṛtropākhyānānte BhP 
devānāṃ śuddhasattvānāṃ ṛṣīṇāṃ cāmalātmanām 
bhaktir mukundacaraṇe na prāyeṇopajāyate  Hbhv 
śrīmadbhaktyai namas tasyai yasyā māthāmtyamandaram 
yatprabhāveṇa lolo 'yaṃ kīṭo 'py uddhartum icchati  Hbhv 
atha śrībhagavadbhaktimāhātmyaṃ
tatrādau bhaktimataḥ kathañcid āpatite'pi pāpe prāyaścittāntaranirasanatvam 
pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye nāradāmbarīṣasaṃvāde PadmaP 
yathāgniḥ susamṛddhārciḥ karoty edhāṃsi bhasmasāt 
pāpāni bhagavadbhaktis tathā dahati tatkṣaṇāt  Hbhv 
ṣaṣṭhe ajāmilopākhyānārambhe BhP 
kecit kevalayā bhaktyā vāsudevaparāyaṇāḥ 
aghaṃ dhunvanti kārtsnyena nīhāram iva bhāskaraḥ  Hbhv 
ekādaśe ca śrībhagavaduddhavasaṃvāde BhP 
yathāgniḥ susamṛddhārciḥ karoty edhāṃsi bhasmasāt 
tathā madviṣayā bhaktir uddhavaināṃsi kṛtsnaśaḥ  Hbhv 
ataivoktaṃ tatraiva śrīkarabhājanena BhP  
svapādamūlaṃ bhajataḥ priyasya
tyaktānyabhāvasya hariḥ pareśaḥ 
vikarma yac cotpatitaṃ kathañcid
dhunoti sarvaṃ hṛdi sanniviṣṭaḥ  Hbhv 
dvārakāmāhātmye candraśarmāṇaṃ prati śrībhagavatā
madbhaktiṃ vahatāṃ puṃsām iha loke pare'pi vā 
nāśubhaṃ vidyate kiñcit kulakoṭiṃ nayed ditam  Hbhv 
viṣayabhoge'pi taddoṣanirākaratvam
ekādaśaskandhe tatraiva BhP 
bādhyamāno 'pi madbhakto viṣayair ajitendriyaḥ 
prāyaḥ pragalbhayā bhaktyā viṣayair nābhibhūyate  Hbhv 
karmādhikāranirasanatvaṃ
tatraiva BhP 
tāvat karmāṇi kurvīta na nirvidyeta yāvatā 
matkathāśravaṇādau vā śraddhā yāvan na jāyate  Hbhv 
ataivoktaṃ prathamaskandhe BhP 
tyaktvā svadharmaṃ caraṇāmbujaṃ harer
bhajann apakvo 'tha patet tato yadi 
yatra kva vābhadram abhūd amuṣya kiṃ
ko vārtha āpto 'bhajatāṃ svadharmataḥ  Hbhv 
ekāntilakṣaṇe yac ca likhitaṃ śaraṇāgatau 
lekhyaṃ ca tattadvacanair etat sudṛḍhatām iyāt  Hbhv 
manaḥprasādakatvam
prathamaskandhe BhP 
sa vai puṃsāṃ paro dharmo yato bhaktir adhokṣaje 
ahaituky apratihatā yayātmā suprasīdati  Hbhv 
ataivoktam ekādaśe BhP 
dharmaḥ satyadayopeto vidyā vā tapasānvitā 
madbhaktyāpetam ātmānaṃ na samyak prapunāti hi  Hbhv 
tatraiva BhP 
bhaktiḥ punāti manniṣṭhā śvapākān api sambhavāt  Hbhv 
ṣaṣṭhe BhP 
etāvān eva loke'smin puṃsāṃ dharmaḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ 
bhaktiyogo bhagavati tannāmagrahaṇādibhiḥ  Hbhv 
ataivoktaṃ pādme
kiṃ tasya bahubhiḥ mantraiḥ śāstraiḥ kiṃ bahuvistaraiḥ 
vājapeyasahasraiḥ kiṃ bhaktir yasya janārdane  Hbhv 
sarvaguṇādisevyatākāritvam
pañcamaskandhe prahlādoktau BhP 
yasyāsti bhaktir bhagavaty akiñcanā
sarvair guṇais tatra samāsate surāḥ 
harāv abhaktasya kuto mahadguṇā
manorathenāsati dhāvato bahiḥ  Hbhv 
caturthe śrīdhruvaṃ prati manūtkau BhP 
tvaṃ pratyagātmani tadā bhagavaty ananta
ānandamātra upapannasamastaśaktau 
bhaktiṃ vidhāya paramāṃ śanakair avidyā
granthiṃ vibhetsyasi mamāham iti prarūḍham  Hbhv 
śrīpṛthuṃ prati śrīsanakādibhiḥ BhP 
yatpādapaṅkajapalāśavilāsabhaktyā
karmāśayaṃ grathitam udgrathayanti santaḥ 
tadvan na riktamatayo yatayo 'pi ruddha
srotogaṇās tam araṇaṃ bhaja vāsudevam  Hbhv 
sarvamārgādhikatvam
tṛtīye śrīkāpileye BhP 
na yujyamānayā bhaktyā bhagavaty akhilātmani 
sadṛśo 'sti śivaḥ panthā yogināṃ brahmasiddhaye  Hbhv 
ṣaṣṭhe ca BhP 
sadhrīcīno hy ayaṃ loke panthāḥ kṣemo 'kutobhayaḥ 
suśīlāḥ sādhavo yatra nārāyaṇaparāyaṇāḥ  Hbhv 
ataivoktaṃ dvitīye śrībādarāyaṇinā BhP 
na hy ato 'nyaḥ śivaḥ panthā viśataḥ saṃsṛtāv iha 
vāsudeve bhagavati bhaktiyogo yato bhavet  Hbhv 
bhagavān brahma kārtsnyena trir anvīkṣya manīṣayā 
tad adhyavasyat kūṭastho ratir ātmany ato bhavet  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye śrīnāradoktaṃ  
yathā samastalokānāṃ jīvanaṃ salilaṃ smṛtam 
tathā samastasiddhīnāṃ jīvanaṃ bhaktir iṣyate  Hbhv 
jīvanti jantavaḥ sarve yathā mātaramāśritāḥ 
tathā bhaktiṃ samāśritya sarve jīvanti dhārmikāḥ  Hbhv 
dhvajāropaṇamāhātmye śrīviṣṇudūtoktau
mahāpātakayukto vā yukto vā sarvapātakaiḥ 
īpsitāṃ bhagavadbhaktyā labhate paramāṃ gatim  Hbhv 
pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye yamabrāhmaṇasaṃvāde
apatyaṃ draviṇaṃ dārā hārā harmyaṃ hayā gajāḥ 
sukhāni svargamokṣau ca na dūre haribhaktitaḥ  Hbhv 
prathamaskandhe BhP 
vāsudeve bhagavati bhaktiyogaḥ prayojitaḥ 
janayaty āśu vairāgyaṃ jñānaṃ ca yad ahaitukam  Hbhv 
ekādaśe ca BhP 
yat karmabhir yat tapasā jñānavairāgyataś ca yat 
yogena dāmadharmeṇa śreyobhir itarair api  Hbhv 
sarvaṃ madbhaktiyogena madbhakto labhate'ñjasā 
svargāpavargaṃ maddhāma kathañcid yadi vāñchati  Hbhv 
ataivoktaṃ dvitīye BhP 
akāmaḥ sarvakāmo vā mokṣakāma udāradhīḥ 
tīvreṇa bhaktiyogena yajeta puruṣaṃ param  Hbhv 
mokṣādhikatvam
tṛtīye kāpileye BhP 
animittā bhāgavatī bhaktiḥ siddher garīyasī 
jarayaty āśu yā koṣaṃ nigīrṇam analo yathā  Hbhv 
pañcame śrīṛṣabhadevacaritānte BhP 
yasyām eva kavaya ātmānam avirataṃ vividhavṛjinasaṃsāraparitāpopatapyamānam anusavanaṃ
snāpayantas tayaiva parayā nirvṛtyā hy apavargam ātyantikaṃ paramapuruṣārtham api
svayam āsāditaṃ no evādriyante bhagavadīyatvenaiva parisamāptasarvārthāḥ  Hbhv 
dvādaśe ca śrīmārkaṇḍeyam uddiśya śrīśivoktau BhP 
naivecchaty āśiṣaḥ kvāpi brahmarṣir mokṣam apy uta 
bhaktiṃ parāṃ bhagavati labdhavān puruṣe'vyaye  Hbhv 
ataivoktaṃ pañcame śrībhagavantam uddiśya bādarāyaṇinā BhP 
yo dustyajān kṣitisutasvajanārthadārān
prārthyāṃ śriyaṃ suravaraiḥ sadayāvalokām 
naicchan nṛpas taducitaṃ mahatāṃ madhudviṭ
sevānuraktamanasām abhavo 'pi phalguḥ  Hbhv 
ekādaśe ca bhagavatā BhP 
na pārameṣṭhyaṃ na mahendradhiṣṇyaṃ
na sārvabhaumaṃ na rasādhipatyam 
na yogasiddhīr apunarbhavaṃ vā
mayy arpitātmecchati mad vinānyat  Hbhv 
ataivoktaṃ ṣaṣṭhe śrīrudreṇa BhP 
vāsudeve bhagavati bhaktim udvahatāṃ nṝṇām 
jñānavairāgyavīryāṇāṃ neha kaścid vyapāśrayaḥ  Hbhv 
viṣṇupurāṇe ca śrīprahlādena ViP 
dharmārthakāmaiḥ kiṃ tasya muktis tasya kare sthitā 
samastajagatāṃ mūle yasya bhaktiḥ sthitā tvayi  Hbhv 
ataivoktaṃ nārasiṃhe
patreṣu puṣpeṣu phaleṣu toyesv
akrītalabhyeṣu sadaiva satsu 
bhaktyā sulabhye puruṣe purāṇe
muktau kim arthaṃ kriyate prayatnaḥ  Hbhv 
ataivoktaṃ prathamaskandhe BhP 
ātmārāmāś ca munayo nirgranthā apy urukrame 
kurvanty ahaitukīṃ bhaktim itthambhūtaguṇo hariḥ  Hbhv 
śrīvaikuṇṭhalokaprāpakatvam
vāmane
yeṣāṃ cakragadāpāṇau bhaktir avyabhicāriṇī 
te yānti niyataṃ sthānaṃ yatra yogeśvaro hariḥ  Hbhv 
skānde
munir jāpyaparo nityaṃ dṛḍhabhaktir jitendriyaḥ 
svagṛhe'pi vasan yāti tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam  Hbhv 
tṛtīyaskandhe śrīvaikuṇṭhavarṇane BhP 
yac ca vrajanty animiṣāṃ ṛṣabhānuvṛttyā
dūre yamā hy upari naḥ spṛhaṇīyaśīlāḥ 
bhartur mithaḥ suyaśasaḥ kathanānurāga
vaiklavyabāṣpakalayā pulakīkṛtāṅgāḥ  Hbhv 
daśame ca śrībrahmastutau BhP 
pureha bhūman bahavo 'pi yoginas
tvadarpitehā nijakarmalabdhayā 
vibudhya bhaktyaiva kathopanītayā
prapedire'ñjo 'cyuta te gatiṃ parām  Hbhv 
bṛhannāradīye bhagavattoṣapraśnottare 
sarvadevamayo viṣṇuḥ śaraṇārtipranāśanaḥ 
svabhaktavatsalo devo bhaktyā tuṣyati nānyathā  Hbhv 
saptamaskandhe śrīprahlādasya bālopadeśe BhP 
nālaṃ dvijatvaṃ devatvaṃ ṛṣitvaṃ vāsurātmajāḥ 
prīṇanāya mukundasya na vṛttaṃ na bahujñatā  Hbhv 
na dānaṃ na tapo nejyā na śaucaṃ na vratāni ca 
prīyate'malayā bhaktyā harir anyad viḍambanam  Hbhv 
śrīnṛsiṃhastutau ca BhP 
manye dhanābhijanarūpatapaḥśrutaujas
tejaḥprabhāvabalapauruṣabuddhiyogāḥ 
nārādhanāya hi bhavanti parasya puṃso
bhaktyā tutoṣa bhagavān gajayūthapāya  Hbhv 
anyatrāpi Padyāvalī 
vyādhasyācaraṇaṃ dhruvasya ca vayo vidyā gajendrasya kā
kubjāyāḥ kim u nāma rūpam adhikaṃ kiṃ tat sudāmno dhanam 
vaṃśaḥ ko vidurasya yādavapater ugrasya kiṃ pauruṣaṃ
bhaktyā tuṣyati kevalaṃ na ca guṇair bhaktipriyo mādhavaḥ  Hbhv 
ataivoktaṃ śrībhagavatā Gītā 
patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ toyaṃ yo me bhaktyā prayacchati 
tad ahaṃ bhaktyupahṛtam aśnāmi prayatātmanaḥ  Hbhv 
prathamaskandhe śrīhanumatoktam
na janma nūnaṃ mahato na saubhagaṃ
na vāṅ na buddhir nākṛtis toṣahetuḥ 
tair yad visṛṣṭān api no vanaukasaś
cakāra sakhe bata lakṣmaṇāgrajaḥ  Hbhv 
śrībhagavatsaṅgamakatvam
śrībhagavadgītāsu 
bhaktyā tv ananyayā śakya aham evaṃvidho 'rjuna 
jñātuṃ draṣṭuṃ ca tattvena praveṣṭuṃ ca paraṃtapa  Hbhv 
ekādaśaskandhe ca śrībhagavaduddhavasaṃvāde BhP 
yathāgninā hemamalaṃ jahāti
dhmātaṃ punaḥ svaṃ bhajate ca rūpam 
ātmā ca karmānuśayaṃ vidhūya
madbhaktiyogena bhajaty atho mām  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca BhP 
bhaktyoddhavānapāyinyā sarvalokamaheśvaram 
sarvotpattyapyayaṃ brahma kāraṇaṃ mopayāti saḥ  Hbhv 
śrībhagavadvaśīkāratvam
pādme kārttikamāhātmye śrīnāradaśaunakasaṃvāde
bhuktiṃ muktiṃ harir dadyāt arcito 'nyatra sevinām 
bhaktiṃ ca dadāty eṣa yato vaśyakarī hareḥ  Hbhv 
tatraiva vaiśākhamāhātmye 
śrīnāradāmbarīṣasaṃvāde
māyājāniramāyo 'sau bhaktyā rājan na māyayā 
sādhyate sādhupuruṣaiḥ svayaṃ jānāti tad bhavān  Hbhv 
ekādaśaskandhe ca tatraiva BhP 
na sādhayati māṃ yogo na sāṅkhyaṃ dharma uddhava 
na svādhyāyas tapas tyāgo yathā bhaktir mamorjitā  Hbhv 
dharmaḥ satyadayopeto vidyā vā tapasānvitā 
madbhaktyāpetam ātmānaṃ na samyak prapunāti hi  Hbhv 
svataḥ paramapuruṣārthatā
tṛtīyaskandhe śrīkāpileye BhP 
sālokyasārṣṭisāmīpya sārūpyaikatvam apy uta 
dīyamānaṃ na gṛhṇanti vinā matsevanaṃ janāḥ  Hbhv 
navamaskandhe cāmbarīṣopākhyāne śrībhagavaduktau BhP 
matsevayā pratītaṃ te sālokyādicatuṣṭayam 
necchanti sevayā pūrṇāḥ kuto 'nyat kālaviplutam  Hbhv 
iti 
māhātmyaṃ yac ca bhagavadbhaktānāṃ likhitaṃ purā 
tadbhakter api vijñeyaṃ teṣāṃ bhaktyaiva tattvataḥ  Hbhv 
tathā pūjā tadaṅgānāṃ śrīmannāmno 'parasya ca 
draṣṭavyam iha māhātmyaṃ teṣāṃ bhaktyaṅgatā yataḥ  Hbhv 
atha śrīmadbhagavadbhaktinityatā
yāvaj jano bhajati no bhuvi viṣṇubhakti
vārtāsudhārasaviśeṣarasaikasāram 
tāvaj jarāmaraṇajanmaśatābhighāta
duḥkhāni tāni labhate bahudehajāni  Hbhv 
daśame brahmastutau BhP 
śreyaḥsṛtiṃ bhaktim udasya te vibho
kliśyanti ye kevelabodhalabdhaye 
teṣām asau kleśala eva śiṣyate
nānyad yathā sthūlatuṣāvaghātinām  Hbhv 
ekādaśe BhP 
mukhabāhūrupādebhyaḥ puruṣasyāśramaiḥ saha 
catvāro jajñire varṇā guṇair viprādayaḥ pṛthak  Hbhv 
ya evaṃ puruṣaṃ sākṣād ātmaprabhavam īśvaram 
na bhajanty avajānanti sthānād bhraṣṭāḥ patanty adhaḥ  Hbhv 
ataivoktaṃ śrībhagavatā Gītā  
na māṃ duṣkṛtino mūḍhāḥ prapadyante narādhamāḥ 
māyayāpahṛtajñānā āsuraṃ bhāvam āśritāḥ  Hbhv 
nityatvaṃ yad yad aṅgānāṃ bhakter vilikhitaṃ purā 
tena tenaiva nityatvam asyāṃ saṃsādhitaṃ param  Hbhv 
lakṣaṇāni ca tadbhakteḥ śrīmadbhāgavatādiṣu 
khyātāni śravaṇādīni likhyante'thāpi kānicit  Hbhv 
atha śrīmadbhaktilakṣaṇāni
tatra sāmānyalakṣaṇam
tṛtīyaskandhe śrīkāpileye BhP  
devānāṃ guṇaliṅgānām ānuśravikakarmaṇām 
sattva evaikamanaso vṛttiḥ svābhāvikī tu yā 
animittā bhāgavatī bhaktiḥ siddher garīyasī  Hbhv 
atha viśeṣasādhanabhaktilakṣaṇāni
gautamīyatantre 
devatāyāṃ ca mantre ca tathā mantraprade gurau 
bhaktir aṣṭavidhā yasya tasya kṛṣṇaḥ prasīdati  Hbhv 
tadbhaktajanavātsalyaṃ pūjāyāṃ cānumodanam

mūrkhonmattavyasanino virūpān māyinas tathā 
nyūnāṅgānadhamāṃś caiva nopahāsen na dūṣayet  Hbhv 
parasya daṇḍaṃ nodyacchet śikṣārthaṃ putraśiṣyayoḥ 
nānulepanam ādadyād asnātaḥ snātakī kvacit  Hbhv 
na cāpi raktavāsāḥ syāc citravāsadharo 'pi vā 
kṣurakarmaṇi cānte ca strīsambhoge ca putraka 
snāyīta celavān prājñaḥ kaṭabhūmim upetya ca  Hbhv 
yugapaj jalam agniṃ ca bibhṛyān na vicakṣaṇaḥ 
nācakṣīta dhayantīṃ gāṃ jalaṃ nāñjalinā pibet  Hbhv 
śaucakāleṣu sarveṣu guruṣv alpeṣu vā punaḥ 
na vilambeta śaucārthaṃ na mukhenānalaṃ dhamet  Hbhv 
vipurṣo makṣikādyāś ca hastasaṅgād adoṣiṇaḥ 
ajāśvau muhato medhyau na gor vatsasya cānanam  Hbhv 
mātuḥ prasnavane medhyaṃ śakuniḥ phalapātane 
udakyāśaucinagnāṃś ca sūtikāntyācasāyinaḥ 
spṛṣṭvā snāyīta śaucārthaṃ tathaiva mṛtahāriṇaḥ  Hbhv 
nāraṃ spṛṣṭvāsthi sasnehaṃ snātaḥ śudhyati mānavaḥ 
ācamyaiva tu nisnehaṃ gām ālabhyārkam īkṣya vā  Hbhv 
na cālapej janaṃ dviṣṭaṃ vīrahīnāṃ tathā striyam 
devatātithisacchāstrayajñasiddhādinindakaiḥ  Hbhv 
kṛtvā tu sparśatālāpaṃ śudhyed arkāvalokanāt 
avalokya tathodakyām antyajān patitaṃ śaṭham 
vidharmisūtikāṣaṇḍavivastrānyāvasāyinaḥ  Hbhv 
mṛtaniryātakāś caiva paradāraratāś ca ye 
etad eva hi kartavyaṃ prājñaiḥ śodhanam ātmanaḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
yac cāpi kurvato nātmā jugupsām eti putraka 
tat kartavyam aśaṅkena yan na gopyaṃ mahājane  Hbhv 
bhaviṣyottare śrīkṛṣṇayudhiṣṭhirasaṃvāde
upāsate na ye pūrvāṃ dvijāḥ sandhyāṃ na paścimām 
sarvāms tān dhārmiko rājā śūdrakarmaṇi yojayet  Hbhv 
dūrād āvasathān mūtraṃ dūrāt pādāvasecanam 
ucchiṣṭotsarjanaṃ bhūpa sadā kāryā hitaiṣiṇā  Hbhv 
ucchiṣṭau na spṛśec chīrṣaṃ sarve prāṇās tadāśrayāḥ 
keśagrāhān prahārāṃś ca śirasy etāni varjayet 
na pāṇibhyām ubhābhyāṃ tu kaṇḍūyāj jātu vai śiraḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
suvāsinīr gurviṇīś ca vṛddhaṃ bālāturau tathā 
bhojayet saṃskṛtānn eva prathamaṃ caramaṃ gṛhī  Hbhv 
aghaṃ sa kevalaṃ bhuṅkte vṛddhe govāhanādike 
yo bhuṅkte pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha prekṣatām apradāya ca  Hbhv 
varjayed dadhiśaktuṃ ca rātrau dhānāś ca vāsare  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
srajaś ca nāvakarṣeta na bahir dhārayeta ca 
gṛhe pārāvatā dhanyāḥ śukāś ca sahasārikāḥ  Hbhv 
kaurme vyāsagītāyām
tṛṇaṃ vā yadi vā śākaṃ mūlaṃ vā jalam eva vā 
parasyāpaharan jantur narakaṃ pratipadyate  Hbhv 
na rājñaḥ pratigṛhṇīyān na śūdrāt patitād api 
nānyasmād yācakatvaṃ ca ninditād varjayed budhaḥ  Hbhv 
nityaṃ yācanako na syāt punas tatraiva yācayet 
prāṇān apaharaty eṣa yācakas tasya durmatiḥ  Hbhv 
na devadravyahārī syād viśeṣeṇa dvijottamāḥ 
brahmasvaṃ ca nāpahared āpady api kadācana  Hbhv 
na viṣaṃ viṣam ity āhur brahmasvaṃ viṣam ucyate 
devasvaṃ vāpi yatnena sadā pariharet tataḥ  Hbhv 
na dharmasyāpadeśena pāpaṃ kṛtvā vrataṃ caret 
vratena pāpaṃ pracchādya kurvan strīśūdradambhanam 
pretyeha cedṛśo vipro garhyeta brahmavādibhiḥ  Hbhv 
devadrohād gurudrohaḥ koṭikoṭiguṇādhikaḥ 
jñānāpavāo nāstikyaṃ tasmād koṭiguṇādhikam  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
himavadvindhyayor madhye pūrvapaścimayoḥ śubham 
muktvā samudrayor deśaṃ nānyatra nivased dvijaḥ  Hbhv 
kṛṣṇo vā yatra carati mṛgo nityaṃ svabhāvataḥ 
puṇyāś ca viśrutā nadyas tatra vā nivased dvijaḥ 
ardhakrośān nadīkulaṃ varjayitvā dvijottamāḥ  Hbhv 
kiṃ ca
agninā bhasmanā caiva salilena viśeṣataḥ 
dvāreṇa stambhamārgeṇa padbhiḥ paṅktir vibhidyate 
parakṣetre carantīṃ gāṃ na cācakṣīta kasyacit  Hbhv 
naṣuryapariveśaṃ vā nendracāpaṃ na cāgnikam 
parasmai kathayed vidvān śaśinaṃ vā kathaṃcana 
tithiṃ pakṣasya na brūyān nakṣatrāṇi vinirdiśet  Hbhv 
na devaguruviprāṇāṃ dīyamānaṃ tu vārayet 
nindayed yo gurūn devān vedaṃ vā sopabṛṃhitam 
kalpakoṭiśataṃ sāgraṃ raurave pacyate naraḥ  Hbhv 
tūṣṇīm āsīta nindāyāṃ na brūyāt kiṃcid uttaram 
karṇau pidhāya gantavyaṃ na cainam avalokayet  Hbhv 
varjayed rahasyaṃ ca pareṣāṃ gūhayed budhaḥ 
vivādaṃ svajanaiḥ sārdhaṃ na kuryād vai kadācana  Hbhv 
na pāpaṃ pāpinaṃ brūyād apāpaṃ vā dvijottamāḥ  Hbhv 
nekṣetodyantam ādityaṃ śaśinaṃ vā nimittataḥ  Hbhv 
āstaṃ yāntaṃ na vāristhaṃ nopasṛṣṭaṃ na madhyagam 
tirohitaṃ vāsasā vā na darśāntaragāminam  Hbhv 
nagnāṃ striyaṃ pumāṃsaṃ vā purīṣaṃ mūtram eva vā 
patitavyaṅgacāṇḍālān ucchiṣṭānucchiṣṭān nāvalokayet  Hbhv 
na muktabandhanāṃ gāṃ vā nonmattaṃ mattam eva vā 
spṛśen na bhojane patnīṃ nainām īkṣeta mehatīm  Hbhv 
kṣubantīṃ jṛmbhamāṇāṃ vā nāsanasthāṃ yathā sukham 
nodake cātmano rūpaṃ nakulaṃ śvabhram eva vā  Hbhv 
na śūdrāya matiṃ dadyāt kṛṣaraṃ pāyasaṃ dadhi 
nocchiṣṭaṃ vā ghṛtamadhu na ca kṛṣṇājinaṃ haviḥ  Hbhv 
na kuryāt kasyacit pīḍāṃ sutaṃ śiṣyaṃ ca tāḍayet 
nātmānam avamanyeta dainyaṃ yatnena varjayet 
na ca śiṣyānnaṃ satkuryān nātmānaṃ śaṃsayed budhaḥ  Hbhv 
na nadīṃ ca nadīṃ brūyāt parvateṣu na parvatam 
āvaset tena naivāpi yas tyajet sahavāsinam  Hbhv 
śiro 'bhyaṅgāvaśiṣṭena talenāṅgaṃ na lepayet 
romāṇi ca rahasyāni svāni khāni na ca spṛśet  Hbhv 
na pāṇipādavāṅnetracāpalāni samāśrayet 
nābhihanyāj jalaṃ padbhyāṃ pāṇinā na kadācana  Hbhv 
na ghātayed iṣṭakābhiḥ phalāni na phalena ca 
na mlecchabhāṣaṇaṃ śikṣen na karṣec ca padāsanam  Hbhv 
notsaṅge bhakṣayed bhakṣyān gāṃ ca saṃveśayen na hi 
nākṣaiḥ krīḍen na dhāveta strībhir vādaṃ ca cācaret  Hbhv 
na dantair nakhalomāni chindyāt suptaṃ na bodhayet 
na bālātapam āsevet pretadhūmaṃ vivarjayet  Hbhv 
naikaḥ supyāt śūnyagṛhe svayaṃ nopānahau haret 
nākāraṇād vā niṣṭhīven na bāhubhyāṃ nadīṃ taret  Hbhv 
na pādakṣālanaṃ kuryāt pādenaiva kadācana 
nāgnau pratāpayet pādau na kāṃsye dhārayed budhaḥ  Hbhv 
nābhipratārayed devān brāhmaṇān gām athāpi vā 
na spṛśet pāninocchiṣṭo viprā gobrāhmaṇānalān 
na caivānnaṃ padā vāpi na devapratimāṃ spṛśet  Hbhv 
nottared anupaspṛśya sravantīṃ no vyatikramet 
caityaṃ bṛhmaṃ naiva chindyān nāpsu ṣṭhīvanam utsṛjet 
na cāgniṃ laṅghayed dhīmān nopadadhyād adhaḥ kvacit  Hbhv 
na cainaṃ pādataḥ kuryāt tilabaddhaṃ niśi tyajet 
na kūpam avaroheta nācakṣītāśuciḥ kvacit  Hbhv 
agnau na prakṣiped agniṃ nādbhiḥ praśamayet tathā 
suhṛnmaraṇam ārtiṃ vā na svayaṃ śrāvayet parān 
apaṇyam atha paṇyaṃ vā vikrayaṃ na prayojayet  Hbhv 
puṇyasthānodakasthāne sīmāntaṃ vā kṛṣen na tu 
bhindyāt pūrvasamayaṃ satryopetaṃ kadācana  Hbhv 
parasparaṃ paśūn vyālān pakṣiṇo na ca yodhayet 
kārayitvā svakarmāṇi kārūn vidvān na vañcayet  Hbhv 
bahir gandhaṃ ca kudvārapraveśaṃ ca vivarjayet 
naikaś caret sabhāṃ vipraḥ samavāyaṃ ca varjayet  Hbhv 
na vījayed vā vastreṇa na devāyatane svapet 
nāgnigobrāhmaṇādīnām antareṇa vrajet kvacit  Hbhv 
nākrāmet kāmataś chāyāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ gavām api 
svāntu nākrāmayec chāyaṃ patitādyair na rogibhiḥ  Hbhv 
nāśnīyāt payasā takraṃ na bījāny upabījayet 
vivatsāyāś ca goḥ kṣīram auṣṭraṃ vā nirdaśasya ca 
āvikaṃ sandhinīkṣīram apeyaṃ manur abravīt  Hbhv 
hantakāram athāgryaṃ vā bhikṣāṃ vā śaktito dvijaḥ 
dadyād atithaye nityaṃ budhyeta parameśvaram  Hbhv 
bhikṣām āhur grāsamātram agryaṃ tasmāc caturguṇam 
puṣkalaṃ hantakāraṃ tu tac caturguṇam iṣyate  Hbhv 
mārkaṇḍeye
bhojanaṃ hantakāraṃ vā agryaṃ bhikṣām athāpi vā 
adattvā tu na bhoktavyaṃ yathāvibhavam ātmanaḥ  Hbhv 
kāśīkhaṇḍe
naivotkaṭāsane'śnīyān nāgnau vastv aśuci kṣipet 
śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā paraśrāddhe yo 'śnīyāj jñānavarjitaḥ 
dātuḥ śrāddhaphalaṃ nāsti bhoktā kilbiṣabhug bhavet  Hbhv 
notpāṭayel lomanakhaṃ daśanena kadācana 
karajaiḥ karajacchedaṃ kareṇaiva vivarjayet  Hbhv 
apadvāre na gantavyaṃ svaveśmaparaveśmanoḥ 
utkocadyutadautyārthadravyaṃ dūrāt parityajet  Hbhv 
niṣṭhīvanaṃ ca śleṣmāṇaṃ gṛhād dūre vinikṣipet 
uddhṛtya pañca mṛtpiṇḍān snāyāt parajalāśaye 
anuddhṛtya ca tatkartur enasaḥ syāt turīyabhāk  Hbhv 
brāhme
yas tu pāṇitale bhuṅkte yas tu phutkārasaṃyutam 
prasṛtāṅgulibhir yas tu tasya gomāṃsavac ca tat  Hbhv 
atrismṛtau
nyūnādhikastanī yā gaur yāthavābhakṣyacāriṇī 
tayor dugdhaṃ na hotavyaṃ na pātavyaṃ kadācana  Hbhv 
ajā gāvo mahiṣyaś ca yāmedhyam api bhakṣayet 
havye kavye ca taddugdhaṃ gomayaṃ ca vivarjayet  Hbhv 
aṅgulyā dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca pratyakṣalavaṇaṃ tathā 
mṛttikāprāśanaṃ caiva tulyaṃ gomāṃsabhakṣaṇaiḥ  Hbhv 
atrāpavādo manusmṛtau
sāmudraṃ saindhavaṃ caiva lavaṇe paramādbhute 
pratyakṣe api te grāhye niṣedhas tv anyagocaraḥ  Hbhv 
atrismṛtau
divā kapitthacchāyā ca niśāyāṃ dadhibhojanam 
kārpāsaṃ dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca śakrād api haret śriyam  Hbhv 
viṣṇusmṛtau ca
kapilāyāḥ payaḥ pītvā śūdras tu narakaṃ vrajet 
homaśeṣaṃ pibed vipro vipraḥ syād anyathā paśuḥ  Hbhv 
parihartuṃ punar lekhaṃ tattatśāstroktam anyathā 
yad atra likhitaṃ kiñcit tat kṣantavyaṃ mahātmabhiḥ  Hbhv 
ācārāś cedṛśāḥ santi pare'pi bahulāḥ satām 
te lokaśāstrato jñeyā apekṣyā yadi vaiṣṇavaiḥ  Hbhv 
nityatvam eṣāṃ māhātmyam apy atra likhitāt purā 
sadācārasya nityatvān māhātmyāc ca susidhyati  Hbhv 
iti śrīgopālabhaṭṭavilikhite śrībhagavadbhaktivilāse
nityakṛtyasamāpano nāma
ekādaśo vilāsaḥ
